Chapter 1: upanayanādhyāyaḥ [upanayana-adhyāya]

jayati jagataḥ prasūtirviśvātmā sahajabhūṣaṇaṃ nabhasaḥ | drutakanakasadṛśadaśaśatamayūkhamālārcitaḥ savitā || 1 ||
prathamamunikathitamavitathamavalokya granthavistarasya artham | nātilaghuvipularacanābhirudyataḥ spaṣṭamabhidhātum || 2 ||
muniviracitamidamiti yaccirantanaṃ sādhu na manujagrathitam | tulye'rthe'kṣarabhedādamantrake kā viśeṣoktiḥ || 3 ||
kṣititanayadivasavāro na śubhakṛditi yadi pitāmahaprokte | kujadinamaniṣṭamiti vā ko'tra viśeṣo nṛdivyakṛteḥ || 4 ||
[ kṛte ] ābrahmādiviniḥsṛtamālokya granthavistaraṃ kramaśaḥ | kriyamāṇakameva etatsamāsato'to mamotsāhaḥ || 5 ||
āsīttamaḥ kiledaṃ tatrāpāṃ taijase'bhavaddhaime | svarbhūśakale brahmā viśvakṛdaṇḍe'rkaśaśinayanaḥ || 6 ||
kapilaḥ pradhānamāha dravyādīn kaṇakabhugasya viśvasya | kālaṃ kāraṇameke svabhāvamapare jaguḥ karma || 7 ||
tadalamativistareṇa prasaṅgavādārthanirṇayo'timahān | jyotiḥśāstrāṅgānāṃ vaktavyo nirṇayo'tra mayā || 8 ||
jyotiḥśāstramanekabhedaviṣayaṃ skandhatrayādhiṣṭhitaṃ tatkārtsnyopanayasya nāma munibhiḥ saṃkīrtyate saṃhitā | skandhe'smin gaṇitena yā grahagatistantrābhidhānastvasau horānyo'ṅgaviniścayaśca kathitaḥ skandhastṛtīyo'paraḥ || 9 ||
vakrānuvakrāstamayodayādyāstārāgrahāṇāṃ karaṇe mayoktāḥ | horāgataṃ vistaraśaśca janmayātrāvivāhaiḥ saha pūrvamuktam || 10 ||
praśnapratipraśnakathāprasaṅgān svalpopayogān grahasambhavāmśca | santyajya phalgūni ca sārabhūtaṃ bhūtārthamarthaiḥ sakalaiḥ pravakṣye || 11 ||

Chapter 2: sāṃvatsarasūtrādhyāyaḥ [sāṃvatsarasūtra-adhyāya]

athātaḥ sāṃvatsarasūtraṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || 0(a) ||
tatra sāṃvatsaro'bhijātaḥ priyadarśano vinītaveṣaḥ satyavāganasūyakaḥ samaḥ susaṃhitopacitagātrasandhiravikalaścārukaracaraṇanakhanayanacibukadaśanaśravaṇalalāṭabhrūttamāṅgo vapuṣmān gambhīrodāttaghoṣaḥ | prāyaḥ śarīrākārānuvarttino hi guṇā doṣāśca bhavanti || 0(b) || [ anuvartino ] tatra guṇāḥ—śucirdakṣaḥ pragalbho vāggmī pratibhānavāndeśakālavitsāttviko na parṣadbhīruḥ sahādhyāyibhiranabhibhavanīyaḥ kuśalo'vyasanī śāntikapauṣṭikābhicārasnānavidyābhijño vibudhārcanavratopavāsanirataḥ svatantrāścaryotpāditaprabhāvaḥ pṛṣṭābhidhāyyanyatra daivāt yayādgrahagaṇitasaṃhitāhorāgranthārthavetteti || 0(c) ||
[ vāgmī ] tatra grahagaṇite pauliśaromakavāsiṣṭhasaurapaitāmaheṣu pañcasveteṣu siddhānteṣu yugavarṣāyanartumāsapakṣāhorātrayāmamuhūrtanāḍī prāṇatruṭitruṭyādyavayavādikasya kālasya kṣetrasya ca vettā || 0(d) ||
[ nāḍīvināḍī | ādyasya ] caturṇāṃ ca mānānāṃ saurasāvananākṣatracāndrāṇāmadhimāsakāvamasambhavasya ca kāraṇābhijñaḥ || 0(e) ||
ṣaṣṭyabdayugavarṣamāsadinahorādhipatīnāṃ pratipatticchedavit || 0(f) ||
[ pratipattivi ] saurādīnāṃ ca mānānāmasadṛśasadṛśa yogyāyogyatvapratipādanapaṭuḥ || 0(g) ||
[ sadṛśāsadṛśa ] siddhāntabhede'pyayananivṛttau pratyakṣaṃ samamaṇḍalalekhāsamprayogābhyuditāṃśakānāṃ chāyājalayantradṛggaṇitasāmyena pratipādanakuśalaḥ || 0(h) ||
[ ca ] sūryādīnāṃ ca grahāṇāṃ śīghramandayāmyottaranīcoccagatikāraṇābhijñaḥ || 0(i) ||
sūryacandramasośca grahaṇe grahaṇādimokṣakāladikpramāṇasthitivimardavarṇādeśānāmanāgatagrahasamāgamayuddhānāmādeṣṭā || 0(j) ||
[ deśānām ] pratyekagrahabhramaṇayojanakakṣyāpramāṇaprativiṣayayojanaparicchedakuśalaḥ || 0(k) ||
[ kuśalo ] bhūbhagaṇabhramaṇasaṃsthānādyakṣāvalambakāharvyāsacaradalakālarāśyudayacchāyānāḍīkaraṇaprabhṛtiṣu kṣetrakālakaraṇeṣvabhijñaḥ || 0(l) ||
nānācodyapraśnabhedopalabdhijanitavāksāro nikaṣasantāpābhiniveśaiḥ kanakasyevādhikataramamalīkṛtasya vaktā tantrajño bhavati || 0(m) ||
[ viśuddhasya | śāstrasya | uktañca ] na pratibaddhaṃ gamayati vakti na ca praśnamekamapi pṛṣṭaḥ | nigadati na ca śiṣyebhyaḥ sa kathaṃ śāstrārthavijjñeyaḥ || 1 ||
grantho'nyathānyathārthaṃ karaṇaṃ yaścānyathā karotyabudhaḥ | sa pitāmahamupagamya stauti naro vaiśikenāryām || 2 ||
[ arthaḥ ] tantre suparijñāte lagne chāyāmbuyantrasaṃvidite | horārthe ca surūḍhe nādeṣṭurbhāratī vandhyā || 3 ||
uktan cāryaviṣṇuguptena | apyarṇavasya puruṣaḥ prataran kadā cid | āsādayedanilavegavaśena pāram | na tvasya kālapuruṣākhyamahārṇavasya | gacchetkadā cidanṛṣirmanasāpi pāram || 4 ||
horāśāstre'pi rāśihorādreṣkāṇanavāṃśakadvādaśabhāgatriṃśadbhāgabalābalaparigraho grahāṇāṃ diksthānakālaceṣṭābhiranekaprakārabalanirdhāraṇaṃ prakṛtidhātudravyajāticeṣṭādiparigraho niṣekajanmakālavismāpanapratyayādeśasadyomaraṇāyurdāyadaśāntardaśāṣṭakavargarājayogacandrayogadvigrahādiyogānāṃ nābhasādīnāṃ ca yogānām phalānyāśrayabhāvāvalokananiryāṇagatyanūkāni tatkāla praśnaśubhāśubhanimittāni vivāhādīnāṃ ca karmanāṃ karaṇam || 4(b) ||
[ ca | tātkālika ] yātrāyāṃ tu tithidivasakaraṇanakṣatramuhūrtavilagnayogadehaspandanasvapnavijayasnānagrahayajñagaṇayāgāgniliṅgahastyaśveṅgitasenāpravādaceṣṭādigrahaṣāḍguṇyopāyamaṅgalāmaṅgalaśakunasainyaniveśabhūmayo'gnivarṇā mantricaradūtāṭavikānāṃ yathākālaṃ prayogāḥ paradurgopalambhopāyaścetyuktaṃ cācāryaiḥ || 4(c) ||
[ ca ] jagati prasāritamivālikhitamiva matau niṣiktamiva hṛdaye | śāstraṃ yasya sabhagaṇaṃ nādeśā niṣphalāstasya || 5 ||
[ niḥphalās ] saṃhitāpāragaśca daivacintako bhavati | yatra ete saṃhitāpadārthāḥ || 5(b) ||
dinakarādīnāṃ grahāṇāṃ cārāsteṣu ca teṣāṃ prakṛtivikṛtipramāṇavarṇakiraṇadyutisaṃsthānāstamanodayamārgamārgāntaravakrānuvakrarkṣagrahasamāgamacārādibhiḥ phalāni nakṣatrakūrmavibhāgena deśeṣvagastyacāraḥ | saptarṣicāraḥ |grahabhaktayo nakṣatravyūhagrahaśṛṅgāṭakagrahayuddhagrahasamāgamagrahavarṣaphalagarbhalakṣaṇarohiṇīsvātyāṣāḍhīyogāḥ sadyovarṣakusumalatāparidhipariveṣaparighapavanolkādigdāhakṣiticalanasandhyārāgagandharvanagararajonirghātārghakāṇḍasasyajanmendradhvajendracāpavāstuvidyāṅgavidyāvāyasavidyāntaracakramṛgacakraśvacakravātacakraprāsādalakṣaṇapratimālakṣaṇapratiṣṭhāpanavṛkṣāyurvedodagārgalanīrājanakhañjanakotpātaśāntimayūracitrakaghṛtakambalakhaḍgapaṭṭakṛkavākukūrmago'jāśvebhapurūṣastrīlakṣaṇānyantaḥpuracintāpiṭakalakṣaṇopānacchedavastracchedacāmaradaṇḍaśayanāsanalakṣaṇaratnaparīkṣā dīpalakṣaṇaṃ dantakāṣṭhādyāśritāni śubhāśubhāni nimittāni sāmānyāni ca jagataḥ pratipuruṣaṃ pārthive ca pratikṣaṇamananyakarmābhiyuktena daivajñena cintayitavyāni | na caikākinā śakyante'harniśamavadhārayituṃ nimittāni | tasmātsubhṛtenaiva daivajñena anye'pitadvidaścatvāraḥ kartavyāḥ |tatraikenaindrī cāgneyī ca digavalokayitavyā | yāmyā nairṛtī cānyenaivaṃ vāruṇī vāyavyā cottarā caiśāni ceti | yasmādulkāpātādīni śīghramapagacchatīti | tasyāścākāravarṇasnehapramānādigraharkṣopaghātādibhiḥ phalāni bhavanti || 5(d) || [ agasticāraḥ | khañjana | puruṣa | śayyā | bhartavyāḥ | nimittāni | upagacchati | teṣāṃ ] uktaṃ ca gargeṇa maharṣiṇā | kṛtsnāṅgopāṅgakuśalaṃ horāgaṇitanaiṣṭhikam || 6 ||
yo na pūjayate rājā sa nāśamupāgacchati || 6 ||
vanaṃ samāśritā ye'pi nirmamā niṣparigrahāḥ | api te paripṛcchanti jyotiṣāṃ gatikovidam || 7 ||
apradīpā yathā rātriranādityaṃ yathā nabhaḥ | tathāsāṃvatsaro rājā bhramyatyandha ivādhvani || 8 ||
muhūrtatithinakṣatramṛtavaścāyane tathā | sarvāṇyevākulāni syurna syātsāṃvatsaro yadi || 9 ||
[ muhūrtaṃ ] tasmād rājñādhigantavyo vidvān sāṃvatsaro'graṇīḥ | jayaṃ yaśaḥ śriyaṃ bhogācchreyaśca samabhīpsatā || 10 ||
nāsāṃvatsarike deśe vastavyaṃ bhūtimicchatā | cakṣurbhūto hi yatraiṣa pāpaṃ tatra na vidyate || 11 ||
na sāṃvatsarapāṭhī ca narakeṣūpapadyate | brahmalokapratiṣṭhāṃ ca labhate daivacintakaḥ || 12 ||
granthataścārthataścaitatkṛtsnaṃ jānati yo dvijaḥ | agrabhuksa bhavecchrāddhe pūjitaḥ paṅktipāvanaḥ || 13 ||
mlecchā hi yavanāsteṣu samyak śāstramidaṃ sthitam | ṛṣivatte'pi pūjyante kiṃ punardaivaviddvijaḥ || 14 ||
kuhakāveśapihitaiḥ karṇopaśrutihetubhiḥ | kṛtādeśo na sarvatra praṣṭavyo na sa daivavit || 15 ||
aviditvaiva yacchāstraṃ daivajñatvaṃ prapadyate | sa paṅktidūṣakaḥ pāpo jñeyo nakṣatrasūcakaḥ || 16 ||
[ yaḥ ] nakṣatrasūcakoddiṣṭamupahāsaṃ karoti yaḥ | sa vrajatyandhatāmisraṃ sārdhamṛkṣaviḍambinā || K(18) ||
nagaradvāraloṣṭasya yadvatsyādupayācitam | ādeśastadvadajñānāṃ yaḥ satyaḥ sa vibhāvyate || 17 ||
sampattyā yojitādeśastadvicchinnakathāpriyaḥ | mattaḥ śāstraikadeśena tyājyastādṛgmahīkṣitā || 18 ||
yastu samyagvijānāti horāgaṇitasaṃhitāḥ | abhyarcyaḥ sa narendreṇa svīkartavyo jayaiṣiṇā || 19 ||
na tatsahasraṃ kariṇāṃ vājināṃ ca caturguṇam | karoti deśakālajño yathaikodaivacintakaḥ || 20 ||
[ yadeko ] duḥsvapnadurvicintitaduṣprekṣitaduṣkṛtāni karmāṇi | kṣipraṃ prayānti nāśaṃ śaśinaḥ śrutvā bhasaṃvādam || 21 ||
na tathecchati bhūpateḥ pitā jananī vā svajano'tha vā suhṛt | svayaśo'bhivivṛddhaye yathā hitamāptaḥ sabalasya daivavit || 22 ||

Chapter 3: ādityacārādhyāyaḥ [ādityacāra-adhyāya]

āśleṣārdhāddakṣiṇamuttaramayanaṃ raverdhaniṣṭhādyam | nūnaṃ kadā cidāsīd yenoktam pūrvaśāstreṣu || 1 ||
sāmpratamayanaṃ savituḥ karkaṭakādyaṃ mṛgāditaścānyat | uktābhāvo vikṛtiḥ pratyakṣaparīkṣaṇairvyaktiḥ || 2 ||
dūrasthacihnavedhādudaye'stamaye'pi vā sahasrāṃśoḥ | chāyāpraveśanirgamacihnairvā maṇḍale mahati || 3 ||
aprāpya makaramarko vinivṛtto hanti sāparām yāmyām | karkaṭakamasamprāpto vinivṛttaścottarāṃ saindrīm || 4 ||
uttaramayanamatītya vyāvṛttaḥ kṣemasasyavṛddhikaraḥ | prakṛtisthaścāpyevaṃ vikṛtagatirbhayakṛduṣṇāṃśuḥ || 5 ||
satamaskaṃ parva vinā tvaṣṭā nāmārkamaṇḍalaṃ kurute | sa nihanti sapta bhūpān janāṃśca śastrāgnidurbhikṣaiḥ || 6 ||
tāmasakīlakasaṃjñā rāhusutāḥ ketavastrayastriṃśat | varṇasthānākāraistāndṛṣṭvārke phalaṃ brūyāt || 7 ||
te cārkamaṇḍalagatāḥ pāpaphalāścandramaṇḍale saumyāḥ | dhvāṅkṣakabandhapraharaṇarūpāḥ pāpāḥ śaśāṅke'pi || 8 ||
teṣāmudaye rūpāṇyambhaḥ kaluṣaṃ rajovṛtaṃ vyoma | nagataruśikharāmardī saśarkaro mārutaścaṇḍaḥ || 9 ||
[ vimardī ] ṛtuviparītāstaravo dīptā mṛgapakṣiṇo diśāṃ dāhāḥ | nirghātamahīkampādayo bhavantyatra cotpātāḥ || 10 ||
na pṛthakphalāni teṣāṃ śikhikīlakarāhudarśanāni yadi | tadudayakāraṇameṣāṃ ketvādīnām phalaṃ brūyāt || 11 ||
yasminyasmindeśe darśanamāyānti sūryabimbasthā | tasmiṃstasminvyasanaṃ mahīpatīnām parijñeyam || 12 ||
kṣutpramlānaśarīrā munayo'pyutsṛṣṭadharmasaccaritāḥ | nirmāṃsabālahastāḥ kṛcchreṇāyānti paradeśam || 13 ||
[ paradeśān ] taskaraviluptavittāḥ pradīrghaniḥśvāsamukulitākṣipuṭāḥ | santaḥ sannaśarīrāḥ śokodbhavavāṣpa ruddhadṛśaḥ || 14 ||
[ bāṣpa ] kṣāmā jugupsamānāḥ svanṛpatiparacakrapīḍitā manujāḥ | svanṛpaticaritaṃ karma na purā kṛtaṃ prabruvantyanye || 15 ||
[ ca | parākṛtaṃ | purākṛtaṃ ] garbheṣvapi niṣpannā vārimuco na prabhūtavārimucaḥ | sarito yānti tanutvaṃ kva citkvacijjāyate sasyam || 16 ||
daṇḍe narendramṛtyurvyādhibhayaṃ syātkabandhasaṃsthāne | dhvāṅkṣe ca taskarabhayaṃ durbhikṣaṃ kīlake'rkasthe || 17 ||
[ kavandhasaṃsthāne ] rājopakaraṇarūpaiśchatradhvajacāmarādibhirviddhaḥ | rājānyatvakṛdarkaḥ sphuliṅgadhūmādibhirjanahā || 18 ||
eko durbhikṣakaro dvyādyāḥ syurnarapatervināśāya | sitaraktapītakṛṣṇaistairviddho'rko'nuvarṇaghnaḥ || 19 ||
dvaśyante ca yataste ravibimbasyotthitā mahotpātāḥ | āgacchati lokānāṃ tenaiva bhayaṃ pradeśena || 20 ||
[ dṛśyante ] ūrdhvakaro divasakarastāmraḥ senāpatiṃ vināśayati | pīto narendraputraṃ śvetastu purohitaṃ hanti || 21 ||
citro'tha vāpi dhūmro raviraśmirvyākulāṃ karotyūrdham | taskaraśastranipātairyadi salilaṃ nāśu pātayati || 22 ||
[ vyākulāṃ | mahīm ] tāmraḥ kapilo vārkaḥ śiśire harikuṅkumacchaviśca madhau | āpāṇḍukanakavarṇo grīṣme varṣāsu śuklaśca || 23 ||
śaradi kamalodarābho hemante rudhirasannibhaḥ śastaḥ | prāvṛṭkāle snigdhaḥ sarvartunibho'pi śubhadāyī || 24 ||
rūkṣaḥ śveto viprān raktābhaḥ kṣatriyānvināśayati | pīto vaiśyān kṛṣṇastato aparācchubhakaraḥ snigdhaḥ || 25 ||
grīṣme rakto bhayakṛdvarṣāsvasitaḥ karotyanāvṛṣṭim | hemante pīto'rkaḥ karoti na cireṇa rogabhayam || 26 ||
[ acireṇa ] suracāpapāṭitatanurnṛpativirodhapradaḥ sahasrāṃśuḥ | prāvṛṭkāle sadyaḥ karoti vimaladyutirvṛṣṭim || 27 ||
varṣākāle vṛṣṭiṃ karoti sadyaḥ śirīṣapuṣpābhaḥ | śikhipatranibhaḥ salilaṃ na karoti dvādaśābdāni || 28 ||
śyāme'rke kīṭabhayaṃ bhasmanibhe bhayamuśanti paracakrāt | yasyarkṣe sacchidrastasya vināśaḥ kṣitīśasya || 29 ||
śaśarudhiranibhe bhānau nabhastalasthe bhavanti saṅgrāmāḥ | śaśisadṛśe nṛpatibadhaḥ kṣipraṃ cānyo nṛpo bhavati || 30 ||
[ nṛpativaddhaḥ ] kṣutmārakṛt ghaṭanibhaḥ khaṇḍo janahā vidīdhitirbhayadaḥ | toraṇarūpaḥ purahā chatranibho deśanāśāya || 31 ||
[ nṛpahā ] dhvajacāpanibhe yuddhāni bhāskare vepane ca rūkṣe ca | kṛṣṇā rekhā savitari yadi hanti tato nṛpaṃ sacivaḥ || 32 ||
[ nṛpaṃ tataḥ ] dinakaramudayāstasaṃsthitamulkāśanividyuto yadā hanyuḥ | narapatimaraṇaṃ vindyāttadānyarājapratiṣṭhā ca || 33 ||
[ divasakaram | udayasaṃsthitam | pratiṣṭhāṃ ] pratidivasamahimakiraṇaḥ pariveṣī sandhyayordvayoratha vā | rakto'stameti raktoditaśca bhūpaṃ karotyanyam || 34 ||
praharaṇasadṛśairjaladaiḥ sthagitaḥ sandhyādvaye'pi raṇakārī | mṛgamahiṣavihagakharakarabhasadṛśarūpaiśca bhayadāyī || 35 ||
dinakarakarābhitāpādṛkṣamavāpnoti sumahatīm pīḍām | bhavati tu paścācchuddhaṃ kanakamiva hutāśaparitāpāt || 36 ||
divasakṛtaḥ pratisūryo jalakṛdudagdakṣiṇe sthito'nilakṛt | ubhayasthaḥ salilabhayaṃ nṛpamupari nihantyadho janahā || 37 ||
rudhiranibho viyatyavanipāntakaro na cirātparuṣarajo'ruṇīkṛtatanuryadi vā dinakṛt | asitavicitranīlaparuṣo janaghātakaraḥ khagamṛgabhairavasvararutaiśca niśādyumukhe || 38 ||
amalavapuravakramaṇḍalaḥ sphuṭavipulāmaladīrghadīdhitiḥ | avikṛtatanuvarṇacihnabhṛjjagati karoti śivaṃ divākaraḥ || 39 ||

Chapter 4: candracārādhyāyaḥ [candracāra-adhyāya]

nityamadhaḥsthasyendorbhābhirbhānoḥ sitaṃ bhavatyardham | svacchāyayānyadasitaṃ kumbhasyevātapasthasya || 1 ||
salilamaye śaśini raverdīdhitayo mūrchitāstamo naiśam | kṣapayanti darpaṇodara nihitā iva mandirasyāntaḥ || 2 ||
[ nihatā ] tyajato'rkatalaṃ śaśinaḥ paścādavalambate yathā śauklyam | dinakaravaśāttathendoḥ prakāśate'dhaḥ prabhṛtyudayaḥ || 3 ||
pratidivasamevamarkātsthānaviśeṣeṇa śauklyaparivṛddhiḥ | bhavati śaśino'parāhṇe paścādbhāge ghaṭasyeva || 4 ||
aindrasya śītakiraṇo mūlāṣāḍhādvayasya cāyātaḥ | yāmyena vījajalacarakānanahā vahnibhayadaśca || 5 ||
[ vā yātaḥ | bīja ] dakṣiṇapārśvena gataḥ śaśī viśākhānurādhayoḥ pāpaḥ | madhyena tu praśastaḥ pitṛdevaviśākhayoścāpi || 6 ||
[ pitryasya ] ṣaḍanāgatāni pauṣṇāddvādaśa raudrācca madhyayogīni | jyeṣṭhādyāni navarkṣāṇyuḍupatinātītya yujyante || 7 ||
unnatamīṣacchṛṅgaṃ nausaṃsthāne viśālatā coktā | nāvikapīḍā tasminbhavati śivaṃ sarvalokasya || 8 ||
arddhonnate ca lāṅgalamiti pīḍā tadupajīvināṃ tasmin | prītiśca nirnimittaṃ manujapatīnāṃ subhikṣaṃ ca || 9 ||
dakṣiṇaviṣāṇamardhonnataṃ yadā duṣṭalāṅgalākhyaṃ tat | pāṇḍyanareśvaranidhanakṛdudyogakaraṃ balānāṃ ca || 10 ||
samaśaśini subhikṣakṣemavṛṣṭayaḥ prathamadivasasadṛśāḥ syuḥ | daṇḍavadudite pīḍā gavāṃ nṛpaścogradaṇḍo'tra || 11 ||
kārmukarūpe yuddhāni yatra tu jyā tato jayasteṣām | sthānaṃ yugamiti yāmyottarāyataṃ bhūmikampāya || 12 ||
yugameva yāmyakoṭyāṃ kiṃ cittuṅgaṃ sa pārśvaśāyīti | vinihanti sārthavāhānvṛṣṭeśca vinigrahaṃ kuryāt || 13 ||
abhyucchrāyādekaṃ yadi śaśino'vāṅmukhaṃ bhavecchṛṅgam | āvarjitamityasubhikṣakāri tadgodhanasyāpi || 14 ||
avyucchinnā rekhā samantato maṇḍalā ca kuṇḍākhyam | asminmāṇḍalikānāṃ sthānatyāgo narapatīnām || 15 ||
proktasthānābhāvādudaguccaḥ kṣemavṛddhivṛṣṭikaraḥ | dakṣiṇatuṅgaścandro durbhikṣabhayāya nirdiṣṭaḥ || 16 ||
śṛṅgeṇaikenendurvilīnamatha vāpyavāṅmukhaṃ śṛṅgam | sampūrṇaṃ cābhinavaṃ dṛṣṭvaiko jīvitādbhraśyet || 17 ||
[ induṃ | aśṛṅgam ] saṃsthānavidhiḥ kathito rūpāṇyasmādbhavanti candramasaḥ | svalpo durbhikṣakaro mahān subhikṣāvahaḥ proktaḥ || 18 ||
madhyatanurvajrākhyaḥ kṣudbhayadaḥ sambhramāya rājñāṃ ca | candro mṛdaṅgarūpaḥ kṣemasubhikṣāvaho bhavati || 19 ||
jñeyo viśālamūrtirnarapatilakṣmīvivṛddhaye candraḥ | sthūlaḥ subhikṣakārī priyadhānyakarastu tanumūrtiḥ || 20 ||
pratyantān kunṛpāṃśca hantyuḍupatiḥ śṛṅge kujenāhate śastrakṣudbhayakṛd yamena śaśijenāvṛṣṭidurbhikṣakṛt | śreṣṭhān hanti nṛpānmahendraguruṇā śukreṇa cālpānnṛpācchukle yāpyamidaṃ phalaṃ grahakṛtaṃ kṛṣṇe yathoktāgamam || 21 ||
bhinnaḥ sitena magadhānyavanānpulindānnepālabhṛṅgimarukacchasurāṣṭramadrān | pāñcālakaikayakulūtakapuruṣādān hanyāduśīnarajanānapi sapta māsān || 22 ||
[ marukucca ] gāndhārasauvīrakasindhukīrāndhānyāni śailāndraviḍādhipāṃśca | dvijāṃśca māsāndaśa śītaraśmiḥ santāpayedvākpatinā vibhinnaḥ || 23 ||
udyuktān saha vāhanairnarapatīṃstraigartakānmālavān kaulindān gaṇapuṅgavānatha śibīnāyodhyakānpārthivān | hanyātkauravamatsyaśuktyadhipatīn rājanyamukhyānapi prāleyāṃśurasṛggrahe tanugate ṣaṇmāsamaryādayā || 24 ||
yaudheyān sacivān sakauravānprāgīśānatha cārjunāyanān | hanyādarkajabhinnamaṇḍalaḥ śītāṃśurdaśamāsapīḍayā || 25 ||
magadhānmathurāṃ ca pīḍayedveṇāyāśca taṭaṃ śaśāṅkajaḥ | aparatra kṛtaṃ yugaṃ vaded yadi bhittvā śaśinaṃ vinirgataḥ || 26 ||
kṣemārogyasubhikṣavināśī śītāṃśuḥ śikhinā yadi bhinnaḥ | kuryādāyudhajīvivināśaṃ caurāṇāmadhikena ca pīḍām || 27 ||
ulkayā yadā śaśī grasta eva hanyate | hanyate tadā nṛpo yasya janmani sthitaḥ || 28 ||
bhasmanibhaḥ paruṣo'ruṇamūrtiḥ śītakaraḥ kiraṇaiḥ parihīṇaḥ | śyāvatanuḥ sphuṭitaḥ sphuraṇo vā kṣuḍḍamarāmayacaurabhayāya || 29 ||
[ kṣutsamarā ] prāleyakundakumudasphaṭikāvadāto yatnādivādrisutayā parimṛjya candraḥ | uccaiḥ kṛto niśi bhaviṣyati me śivāya yo dṛśyate sa bhavitā jagataḥ śivāya || 30 ||
śukle pakṣe sampravṛddhe pravṛddhiṃ brahmakṣatraṃ yāti vṛddhiṃ prajāśca | hīne hānistulyatā tulyatāyāṃ kṛṣṇe sarve tatphalaṃ vyatyayena || 31 ||
yadi kumudamṛṇālahāragaurastithiniyamātkṣayameti varddhate vā | avikṛtagatimaṇḍalāṃśuyogī bhavati nṛṇāṃ vijayāya śītaraśmiḥ || 32 ||

Chapter 5: rāhucārādhyāyaḥ [rāhucāra-adhyāya]

amṛtāsvādaviśeṣāccchinnamapi śiraḥ kilāsurasyedam | prāṇairaparityaktaṃ grahatāṃ yātaṃ vadantyeke || 1 ||
indvarkamaṇḍalākṛtirasitatvātkila na dṛśyate gagane | anyatra parvakālādvarapradānātkamalayoneḥ || 2 ||
mukhapucchavibhaktāṅgaṃ bhujaṅgamākāramupadiśantyanye | kathayantyamūrtamapare tamomayaṃ saiṃhikeyākhyākhyam || 3 ||
yadi mūrto bhavicārī śiro'tha vā bhavati maṇḍalī rāhuḥ | bhagaṇārdhenāntaritau gṛhṇāti kathaṃ niyatacāraḥ || 4 ||
[ antarito ] aniyatacāraḥ khalu cedupalabdhiḥ saṃkhyayā kathaṃ tasya | pucchānanābhidhāno'ntareṇa kasmānna gṛhṇāti || 5 ||
atha tu bhujagendrarūpaḥ pucchena mukhena vā sa gṛhṇāti | mukhapucchāntarasaṃsthaṃ sthagayati kasmānna bhagaṇārdham || 6 ||
rāhudvayaṃ yadi syādgraste'stamite'tha vodite candre | tatsamagatinānyena grastaḥ sūryo'pi dṛśyate || 7 ||
bhūcchāyāṃ svagrahaṇe bhāskaramarkagrahe praviśatīnduḥ | pragrahaṇamataḥ paścānnendorbhānośca pūrvārdhāt || 8 ||
vṛkṣasya svacchāyā yathaikapārśve bhavati dīrghacayā | niśi niśi tadvadbhūmerāvaraṇavaśāddineśasya || 9 ||
[ ekapārśvena | dīrghā ca ] sūryātsaptamarāśau yadi codagdakṣiṇena nātigataḥ | candraḥ pūrvābhimukhaśchāyāmaurvīm tadā viśati || 10 ||
candro'dhaḥsthaḥ sthagayati ravimambudavatsamāgataḥ paścāt | pratideśamataścitraṃ dṛṣṭivaśādbhāskaragrahaṇam || 11 ||
āvaraṇaṃ mahadindoḥ kuṇṭhaviṣāṇastato'rdhasaṃcchannaḥ | svalpam raveryato'tastīkṣṇaviṣāṇo ravirbhavati || 12 ||
evamuparāgakāraṇamuktamidaṃ divyadṛgbhirācāryaiḥ | rāhurakāraṇamasminnityuktaḥ śāstrasadbhāvaḥ || 13 ||
yo'sāvasuro rāhustasya varo brahmaṇāyamājñaptaḥ | āpyāyanamuparāge dattahutāṃśena te bhavitā || 14 ||
tasmin kāle sānnidhyamasya tenopacaryate rāhuḥ | yāmyottarā śaśigatirgaṇite'pyupacaryate tena || 15 ||
na kathaṃ cidapi nimittairgrahaṇaṃ vijñāyate nimittāni | anyasminnapi kāle bhavantyathotpātarūpāṇi || 16 ||
pañcagrahasaṃyogānna kila grahaṇasya sambhavo bhavati | tailaṃ ca jale'ṣṭamyāṃ na vicintyamidaṃ vipaścidbhiḥ || 17 ||
avanatyārke grāso digjñeyā valanayāvanatyā ca | tithyavasānādvelā karaṇe kathitāni tāni mayā || 18 ||
ṣaṇmāsottaravṛddhyā parveśāḥ sapta devatāḥ kramaśaḥ | brahmaśaśīndrakuberā varuṇāgniyamāśca vijñeyāḥ || 19 ||
brāhme dvijapaśuvṛddhiḥ kṣemārogyāṇi sasyasampacca | tadvatsaumye tasminpīḍā viduṣāmavṛṣṭiśca || 20 ||
[ vṛddhikṣemārogyāṇi ] aindre bhūpavirodhaḥ śāradasasyakṣayo na ca kṣemam | kaubere'rthapatīnāmarthavināśaḥ subhikṣaṃ ca || 21 ||
vāruṇamavanīśāśubhamanyeṣāṃ kṣemasasyavṛddhikaram | āgneyaṃ mitrākhyaṃ sasyārogyābhayāmbukaram || 22 ||
yāmyaṃ karotyavṛṣṭiṃ durbhikṣaṃ saṃkṣayaṃ ca sasyānām | yadataḥ paraṃ tadaśubhaṃ kṣutmārāvṛṣṭidaṃ parva || 23 ||
velāhīne parvaṇi garbhavipattiśca śastrakopaśca | ativele kusumaphalakṣayo bhayaṃ sasyanāśaśca || 24 ||
hīnātiriktakāle phalamuktaṃ pūrvaśāstradṛṣṭatvāt | sphuṭagaṇitavidaḥ kālaḥ kathañcidapi nānyathā bhavati || 25 ||
yadyekasminmāse grahaṇaṃ ravisomayostadā kṣitipāḥ | svabalakṣobhaiḥ saṃkṣayamāyāntyatiśastrakopaśca || 26 ||
grastāv uditāstamitau śāradadhānyāvanīśvarakṣayadau | sarvagrastau durbhikṣamarakadau pāpasandṛṣṭau || 27 ||
ardhoditoparakto naikṛtikān hanti sarvayajñāṃśca | agnyupajīviguṇādhikaviprāśramiṇo yuge'bhyuditaḥ || 28 ||
[ ayugābhyuditaḥ ] karṣakapākhaṇḍivaṇikkṣatriyabalanāyakāndvitīyāṃśe | kārukaśūdramlecchān khatṛtīyāmśe samantrijanān || 29 ||
[ pāṣaṇḍi | dvitīye'ṃśe ] madhyāhne narapatimadhyadeśahā śobhanaśca dhānyārghaḥ | tṛṇabhugamātyāntaḥpuravaiśyaghnaḥ pañcame khāṃśe || 30 ||
strīśūdrān ṣaṣṭhe'ṃśe dasyupratyantahāstamayakāle | yasmin khāṃśe mokṣastatproktānāṃ śivaṃ bhavati || 31 ||
dvijanṛpatīnudagayane viṭśūdrāndakṣiṇāyane hanti | rāhurudagādidṛṣṭaḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ hanti viprādīn || 32 ||
mlecchānvidiksthito yāyinaśca hanyāddhutāśasaktāṃśca | salilacaradantighātī yāmyenodaggavāmaśubhaḥ || 33 ||
pūrveṇa salilapūrṇāṃ karoti vasudhāṃ samāgato daityaḥ | paścātkarṣakasevakabījavināśāya nirdiṣṭaḥ || 34 ||
pāñcālakaliṅgaśūrasenāḥ kāmbojoḍrakirātaśastravārttāḥ | jīvanti ca ye hutāśavṛttyā te pīḍāmupayānti meṣasaṃsthe || 35 ||
gopāḥ paśavo'tha gomino manujā ye ca mahattvamāgatāḥ | pīḍāmupayānti bhāskare graste śītakare'tha vā vṛṣe || 36 ||
mithune pravarāṅganā nṛpā nṛpamātrā balinaḥ kalāvidaḥ | yamunātaṭajāḥ sabāhlikā matsyāḥ suhmajanaiḥ samanvitāḥ || 37 ||
ābhīrāñśabarān sapahlavānmallānmatsyakurūñchakānapi | pāñcālānvikalāṃśca pīḍayatyannaṃ cāpi nihanti karkaṭe || 38 ||
siṃhe pulindagaṇamekalasattvayuktān rājopamānnarapatīnvanagocarāṃśca | ṣaṣṭhe tu sasyakavilekhakageyasaktān hantyaśmakatripuraśāliyutāṃśca deśān || 39 ||
tulādhare'vantyaparāntyasādhūnvaṇigdaśārṇānmarukacchapāṃśca | alinyathodumbaramadracolāndrumān sayaudheyaviṣāyudhīyān || 40 ||
[ bharukacchapāṃś ] dhanvinyamātyavaravājividehamallānpāñcālavaidyavaṇijo viṣamāyudhajñān | hanyānmṛge tu jhaṣamantrikulāni nīcānmantrauṣadhīṣu kuśalān sthavirāyudhīyān || 41 ||
kumbhe'ntargirijān sapaścimajanānbhārodvahāṃstaskarānābhīrāndaradāryasiṃhapurakān hanyāttathā barbarān | mīne sāgarakūlasāgarajaladravyāṇi vanyān janānprājñānvāryupajīvinaśca bhaphalaṃ kūrmopadeśādvadet || 42 ||
[ mānyān ] savyāpasavyalehagrasananirodhāvamardanārohāḥ | āghrātaṃ madhyatamastamo'ntya iti te daśa grāsāḥ || 43 ||
savyagate tamasi jagajjalaplutaṃ bhavati muditamabhayaṃ ca | apasavye narapatitaskarāvamardaiḥ prajānāśaḥ || 44 ||
jihvopaleḍhi paritastimiranudo maṇḍalaṃ yadi sa lehaḥ | pramuditasamastabhūtā prabhūtatoyā ca tatra mahī || 45 ||
[ jihvevaleḍhi ] grasanamiti yadā tryaṃśaḥ pādo vā gṛhyate'tha vāpyardham | sphītanṛpavittahāniḥ pīḍā ca sphītadeśānām || 46 ||
paryanteṣu gṛhītvā madhye piṇḍīkṛtaṃ tamastiṣṭhet | sa nirodho vijñeyaḥ pramodakṛtsarvabhūtānām || 47 ||
avamardanamiti niḥśeṣameva sañchādya yadi ciraṃ tiṣṭhet | hanyātpradhānabhūpānpradhānadeśāṃśca timiramayaḥ || 48 ||
[ pradhānadeśānpradhānabhūpāṃś ] vṛtte grahe yadi tamastatkṣaṇamāvṛtya dṛśyate bhūyaḥ | ārohaṇamityanyonyamardanairbhayakaraṃ rājñām || 49 ||
darpaṇa ivaikadeśe sabāṣpaniḥśvāsamārutopahataḥ | dṛśyetāghrātaṃ tatsuvṛṣṭivṛddhyāvahaṃ jagataḥ || 50 ||
[ savāṣpa ] madhye tamaḥ praviṣṭaṃ vitamaskaṃ maṇḍalaṃ ca yadi paritaḥ | tanmadhyadeśanāśaṃ karoti kukṣyāmayabhayaṃ ca || 51 ||
paryanteṣvatibahulaṃ svalpaṃ madhye tamastamontyākhye | sasyānāmītibhayaṃ bhayamasmiṃstaskarāṇāṃ ca || 52 ||
śvete kṣemasubhikṣaṃ brāhmaṇapīḍāṃ ca nirdiśed rāhau | agnibhayamanalavarṇe pīḍā ca hutāśavṛttīnām || 53 ||
harite rogolbaṇatā sasyānāmītibhiśca vidhvaṃsaḥ | kapile śīghragasattvamlecchadhvaṃso'tha durbhikṣam || 54 ||
[ ulvaṇatā ] aruṇakiraṇānurūpe durbhikṣāvṛṣṭayo vihagapīḍā | ādhūmre kṣemasubhikṣamādiśetmandavṛṣṭiṃ ca || 55 ||
kāpotāruṇakapilaśyāvābhe kṣudbhayaṃ vinirdeśyam | kāpotaḥ śūdrāṇāṃ vyādhikaraḥ kṛṣṇavarṇaśca || 56 ||
vimalakamaṇipītābho vaiśyadhvaṃsī bhavetsubhikṣāya | sārciṣmatyagnibhayaṃ gairikarūpe tu yuddhāni || 57 ||
dūrvākāṇḍaśyāme hāridre vāpi nirdiśetmarakam | aśanibhayasampradāyī pāṭalakusumopamo rāhuḥ || 58 ||
[ pāṭali ] pāṃśuvilohitarūpaḥ kṣatradhvaṃsāya bhavati vṛṣṭeśca | bālaravikamalasuracāparūpabhṛt śastrakopāya || 59 ||
paśyan grastaṃ saumyo ghṛtamadhutailakṣayāya rājṇāṃ ca | bhaumaḥ samaravimardaṃ śikhikopaṃ taskarabhayaṃ ca || 60 ||
śukraḥ sasyavimardaṃ nānākleśāṃśca janayati dharitryām | ravijaḥ karotyavṛṣṭiṃ durbhikṣaṃ taskarabhayaṃ ca || 61 ||
yadaśubhamavalokanābhiruktaṃ grahajanitaṃ grahaṇe pramokṣaṇe vā | surapatiguruṇāvalokite tacchamamupayāti jalairivāgniriddhaḥ || 62 ||
graste kramānnimittaiḥ punargraho māsaṣaṭkaparivṛddhyā | pavanolkāpātarajaḥ kṣitikampatamo'śaninipātaiḥ || 63 ||
āvantikā janapadāḥ kāverīnarmadātaṭāśrayiṇaḥ | dṛptāśca manujapatayaḥ pīḍyante kṣitisute graste || 64 ||
antarvedīṃ sarayūṃ nepālaṃ pūrvasāgaraṃ śoṇam | strīnṛpayodhakumārān saha vidvadbhirbudho hanti || 65 ||
grahaṇopagate jīve vidvannṛpamantrigajahayadhvaṃsaḥ | sindhutaṭavāsināmapyudagdiśaṃ saṃśritānāṃ ca || 66 ||
bhṛgutanaye rāhugate dāśeraka kaikayāḥ sayaudheyāḥ | āryāvarttāḥ śibayaḥ strīsacivagaṇāśca pīḍyante || 67 ||
[ daserakāḥ ] saure marubhavapuṣkara saurāṣṭrikadhātavo'rbudāntyajanāḥ | gomantapāriyātrāśritāśca nāśaṃ vrajantyāśu || 68 ||
[ saurāṣṭrā | gomantaḥ pāriyātrā ] kārttikyāmanalopajīvimagadhānprācyādhipān kośalān kalmāṣānatha śūrasenasahitān kāśīśca santāpayet | hanyādāśu kaliṅgadeśanṛpatiṃ sāmātyabhṛtyaṃ tamo dṛṣṭaṃ kṣatriyatāpadaṃ janayati kṣemaṃ subhikṣānvitam || 69 ||
[ hanyād ca ] kāśmīrakān kauśalakān sapuṇḍrānmṛgāṃśca hanyādaparāntakāṃśca | ye somapāstāṃśca nihanty saumye suvṛṣṭikṛtkṣemasubhikṣakṛcca || 70 ||
pauṣe dvijakṣatrajanoparodhaḥ sasaindhavākhyāḥ kukurā videhāḥ | dhvaṃsaṃ vrajantyatra ca mandavṛṣṭiṃ bhayaṃ ca vindyādasubhikṣayutam || 71 ||
māghe tu mātṛpitṛbhaktavasiṣṭhagotrān svādhyāyadharmaniratān kariṇasturaṅgān | vaṅgāṅgakāśimanujāṃśca dunoti rāhurvṛṣṭiṃ ca karṣakajanābhimatāṃ karoti || 72 ||
[ anumatāṃ ] pīḍākaraṃ phālgunamāsi parva vaṅgāśmakāvantikamekalānām | nṛtyajñasasyapravarāṅganānāṃ dhanuṣkarakṣatratapasvināṃ ca || 73 ||
[ vantaka | nṛttajña ] caitryāṃ tu citrakaralekhageyasaktān rūpopajīvinigamajñahiraṇyapaṇyān | pauṇḍrauḍrakaikayajanānatha cāśmakāṃśca tāpaḥ spṛśatyamarapo'tra vicitravarṣī || 74 ||
[ caitre ] vaiśākhamāse grahaṇe vināśamāyānti karpāsatilāḥ samudgāḥ | ikṣvākuyaudheyaśakāḥ kaliṅgāḥ sopaplavāḥ kintu subhikṣamasmin || 75 ||
[ māsi | sopadravāḥ ] jyeṣṭhe narendradvijarājapatnyaḥ sasyāni vṛṣṭiśca mahāgaṇāśca | pradhvaṃsamāyānti narāśca saumyāḥ sālvaiḥ sametāśca niṣādasaṅghāḥ || 76 ||
[ jyaiṣṭhe ] āṣāḍhaparvaṇyudapānavapranadīpravāhānphalamūlavārttān | gāndhārakāśmīrapulindacīnān hatānvadedmaṇḍalavarṣamasmin || 77 ||
kāśmīrān sapulindacīnayavanān hanyātkurukṣetrajān gāndhārānapi madhyadeśasahitānvṛṣṭo grahaḥ śrāvaṇe | kāmbojaikaśaphāṃśca śāradamapi tyaktvā yathoktānimānanyatra pracurānnahṛṣṭamanujairdhātrīṃ karotyāvṛtām || 78 ||
kaliṅgavaṅgānmagadhān surāṣṭrānmlecchān suvīrāndaradāśmakāṃśca | strīṇāṃ ca garbhānasuro nihanti subhikṣakṛdbhādrapade'bhyupetaḥ || 79 ||
[ daradāñchakāṃś ] kāmbojacīnayavanān saha śalyahṛdbhirbāhlīkasindhutaṭavāsijanāṃśca hanyāt | ānarttapauṇḍrabhiṣajaśca tathā kirātāndṛṣṭo'suro'śvayuji bhūrisubhikṣakṛcca || 80 ||
[ vālhīka | ānarta ] hanukukṣipāyubhedā dvirdviḥ sañchardanaṃ ca jaraṇaṃ ca | madhyāntayośca vidaraṇamiti daśa śaśisūryayormokṣāḥ || 81 ||
āgneyyāmapagamanaṃ dakṣiṇahanubhedasaṃjñitaṃ śaśinaḥ | sasyavimardo mukharugnṛpapīḍā syātsuvṛṣṭiśca || 82 ||
pūrvottareṇa vāmo hanubhedo nṛpakumārabhayadāyī | mukharogaṃ śastrabhayaṃ tasminvindyātsubhikṣaṃ ca || 83 ||
dakṣiṇakukṣivibhedo dakṣiṇapārśvena yadi bhavenmokṣaḥ | pīḍā nṛpaputrāṇāmabhiyojyā dakṣiṇā ripavaḥ || 84 ||
vāmastu kukṣibhedo yadyuttaramārgasaṃsthito rāhuḥ | strīṇāṃ garbhavipattiḥ sasyāni ca tatra madhyāni || 85 ||
nairṛtavāyavyasthau dakṣiṇavāmau tu pāyubhedau dvau | guhyarugalpā vṛṣṭirdvayostu rājñīkṣayo vāme || 86 ||
pūrveṇa pragrahaṇaṃ kṛtvā prāgeva cāpasarpeta | sañchardanamiti tatkṣemasasyahārdipradaṃ jagataḥ || 87 ||
prākpragrahaṇaṃ yasminpaścādapasarpaṇaṃ tu tajjaraṇam | kṣucchastrabhayodvignā na śaraṇamupayānti tatra janāḥ || 88 ||
[ udvignāḥ kva ] madhye yadi prakāśaḥ prathamaṃ tanmadhyavidaraṇaṃ nāma | antaḥkopakaraṃ syātsubhikṣadaṃ nātivṛṣṭikaram || 89 ||
paryanteṣu vimalatā bahulaṃ madhye tamo'ntyadaraṇākhyaḥ | madhyākhyadeśanāśaḥ śāradasasyakṣayaścāsmin || 90 ||
[ anta ] ete sarve mokṣā vaktavyā bhāskare'pi kintvatra | pūrvā dik śaśini yathā tathā ravau paścimā kalpyā || 91 ||
mukte saptāhāntaḥ pāṃśunipāto'nnasaṃkṣayaṃ kurute | nīhāro rogabhayaṃ bhūkampaḥ pravaranṛpamṛtyum || 92 ||
ulkā mantrivināśaṃ nānāvarṇā ghanāśca bhayamatulam | stanitaṃ garbhavināśaṃ vidyunnṛpadaṃṣṭriparipīḍām || 93 ||
pariveṣo rukpīḍāṃ digdāho nṛpabhayaṃ ca sāgnibhayaṃ | rūkṣo vāyuḥ prabalaścaurasamutthaṃ bhayaṃ dhatte || 94 ||
nirghātaḥ suracāpaṃ daṇḍaśca kṣudbhayaṃ saparacakram | grahayuddhe nṛpayuddhaṃ ketuśca tadeva sandṛṣṭaḥ || 95 ||
[ grahayuddhaṃ ] avikṛtasalila nipātaiḥ saptāhāntaḥ subhikṣamādeśyam | yaccāśubhaṃ grahaṇajaṃ tatsarvaṃ nāśanupayāti || 96 ||
[ nipāte ] somagrahe nivṛtte pakṣānte yadi bhavedgraho'rkasya | tatrānayaḥ prajānāṃ dampatyorvairamanyonyam || 97 ||
arkagrahāttu śaśino grahaṇaṃ yadi dṛśyate tato viprāḥ | naikakratuphalabhājo bhavanti muditāḥ prajāścaiva || 98 ||

Chapter 6: bhaumacārādhyāyaḥ [bhaumacāra-adhyāya]

yadyudayarkṣādvakraṃ karoti navamāṣṭasaptamarkṣeṣu | tadvaktrāmuṣṇamudaye pīḍākaramagnivārttānām || 1 ||
[ vakram vaktram ] dvādaśadaśamaikādaśanakṣatrādvakrite kuje'śrumukham | dūṣayati rasānudaye karoti rogānavṛṣṭiṃ ca || 2 ||
vyālaṃ trayodaśarkṣāccaturdaśādvā vipacyate'stamaye | daṃṣṭrivyālamṛgebhyaḥ karoti pīḍāṃ subhikṣaṃ ca || 3 ||
rudhirānanamiti vaktraṃ pañcadaśāt ṣoḍaśācca vinivṛtte | tatkālaṃ mukharogaṃ sabhayaṃ ca subhikṣamāvahati || 4 ||
asimuśalaṃ saptadaśādaṣṭādaśato'pi vā tadanuvakre | dasyugaṇebhyaḥ pīdāṃ karotyavṛṣṭiṃ saśastrabhayām || 5 ||
bhāgyāryamodite yadi nivartate vaiśvadaivate bhaumaḥ | prājāpatye'stamitastrīnapi lokānnipīḍayati || 6 ||
śravaṇoditasya vakraṃ puṣye mūrdhābhiṣiktapīḍākṛt | yasminnṛkṣe'bhyuditastaddigvyūhān janān hanti || 7 ||
madhyena yadi maghānāṃ gatāgataṃ lohitaḥ karoti tataḥ | pāṇḍyo nṛpo vinaśyati śastrodyogādbhayamavṛṣṭiṃ || 8 ||
bhittvā maghā viśākhāṃ bhindanbhaumaḥ karoti durbhikṣam | marakaṃ karoti ghoraṃ yadi bhittvā rohiṇīṃ yāti || 9 ||
[ maghāṃ ] dakṣiṇato rohiṇyās caranmahījo'rghavṛṣṭinigrahakṛt | dhūmāyan saśikho vā vinihanyātpāriyātrasthān || 10 ||
prājāpatye śravaṇe mūle triṣu cottareṣu śākre ca | vicaran ghananivahānāmupaghātakaraḥ kṣamātanayaḥ || 11 ||
[ tisṛṣūttarāsu ] cārodayāḥ praśastāḥ śravaṇamaghāditya hastamūleṣu | ekapadāśviviśākhāprājāpatyeṣu ca kujasya || 12 ||
[ mūlahasteṣu ] vipulavimalamūrtiḥ kiṃśukāśokavarṇaḥ sphuṭaruciramayūkhastaptatāmraprabhābhaḥ | vicarati yadi mārgaṃ cottaraṃ medinījaḥ śubhakṛdavanipānāṃ hārdidaśca prajānām || 13 ||

Chapter 7: budhacārādhyāyaḥ [budhacāra-adhyāya]

notpātaparityaktaḥ kadā cidapi candrajo vrajatyudayam | jaladahanapavanabhayakṛddhānyārghakṣayavivṛddhau vā || 1 ||
vicaracchravaṇadhaniṣṭhāprajāpatyendu vaiśvadevāni | mṛdnan himakaratanayaḥ karotyavṛṣṭiṃ sarogabhayām || 2 ||
[ prājāpatya | viśvadaivāni ] raudrādīni maghāntānyupāśrite candraje prajāpīḍā | śastranipātakṣudbhayarogānāvṛṣṭisantāpaiḥ || 3 ||
hastādīni caran ṣaḍṛkṣāṇyupapīḍayan gavāmaśubhaḥ | sneharasārghavivṛddhiṃ karoti corvīṃ prabhūtānnām || 4 ||
[ vicaran ] āryamṇaṃ hautabhujaṃ bhadrapadāmuttrarāṃ yameśaṃ ca | candrasya suto nighnanprāṇabhṛtāṃ dhātusaṃkṣayakṛt || 5 ||
āśvinavāruṇamūlānyupamṛdnan revatīṃ ca candrasutaḥ | paṇyabhiṣagnaujīvikasalilajaturagopaghātakaraḥ || 6 ||
pūrvādyṛkṣatritayādekamapīndoḥ suto'bhimṛdnīyāt | kṣucchastrataskarāmayabhayapradāyī caran jagataḥ || 7 ||
prākṛtavimiśrasaṃkṣiptatīkṣṇayogāntaghorapāpākhyāḥ | sapta parāśaratantre nakṣatraiḥ kīrtitā gatayaḥ || 8 ||
prākṛtasaṃjñā vāyavyayāmyapaitāmahāni bahulāśca | miśrā gatiḥ pradiṣṭā śaśiśivapitṛbhujagadevāni || 9 ||
[ bhujagadaivāni ] saṃkṣiptāyāṃ puṣyaḥ punarvasuḥ phalgunīdvayaṃ ceti | tīkṣṇāyāṃ bhadrapadādvayaṃ saśākrāśvayukpauṣṇam || 10 ||
yogāntiketi mūlaṃ dve cāṣāḍhe gatiḥ sutasyendoḥ | ghorā śravaṇastvāṣṭraṃ vasudaivaṃ vāruṇaṃ caiva || 11 ||
[ vasudevaṃ ] pāpākhyā sāvitraṃ maitraṃ śakrāgnidaivataṃ ceti | udayapravāsadivasaiḥ sa eva gatilakṣaṇaṃ prāha || 12 ||
catvāriṃśattriṃśaddvisametā viṃśatirdvinavakaṃ ca | nava māsārdhaṃ daśa caikasaṃyutāḥ prākṛtādyānām || 13 ||
prākṛtagatyāmārogyavṛṣṭisasyapravṛddhayaḥ kṣemam | saṃkṣiptamiśrayormiśrametadanyāsu viparītam || 14 ||
ṛjvyativakrāvakrā vikalā ca matena devalasyaitāḥ | pañcacaturdvyekāhā ṛjvyādīnāṃ ṣaḍabhyastāḥ || 15 ||
ṛjvī hitā prajānāmativakrārghaṃ gatirvināśayati | śastrabhayadā ca vakrā vikalā bhayarogasaṃjananī || 16 ||
[ ativakrārthaṃ ] pauṣāṣāḍhaśrāvaṇavaiśākheṣvindujaḥ samāgheṣu | vṛṣṭo bhayāya jagataḥ śubhaphalakṛtproṣitasteṣu || 17 ||
kārtike aśvayuji vā yadi māse dṛśyate tanubhavaḥ śiśirāṃśoḥ | śastracaurahutabhuggadatoyakṣudbhayāni ca tadā vidadhāti || 18 ||
[ kārttike ] ruddhāni saumye'stagate purāṇi yānyudgate tānyupayānti mokṣam | anye tu paścādudite vadanti lābhaḥ purāṇāṃ bhavati tajjñāḥ || 19 ||
[ astamite ] hemakāntiratha vā śukavarṇaḥ sasyakena maṇinā sadṛśo vā | snigdhamūrtiralaghuśca hitāya vyatyaye na śubhakṛt śaśiputraḥ || 20 ||

Chapter 8: bṛhaspaticārādhyāyaḥ [bṛhaspaticāra-adhyāya]

nakṣatreṇa sahodayamupagacchati yena devapatimantrī | tatsaṃjñaṃ vaktavyaṃ varṣaṃ māsakrameṇaiva || 1 ||
varṣāṇi kārttikādīnyāgneyādbhadvayānuyogīni | kramaśastribhaṃ tu pañcamamupāntyamantyaṃ ca yadvarṣam || 2 ||
śakaṭānalopajīvakagopīḍā vyādhiśastrakopaśca | vṛddhistu raktapītakakusumānāṃ kārttike varṣe || 3 ||
saumye'bde'nāvṛṣṭirmṛgākhuśalabhāṇḍajaiśca sasyavadhaḥ | vyādhibhayaṃ mitrairapi bhūpānāṃ jāyate vairam || 4 ||
śubhakṛjjagataḥ pauṣo nivṛttavairāḥ parasparaṃ kṣitipāḥ | dvitriguṇo dhānyārghaḥ pauṣṭikakarmaprasiddhiśca || 5 ||
pitṛpūjāparivṛddhirmāghe hārdiśca sarvabhūtānām | ārogyavṛṣṭidhānyārghasampado mitralābhaśca || 6 ||
phālgunavarṣe vindyātkva citkva citkṣemavṛṣṭisasyāni | daurbhāgyaṃ pramadānāṃ prabalāścaurā nṛpāścogrāḥ || 7 ||
caitre mandā vṛṣṭiḥ priyamannaṃ kṣemamavanipā mṛdavaḥ | vṛddhiśca kośadhānyasya bhavati pīḍā ca rūpavatām || 8 ||
vaiśākhe dharmaratā vigatabhayāḥ pramuditāḥ prajāḥ sanṛpāḥ | yajñakriyāprāvṛttirniṣpattiḥ sarvasasyānām || 9 ||
[ dharmaparā ] jyaiṣṭhe jātikuladhanaśreṇīśreṣṭhā nṛpāḥ sadharmajñāḥ | pīḍyante dhānyāni ca hitvā kaṅguṃ śamījātim || 10 ||
āṣāḍhe jāyante sasyāni kva cidavṛṣṭiranyatra | yogakṣemaṃ madhyaṃ vyagrāśca bhavanti bhūpālāḥ || 11 ||
śrāvaṇavarṣe kṣemaṃ samyaksasyāni pākamupayānti | kṣudrā ye pākhaṇḍāḥ pīḍyante ye ca tadbhaktāḥ || 12 ||
[ pāṣaṇḍāḥ ] bhādrapade vallījaṃ niṣpattiṃ yāti pūrvasasyaṃ ca | na bhavatyaparaṃ sasyaṃ kva citsubhikṣaṃ kvacicca bhayam || 13 ||
āśvayuje'bde'jasraṃ patati jalaṃ pramuditāḥ prajāḥ kṣemam | prāṇacayaḥ prāṇabhṛtāṃ sarveṣāmannabāhulyam || 14 ||
udagārogyasubhikṣakṣemakaro vākpatiścaranbhānām | yāmye tadviparīto madhyena tu madhyaphaladāyī || 15 ||
vicaranbhadvayamiṣṭastatsārdhaṃ vatsareṇa madhyaphalaḥ | sasyānāṃ vidhvaṃsī vicaredadhikaṃ yadi kadā cit || 16 ||
analabhayamanalavarṇe vyādhiḥ pīte raṇāgamaḥ śyāme | harite ca taskarebhyaḥ pīḍā rakte tu śastrabhayam || 17 ||
dhūmābhe'nāvṛṣṭistridaśagurau nṛpavadho divā dṛṣṭe | vipule'male sutāre rātrau dṛṣṭe prajāḥ svasthāḥ || 18 ||
rohiṇyo'nalabhaṃ ca vatsaratanurnābhistvaṣāḍhadvayaṃ sārpaṃ hṛtpitṛdaivataṃ ca kusumaṃ śuddhaiḥ śubhaṃ taiḥ phalam | dehe krūranipīḍite'gnyanilajaṃ nābhyāṃ bhayaṃ kṣutkṛtaṃ puṣpe mūlaphalakṣayo'tha hṛdaye sasyasya nāśo dhruvam || 19 ||
gatāni varṣāṇi śakendrakālāddhatāni rudrairguṇayeccaturbhiḥ | navāṣṭapañcāṣṭa yutāni kṛtvā vibhājayec śūnyaśarāgarāmaiḥ || 20 ||
labdhena yuktaṃ śakabhūpakālaṃ saṃśodhya ṣaṣṭyā viṣayairvibhajya | yugāni nārāyaṇapūrvakāṇi labdhāni śeṣāḥ kramaśaḥ samāḥ syuḥ || 21 ||
[ phalena ] ekaikamabdeṣu navāhateṣu dattvā pṛthagdvādaśakaṃ krameṇa | hṛtvā caturbhirvasudevatādyānyuḍūni śeṣāṃśakapūrvamabdam || 22 ||
viṣṇuḥ surejyo balabhiddhutāśastvaṣṭottaraproṣṭhapadādhipaśca | kramād yugeśāḥ pitṛviśvasomaśakrānalākhyāśvibhagāḥ pradiṣṭāḥ || 23 ||
[ somāḥ ] saṃvatsaro'gniḥ parivatsaro'rka idādikaḥ śītamayūkhamālī | prajāpatiścāpyanuvatsaraḥ syādidvatsaraḥ śailasutāpatiśca || 24 ||
vṛṣṭiḥ samādye pramukhe dvitīye prabhūtatoyā kathitā tṛtīye | paścājjalaṃ muñcati yaccaturthaṃ svalpodakaṃ pañcamamabdamuktam || 25 ||
catvāri mukhyāni yugānyathaiṣāṃ viṣṇvindrajīvānaladaivatāni | catvāri madhyāni ca madhyamāni catvāri cāntyānyadhamāni vindyāt || 26 ||
ādyaṃ dhaniṣṭāṃśamabhiprapanno māghe yadā yātyudayaṃ surejyaḥ | ṣaṣṭyabdapūrvaḥ prabhavaḥ sa nāmnā prapadyate bhūtahitastadābdaḥ || 27 ||
[ pravartate ] kva cittvavṛṣṭiḥ pavanāgnikopaḥ santītayaḥ śleṣmakṛtāśca rogāḥ | saṃvatsare'sminprabhave pravṛtte na duḥkhamāpnoti janastathāpi || 28 ||
tasmāddvitīyo vibhavaḥ pradiṣṭaḥ śuklastṛtīyaḥ parataḥ pramodaḥ | prajāpatiśceti yathottarāṇi śastāni varṣāṇi phalānyathaiṣām || 29 ||
[ caiṣām ] niṣpannaśālīkṣuyavādisasyāṃ bhayairvimuktāmupaśāntavairām | saṃhṛṣṭalokāṃ kalidoṣamuktāṃ kṣatraṃ tadā śāsti ca bhūtadhātrīm || 30 ||
ādyo'ṅgirāḥ śrīmukhabhāvasāhvau yuvā sudhāteti yuge dvitīye | varṣāṇi pañcaiva yathākrameṇa trīṇyatra śastāni same pare dve || 31 ||
[ yuvātha dhāteti ] triṣvādyavarṣeṣu nikāmavarṣī devī nirātaṅkabhayaśca lokaḥ | abdadvaye'ntye'pi samā suvṛṣṭiḥ kintvatra rogāḥ samarāgamaśca || 32 ||
[ aṅgirādyeṣu | ādyavarṣeṣu | bhayāś ] śākre yuge pūrvamatheśvarākhyaṃ varṣaṃ dvitīyaṃ bahudhānyamāhuḥ | pramāthinaṃ vikramamapyathānyadvṛṣaṃ ca vindyādgurucārayogāt || 33 ||
[ ato'nyad ] ādyaṃ dvitīyaṃ ca śubhe tu varṣe kṛtānukāraṃ kurutaḥ prajānām | pāpaḥ pramāthī vṛṣavikramau tu subhikṣadau rogabhayapradau ca || 34 ||
śreṣṭhaṃ ca caturthasya yugasya pūrvaṃ yaccitrabhānuṃ kathayanti varṣam | madhyaṃ dvitīyaṃ tu subhānusañjñaṃ rogapradaṃ mṛtyukaraṃ na taṃ ca || 35 ||
[ na tacca ] tāraṇaṃ tadanu bhūrivāridaṃ sasyavṛddhimuditātipārthivam | pañcamaṃ vyayamuśanti śobhanaṃ manmathaprabalamutsavākulam || 36 ||
[ muditaṃ ca ] tvāṣṭre yuge sarvajidādya uktaḥ saṃvatsaro'nyaḥ khalu sarvadhārī | tasmādvirodhī vikṛtaḥ kharaśca śasto dvitīyo'tra bhayāya śeṣāḥ || 37 ||
nandano'tha vijayo jayastathā manmatho'sya parataśca durmukhaḥ | kāntamatra yuga āditastrayaṃ manmathaḥ samaphalo'dhamo'paraḥ || 38 ||
hemalamba iti saptame yuge syādvilambi parato vikāri ca | śarvarīti tadanu plavaḥ smṛto vatsaro guruvaśena pañcamaḥ || 39 ||
ītiprāyā pracurapavanā vṛṣṭirabde tu pūrve mandaṃ sasyaṃ na bahusalilaṃ vatsare'to dvitīye | atyudvegaḥ pracurasalilaḥ syāttṛtīyaścaturtho durbhikṣāya plava iti tataḥ śobhano bhūritoyaḥ || 40 ||
[ itiprāyaḥ ] vaiśve yuge śokahṛdityathādyaḥ saṃvatsaro'taḥ śubhakṛddvitīyaḥ | krodhī tṛtīyaḥ parataḥ krameṇa viśvāvasuśceti parābhavaśca || 41 ||
[ śobhakṛd ] pūrvāparau prītikarau prajānāmeṣāṃ tṛtīyo bahudoṣado'bdaḥ | antyau samau kintu parābhave'gniḥ śastrāmayārtirdvijagobhayaṃ ca || 42 ||
ādyaḥ plavaṅgo navame yuge'bdaḥ syātkīlako'nyaḥ parataśca saumyaḥ | sādhāraṇo rodhakṛdityathaivaṃ śubhapradau kīlakasaumyasaṃjñau || 43 ||
[ athābdaḥ ] kaṣṭaḥ plavaṅgo bahuśaḥ prajānāṃ sādhāraṇe'lpaṃ jalamītayaśca | yaḥ pañcamo rodhakṛdityathābdaścitraṃ jalam tatra ca sasyasampat || 44 ||
indrāgnidaivaṃ daśamaṃ yugaṃ yattatrādyavarṣaṃ paridhāvisaṃjñam | pramādinaṃ vikramamapyato'nyatsyād rākṣasaṃ cānalasaṃjñitaṃ ca || 45 ||
[ tarādyamabdaṃ | pramādyathānandamataḥ paraṃ yat ] paridhāvini madhyadeśanāśo nṛpahānirjalamalpamagnikopaḥ | alasastu janaḥ pramādisaṃjñe ḍamaraṃ raktakapuṣpabījanāśaḥ || 46 ||
vikramaḥ sakalalokanandano rākṣasaḥ kṣayakaro'nalastathā | grīṣmadhānyajanano'tra rākṣaso vahnikopamarakaprado'nalaḥ || 47 ||
[ tatparaḥ ] ekādaśe piṅgalakālayuktasiddhārtharaudrāḥ khalu durmatiśca | ādye tu vṣṛṭirmahatī sacaurā śvāso hanūkampayutaśca kāsaḥ || 48 ||
yatkālayuktaṃ tadanekadoṣaṃ siddhārthasaṃjñe bahavo guṇāśca | raudro'tiraudraḥ kṣayakṛtpradiṣṭo yo durmatirmadhyamavṛṣṭikṛtsaḥ || 49 ||
bhāgye yuge dundubhisaṃjñamādyaṃ sasyasya vṛddhiṃ mahatīṃ karoti | aṅgārasaṃjñaṃ tadanu kṣayāya nareśvarāṇāṃ viṣamā ca vṛṣṭiḥ || 50 ||
[ udgārisaṃjñaṃ ] raktākṣamabdaṃ kathitaṃ tṛtīyaṃ tasminbhayaṃ daṃṣṭrikṛtaṃ gadāśca | krodhaṃ bahukrodhakaraṃ caturthaṃ rāṣṭrāṇi śūnyīkurute virodhaiḥ || 51 ||
kṣayamiti yugasyāntyasyāntyaṃ bahukṣayakārakaṃ janayati bhayaṃ tadviprāṇāṃ kṛṣībalavṛddhidam | upacayakaraṃ viṭśūdrāṇāṃ parasvahṛtāṃ tathā kathitamakhilaṃ ṣaṣṭyabde yattadatra samāsataḥ || 52 ||
akaluṣāṃśujaṭilaḥ pṛthumūrtiḥ kumudakundakusumasphaṭikābhaḥ | grahahato na yadi satpathavartī hitakaro amaragururmanujānām || 53 ||
[ hatakiro ]

Chapter 9: śukracārādhyāyaḥ [śukracāra-adhyāya]

nāgagajairāvatavṛṣabhagojaradgavamṛgājadahanākhyāḥ | aśvinyādyāḥ kaiścittribhāḥ kramādvīthayaḥ kathitāḥ || 1 ||
nāgā tu pavanayāmyānalāni paitāmahāttribhāstisraḥ | govīthyāmaśvinyaḥ pauṣṇaṃ dve cāpi bhadrapade || 2 ||
jāradgavyāṃ śravaṇāttribhaṃ mṛgākhyā tribhaṃ tu maitrādyam | hastaviśākhātvāṣṭrāṇyajetyaṣāḍhādvayaṃ dahanā || 3 ||
tisrastisrastāsāṃ kramādudaṅmadhyayāmyamārgasthāḥ | tāsāmapyuttaramadhyadakṣiṇena sthitaikaikā || 4 ||
[ dakṣiṇāvasthitaikaikā ] vīthīmārgānapare kathayanti yathāsthitānbhamārgasya | nakṣatrāṇāṃ tārā yāmyottaramadhyamāstadvat || 5 ||
uttaramārgo yāmyādi nigadito madhyamastu bhāgyādyaḥ | dakṣiṇamārgavāṣāḍhādi kaiścidevaṃ kṛtā mārgāḥ || 6 ||
jyautiṣamāgamaśāstraṃ vipratipattau na yogyamasmākam | svayamevā vikalpayituṃ kintu bahūnāṃ mataṃ vakṣye || 7 ||
[ jyotisam ] uttaravīthiṣu śukraḥ subhikṣaśivakṛdgato'stamudayaṃ ca | madhyāsu madhyaphaladaḥ kaṣṭaphalo dakṣiṇasthāsu || 8 ||
[ vā ] atyuttamottamonaṃ samamadhyanyūnamadhamakaṣṭaphalam | kaṣṭataraṃ saumyādyāsu vīthiṣu yathākramaṃ brūyāt || 9 ||
[ kaṣṭatamaṃ ] bharaṇīpūrvaṃ maṇḍalamṛkṣacatuṣkaṃ subhikṣakaramādyam | vaṅgāṅgamahiṣabāhlikakaliṅgadeśeṣu bhayajananam || 10 ||
[ vāhlika ] atroditamārohedgraho'paro yadi sitaṃ tato hanyāt | bhadrāśvaśūrasenakayaudheyakakoṭivarṣanṛpān || 11 ||
bhacatuṣṭayamārdrādyaṃ dvitīyamamitāmbusasyasampattyai | viprāṇāmaśubhakaraṃ viśeṣataḥ krūraceṣṭānām || 12 ||
anyenātrākrānte mlecchāṭavikaśvajīvigomantān | gonardanīcaśūdrānvaidehāṃścānayaḥ spṛśati || 13 ||
[ & ātavikā ] vicaranmaghādipañcakamuditaḥ sasyapraṇāśakṛcchukraḥ | kṣuttaskarabhayajanano nīconnatisaṅkarakaraśca || 14 ||
pitryādye'vaṣṭabdho hantyanyenāvikācchabaraśūdrān | puṇḍrāparāntyaśūlikavanavāsidraviḍasāmudrān || 15 ||
svātyādyaṃ bhatritayaṃ maṇḍalametaccaturthamabhayakaram | brahmakṣatrasubhikṣābhivṛddhaye mitrabhedāya || 16 ||
atrākrānte mṛtyuḥ kirātabhartuḥ pinaṣṭi cekṣvākūn | pratyantāvantipulindataṅgaṇācchūrasenāṃśca || 17 ||
jyeṣṭhādyaṃ pañcarkṣaṃ kṣuttaskararogadam prabādhayate | kāśmīrāśmakamatsyān sacārudevīnavantīṃśca || 18 ||
atrāroheddraviḍābhīrāmbaṣṭhatrigartasaurāṣṭrān | nāśayanti sindhusauvīrakāṃśca kāśīśvarasya vadhaḥ || 19 ||
[ ārohe'trābhīrāndraviḍāmbaṣṭha ] ṣaṣṭhaṃ ṣaṇnakṣatraṃ śubhametanmaṇḍalaṃ dhaniṣṭhādyam | bhūridhanagokulākulamanalpadhānyaṃ kva citsabhayam || 20 ||
atrārohecchūlikagāndhārāvantayaḥ prapīḍyante | vaidehavadhaḥ pratyantayavanaśakadāsaparivṛddhiḥ || 21 ||
[ ārohe ] aparasyāṃ svātyādyaṃ jyeṣṭhādyaṃ cāpi maṇḍalaṃ śubhadam | pitryādyaṃ pūrvasyāṃ śeṣāṇi yathoktaphaladāni || 22 ||
dṛṣṭo'nastamite bhayakṛtkṣudrogakṛtsamastamahaḥ | ardhadivase ca sendurnṛpabalapurabhedakṛcchukraḥ || 23 ||
[ anastagate'rke | arthadivasaṃ ] bhindan gato'nalarkṣaṃ kūlātikrāntavārivāhābhiḥ | avyaktatuṅganimnā samā saridbhirbhavati dhātrī || 24 ||
prājāpatye śakaṭe bhinne kṛtveva pātakaṃ vasudhā | keśāsthiśakalaśabalā kāpālamiva vrataṃ dhatte || 25 ||
saumyopagato rasasasyasaṃkṣayāyośanāḥ samuddiṣṭaḥ | ārdrāgatastu kośalakaliṅgahā salilanikarakaraḥ || 26 ||
aśmakavaidarbhāṇāṃ punarvasusthe site mahānanayaḥ | puṣye puṣṭā vṛṣṭirvidyādhararaṇavimardaśca || 27 ||
[ vidyādhara ] āśleṣāsu bhujaṅgamadāruṇapīḍāvahaścaracchukraḥ | bhindanmaghāṃ mahāmātradoṣakṛdbhūrivṛṣṭikaraḥ || 28 ||
bhāgye śabarapulindapradhvaṃsakaro'mbunivahamokṣāya | āryamṇe kurujāṅgalapāñcālaghnaḥ saliladāyī || 29 ||
kauravacitrakarāṇāṃ haste pīḍā jalasya ca nirodhaḥ | kūpakṛdaṇḍajapīḍā citrāsthe śobhanā vṛṣṭiḥ || 30 ||
svātau prabhūtavṛṣṭirdūtavaṇignāvikān spṛśatyanayaḥ | aindrāgne'pi suvṛṣṭirvaṇijāṃ ca bhayaṃ vijānīyāt || 31 ||
maitre kṣatravirodho jyeṣṭhāyāṃ kṣatramukhyasantāpaḥ | maulikabhiṣajāṃ mūle triṣvapi caiteṣvanāvṛṣṭiḥ || 32 ||
āpye salilajapīḍā viśveśe vyādhayaḥ prakupyanti | śravaṇe śravaṇavyādhiḥ pākhaṇḍibhayaṃ dhaniṣṭhāsu || 33 ||
[ pāṣaṇḍi ] śatabhiṣaji śauṇḍikānāmajaikabhe dyūtajīvināṃ pīḍāṃ | kurupāñcālānāmapi karoti cāsmin sitaḥ salilam || 34 ||
[ ajaikape | pīḍā ] āhirbudhnye phalamūlatāpakṛd yāyināṃ ca revatyām | aśvinyāṃ hayapānāṃ yāmye tu kirātayavanānām || 35 ||
caturdaśīṃ pañcadaśīṃ tathāṣṭamīṃ tamisrapakṣasya tithiṃ bhṛgoḥ sutaḥ | yadā vrajeddarśanamastameti vā tadā mahī vārimayīva lakṣyate || 36 ||
[ caturdaśe pañcadaśe tathāṣṭame | tithau ] gururbhṛguścāparapūrvakāṣṭhayoḥ parasparaṃ saptamarāśigau yadā | tadā prajā rugbhayaśokapīḍitā na vāri paśyanti purandarojjhitam || 37 ||
yadā sthitā jīvabudhārasūryajāḥ sitasya sarve'grapathānuvartinaḥ | nṛnāgavidyādharasaṅgarāstadā bhavanti vātāśca samucchritāntakāḥ || 38 ||
na mitrabhāve suhṛdo vyavasthitāḥ kriyāsu samyagna ratā dvijātayaḥ | na cālpamapyambu dadāti vāsavo bhinatti vajreṇa śirāṃsi bhūbhṛtām || 39 ||
śanaiścare mlecchaviḍālakuñjarāḥ kharā mahiṣyo'sitadhānyaśūkarāḥ | pulindaśūdrāśca sadakṣiṇāpathāḥ kṣayaṃ vrajantyakṣimarudgadodbhavaiḥ || 40 ||
nihanti śukraḥ kṣitije'grataḥ prajāṃ hutāśaśastrakṣudavṛṣṭitaskaraiḥ | carācaraṃ vyaktamathottarāpathaṃ diśo'gnividyudrajasā ca pīḍyet || 41 ||
[ prajā ] bṛhaspatau hanti puraḥsthite sitaḥ sitaṃ samastaṃ dvijagosurālayān | diśaṃ ca pūrvāṃ karakāsṛjo'mbudā gale gadā bhūri bhavecca śāradam || 42 ||
saumyo'stodayoḥ puro bhṛgusutasyāvasthitastoyakṛd rogānpittajakāmalāṃśca kurute puṣṇāti ca graiṣmikān | hanyātpravrajitāgnihotrikabhiṣagraṅgopajīvyān hayānvaiśyān gāḥ saha vāhanairnarapatīnpītāni paścāddiśam || 43 ||
[ kāmalāṃ | kāmalāmś | kāmalāś | graiṣmikam ] śikhibhayamanalābhe śastrakopaśca rakte kanakanikaṣagaure vyādhayo daityapūjye | haritakapilarūpe śvāsakāsaprakopaḥ patati na salilaṃ khādbhasmarūkṣāsitābhe || 44 ||
dadhikumudaśaśāṅkakāntibhṛtsphuṭavikasatkiraṇo bṛhattanuḥ | sugatiravikṛto jayānvitaḥ kṛtayugarūpakaraḥ sitāhvayaḥ || 45 ||

Chapter 10: śanaiścaracārādhyāyaḥ [śanaiścaracāra-adhyāya]

śravaṇānilahastārdrābharaṇībhāgyopagaḥ suto'rkasya | pracurasalilopagūḍhāṃ karoti dhātrīṃ yadi snigdhaḥ || 1 ||
ahivaruṇapurandaradaivateṣu sukṣemakṛnna cātijalam | kṣucchastrāvṛṣṭikaro mūle pratyekamapi vakṣye || 2 ||
turagaturagopacārakakavivaidyāmātyahārkajo'śvigataḥ | yāmye nartakavādakageyajñakṣudranaikṛtikān || 3 ||
bahulāsthe pīḍyante saure'gnyupajīvinaścamūpāśca | rohiṇyāṃ kośalamadrakāśipañcālaśākaṭikāḥ || 4 ||
mṛgaśirasi vatsayājakayajamānāryajanamadhyadeśās ca | raudrasthe pārataramaṭhāstailikarajakacaurāśca || 5 ||
[ pāratarātailikarajaka ] āditye pāñcanadapratyantasurāṣṭrasindhusauvīrāḥ | puṣye ghāṇṭhikaghauṣikayavanavaṇikkitavakusumāni || 6 ||
sārpe jalaruhasarpāḥ pitrye bāhlīkacīnagāndhārāḥ | śūlikapāratavaiśyāḥ koṣṭhāgārāṇi vaṇijaśca || 7 ||
bhāgye rasavikrayiṇaḥ paṇyastrīkanyakāmahārāṣṭrāḥ | āryamṇe nṛpaguḍalavaṇabhikṣukāmbūni takṣaśilā || 8 ||
haste nāpitacākrikacaurabhiṣaksūcikā dvipagrāhāḥ | bandhakyaḥ kauśalakā mālākārāśca pīḍyante || 9 ||
citrāsthe pramadājanalekhakacitrajñacitrabhāṇḍāni | svātau māgadhacaradūtasūtapotaplavanaṭādyāḥ || 10 ||
aindrāgnākhye traigartacīnakaulūtakuṅkumaṃ lākṣā | sasyānyatha māñjiṣṭhaṃ kausumbhaṃ ca kṣayaṃ yāti || 11 ||
maitre kulūtataṅgaṇakhasakāśmīrāḥ samantricakracarāḥ | upatāpaṃ yānti ca ghāṇṭikā vibhedaśca mitrāṇām || 12 ||
jyeṣṭhāsu nṛpapurohitanṛpasatkṛtaśūragaṇakulaśreṇyaḥ | mūle tu kāśikośalapāñcālaphalauṣadhīyodhāḥ || 13 ||
āpye'ṅgavaṅgakauśalagirivrajā magadhapuṇḍramithilāśca | upatāpaṃ yānti janā vasanti ye tāmraliptyāṃ ca || 14 ||
viśveśvare'rkaputraścarandaśārṇānnihanti yavanāṃśca | ujjayinīṃ śabarānpāriyātrikān kuntibhojāṃśca || 15 ||
śravaṇe rājādhikṛtānviprāgryabhiṣakpurohitakaliṅgān | vasubhe magadheśajayo vṛddhiśca dhaneṣvadhikṛtānām || 16 ||
sāje śatabhiṣaji bhiṣakkaviśauṇḍikapaṇyanīti vṛttīnām | āhirbudhnye nadyo yānakarāḥ strīhiraṇyaṃ ca || 17 ||
[ varttānām ] revatyāṃ rājabhṛtāḥ krauñcadvīpāśritāḥ śaratsasyam | śabarāśca nipīḍyante yavanāśca śanaiścare carati || 18 ||
yadā viśākhāsu mahendramantrī sutaśca bhānordahanarkṣayātaḥ | tadā prajānāmanayo'tighoraḥ puraprabhedo gatayorbhamekam || 19 ||
aṇḍajahā ravijo yadi citraḥ kṣudbhayakṛd yadi pītamayūkhaḥ | śastrabhayāya ca raktasavarṇo bhasmanibho bahuvairakaraśca || 20 ||
vaidūryakāntivimalaḥ śubhakṛtprajānāṃ bāṇātasīkusumavarṇanibhaśca śastaḥ | yaṃ cāpi varṇamupagacchati tatsavarṇān sūryātmajaḥ kṣayatīti munipravādaḥ || 21 ||
[ pañcāpi ]

Chapter 11: ketucārādhyāyaḥ [ketucāra-adhyāya]

gārgīyaṃ śikhicāraṃ pārāśaramasitadevalakṛtaṃ ca | anyāṃśca bahūndṛṣṭvā kriyate'yamanākulaścāraḥ || 1 ||
darśanamastamayo vā na gaṇitavidhināsya śakyate jñātum | divyāntarikṣabhaumāstrividhāḥ syuḥ ketavo yasmāt || 2 ||
ahutāśe'nalarūpaṃ yasmiṃstatketurūpamevoktam | khadyotapiśācālayamaṇiratnādīnparityajya || 3 ||
dhvajaśastrabhavanataruturagakuñjarādyeṣvathāntarikṣāste | divyā nakṣatrasthā bhaumāḥ syurato'nyathā śikhinaḥ || 4 ||
śatamekādhikameke sahasramapare vadanti ketūnām | bahurūpamekameva prāha munirnāradaḥ ketum || 5 ||
yadyeko yadi bahavaḥ kimanena phalaṃ tu sarvathā vācyam | udayāstamayaiḥ sthānaiḥ sparśairādhūmanairvarṇaiḥ || 6 ||
yāvantyahāni dṛśyo māsāstāvanta eva phalapākaḥ | māsairabdāṃśca vadetprathamātpakṣatrayātparataḥ || 7 ||
hrasvastanuḥ prasannaḥ snigdhastv ṛjuracirasaṃsthitaḥ śuklaḥ | udito'tha vābhivṛṣṭaḥ subhikṣasaukhyāvahaḥ ketuḥ || 8 ||
[ vāpyabhidṛṣṭaḥ ] uktaviparītarūpo na śubhakaro dhūmaketurutpannaḥ | indrāyudhānukārī viśeṣato dvitricūlo vā || 9 ||
hāramaṇihemarūpāḥ kiraṇākhyāḥ pañcaviṃśatiḥ saśikhāḥ | prāgaparadiśordṛśyā nṛpativirodhāvahā ravijāḥ || 10 ||
śukadahanabandhujīvakalākṣākṣatajopamā hutāśasutāḥ | āgneyyāṃ dṛśyante tāvantaste'pi śikhibhayadāḥ || 11 ||
vakraśikhā mṛtyusutā rūkṣāḥ kṛṣṇāśca te'pi tāvantaḥ | dṛśyante yāmyāyāṃ janamarakāvedinaste ca || 12 ||
darpaṇavṛttākārā viśikhāḥ kiraṇānvitā dharātanayāḥ | kṣudbhayadā dvāviṃśatiraiśānyāmambutailanibhāḥ || 13 ||
śaśikiraṇarajatahimakumudakundakusumopamāḥ sutāḥ śaśinaḥ | uttarato dṛśyante trayaḥ subhikṣāvahāḥ śikhinaḥ || 14 ||
brahmasuta eka eva triśikho varṇaistribhiryugāntakaraḥ | aniyatadiksamprabhavo vijñeyo brahmadaṇḍākhyaḥ || 15 ||
śatamabhihitamekasametametadekena virahitānyasmāt | kathayiṣye ketūnāṃ śatāni nava lakṣaṇaiḥ spaṣṭaiḥ || 16 ||
saumyaiśānyorudayaṃ śukrasutā yānti caturaśītyākhyāḥ | vipulasitatārakāste snigdhāśca bhavanti tīvraphalāḥ || 17 ||
snigdhāḥ prabhāsametā dviśikhāḥ ṣaṣṭiḥ śanaiścarāṅgaruhāḥ | atikaṣṭaphalā dṛśyāḥ sarvatraite kanakasaṃjñāḥ || 18 ||
vikacā nāma gurusutāḥ sitaikatārāḥ śikhāparityaktāḥ | ṣaṣṭiḥ pañcabhiradhikā snigdhā yāmyāśritāḥ pāpāḥ || 19 ||
nātivyaktāḥ sūkṣmā dīrghāḥ śuklā yatheṣṭadikprabhavāḥ | budhajāstaskarasaṃjñāḥ pāpaphalāstvekapañcāśat || 20 ||
kṣatajānalānurūpāstricūlatārāḥ kujātmajāḥ ṣaṣṭiḥ | nāmnā ca kauṅkumāste saumyāśāsaṃsthitāḥ pāpāḥ || 21 ||
triṃśatyadhikā rāhoste tāmasakīlakā iti khyātāḥ | raviśaśigā dṛśyante teṣāṃ phalamarkacāroktam || 22 ||
viṃśatyadhikamanyacchatamagnerviśvarūpasaṃjñānām | tīvrānalabhayadānāṃ jvālāmālākulatanūnām || 23 ||
śyāmāruṇā vitārāścāmararūpā vikīrṇadīdhitayaḥ | aruṇākhyā vāyoḥ saptasaptatiḥ pāpadāḥ paruṣāḥ || 24 ||
tārāpuñjanikāśā gaṇakā nāma prajāpateraṣṭau | dve ca śate caturadhike caturasrā brahmasantānāḥ || 25 ||
[ caturaśrā ] kaṅkā nāma varuṇajā dvātriṃśadvaṃśagulmasaṃsthānāḥ | śaśivatprabhāsametāstīvraphalāḥ ketavaḥ proktāḥ || 26 ||
ṣaṇṇavatiḥ kālasutāḥ kabandhasaṃjñāḥ kabandhasaṃsthānāḥ | puṇḍrābhayapradāḥ syurvirūpatārāśca te śikhinaḥ || 27 ||
[ caṇḍa ] śuklavipulaikatārā nava vidiśāṃ ketavaḥ samutpannāḥ | evaṃ ketusahasraṃ viśeṣameṣāmato vakṣye || 28 ||
udagāyato mahān snigdhamūrtiraparodayī vasāketuḥ | sadyaḥ karoti marakaṃ subhikṣamapyuttamaṃ kurute || 29 ||
tallakṣaṇo'sthiketuḥ sa tu rūkṣaḥ kṣudbhayāvahaḥ proktaḥ | snigdhastādṛkprācyāṃ śastrākhyo ḍamaramarakāya || 30 ||
dṛśyo'māvāsyāyāṃ kapālaketuḥ sadhūmraraśmiśikhaḥ | prāṅ nabhaso'rdhavicārī kṣutmarakāvṛṣṭirogakaraḥ || 31 ||
prāgvaiśvānara mārge śūlāgraḥ śyāvarūkṣatāmrārciḥ | nabhasastribhāgagāmī raudra iti kapālatulyaphalaḥ || 32 ||
[ vaśvānara | vaiśvānara ] aparasyāṃ calaketuḥ śikhayā yāmyāgrayāṅgulocchritayā | gacched yathā yathodaktathā tathā dairghyamāyāti || 33 ||
saptamunīn saṃspṛśya dhruvamabhijitameva ca pratinivṛttaḥ | nabhaso'rdhamātramitvā yāmyenāstaṃ samupayāti || 34 ||
hanyātprayāgakūlād yāvadavantīṃ ca puṣkarāraṇyam | udagapi ca devikāmapi bhūyiṣṭhaṃ madhyadeśākhyam || 35 ||
[ puṣkarāṇyam ] anyānapi sa deśān kva citkva ciddhanti rogadurbhikṣaiḥ | daśa māsānphalapāko'sya kaiścidaṣṭādaśa proktaḥ || 36 ||
prāgardharātradṛśyo yāmyāgraḥ śvetaketuranyaśca | ka iti yugākṛtirapare yugapattau saptadinadṛśyau || 37 ||
snigdhau subhikṣaśivadāvathādhikaṃ dṛśyate kanāmā yaḥ | daśa varṣāṇyupatāpaṃ janayati śastraprakopakṛtam || 38 ||
śveta iti jaṭākāro rūkṣaḥ śyāvo viyattribhāgagataḥ | vinivartate'pasavyaṃ tribhāgaśeṣāḥ prajāḥ kurute || 39 ||
ādhūmrayā tu śikhayā darśanamāyāti kṛttikāsaṃsthaḥ | jñeyaḥ sa raśmiketuḥ śvetasamānaṃ phalaṃ dhatte || 40 ||
dhruvaketuraniyatagatipramāṇavarṇākṛtirbhavati viṣvak | divyāntarikṣabhaumo bhavatyayaṃ snigdha iṣṭaphalaḥ || 41 ||
senāṅgeṣu nṛpāṇāṃ gṛhataruśaileṣu cāpi deśānām | gṛhiṇāmupaskareṣu ca vināśināṃ darśanaṃ yāti || 42 ||
kumuda iti kumudakāntirvāruṇyāṃ prākśikho niśāmekām | dṛṣṭaḥ subhikṣamatulaṃ daśa kila varṣāṇi sa karoti || 43 ||
sakṛdekayāmadṛśyaḥ susūkṣmatāro'pareṇa maṇiketuḥ | ṛjvī śikhāsya śuklā stanodgatā kṣīradhāreva || 44 ||
udayanneva subhikṣaṃ caturo māsān karotyasau sārdhān | prādurbhāvaṃ prāyaḥ karoti ca kṣudrajantūnām || 45 ||
jalaketurapi ca paścātsnigdhaḥ śikhayāpareṇa connatayā | nava māsān sa subhikṣaṃ karoti śāntiṃ ca lokasya || 46 ||
bhavaketurekarātraṃ dṛśyaḥ prāksūkṣmatārakaḥ snigdhaḥ | harilāṅgūlopamayā pradakṣiṇāvartayā śikhayā || 47 ||
yāvata eva muhūrtāndarśanamāyāti nirdiśetmāsān | tāvadatulaṃ subhikṣaṃ rūkṣe prāṇāntikān rogān || 48 ||
apareṇa padmaketurmṛṇālagauro bhavenniśāmekām | sapta karoti subhikṣaṃ varṣāṇyatiharṣayuktāni || 49 ||
āvarta iti niśārdhe savyaśikho'ruṇanibho'pare snigdhaḥ | yāvatkṣaṇān sa dṛśyastāvanmāsān subhikṣakaraḥ || 50 ||
paścātsandhyākāle saṃvarto nāma dhūmratāmraśikhaḥ | ākramya viyattryaṃśaṃ śūlāgrāvasthito raudraḥ || 51 ||
yāvata eva muhūrtāndṛśyo varṣāṇi hanti tāvanti | bhūpācchastranipātairudayarkṣaṃ cāpi pīḍayati || 52 ||
ye śastāstān hitvā ketubhirādhūpite atha vā spṛṣṭe | nakṣatre bhavati vadho yeṣāṃ rājñāṃ pravakṣye tān || 53 ||
[ ādhūmite ] aśvinyāmaśmakapaṃ bharaṇīṣu kirātapārthivaṃ hanyāt | bahulāsu kaliṅgeśaṃ rohiṇyāṃ śūrasenapatim || 54 ||
auśīnaramapi saumye jalajājīvādhipaṃ tathārdrāsu | āditye'śmaka nāthānpuṣye maghadhādhipaṃ hanti || 55 ||
[ nāthaṃ ] asikeśaṃ bhaujaṅge pitrye'ṅgaṃ pāṇḍyanāthamapi bhāgye | aujjayinikamāryamṇe sāvitre daṇḍakādhipatim || 56 ||
[ aujjayanikam ] citrāsu kurukṣetrādhipasya maraṇaṃ samādiśettajjñaḥ | kāśmīrakakāmbojau nṛpatī prābhañjane na staḥ || 57 ||
ikṣvākuralaka nāthaśca hanyate yadi bhavedviśākhāsu | maitre puṇḍrādhipatirjyeṣṭhāsu ca sārvabhaumavadhaḥ || 58 ||
[ nāthau | nātho | jyeṣṭhāsvatha ] mūle'ndhramadrakapatī jaladeve kāśipo maraṇameti | yaudheyakārjunāyanaśivicaidyānvaiśvadeve ca || 59 ||
hanyātkaikayanāthaṃ pāñcanadaṃ siṃhalādhipaṃ vāṅgam | naimiṣanṛpaṃ kirātaṃ śravaṇādiṣu ṣaṭsvimān kramaśaḥ || 60 ||
ulkābhitāḍitaśikhaḥ śikhī śivaḥ śivataro'tidṛṣṭo yaḥ | aśubhaḥ sa eva colāvagāṇasitahūṇacīnānām || 61 ||
[ abhivṛṣṭo ] namrā yataḥ śikhiśikhābhisṛtā yato vā ṛkṣaṃ ca yatspṛśati tatkathitāṃśca deśān | divyaprabhāvanihatān sa yathā garutmānbhuṅkte gato narapatiḥ parabhogibhogān || 62 ||

Chapter 12: agastyacārādhyāyaḥ [agastyacāra-adhyāya]

samudro'ntaḥ śailairmakaranakharotkhātaśikharaiḥ kṛtastoyocchittyā sapadi sutarāṃ yena ruciraḥ | patanmuktāmiśraiḥ pravaramaṇiratnāmbunivahaiḥ surānpratyādeṣṭuṃ mitamukuṭaratnāniva purā || 1 ||
[ sita ] yena cāmbuharaṇe'pi vidrumairbhūdharaiḥ samaṇiratnavidrumaiḥ | nirgataistaduragaiśca rājitaḥ sāgaro'dhikataraṃ virājitaḥ || 2 ||
prasphurattimijalebhajihmagaḥ kṣiptaratnanikaro mahodadhiḥ | āpadāṃ padagato'pi yāpito yena pītasalilo'maraśriyam || 3 ||
pracalattimiśuktijaśaṅkhacitaḥ salile'pahṛte'pi patiḥ saritām | sataraṅgasitotpalahaṃsabhṛtaḥ sarasaḥ śaradīva vibharti rucim || 4 ||
[ rucam ] timisitāmbudharaṃ maṇitārakaṃ sphaṭikacandramanambuśaraddyutiḥ | phaṇiphaṇopalaraśmiśikhigrahaṃ kuṭilageśaviyacca cakāra yaḥ || 5 ||
dinakararathamārgavicchittaye'bhyudyataṃ yaccalacchṛṅgamudbhrāntavidyādharāṃsāvasaktapriyāvyagradattāṅkadehāvalambāmbarātyucchritoddhūyamānadhvajaiḥ śobhitam | karikaṭamadamiśraraktāvalehānuvāsānusāridvirephāvalīnottamāṅgaiḥ kṛtānbāṇapuṣpairivottaṃsakāndhārayadbhirmṛgendraiḥ sanāthīkṛtāntardarīnirjharam ||
gaganatalamivollikhantaṃ pravṛddhairgajākṛṣṭaphulladrumatrāsavibhrāntamattadvirephāvalīhṛṣṭamandrasvanaiḥ śailakūṭaistarakṣarkṣaśārdūlaśākhāmṛgādhyāsitaiḥ | rahasi madanasaktayā revayā kāntayevopagūḍhaṃ surādhyāsitodyānamambhośanānnamūlānilāhāraviprānvitaṃ vindhyamastambhayad yaśca tasyodayaḥ śrūyatām || 6 ||
[ abhy | gīta ] udaye ca muneragastyanāmnaḥ kusamāyogamalapradūṣitāni | hṛdayāni satāmiva svabhāvātpunarambūni bhavanti nirmalāni || 7 ||
pārśvadvayādhiṣṭhitacakravākāmāpuṣṇatī sasvanahaṃsapaṅktim | tāmbūlaraktotkaṣitāgradantī vibhāti yoṣeva śaratsahāsā || 8 ||
[ sarit ] indīvarāsannasitotpalānvitā śaradbhramatṣaṭpadapaṅktibhūṣitā | sabhrūlatākṣepakaṭākṣavīkṣaṇā vidagdhayoṣeva vibhāti sasmarā || 9 ||
[ sarit ] indoḥ payodavigamopahitāṃ vibhūtiṃ draṣṭuṃ taraṅgavalayā kumudaṃ niśāsu | unmīlayatyalinilīnadalaṃ supakṣma vāpī vilocanamivāsitatārakāntam || 10 ||
nānāvicitrāmbujahaṃsakokakāraṇḍavāpūrṇataḍāgahastā | ratnaiḥ prabhūtaiḥ kusumaiḥ phalaiśca bhūryacchatīvārghamagastyanāmne || 11 ||
salilamamarapājñayojjhitaṃ yaddhanapariveṣṭitamūrtibhirbhujaṅgaiḥ | phaṇijanitaviṣāgnisampraduṣṭaṃ bhavati śivaṃ tadagastyadarśanena || 12 ||
smaraṇādapi pāpamapākurute kimuta stutibhirvaruṇāṅgaruhaḥ | munibhiḥ kathito'sya yathārghavidhiḥ kathayāmi tathaiva narendrahitam || 13 ||
saṃkhyāvidhānātpratideśamasya vijñāya sandarśanamādiśejjñaḥ | taccojjayinyāmagatasya kanyāṃ bhāgaiḥ svarākhyaiḥ sphuṭabhāskarasya || 14 ||
[ ujjayanyām ] īṣatprabhinne'ruṇaraśmijālairnaiśe'ndhakāre diśi dakṣiṇasyām | sāṃvatsarāveditadigvibhāge bhūpo'rghamurvyāṃ prayataḥ prayacchet || 15 ||
kālodbhavaiḥ surabhibhiḥ kusumaiḥ phalaiśca ratnaiśca sāgarabhavaiḥ kanakāmbaraiśca | dhenvā vṛṣeṇa paramānnayutaiśca bhakṣyairdadhyakṣataiḥ surabhidhūpavilepanaiśca || 16 ||
narapatirimamarghaṃ śraddadhāno dadhānaḥ pravigatagadadoṣo nirjitārātipakṣaḥ | bhavati yadi ca dadyātsapta varṣāṇi samyagjalanidhi raśanāyāḥ svāmitāṃ yāti bhūmeḥ || 17 ||
[ rasanāyāḥ ] dvijo yathālābhamupāhṛtārghaḥ prāpnoti vedānpramadāśca putrān | vaiśyaśca gāṃ bhūri ghanaṃ ca śūdro rogakṣayaṃ dharmaphalaṃ ca sarve || 18 ||
rogān karoti paruṣaḥ kapilastvavṛṣṭiṃ dhūmro gavāmaśubhakṛtsphuraṇo bhayāya | māñjiṣṭharāgasadṛśaḥ kṣudhamāhavāṃśca kuryādaṇuśca purarodhamagastyanāmā || 19 ||
śātakumbhasadṛśaḥ sphaṭikābhastarpayanniva mahīṃ kiraṇāgraiḥ | dṛśyate yadi tadā pracurānnā bhūrbhavatyabhayarogajanāḍhyā || 20 ||
[ kiraṇaughaiḥ | tataḥ ] ulkayā vinihataḥ śikhinā vā kṣudbhayaṃ marakameva vidhatte | dṛśyate sa kila hastagate'rke rohiṇīmupagate'stamupaiti || 21 ||
[ dhatte ]

Chapter 13: saptarṣicārādhyāyaḥ [saptarṣicāra-adhyāya]

saikāvalīva rājati sasitotpalamālinī sahāseva | nāthavatīva ca dig yaiḥ kauverī saptabhirmunibhiḥ || 1 ||
dhruvanāyakopadeśānnarinartīvottarā bhramadbhiśca | yaiścāramahaṃ teṣāṃ kathayiṣye vṛddhagargamatāt || 2 ||
[ narinarttī ] āsanmaghāsu munayaḥ śāsati pṛthvīṃ yudhiṣṭhire nṛpatau | ṣaḍdvikapañcadviyutaḥ śakakālastasya rājñaśca || 3 ||
ekaikasminnṛkṣe śataṃ śataṃ te caranti varṣāṇām | prāgudayato'pyavivarād rjūnnayati tatra saṃyuktāḥ || 4 ||
[ prāguttarataśca ete sadā udayante sasādhvīkāḥ ] pūrve bhāge bhagavānmarīcirapare sthito vasiṣṭho'smāt | tasyāṅgirāstato'tristasyāsannaḥ pulastyaśca || 5 ||
pulahaḥ kraturiti bhagānāsannā anukrameṇa pūrvādyāt | tatra vasiṣṭhaṃ munivaramupāśritārundhatī sādhvī || 6 ||
[ pūrvādyāḥ ] ulkāśanidhūmādyairhatā vivarṇā viraśmayo hrasvāḥ | hanyuḥ svaṃ svaṃ vargaṃ vipulāḥ snigdhāśca tadvṛddhyai || 7 ||
gandharvadevadānavamantrauṣadhisiddhayakṣanāgānām | pīḍākāro marīcirjñeyo vidyādharāṇāṃ ca || 8 ||
śakayavanadaradapāratakāmbojāṃstāpasānvanopetān | hanti vasiṣṭho'bhihato vivṛddhido raśmisampannaḥ || 9 ||
aṅgiraso jñānayutā dhīmanto brāhmaṇāśca nirdiṣṭāḥ | atreḥ kāntārabhavā jalajānyambhonidhiḥ saritaḥ || 10 ||
rakṣaḥ piśācadānavadaityabhujaṅgāḥ smṛtāḥ pulastyasya | pulahasya tu mūlaphalaṃ kratostu yajñāḥ sayajñabhṛtaḥ || 11 ||

Chapter 14: nakṣatrakūrmādhyāyaḥ [nakṣatrakūrma-adhyāya]

nakṣatratrayavargairāgneyādyairvyavasthitairnavadhā | bhāratavarṣe madhyaprāgādivibhājitā deśāḥ || 1 ||
[ madhyāt ] bhadrārimedamāṇḍavyasālvanīpojjihānasaṃkhyātāḥ | maruvatsaghoṣayāmunasārasvatamatsyamādhyamikāḥ || 2 ||
māthurakopajyotiṣadharmāraṇyāni śūrasenāśca | gauragrīvoddehikapāṇḍuguḍāśvatthapāñcālāḥ || 3 ||
sāketakaṅkakurukālakoṭikukurāśca pāriyātranagaḥ | audumbarakāpiṣṭhalagajāhvayāśceti madhyamidam || 4 ||
atha pūrvasyāmañjanavṛṣabhadhvajapadmamālyavadgirayaḥ | vyāghramukhasuhmakarvaṭacāndrapurāḥ śūrpakarṇāśca || 5 ||
khasamagadhaśibiragirimithilasamataṭoḍrāśvavadanadanturakāḥ | prāgjyotiṣalauhityakṣīrodasamudrapuruṣādāḥ || 6 ||
udayagiribhadragauḍakapauṇḍrotkalakāśimekalāmbaṣṭhāḥ | ekapadatāmraliptakakośalakā vardhamānāśca || 7 ||
[ tāmalipitaka ] āgneyyāṃ diśi kośalakaliṅgavaṅgopavaṅgajaṭharāṅgāḥ | śaulikavidarbhavatsāndhracedikāścordhvakaṇṭhāśca || 8 ||
vṛṣanālikeracarmadvīpā vindhyāntavāsinastripurī | śmaśrudharahemakuḍyavyālagrīvā mahāgrīvāḥ || 9 ||
[ hemakūṭya ] kiṣkindhakaṇṭakasthalaniṣādarāṣṭrāṇi purikadāśārṇāḥ | saha nagnaparṇaśabarairāśleṣādye trike deśāḥ || 10 ||
atha dakṣiṇena laṅkākālājinasaurikīrṇatālikaṭāḥ | girinagaramalayadarduramahendramālindyabharukacchāḥ || 11 ||
kaṅkaṭakaṅkaṇavanavāsiśibikaphaṇikārakoṅkaṇābhīrāḥ | ākaraveṇāvartakadaśapuragonardakeralakāḥ || 12 ||
[ ṭaṅkaṇa | āvantaka ] karṇāṭamahāṭavicitrakūṭanāsikyakollagiricolāḥ | krauñcadvīpajaṭādharakāveryo riṣyamūkaśca || 13 ||
vaidūryaśaṅkhamuktātrivāricaradharmapaṭṭanadvīpāḥ | gaṇarājyakṛṣṇavellūrapiśikaśūrpādrikusumanagāḥ || 14 ||
tumbavanakārmaṇayakayāmyodadhitāpasāśramā ṛṣikāḥ | kāñcīmarucīpaṭṭanaceryāryakasiṃhalā ṛṣabhāḥ || 15 ||
[ kārmaṇeyaka ] baladevapaṭṭanaṃ daṇḍakāvanatimiṅgilāśanā bhadrāḥ | kaccho'tha kuñjaradarī satāmraparṇīti vijñeyāḥ || 16 ||
nairṛtyāṃ diśi deśāḥ pahlavakāmbojasindhusauvīrāḥ | vaḍavāmukhāravāmbaṣṭhakapilanārīmukhānartāḥ || 17 ||
pheṇagiriyavanamārgarakarṇaprāveyapāraśavaśūdrāḥ | barbarakirātakhaṇḍakravyādābhīracañcūkāḥ || 18 ||
[ mākara | kravyāśyā ] hemagirisindhukālakaraivatakasurāṣṭrabādaradraviḍāḥ | svātyādye bhatritaye jñeyaśca mahārṇavo'traiva || 19 ||
aparasyāṃ maṇimānmeghavānvanaughaḥ kṣurārpaṇo'stagiriḥ | aparāntakaśāntikahaihayapraśastādrivokkāṇāḥ || 20 ||
pañcanadaramaṭhapāratatārakṣitijṛṅgavaiśyakanakaśakāḥ | nirmaryādā mlecchā ye paścimadiksthitāste ca || 21 ||
diśi paścimottarasyāṃ māṇḍavyatuṣāratālahalamadrāḥ | aśmakakulūtahalaḍāḥ strīrājyanṛsiṃhavanakhasthāḥ || 22 ||
[ tukhāra | haḍa ] veṇumatī phalgulukā guluhā marukuccacarmaraṅgākhyāḥ | ekavilocanaśūlikadīrghagrīvāsyakeśāśca || 23 ||
uttarataḥ kailāso himavānvasumān girirdhanuṣmāṃśca | krauñco meruḥ kuravastathottarāḥ kṣudramīnāśca || 24 ||
kaikayavasātiyāmunabhogaprasthārjunāyanāgnīdhrāḥ | ādarāntardvīpitrigartaturagānanāḥ śvamukhāḥ || 25 ||
[ ādarśāntadvīpi | turagānanāśvamukhāḥ ] keśadharacipiṭanāsikadāserakavāṭadhānaśaradhānāḥ | takṣaśilapuṣkalāvatakailāvatakaṇṭhadhānāśca || 26 ||
ambaramadrakamālavapauravakacchāradaṇḍapiṅgalakāḥ | māṇahalahūṇakohalaśītakamāṇḍavyabhūtapurāḥ || 27 ||
gāndhārayaśovatihematālarājanyakhacaragavyāśca | yaudheyadāsameyāḥ śyāmākāḥ kṣemadhūrtāśca || 28 ||
aiśānyāṃ merukanaṣṭarājyapaśupālakīrakāśmīrāḥ | abhisāradaradataṅgaṇakulūtasairindhravanarāṣṭrāḥ || 29 ||
[ sairindha ] brahmapuradārvaḍāmaravanarājyakirātacīnakauṇindāḥ | bhallāḥ paṭolajaṭāsurakunaṭakhasaghoṣakucikākhyāḥ || 30 ||
[ bhallāpalola | kunaṭhakhaṣa ] ekacaraṇānuviddhāḥ suvarṇabhūrvasudhanaṃ diviṣṭhāśca | pauravacīranivāsitrinetramuñjādrigāndharvāḥ || 31 ||
[ anuviśvāḥ | vasuvanaṃ | cīranivāsana | gandharvāḥ ] vargairāgneyādyaiḥ krūragrahapīḍitaiḥ krameṇa nṛpāḥ | pāñcālo māgadhikaḥ kāliṅgaśca kṣayaṃ yānti || 32 ||
āvanto'thānarto mṛtyuṃ cāyāti sindhusauvīraḥ | rājā ca hārahauro madreśo'nyaśca kauṇindaḥ || 33 ||

Chapter 15: nakṣatravyūhādhyāyaḥ [nakṣatravyūha-adhyāya]

āgneye sitakusumāhitāgnimantrajñasūtrabhāṣyajñāḥ | ākarikanāpitadvijaghaṭakārapurohitābdajñāḥ || 1 ||
rohiṇyāṃ suvratapaṇyabhūpadhaniyogayuktaśākaṭikāḥ | govṛṣajalacarakarṣakaśiloccayaiśvaryasampannāḥ || 2 ||
mṛgaśirasi surabhivastrābjakusumaphalaratnavanacaravihaṅgāḥ | mṛgasomapīthigāndharvakāmukā lekhahārāśca || 3 ||
raudre vadhabandhānṛtaparadārasteyaśāṭhyabhedaratāḥ | tuṣadhānyatīkṣṇamantrābhicāravetālakarmajñāḥ || 4 ||
āditye satyaudāryaśaucakularūpadhīyaśo'rthayutāḥ | uttamadhānyaṃ vaṇijaḥ sevābhiratāḥ saśilpijanāḥ || 5 ||
puṣye yavagodhūmāḥ śālīkṣuvanāni mantriṇo bhūpāḥ | salilopajīvinaḥ sādhavaśca yajñeṣṭisaktāśca || 6 ||
ahideve kṛtrimakandamūlaphalakīṭapannagaviṣāṇi | paradhanaharaṇābhiratāstuṣadhānyaṃ sarvabhiṣajaśca || 7 ||
pitrye dhanadhānyāḍhyāḥ koṣṭhāgārāṇi parvatāśrayiṇaḥ | pitṛbhaktavaṇigśūrāḥ kravyādāḥ strīdviṣo manujāḥ || 8 ||
prākphalgunīṣu naṭayuvatisubhagagāndharvaśilpipaṇyāni | karpāsalavaṇamakṣikatailāni kumārakāścāpi || 9 ||
[ mākṣika ] āryamṇe mārdavaśaucavinayapākhaṇḍidānaśāstraratāḥ | śobhanadhānyamahādhanakarmānuratāḥ samanujendrāḥ || 10 ||
[ pāṣaṇḍi ] haste taskarakuñjararathikamahāmātraśilpipaṇyāni | tuṣadhānyaṃ śrutayuktā vaṇijastejoyutāścātra || 11 ||
tvāṣṭre bhūṣaṇamaṇirāgalekhyagāndharvagandhayuktijñāḥ | gaṇitapaṭutantuvāyāḥ śālākyā rājadhānyāni || 12 ||
svātau khagamṛgaturagā vaṇijo dhānyāni vātabahulāni | asthirasauhṛdalaghusattvatāpasāḥ paṇyakuśalāśca || 13 ||
indrāgnidaivate raktapuṣpaphalaśākhinaḥ satilamudgāḥ | karpāsamāṣacaṇakāḥ purandarahutāśabhaktāśca || 14 ||
maitre śauryasametā gaṇanāyakasādhugoṣṭhiyānaratāḥ | ye sādhavaśca loke sarvaṃ ca śaratsamutpannam || 15 ||
paurandare'tiśūrāḥ kulavittayaśo'nvitāḥ parasvahṛtaḥ | vijigīṣavo narendrāḥ senānāṃ cāpi netāraḥ || 16 ||
mūle bheṣajabhiṣajo gaṇamukhyāḥ kusumamūlaphalavārtāḥ | bījānyatidhanayuktāḥ phalamūlairye ca vartante || 17 ||
[ vārttāḥ ] āpye mṛdavo jalamārgagāminaḥ satyaśaucadhanayuktāḥ | setukaravārijīvakaphalakusumānyambujātāni || 18 ||
viśveśvare mahāmātramallakarituragadevatāsaktāḥ | sthāvarayodhā bhogānvitāśca ye tejasā yuktāḥ || 19 ||
[ bhaktāḥ | caujasā ] śravaṇe māyāpaṭavo nityodyuktāśca karmasu samarthāḥ | utsāhinaḥ sadharmā bhāgavatāḥ satyavacanāśca || 20 ||
vasubhe mānonmuktāḥ klībācalasauhṛdāḥ striyāṃ dveṣyāḥ | dānābhiratā bahuvittasaṃyutāḥ śamaparāśca narāḥ || 21 ||
[ klībāś | dvaṣyāḥ | dveṣyāḥ ] varuṇeśe pāśikamatsyabandhajalajāni jalacarājīvāḥ | saukarikarajakaśauṇḍikaśākunikāścāpi varge'smin || 22 ||
āje taskarapaśupālahiṃsrakīnāśanīcaśaṭhaceṣṭāḥ | dharmavratairvirahitā niyuddhakuśalāśca ye manujāḥ || 23 ||
āhirbudhnye viprāḥ kratudānatapoyutā mahāvibhavāḥ | āśramiṇaḥ pākhaṇḍā nareśvarāḥ sāradhānyaṃ ca || 24 ||
[ āhirbudhnyu | pāṣaṇḍā ] pauṣṇe salilajaphalakusumalavaṇamaṇiśaṅkhamauktikābjāni | surabhikusumāni gandhā vaṇijo naukarṇadhārāśca || 25 ||
aśvinyāmaśvaharāḥ senāpativaidyasevakāsturagāḥ | turagārohā vaṇijo rūpopetāsturagarakṣāḥ || 26 ||
[ turagārohāśca vanig ] yāmye'sṛkpiśitabhujaḥ krūrā vadhabandhatāḍanāsaktāḥ | tuṣadhānyaṃ nīcakulodbhavā vihīnāśca sattvena || 27 ||
pūrvātrayaṃ sānalamagrajānāṃ rājñāṃ tu puṣyeṇa sahottarāṇi | sapauṣṇamaitraṃ pitṛdaivataṃ ca prajāpaterbhaṃ ca kṛṣīvalānām || 28 ||
ādityahastābhijidāśvināni vaṇigjanānāṃ pravadanti tāni | mūlatrinetrānilavāruṇāni bhānyugrajāteḥ prabhaviṣṇutāyāḥ || 29 ||
[ bhāni | prabhaviṣṇutāyām ] saumyaindracitrāvasudaivatāni sevājanasvāmyamupāgatāni | sārpaṃ viśākhā śravaṇo bharaṇyaścaṇḍālajāterabhinirdiśanti || 30 ||
[ iti nirdaśanti ] raviravisutabhogamāgataṃ kṣitisutabhedanavakradūṣitam | grahaṇagatamatholkayā hataṃ niyatamuṣākarapīḍitaṃ ca yat || 31 ||
tadupahatamiti pracakṣate prakṛtiviparyayayātameva vā | nigaditaparivargadūṣaṇaṃ kathitaviparyayagaṃ samṛddhaye || 32 ||

Chapter 16: grahabhaktiyogādhyāyaḥ [grahabhaktiyoga-adhyāya]

prāṅ narmadārdhaśoṇoḍravaṅgasuhmāḥ kaliṅgabāhlīkāḥ | śakayavanamagadhaśabaraprāgjyotiṣacīnakāmbojāḥ || 1 ||
mekalakirātaviṭakā bahirantaḥ śailajāḥ pulindāśca | draviḍānāṃ prāgardhaṃ dakṣiṇakūlaṃ ca yamunāyāḥ || 2 ||
campodumbarakauśāmbicedivindhyāṭavīkaliṅgāśca | puṇḍrā golāṅgūlaśrīparvatavardhamānāni || 3 ||
[ vardhamānāśca ] ikṣumatītyatha taskarapāratakāntāragopabījānām | tuṣadhānyakaṭukatarukanakadahanaviṣasamaraśūrāṇām || 4 ||
bheṣajabhiṣakcatuṣpadakṛṣikaranṛpahiṃsrayāyicaurāṇām | vyālāraṇyayaśoyutatīkṣṇāṇāṃ bhāskaraḥ svāmī || 5 ||
girisaliladurgakośalabharukacchasamudraromakatuṣārāḥ | vanavāsitaṅgaṇahalastrīrājyamahārṇavadvīpāḥ || 6 ||
[ tukhārāḥ ] madhurarasakusumaphalasalilalavaṇamaṇiśaṅkhamauktikābjānām | śāliyavauṣadhigodhūmasomapākrandaviprāṇām || 7 ||
sitasubhagaturagaratikarayuvaticamūnāthabhojyavastrāṇām | śṛṅginiśācarakārṣakayajñavidāṃ cādhipaścandraḥ || 8 ||
śoṇasya narmadāyā bhīmarathāyāśca paścimārdhasthāḥ | nirvindhyā vetravatī siprā godāvarī veṇā || 9 ||
mandākinī payoṣṇī mahānadī sindhumālatīpārāḥ | uttarapāṇḍyamahendrādrivindhyamalayopagāścolāḥ || 10 ||
draviḍavidehāndhrāśmakabhāsāparakauṅkaṇāḥ samantriṣikāḥ | kuntalakeraladaṇḍakakāntipuramlecchasaṅkariṇaḥ || 11 ||
[ bhāsāpura | saṅkarajāḥ ] nāsikyabhogavardhanavirāṭavindhyādripārśvagā deśāḥ | ye ca pibanti sutoyāṃ tāpīṃ ye ca api gomatīsalilam || K(12) ||
nāgarakṛṣikarapāratahutāśanājīviśastravārtānām | āṭavikadurgakarvaṭavadhikanṛśaṃsāvaliptānām || 12 ||
[ śastravārttānām | vadhaka ] narapatikumārakuñjaradāmbhikaḍimbhābhighātapaśupānām | raktaphalakusumavidrumacamūpaguḍamadyatīkṣṇānām || 13 ||
kośabhavanāgnihotrikadhātvākaraśākyabhikṣucaurāṇām | śaṭhadīrghavairabahvāśināṃ ca vasudhāsuto'dhipatiḥ || 14 ||
lohityaḥ sindhunadaḥ sarayūrgāmbhīrikā rathākhyā ca | gaṅgākauśikyādyāḥ sarito vaidehakāmbojāḥ || 15 ||
mathurāyāḥ pūrvārdhaṃ himavadgomantacitrakūṭasthāḥ | saurāṣṭrasetujalamārgapaṇyabilaparvatāśrayiṇaḥ || 16 ||
udapānayantragāndharvalekhyamaṇirāgagandhayuktividaḥ | ālekhyaśabdagaṇitaprasādhakāyuṣyaśilpajñāḥ || 17 ||
carapuruṣakuhakajīvakaśiśukaviśaṭhasūcakābhicāraratāḥ | dūtanapuṃsakahāsyajñabhūtatantrendrajālajñāḥ || 18 ||
ārakṣakanaṭanartakaghṛtatailasnehabījatiktāni | vratacārirasāyanakuśalavesarāścandraputrasya || 19 ||
sindhunadapūrvabhāgo mathurāpaścārdhabharatasauvīrāḥ | srughnaudīcyavipāśāsaricchatadrū ramaṭhaśālvāḥ || 20 ||
[ udīcya | sālvāḥ ] traigartapauravāmbaṣṭhapāratā vāṭadhānayaudheyāḥ | sārasvatārjunāyanamatsyārdhagrāmarāṣṭrāṇi || 21 ||
[ pauraba ] hastyaśvapurohitabhūpamantrimāṅgalyapauṣṭikāsaktāḥ | kāruṇyasatyaśaucavratavidyādānadharmayutāḥ || 22 ||
pauramahādhanaśabdārthavedaviduṣo'bhicāranītijñāḥ | manujeśvaropakaraṇaṃ chatradhvajacāmarādyaṃ ca || 23 ||
śaileyakuṣṭhamāṃsītagararasasaindhavāni vallījam | madhurarasamadhūcchiṣṭāni corakaśceti jīvasya || 24 ||
[ kaṣṭha ] takṣaśilamartikāvatabahugirigāndhārapuṣkalāvatakāḥ | prasthalamālavakaikayadāśārṇośīnarāḥ śibayaḥ || 25 ||
[ mārtikāvata ] ye ca pibanti vitastāmirāvatīṃ candrabhāgasaritaṃ ca | ratharajatākarakuñjaraturagamahāmātradhanayuktāḥ || 26 ||
surabhikusumānulepanamaṇivajravibhūṣaṇāmburuhaśayyāḥ | varataruṇayuvatikāmopakaraṇamṛṣṭānnamadhurabhujaḥ || 27 ||
udyānasalilakāmukayaśaḥ sukhaudāryarūpasampannāḥ | vidvadamātyavaṇigjanaghaṭakṛccitrāṇḍajāstriphalāḥ || 28 ||
kauśeyapaṭṭakambalapatraurṇikarodhrapatracocāni | jātīphalāguruvacāpippalyaścandanaṃ ca bhṛgoḥ || 29 ||
ānartārbudapuṣkarasaurāṣṭrābhīraśūdraraivatakāḥ | naṣṭā yasmindeśe sarasvatī paścimo deśaḥ || 30 ||
kurubhūmijāḥ prabhāsaṃ vidiśā vedasmṛtī mahītaṭajāḥ | khalamalinanīcatailikavihīnasattvopahatapuṃstvāḥ || 31 ||
bāndhanaśākunikāśucikaivartavirūpavṛddhasaukarikāḥ | gaṇapūjyaskhalitavrataśabarapulindārthaparihīnāḥ || 32 ||
[ bandhana ] kaṭutiktarasāyanavidhavayoṣito bhujagataskaramahiṣyaḥ | kharakarabhacaṇakavātalaniṣpāvāścārkaputrasya || 33 ||
[ vātula ] giriśikharakandaradarīviniviṣṭā mlecchajātayaḥ śūdrāḥ | gomāyubhakṣaśūlikavokkāṇāśvamukhavikalāṅgāḥ || 34 ||
kulapāṃsanahiṃsrakṛtaghnacauraniḥsatyaśaucadānāśca | kharacaraniyuddhavittīvraroṣagarttāśrayā nīcāḥ || 35 ||
[ garbhāśayā ] upahatadāmbhikarākṣasanidrābahulāśca jantavaḥ sarve | dharmeṇa ca saṃtyaktā māṣatilāścārkaśaśiśatroḥ || 36 ||
giridurgapahlavaśvetahūṇacolāvagāṇamarucīnāḥ | pratyantadhanimahecchavyavasāyaparākramopetāḥ || 37 ||
paradāravivādaratāḥ pararandhrakutūhalā madotsiktāḥ | mūrkhādhārmikavijigīṣavaśca ketoḥ samākhyātāḥ || 38 ||
udayasamaye yaḥ snigdhāṃśurmahānprakṛtisthito yadi ca na hato nirghātolkārajograhamardanaiḥ | svabhavanagataḥ svoccaprāptaḥ śubhagrahavīkṣitaḥ sa bhavati śivasteṣāṃ yeṣāṃ prabhuḥ parikīrtitaḥ || 39 ||
abhihitaviparītalakṣaṇe kṣayamupagacchati tatparigrahaḥ | ḍamarabhayagadāturā janā narapatayaśca bhavanti duḥkhitāḥ || 40 ||
[ lakṣanaiḥ ] yadi na ripukṛtaṃ bhayaṃ nṛpāṇāṃ svasutakṛtaṃ niyamādamātyajaṃ vā | bhavati janapadasya cāpyavṛṣṭyā gamanamapūrvapurādrinimnagāsu || 41 ||

Chapter 17: grahayuddhādhyāyaḥ [grahayuddha-adhyāya]

yuddhaṃ yathā yadā vā bhaviṣyamādiśyate trikālajñaiḥ | tadvijñānaṃ karaṇe mayā kṛtaṃ sūryasiddhānte || 1 ||
[ bhaviṣyad | siddhāntāt ] viyati caratāṃ grahāṇāmuparyuparyātmamārgasaṃsthānām | atidūrāddṛgviṣaye samatāmiva samprayātānām || 2 ||
āsannakramayogādbhedollekhāṃśumardanāsavyaiḥ | yuddhaṃ catuṣprakāraṃ parāśarādyairmunibhiruktam || 3 ||
[ asavyaḥ ] bhede vṛṣṭivināśo bhedaḥ suhṛdāṃ mahākulānāṃ ca | ullekhe śastrabhayaṃ mantrivirodhaḥ priyānnatvam || 4 ||
amśuvirodhe yuddhāni bhūbhṛtāṃ śastrarukkṣudavamardāḥ | yuddhe cāpyapasavye bhavanti yuddhāni bhūpānām || 05 ||
ravirākrando madhye pauraḥ pūrve'pare sthito yāyī | paurā budhagururavijā nityaṃ śītāṃśurākrandaḥ || 6 ||
[ ākrandraḥ ] ketukujarāhuśukrā yāyina ete hatā ghnanti | ākrandayāyipaurān jayino jayadāḥ svavargasya || 7 ||
[ grahā hanyuḥ | jayadā ] paure paureṇa hate paurāḥ paurānnṛpānvinighnanti | evaṃ yāyyākrandā nāgarayāyigrahāścaiva || 8 ||
[ yāyyākrandau ] dakṣiṇadiksthaḥ paruṣo vepathuraprāpya sannivṛtto'ṇuḥ | adhirūḍho vikṛto niṣprabho vivarṇaśca yaḥ sa jitaḥ || 9 ||
uktaviparītalakṣaṇasampanno jayagato vinirdeśyaḥ | vipulaḥ snigdho dyutimāndakṣiṇadikstho'pi jayayuktaḥ || 10 ||
[ vinirdiṣṭaḥ ] dvāvapi mayūkhayuktau vipulau snigdhau samāgame bhavataḥ | tatra anyonyaṃ prītirviparītāvātmapakṣaghnau || 11 ||
[ anyonyaprītir ] yuddhaṃ samāgamo vā yadyavyaktau svalakṣaṇairbhavataḥ | bhuvi bhūbhṛtāmapi tathā phalamavyaktaṃ vinirdeśyam || 12 ||
[ tu lakṣaṇair ] guruṇā jite'vanisute bāhlīkā yāyino'gnivārtāśca | śaśijena śūrasenāḥ kaliṅgaśālvāśca pīḍyante || 13 ||
[ agnivārttāśca | sālvāś ] saureṇāre vijite jayanti paurāḥ prajāśca sīdanti | koṣṭhāgāramlecchakṣatriyatāpaśca śukrajite || 14 ||
[ koṣṭhāgāra ] bhaumena hate śaśije vṛkṣasarittāpasāśmakanarendrāḥ | uttaradiksthāḥ kratudīkṣitāśca santāpamāyānti || 15 ||
guruṇā jite budhe mlecchaśūdracaurārthayuktapaurajanāḥ | traigartapārvatīyāḥ pīḍyante kampate ca mahī || 16 ||
[ budhe jite ] ravijena budhe dhvaste nāvikayodhābjasadhanagarbhiṇyaḥ | bhṛguṇā jite'gnikopaḥ sasyāmbudayāyividhvaṃsaḥ || 17 ||
jīve śukrābhihate kulūtagāndhārakaikayā madrāḥ | śālvā vatsā vaṅgā gāvaḥ sasyāni pīḍyante || 18 ||
[ sālvā | naśyanti ] bhaumena hate jīve madhyo deśo nareśvarā gāvaḥ | saureṇa cārjunāyanavasātiyaudheyaśibiviprāḥ || 19 ||
śaśitanayenāpi jite bṛhaspatau mlecchasatyaśastrabhṛtaḥ | upayānti madhyadeśaśca saṃkṣayaṃ yacca bhaktiphalam || 20 ||
śukre bṛhaspatijite yāyī śreṣṭho vināśamupayāti | brahmakṣatravirodhaḥ salilaṃ ca na vāsavastyajati || 21 ||
[ hate ] kośalakaliṅgavaṅgā vatsā matsyāśca madhyadeśayutāḥ | mahatīṃ vrajanti pīḍāṃ napuṃsakāḥ śūrasenāśca || 22 ||
kujavijite bhṛgutanaye balamukhyavadho narendrasaṃgrāmāḥ | saumyena pārvatīyāḥ kṣīravināśo'lpavṛṣṭiśca || 23 ||
ravijena site vijite guṇamukhyāḥ śastrajīvinaḥ kṣatram | jalajāśca nipīḍyante sāmānyaṃ bhaktiphalamanyat || 24 ||
[ gaṇamukhyāḥ ] asite sitena nihate'rghavṛddhirahivihagamānināṃ pīḍā | kṣitijena taṅgaṇāndhroḍrakāśibāhlīkadeśānām || 25 ||
saumyena parābhūte mande'ṅgavaṇigvihaṅgapaśunāgāḥ | santāpyante guruṇā strībahulā mahiṣakaśakāśca || 26 ||
ayaṃ viśeṣo'bhihito hatānāṃ kujajñavāgīśasitāsitānām | phalaṃ tu vācyaṃ grahabhaktito'nyad yathā tathā ghnanti hatāḥ svabhaktīḥ || 27 ||

Chapter 18: śaśigrahasamāgamādhyāyaḥ [śaśigrahasamāgama-adhyāya]

bhānāṃ yathāsambhavamuttareṇa yāto grahāṇāṃ yadi vā śaśāṅkaḥ | pradakṣiṇaṃ tacchubhadaṃ nṛpāṇāṃ yāmyena yāto na śivaḥ śaśāṅkaḥ || 1 ||
[ śubhakṛnnarāṇāṃ ] candramā yadi kujasya yātyudakpārvatīyabalaśālināṃ jayaḥ | kṣatriyāḥ pramuditāḥ sayāyino bhūridhānyamuditā vasundharā || 2 ||
uttarataḥ svasutasya śaśaṅkaḥ paurajayāya subhikṣakaraśca | sasyacayaṃ kurute janahārdiṃ kośacayaṃ ca narādhipatīnām || 3 ||
bṛhaspateruttarage śaśāṅke pauradvijakṣatriyapaṇḍitānām | dharmasya deśasya ca madhyamasya vṛddhiḥ subhikṣaṃ muditāḥ prajāśca || 4 ||
bhārgavasya yadi yātyudak śaśī kośayuktagajavājivṛddhidaḥ | yāyināṃ ca vijayo dhanuṣmatāṃ sasyasampadapi cottamā tadā || 5 ||
ravijasya śaśī pradakṣiṇaṃ kuryāccetpurabhūbhṛtāṃ jayaḥ | śakabāhlikasindhupahlavā mudabhājo yavanaiḥ samanvitāḥ || 6 ||
[ mudbhājo ] yeṣāmudaggaccchati bhagrahāṇāṃ prāleyaraśmirnirupadravaśca | taddravyapauretarabhaktideśānpuṣṇāti yāmyena nihanti tāni || 7 ||
śaśini phalamudaksthe yadgrahasyopadiṣṭaṃ bhavati tadapasavye sarvameva pratīpam | iti śaśisamavāyāḥ kīrtitā bhagrahāṇāṃ na khalu bhavati yuddhaṃ sākamindorgraharkṣaiḥ || 8 ||
[ udakasthe | kīrttitā ]

Chapter 19: grahavarṣaphalādhyāyaḥ [grahavarṣaphala-adhyāya]

sarvatra bhūrviralasasyayutā vanāni daivādbibhakṣayiṣudaṃṣṭrisamāvṛtāni | nadyaśca naiva hi payaḥ pracuraṃ sravanti rugbheṣajāni na tathātibalānvitāni || 1 ||
[ syandanti | ca | sravantyo ] tīkṣṇaṃ tapatyaditijaḥ śiśire'pi kāle nātyambudā jalamuco'calasannikāśāḥ | naṣṭaprabharkṣagaṇaśītakaraṃ nabhaśca sīdanti tāpasakulāni sagokulāni || 2 ||
hastyaśvapattimadasahyabalairupetā bāṇāsanāsimuśalātiśayāścaranti | ghnanto nṛpā yudhi nṛpānucaraiśca deśān saṃvatsare dinakarasya dine'tha māse || 3 ||
vyāptaṃ nabhaḥ pracalitācalasannikāśairvyālāñjanāligavalacchavibhiḥ payodaiḥ | gāṃ pūrayadbhirakhilāmamalābhiradbhirutkaṇṭhitena guruṇā dhvanitena cāśāḥ || 4 ||
[ utkaṇṭhakena ] toyāni padmakumudotpalavantyatīva phulladrumāṇyupavanānyalināditāni | gāvaḥ prabhūtapayaso nayanābhirāmā rāmā ratairavirataṃ ramayanti rāmān || 5 ||
godhūmaśāliyavadhānyavarekṣuvāṭā bhūḥ pālyate nṛpatibhirnagarākarāḍhyā | cityaṅkitā kratuvareṣṭivighuṣṭanādā saṃvatsare śiśiragorabhisampravṛtte || 6 ||
vātoddhataścarati vahniratipracaṇḍo grāmānvanāni nagarāṇi ca sandidhakṣuḥ | hāheti dasyugaṇapātahatā raṭanti niḥsvīkṛtā vipaśavo bhuvi martyasaṃghāḥ || 7 ||
abhyunnatā viyati saṃhatamūrtayo'pi muñcanti kutra cidapaḥ pracuraṃ payodāḥ | sīmni prajātamapi śoṣamupaiti sasyaṃ niṣpannamapyavinayādapare haranti || 8 ||
[ na kva cid ] bhūpā na samyagabhipālanasaktacittāḥ pittottharukpracuratā bhujagaprakopaḥ | evaṃvidhairupahṛtā bhavati prajeyaṃ saṃvatsare'vanisutasya vipannasasyā || 9 ||
[ upahatā ] māyendrajālakuhakākaranāgarāṇāṃ gāndharvalekhyagaṇitāstravidāṃ ca vṛddhiḥ | piprīṣayā nṛpatayo'dbhutadarśanāni ditsanti tuṣṭijananāni parasparebhyaḥ || 10 ||
vārtā jagatyavitathā vikalā trayī ca samyakcaratyapi manoriva daṇḍanītiḥ | adhyakṣara svabhiniviṣṭadhiyo'pi ke cidānvīkṣikīṣu ca paraṃ padamīhamānāḥ || 11 ||
[ vārttā | adhyakṣaraṃ | atra ] hāsyajñadūtakavibālanapuṃsakānāṃ yuktijñasetujalaparvatavāsināṃ ca | hārdiṃ karoti mṛgalāñchanajaḥ svake'bde māse'tha vā pracuratā bhuvi cauṣadhīnām || 12 ||
[ pracuratāṃ ] dhvaniruccarito'dhvare dyugāmī vipulo yajñamuṣāṃ manāṃsi bhindan | vicaratyaniśaṃ dvijottamānāṃ hṛdayānandakaro'dhvarāṃśabhājām || 13 ||
kṣitiruttamasasyavatyanekadvipapattyaśvadhanorugokulāḍhyā | kṣitipairabhipālanapravṛddhā dyucaraspardhijanā tadā vibhāti || 14 ||
vividhairviyadunnataiḥ payodairvṛtamurvīṃ payasābhitarpayadbhiḥ | surarājaguroḥ śubhe tu varṣe bahusasyā kṣitiruttamarddhiyuktā || 15 ||
