māṃsaudanamadyaiḥ piśācadititanayadānavāḥ pūjyāḥ | abhyañjanāñjanatilaiḥ pitaro māṃsaudanaiścāpi || 30 ||
sāmayajurbhirmunayastv ṛgbhirgandhaiśca dhūpamālyayutaiḥ | aśleṣakavarṇaistrimadhureṇa cābhyarcayednāgān || 31 ||
dhūpājyāhutimālyairvibudhān ratnaḥ stutipraṇāmaiśca | gandharvānapsaraso gandhairmālyaiśca susugandhaiḥ || 32 ||
[ ratnaiḥ ] śeṣāṃstu sārvavarṇikabalibhiḥ pūjāṃ nyasecca sarveṣām | pratisaravastrapatākābhūṣaṇayajñopavītāni || 33 ||
maṇḍalapaścimabhāge kṛtvāgniṃ dakṣiṇe'tha vā vedyām | ādadyātsambhārāndarbhāndīrghānagarbhāṃśca || 34 ||
lājājyākṣatadadhimadhusiddhārthakagandhasumanaso dhūpaḥ | gorocanāñjanatilāḥ svartujamadhurāṇi ca phalāni || 35 ||
[ dhupān | tilān ] saghṛtasya pāyasasya ca tatra śarāvāṇi taiśca sambhāraiḥ | paścimavedyāṃ pūjāṃ kuryātsnānasya sā vedī || 36 ||
[ snātasya ] tasyāḥ koṇeṣu dṛḍhān kalaśān sitasūtraveṣṭitagrīvān | sakṣīravṛkṣapallavaphalāpidhānānvyavasthāpya || 37 ||
puṣyasnānavimiśreṇāpūrṇānambhasā saratnāṃśca | puṣyasnānadravyāṇyādadyādgargagītāni || 38 ||
jyotiṣmatīṃ trāyamāṇāmabhayāmaparājitām | jīvāṃ viśveśvarīṃ pāṭhāṃ samaṅgāṃ vijayāṃ tathā || 39 ||
sahāṃ ca sahadevīṃ ca pūrṇakośāṃ śatāvarīm | ariṣṭikāṃ śivāṃ bhadrāṃ teṣu kumbheṣu vinyaset || 40 ||
brāhmīṃ kṣemāmajāṃ caiva sarvabījāni kāñcanīm | maṅgalyāni yathālābhaṃ sarvauṣadhyo rasāstathā || 41 ||
[ kāñcanam | rasāṃs ] ratnāni sarvagandhāśca bilvaṃ ca savikaṅkatam | praśastanāmnyaścauṣadhyo hiraṇyaṃ maṅgalāni ca || 42 ||
[ sarvagandhāṃś ] ādāvanaḍuhaścarma jarayā saṃhṛtāyuṣaḥ | praśastalakṣaṇabhṛtaḥ prācīnagrīvamāstaret || 43 ||
tato vṛṣasya yodhasya carma rohitamakṣatam | simhasyātha tṛtīyaṃ syādvyāghrasya ca tataḥ param || 44 ||
catvāryetāni carmāṇi tasyāṃ vedyāmupāstaret | śubhe muhūrte samprāpte puṣyayukte niśākare || 45 ||
bhadrāsanamekatamena kāritaṃ kanakarajatatāmrāṇām | kṣīratarunirmitaṃ vā vinyasyaṃ carmaṇāmupari || 46 ||
trividhastasyocchrāyo hastaḥ pādādhiko'rdhayuktaśca | māṇḍalikānantarajitsamastarājyārthināṃ śubhadaḥ || 47 ||
antardhāya hiraṇyaṃ tatropaviśennareśvaraḥ sumanāḥ | sacivāptapurohitadaivapaurakalyāṇanāmavṛtaḥ || 48 ||
vandijanapauravipraiḥ praghuṣṭapuṇyāhavedanirghoṣaiḥ | samṛdaṅgaśaṅkhatūryairmaṅgalaśabdairhatāniṣṭaḥ || 49 ||
[ viprapraghuṣṭa ] ahatakṣaumanivasanaṃ purohitaḥ kambalena sañchādya | kṛtabalipūjaṃ kalaśairabhiṣiñcetsarpiṣā pūrṇaiḥ || 50 ||
aṣṭāvaṣṭāviṃśatiraṣṭaśataṃ vāpi kalaśaparimāṇam | adhike'dhike guṇottaramayaṃ ca mantro'tra munigītaḥ || 51 ||
ājyaṃ tejaḥ samuddiṣṭamājyaṃ pāpaharaṃ param | ājyaṃ surāṇāmāhāra ājye lokāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ || 52 ||
bhaumāntarikṣaṃ divyaṃ vā yatte kalmaṣamāgatam | sarvaṃ tadājyasaṃsparśātpraṇāśamupagacchatu || 53 ||
[ kalviṣaṃ ] kambalamapanīya tataḥ puṣyasnānāmbubhiḥ saphalapuṣpaiḥ | abhiṣiñcenmanujendraṃ purohito'nena mantreṇa || 54 ||
surāstvāmabhiṣiñcantu ye ca siddhāḥ purātanāḥ | brahmā viṣṇuśca rudraśca sādhyāśca samarudgaṇāḥ || 55 ||
[ śambhuś ] ādityā vasavo rudrā aśvinau ca bhiṣagvarau | aditirdevamātā ca svāhā siddhiḥ sarasvatī || 56 ||
kīrtirlakṣmīrdhṛtiḥ śrīśca sinīvālī kuhūstathā | danuśca surasā caiva vinatā kadrureva ca || 57 ||
devapatnyaśca yā noktā devamātara eva ca | sarvāstvāmabhiṣiñcantu divyāścāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ || 58 ||
nakṣatrāṇi muhūrtāśca pakṣāhorātrasandhayaḥ | saṃvatsarā dineśāśca kalāḥ kāṣṭhāḥ kṣaṇā lavā || 59 ||
sarve tvāmabhiṣiñcantu kālasyāvayavāḥ śubhāḥ | ete cānye ca munayo vedavrataparāyaṇāḥ || 60 ||
saśiṣyāste'bhiṣiñcantu sadārāśca tapodhanāḥ | vaimānikāḥ suragaṇā manavaḥ sāgaraiḥ saha || 61 ||
saritaśca mahābhāgā nāgāḥ kiṃpuruṣāś tathā | vaikhānasā mahābhāgā dvijā vaihāyasāśca ye || 62 ||
saptarṣayaḥ sadārāśca dhruvasthānāni yāni ca | marīciratriḥ pulahaḥ pulastyaḥ kraturaṅgirāḥ || 63 ||
bhṛguḥ sanatkumāraśca sanako'tha sanandanaḥ | sanātanaśca dakṣaśca jaigīṣavyo bhagandaraḥ || 64 ||
ekataśca dvitaścaiva trito jābālikaśyapau | durvāsā durvinītaśca kaṇvaḥ kātyāyanastathā || 65 ||
mārkaṇḍeyo dīrghatapāḥ śunaḥśepho vidūrathaḥ | ūrdhvaḥ saṃvartakaścaiva cyavano'triḥ parāśaraḥ || 66 ||
dvaipāyano yavakrīto devarājaḥ sahānujaḥ | parvatāstaravo vallyaḥ puṇyānyāyatanāni ca || 67 ||
prajāpatirditiścaiva gāvo viśvasya mātaraḥ | vāhanāni ca divyāni sarvalokāścarācarāḥ || 68 ||
agnayaḥ pitarastārā jīmūtāḥ khaṃ diśo jalam | ete cānye ca bahavaḥ puṇyasaṅkīrtanāḥ śubhaiḥ || 69 ||
[ śubhāḥ ] toyaistvāmabhiṣiñcantu sarvotpātanibarhaṇaiḥ | yathābhiṣikto maghavānetairmuditamanasaiḥ || 70 ||
[ kalyāṇam te prakurvantu āyurārogyameva ca ] ityetaiścānyaiścāpyatharvakalpāhitaiḥ sarudragaṇaiḥ | kauṣmāṇḍamahārauhiṇakuberahṛdyaiḥ samṛddhyā ca || 71 ||
[ vihitaiḥ ] āpohiṣṭhātisṛbhirhiraṇyavarṇeti catasṛbhirjaptam | kārpāsikavastrayugaṃ bibhṛyātsnāto narādhipatiḥ || 72 ||
puṇyāhaśaṅkhaśabdairācānto'bhyarcya devaguruviprān | chatradhvajāyudhāni ca tataḥ svapūjāṃ prayuñjīta || 73 ||
āyuṣyaṃ varcasyaṃ rāyaspoṣābhirṛgbhiretābhiḥ | parijaptaṃ vaijayikaṃ navaṃ vidadhyādalaṅkāram || 74 ||
gatvā dvitīyavedīṃ samupaviśeccarmaṇāṃ upari rājā | deyāni caiva carmāṇyuparyuparyevametāni || 75 ||
vṛṣasya vṛṣadaṃśasya rurośca pṛṣatasya ca | teṣāmupari siṃhasya vyāghrasya ca tataḥ param || 76 ||
mukhyasthāne juhuyātpurohito'gniṃ samittilaghṛtādyaiḥ | trinayanaśakrabṛhaspatinārāyaṇanityagatyṛgbhiḥ || 77 ||
indradhvajanirdiṣṭānyagninimittāni daivavidbrūyāt | kṛtvāśeṣasamāptiṃ purohitaḥ prāñjalirbrūyāt || 78 ||
yāntu devagaṇāḥ sarve pūjāmādāya pārthivāt | siddhiṃ dattvā tu vipulāṃ punarāgamanāya ca || 79 ||
[ suvipulām | vai ] nṛpatirato daivajñaṃ purohitaṃ cārcayeddhanairbahubhiḥ | anyāṃśca dakṣiṇīyānyathocitaṃ śrotriyaprabhṛtīn || 80 ||
[ yathārhataḥ ] dattvābhayaṃ prajānāmāghātasthānagānvisṛjya paśūn | bandhanamokṣaṃ kuryādabhyantaradoṣakṛdvarjam || 81 ||
etatprayujyamānaṃ pratipuṣyaṃ sukhayaśo'rthavṛddhikaram | puṣyādvinārdhaphaladā pauṣī śāntiḥ parā proktā || 82 ||
[ puṣyam | purā ] rāṣṭrotpātopasargeṣu rāhoḥ ketośca darśane | grahāvamardane caiva puṣyasnānaṃ samācaret || 83 ||
nāsti loke sa utpāto yo hyanena na śāmyati | maṅgalaṃ cāparaṃ nāsti yadasmādatiricyate || 84 ||
adhirājyārthino rājñaḥ putrajanma ca kāṅkṣataḥ | tatpūrvamabhiṣeke ca vidhireṣa praśasyate || 85 ||
mahendrārthamuvācedam bṛhatkīrtirbṛhaspatiḥ | snānamāyuṣprajāvṛddhisaubhāgyakaraṇaṃ param || 86 ||
anenaiva vidhānena hastyaśvaṃ snāpayettataḥ | tasyāmayavinirmuktaṃ parāṃ siddhimavāpnuyāt || 87 ||
[ snāpayīta yaḥ ]

Chapter 48: paṭṭalakṣaṇādhyāyaḥ [paṭṭalakṣaṇa-adhyāya]

vistaraśo nirdiṣṭaṃ paṭṭāṇāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ yadācāryaiḥ | tatsaṃkṣepaḥ kriyate mayātra sakalārthasampannaḥ || 1 ||
paṭṭaḥ śubhado rājṇāṃ madhye'ṣṭāvaṅgulāni vistīrṇaḥ | sapta narendramahiṣyāḥ ṣaḍ yuvarājasya nirdiṣṭaḥ || 2 ||
caturaṅgulavistāraḥ paṭṭaḥ senāpaterbhavati madhye | dve ca prasādapaṭṭaḥ pañcaite kīrtitāḥ paṭṭāḥ || 3 ||
sarve dviguṇāyāmā madhyādardhena pārśvavistīrṇāḥ | sarve ca śuddhakāñcanavinirmitāḥ śreyaso vṛddhyai || 4 ||
pañcaśikho bhūmipatestriśikho yuvarājapārthivamahiṣyoḥ | ekaśikhaḥ sainyapateḥ prasādapaṭṭo vinā śikhayā || 5 ||
kriyamāṇaṃ yadi patraṃ sukhena vistārameti paṭṭasya | vṛddhijayau bhūmipatestathā prajānāṃ ca sukhasampat || 6 ||
jīvitarājyavināśaṃ karoti madhye vraṇaḥ samutpannaḥ | madhye sphuṭitastyājyo vighnakaraḥ pārśvayoḥ sphuṭitaḥ || 7 ||
aśubhanimittotpattau śāstrajñaḥ śāntimādiśed rājñaḥ | śastanimittaḥ paṭṭo nṛparāṣṭravivṛddhaye bhavati || 8 ||

Chapter 49: khaḍgalakṣaṇādhyāyaḥ [khaḍgalakṣaṇa-adhyāya]

aṅgulaśatārdhamuttama ūnaḥ syātpañcaviṃśatiḥ khaḍgaḥ | aṅgulamānājjñeyo vraṇo'śubho viṣamaparvasthaḥ || 1 ||
[ pañcaviṃśatiṃ ] śrīvṛkṣavardhamānātapatraśivaliṅgakuṇḍalābjānām | sadṛśā vraṇāḥ praśastā dhvajāyudhasvastikānāṃ ca || 2 ||
kṛkalāsakākakaṅkakravyādakabandhavṛścikākṛtayaḥ | khaḍge vraṇā na śubhadā vaṃśānugatāḥ prabhūtāśca || 3 ||
sphuṭito hrasvaḥ kuṇṭho vaṃśacchinno na dṛgmano'nugataḥ | asvana iti cāniṣṭaḥ proktaviparyasta iṣṭaphalaḥ || 4 ||
kvaṇitaṃ maraṇāyoktaṃ parājayāya pravartanaṃ kośāt | svayamudgīrṇe yuddhaṃ jvalite vijayo bhavati khaḍge || 5 ||
nākāraṇaṃ vivṛṇuyānna vighaṭṭayecca paśyenna tatra vadanaṃ na vadecca mūlyam | deśaṃ na cāsya kathayetpratimānayenna naiva spṛśennṛpatiraprayato'siyaṣṭim || 6 ||
gojihvāsaṃsthāno nīlotpalavaṃśapatrasadṛśaśca | karavīrapatraśūlāgramaṇḍalāgrāḥ praśastāḥ syuḥ || 7 ||
niṣpanno na chedyo nikaṣaiḥ kāryaḥ pramāṇayuktaḥ saḥ | mūle mriyate svāmī jananī tasyāgrataśchinne || 8 ||
yasmintsarupradeśe vraṇo bhavettadvadeva khaḍgasya | vanitānāmiva tilako guhye vācyo mukhe dṛṣṭvā || 9 ||
atha vā spṛśati yadaṅgaṃ praṣṭā nistriṃśabhṛttadavadhārya | kośasthasyādeśyo vraṇo'sti śāstraṃ viditvedam || 10 ||
śirasi spṛṣṭe prathame'ṅgule dvitīye lalāṭasaṃsparśe | bhrūmadhye ca tṛtīye netre spṛṣṭe catruthe ca || 11 ||
nāsauṣṭhakapolahanuśravaṇagrīvāṃsake ca pañcādyāḥ | urasi dvādaśasaṃsthastrayodaśe kakṣayorjñeyaḥ || 12 ||
[ nāsoṣṭha | aṃsakeṣu ] stanahṛdayodarakukṣinābhau tu caturdaśādayo jñeyāḥ | nābhimūle kaṭyāṃ guhye caikonaviṃśatitaḥ || 13 ||
[ kukṣinābhīṣu ] ūrvordvāviṃśe syādūrvormadhye vraṇastrayoviṃśe | jānuni ca caturviṃśe jaṅghāyāṃ pañcaviṃśe ca || 14 ||
jaṅghāmadhye gulphe pārṣṇyāṃ pāde tadaṅgulīṣvapi ca | ṣaḍviṃśatikād yāvattriṃśaditi matena gargasya || 15 ||
putramaraṇaṃ dhanāptirdhanahāniḥ sampadaśca bandhaśca | ekādyaṅgulasaṃsthairvraṇaiḥ phalaṃ nirdiśetkramaśaḥ || 16 ||
sutalābhaḥ kalaho hastilabdhayaḥ putramaraṇadhanalābhau | kramaśo vināśavanitāpticittaduḥkhāni ṣaṭprabhṛti || 17 ||
labdhirhāniḥ strīlabdhayo badho vṛddhimaraṇaparitoṣāḥ | jñeyāścaturdaśādiṣu dhanahāniścaikaviṃśe syāt || 18 ||
[ hānistrīlabdhayo ] vittāptiranirvāṇaṃ dhanāgamo mṛtyusampado'svatvam | aiśvaryamṛtyurājyāni ca kramāttriṃśaditi yāvat || 19 ||
parato na viśeṣaphalaṃ viṣamasamasthāstu pāpaśubhaphaladāḥ | kaiścidaphalāḥ pradiṣṭāstriṃśatparato'gramiti yāvat || 20 ||
karavīrotpalagajamadaghṛtakuṅkumakundacampakasagandhaḥ | śubhado'niṣṭo gomūtrapaṅkamedaḥ sadṛśagandhaḥ || 21 ||
kūrmavasāsṛkkṣāropamaśca bhayaduḥkhado bhavati gandhaḥ | vaidūryakanakavidyutprabho jayārogyavṛddhikaraḥ || 22 ||
idamauśanasaṃ ca śastrapānaṃ rudhireṇa śriyamicchataḥ pradīptām | haviṣā guṇavatsutābhilipsoḥ salilenākṣayamicchataśca vittam || 23 ||
vaḍavoṣṭrakareṇudugdhapānaṃ yadi pāpena samīhate'rthasiddhim | jhaṣapittamṛgāśvabastadugdhaiḥ karihastacchidaye satālagarbhaiḥ || 24 ||
ārkaṃ payo huḍuviṣāṇamaṣīsametaṃ pārāvatākhuśakṛtā ca yutaḥ pralepaḥ | śastrasya tailamathitasya tato'sya pānaṃ paścācchitasya na śilāsu bhavedvighātaḥ || 25 ||
[ yutaṃ ] kṣāre kadalyā mathitena yukte dinoṣite pāyitamāyasaṃ yat | samyak śitaṃ cāśmani naiti bhaṅgaṃ na cānyaloheṣvapi tasya kauṇṭhyam || 26 ||

Chapter 50: aṅgavidyādhyāyaḥ [aṅgavidya-adhyāya]

daivajñena śubhāśubhaṃ diguditasthānāhṛtānīkṣatā vācyaṃ praṣṭṛnijāparāṅgaghaṭanāṃ cālokya kālaṃ dhiyā | sarvajño hi carācarātmakatayāsau sarvadarśo vibhuśceṣṭāvyāhṛtibhiḥ śubhāśubhaphalaṃ sandarśayatyarthinām || 1 ||
sthānaṃ puṣpasuhāsibhūriphalabhṛtsusnigdhakṛtticchadāsatpakṣicyutaśastasaṃjñitatarucchāyopagūḍhaṃ samam | devarṣidvijasādhusiddhanilayaṃ satpuṣpasasyokṣitaṃ satsvādūdakanirmalatvajanitāhlādaṃ ca sacchādvalam || 2 ||
[ sacchāḍvalam ] chinnabhinnakṛmikhātakaṇṭakipluṣṭarūkṣakuṭilairna satkujaiḥ | krūrapakṣiyutanindyanāmabhiḥ śuṣkaśīrṇabahuparṇacarmabhiḥ || 3 ||
[ varmabhiḥ ] śmaśānaśūnyāyatanaṃ catuṣpathaṃ tathāmanojñaṃ viṣamaṃ sadoṣaram | avaskarāṅgārakapālabhasmabhiścitaṃ tuṣaiḥ śuṣkatṛṇairnaśobhanam || 4 ||
pravrajitanagnanāpitaripubandhanasaunikaistathā śvapacaiḥ | kitavayatipīḍitairyutamāyudhamādhvīkavikrayairna śubham || 5 ||
[ sūnikais ] prāguttareśāśca diśaḥ praśastāḥ praṣṭurna vāyvambuyamāgnirakṣaḥ | pūrvāhnakāle'sti śubhaṃ na rātrau sandhyādvaye praśnakṛto'parāhṇe || 6 ||
yātrāvidhāne hi śubhāśubhaṃ yatproktaṃ nimittaṃ tadihāpi vācyam | dṛṣṭvā puro vā janatāhṛtaṃ vā praṣṭuḥ sthitaṃ pāṇitale'tha vastre || 7 ||
athāṅgānyūrvoṣṭhastanavṛṣaṇapādaṃ ca daśanā bhujau hastau gaṇḍau kacagalanakhāṅguṣṭhamapi yat | saśaṅkhaṃ kakṣāṃsaṃ śravaṇagudasandhīti puruṣe striyāṃ bhrūnāsāsphigvalikaṭisulekhāṅgulicayam || 8 ||
[ kaṣāṃsaśravaṇa ] jihvā grīvā piṇḍike pārṣṇiyugmaṃ jaṅghe nābhiḥ karṇapālī kṛkāṭī | vaktraṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ jatrujānvasthipārśvaṃ hṛttālvakṣī mehanorastrikaṃ ca || 9 ||
napuṃsakākhyaṃ ca śiro lalāṭamāśvādyasaṃjñairaparaiścireṇa | siddhirbhavejjātu napuṃsakairno rūkṣakṣatairbhagnakṛśaiśca pūrvaiḥ || 10 ||
spṛṣṭe vā cālite vāpi pādāṅguṣṭhe'kṣirugbhavet | aṅgulyāṃ duhituḥ śokaṃ śiroghāte nṛpādbhayam || 11 ||
viprayogamurasi svagātrataḥ karpaṭāhṛtiranarthadā bhavet | syātpriyāptirabhigṛhya karpaṭaṃ pṛcchataścaraṇapādayojituḥ || 12 ||
pādāṅguṣṭhena vilikhedbhūmiṃ kṣetrotthacintayā | hastena pādau kaṇḍūyettasya dāsīmayī ca sā || 13 ||
[ dāsīmayā ] tālabhūrjapaṭadarśane'ṃśukaṃ cintayetkacatuṣāsthibhasmagam | vyādhirāśrayati rajjujālakaṃ valkalaṃ ca samavekṣya bandhanam || 14 ||
pippalīmaricaśuṇṭhivāridai rodhrakuṣṭhavasanāmbujīrakaiḥ | gandhamāṃsiśatapuṣpayā vadetpṛcchatastagarakeṇa cintayet || 15 ||
[ cintanam ] strīpuruṣadoṣapīḍitasarvārthasutārthadhānyatanayānām | dvicatuṣpadakṣitīnāṃ vināśataḥ kīrtitairdṛṣṭaiḥ || 16 ||
[ adhva ] nyagrodhamadhukatindukajambūplakṣāmrabadarajātiphalaiḥ | dhanakanakapuruṣalohāṃśukarūpyaudumbarāptirapi karagaiḥ || 17 ||
[ badari | udumbarāptir ] dhānyaparipūrṇapātraṃ kumbhaḥ pūrṇaḥ kuṭumbavṛddhikarau | gajagośunāṃ purīṣaṃ dhanayuvatisuhṛdvināśakaram || 18 ||
paśuhastimahiṣapaṅkajarajatavyāghrairlabheta sandṛṣṭaiḥ | avidhananivasanamalayajakauśeyābharaṇasaṅghātam || 19 ||
pṛcchā vṛddhaśrāvakasuparivrāḍdarśane nṛbhirvihitā | mitradyūtārthabhavā gaṇikānṛpasūtikārthakṛtā || 20 ||
śākyopādhyāyārhatnirgranthinimittanigamakaivartaiḥ | cauracamūpativaṇijāṃ dāsīyodhāpaṇasthavadhyānām || 21 ||
[ ārhata | nirgrantha ] tāpase śauṇḍike dṛṣṭe proṣitaṃ paśupālanam | hṛdgataṃ pracchakasya syāduñchavṛṭau vipannatā || 22 ||
[ pṛcchakasya ] icchāmi praṣṭuṃ bhaṇa paśyatvāryaḥ samādiśetyukte | saṃyogakuṭumbotthā lābhaiśvaryodgatā cintā || 23 ||
nirdiśeti gadite jayādhvajā pratyavekṣya mama cintitaṃ vada | āśu sarvajanamadhyagaṃ tvayā dṛśyatāmiti ca bandhucaurajā || 24 ||
[ jayādhvagā ] antaḥsthe'ṅge svajana udito bāhyaje bāhya eva pādāṅguṣṭhāṅgulikalanayā dāsadāsījanaḥ syāt | jaṅghe preṣyo bhavati bhaginī nābhito hṛtsvabhāryā pāṇyaṅguṣṭhāṅgulicayakṛtasparśane putrakanye || 25 ||
[ evam ] mātaraṃ jaṭhare mūrdhni guruṃ dakṣiṇavāmakau | bāhū bhrātātha tatpatnī spṛṣṭvaivaṃ cauramādiśet || 26 ||
antaraṅgamavamucya bāhyagasparśanaṃ yadi karoti pṛcchakaḥ | śleṣmamūtraśakṛtastyajantyatho pātayetkaratalasthavastu cet || 27 ||
[ tyajannadhaḥ ] bhṛśamavanāmitāṅgaparimoṭanato'pyatha vā | janadhṛtariktabhāṇḍamavalokya ca caurajanam | hṛtapatitakṣatāsmṛtavinaṣṭabhagnagatonmuṣitamṛtādyaniṣṭaravato labhate na hṛtam || 28 ||
nigaditamidaṃ yattatsarvaṃ tuṣāsthiviṣādikaiḥ saha mṛtikaraṃ pīḍārtānāṃ samaṃ ruditakṣataiḥ | avayavamapi spṛṣṭvāntaḥsthaṃ dṛḍhaṃ marudāhared | atibahu tadā bhuktvānnaṃ saṃsthitaḥ suhito vadet || 29 ||
[ kṣutaiḥ ] lalāṭasparśanācchūkadarśanācchālijaudanam | uraḥsparśāt ṣaṣṭikākhyaṃ grīvāsparśe ca yāvakam || 30 ||
[ annam ] kukṣikucajaṭharajānusparśe māṣāḥ payastilayavāgvaḥ | āsvādayate cauṣṭhau lihate madhuraṃ rasaṃ jñeyam || 31 ||
[ āsvādayataś ] visṛkke sphoṭayejjihvāmāmle vaktraṃ vikūṇayet | kaṭuke'tha kaṣāye'tha hikket ṣṭhīvecca saindhave || 32 ||
[ vispṛkke | kaṭutiktakaṣāyoṣṇair ] śleṣmatyāge śuṣkatiktaṃ tadalpaṃ | śrutvā kravyādaṃ vā prekṣya vā māṃsamiśram | bhrūgaṇḍauṣṭhasparśane śākunaṃ tadbhuktaṃ tenetyuktametannimittam || 33 ||
mūrdhagalakeśahanuśaṅkhakarṇajaṅghaṃ vastiṃ ca spṛṣṭvā gajamahiṣameṣaśūkaragośaśamṛgamahiṣamāṃsayugbhuktam || 34 ||
dṛṣṭe śrute'pyaśakune godhāmatsyāmiṣaṃ vadedbhuktam | garbhiṇyā garbhasya ca nipatanamevaṃ prakalpayetpraśne || 35 ||
puṃstrīnapuṃsakākhye dṛṣṭe'numite puraḥsthite spṛṣṭe | tajjanma bhavati pānānnapuṣpaphaladarśane ca śubham || 36 ||
aṅguṣṭhena bhrūdaraṃ vāṅguliṃ vā spṛṣṭvā pṛcchedgarbhacintā tadā syāt | madhvājyādyairhemaratnapravālairagrasthairvā mātṛdhātryātmajaiśca || 37 ||
garbhayutā jaṭhare karage syād | duṣṭanimittavaśāttadudāsaḥ | karṣati tajjaṭharaṃ yadi pīṭhotpīḍanataṇ karage ca kare'pi || 38 ||
ghrāṇāyā dakṣiṇe dvāre spṛṣṭe māsottaraṃ vadet vāme'bdau karṇa evaṃ mā dvicaturghnaḥ śrutistane || 39 ||
[ dvau ] veṇīmūle trīn sutān kanyake dve karṇe putrānpañca haste trayaṃ ca | aṅguṣṭhānte pañcakaṃ cānupūrvyā pādāṅguṣṭhe pārṣṇiyugme'pi kanyām || 40 ||
savyāsavyorusamsparśe sūte kanyāsutadvayam | spṛṣṭe lalāṭamadhyānte catustritanayā bhavet || 41 ||
śirolalāṭabhrūkarṇagaṇḍaṃ hanuradā galam | savyāpasavyaskandhaśca hastau cibukanālakam || 42 ||
uraḥ kucaṃ dakṣiṇamapyasavyaṃ hṛtpārśvamevaṃ jaṭharaṃ kaṭiśca | sphikpāyusandhyūruyugaṃ ca jānū jaṅghe'tha pādāviti kṛttikādau || 43 ||
iti nigaditametadgātrasaṃsparśalakṣma prakaṭamabhimatāptyai vīkṣya śāstrāṇi samyak | vipulamatirudāro vetti yaḥ sarvametannarapatijanatābhiḥ pūjyate'sau sadaiva || 44 ||

Chapter 51: piṭakalakṣaṇādhyāyaḥ [piṭakalakṣaṇa-adhyāya]

sitaraktapītakṛṣṇā viprādīnāṃ krameṇa piṭakā ye | te kramaśaḥ proktaphalā varṇānāṃ nāgrajātānām || 1 ||
[ agrajādīnām ] susnigdhavyaktaśobhāḥ śirasi dhanacayaṃ mūrdhni saubhāgyamārāddaurbhāgyaṃ bhrūyugotthāḥ priyajanaghaṭanāmāśu duḥśīlatāṃ ca | tanmadhyotthāśca śokaṃ nayanapuṭagatā netrayoriṣṭadṛṣṭiṃ pravrajyāṃ śaṅkhadeśe'śrujalanipatanasthānagā rānti cintām || 2 ||
[ sthānagāśca aticintām ] ghrāṇāgaṇḍe vasanasutadāścauṣṭhayorannalābhaṃ kuryustadvaccibukatalagā bhūri vittaṃ lalāṭe | hanvorevaṃ galakṛtapadā bhūṣaṇānyannapāne śrotre ṣaḍbhūtaṇa gaṇamapi jñānamātmasvarūpam || 3 ||
[ tadbhūṣaṇa ] śiraḥ sandhigrīvāhṛdayakucapārśvorasi gatā ayoghātaṃ ghātaṃ sutatanayalābhaṃ śucamapi | priyaprāptiṃ skandhe'pyaṭanamatha bhikṣārthamasakṛdvināśaṃ kakṣotthā vidadhati dhanānāṃ bahumukham || 4 ||
[ bahusukham ] duḥkhaśatrunicayasya vināśaṃ pṛṣṭhabāhuyugajā racayanti | saṃyamaṃ ca maṇibandhanajātā bhūṣaṇādyamupabāhuyugutthāḥ || 5 ||
[ vighātaṃ ] dhanāptiṃ saubhāgyaṃ śucamapi karāṅgulyudaragāḥ supānānnaṃ nābhau tadadha iha caurairdhanahṛtim | dhanaṃ dhānyaṃ bastau yuvatimatha meḍhre sutanayāndhanaṃ saubhāgyaṃ vā gudavṛṣaṇajātā vidadhati || 6 ||
ūrvoryānāṅganālābhaṃ jānvoḥ śatrujanātkṣatim | śastreṇa jaṅghayorgulphe'dhvabandhakleśadāyinaḥ || 7 ||
sphikpārṣṇipādajātā dhananāśāgamyagamanamadhvānam | bandhanamaṅgulinicaye'ṅguṣṭhe ca jñātilokataḥ pūjām || 8 ||
utpātagaṇḍapiṭakā dakṣiṇato vāmatastvabhīghātāḥ | dhanyā bhavanti puṃsāṃ tadviparītāśca nārīṇām || 9 ||
[ tu ] iti piṭakavibhāgaḥ prokta āmūrdhato'yaṃ vraṇatilakavibhāgo'pyevameva prakalpyaḥ | bhavati maśakalakṣmāvartajanmāpi tadvannigaditaphalakāri prāṇināṃ dehasaṃstham || 10 ||

Chapter 52: vāstuvidyā [vāstu-vidyā]

vāstujñānamathātaḥ kamalabhavānmuniparam parāyātam | kriyate'dhunā mayedam vidagdhasāṃvatsaraprītyai || 1 ||
kimapi kila bhūtamabhavad rundhānaṃ rodasī śarīreṇa | tadamaragaṇena sahasā vinigṛhyādhomukhaṃ nyastam || 2 ||
yatra ca yena gṛhītaṃ vibudhenādhiṣṭhitaḥ sa tatraiva | tadamaramayaṃ vidhātā vāstunaraṃ kalpayāmāsa || 3 ||
uttamamaṣṭābhyadhikaṃ hastaśataṃ nṛpagṛhaṃ pṛthutvena | aṣṭāṣṭonānyevaṃ pañca sapādāni dairghyeṇa || 4 ||
ṣaḍbhiḥ ṣaḍbhirhīnā senāpatisadmanāṃ catuḥṣaṣṭiḥ | evaṃ pañca gṛhāṇi ṣaḍbhāgasamanvitā dairghyam || 5 ||
[ pañca evaṃ vistārāt ] ṣaṣṭiścaturbhirhīnā veśmāni pañca sacivasya | svāṣṭāṃśayuto dairghyaṃ tadardhato rājamahiṣīṇām || 6 ||
[ caturvihīnā ] ṣaḍbhiḥ ṣaḍbhiścaivaṃ yuvarājasyāpavarjitāśītiḥ | tryaṃśānvitā ca dairghyaṃ pañca tadardhaistadanujanānām || 7 ||
nṛpasacivāntaratulyaṃ sāmantapravararājapuruṣāṇām | nṛpayuvarājaviśeṣaḥ kañcukiveśyākalājñānām || 8 ||
adhyakṣādhikṛtānāṃ sarveṣāṃ kośaratitulyam | yuvarājamantrivivaraṃ karmāntādhyakṣadūtānām || 9 ||
[ sarveṣāmeva ] catvāriṃśaddhīnā catuścaturbhistu pañca yāvaditi | ṣaḍbhāgayutā dairghyaṃ daivajñapurodhasorbhiṣajaḥ || 10 ||
vāstuni yo vistāraḥ sa eva cocchrāyaniścayaḥ śubhadaḥ | śālaikeṣu gṛheṣvapi vistārāddviguṇitaṃ dairghyam || 11 ||
cāturvarṇyavyāso dvātriṃśatsā catuścaturhīnā | āṣoḍaśāditi paraṃ nyūnataramatīva hīnānām || 12 ||
[ syāt ] sadaśāṃśaṃ viprāṇāṃ kṣatrasyāṣṭāṃśasaṃyutaṃ dairghyam | ṣaḍbhāgayutaṃ vaiśyasya bhavati śūdrasya pādayutam || 13 ||
nṛpasenāpatigṛhayorantaramānena kośaratibhavane | senāpaticāturvarṇyavivarato rājapuruṣāṇām || 14 ||
atha pāraśavādīnāṃ svamānasaṃyogadalasamaṃ bhavanam | hīnādhikaṃ svamānādaśubhakaraṃ vāstu sarveṣām || 15 ||
[ pārasava ] paśvāśramiṇāmamitaṃ dhānyāyudhavahniratigṛhāṇāṃ ca | necchanti śāstrakārā hastaśatāducchritaṃ parataḥ || 16 ||
senāpatinṛpatīnāṃ saptatisahite dvidhākṛte vyāse | śālā caturdaśahṛte pañcatriṃśaddhṛte'lindaḥ || 17 ||
hastadvātriṃśādiṣu catuścatustritrikatrikāḥ śālāḥ | saptadaśatritayatithitrayodaśakṛtāṅgulābhyadhikāḥ || 18 ||
tritridvidvidvisamāḥ kṣayakramādaṅgulāni caiteṣām | vyekā viṃśatiraṣṭau viṃśatiraṣṭādaśa tritayam || 19 ||
śālātribhāgatulyā kartavyā vīthikā bahirbhavanāt | yadyagrato bhavati sā soṣṇīṣaṃ nāma tadvāstu || 20 ||
sāyāśrayamiti paścātsāvaṣṭambhaṃ tu pārśvasaṃsthitayā | susthitamiti ca samantācchāstrajñaiḥ pūjitāḥ sarvāḥ || 21 ||
vistāraṣoḍaśāṃśaḥ sacaturhasto bhavedgṛhocchrāyaḥ | dvādaśabhāgenono bhūmau bhūmau samastānām || 22 ||
vyāsāt ṣoḍaśabhāgaḥ sarveṣāṃ sadmanāṃ bhavati bhittiḥ | pakveṣṭakākṛtānāṃ dārukṛtānāṃ tu na vikalpaḥ || 23 ||
[ savikalpaḥ | na vikalpaḥ ] ekādaśabhāgayutaḥ sasaptatirnṛpabaleśayorvyāsaḥ | ucchrāyo'ṅgulatulyo dvārasyārdhena viṣkambhaḥ || 24 ||
viprādīnāṃ vyāsātpañcāṃśo'ṣṭādaśāṅgulasametaḥ | sāṣṭāṃśo viṣkambho dvārasya triguṇa ucchrāyaḥ || 25 ||
ucchrāyahastasaṃkhyāparimāṇānyaṅgulāni bāhulyam | śākhādvaye'pi kāryaṃ sārdhaṃ tatsyādudumbarayoḥ || 26 ||
ucchrāyātsaptaguṇādaśītibhāgaḥ pṛthutvameteṣām | navaguṇite'śītyaṃśaḥ stambhasya daśāṃśahīno'gre || 27 ||
samacaturasro rucako vajro'ṣṭāsrirdvivajrako dviguṇaḥ | dvātriṃśatā tu madhye pralīnako vṛtta iti vṛttaḥ || 28 ||
[ samacaturaśro | aṣṭāśris ] stambhaṃ vibhajya navadhā vahanaṃ bhāgo ghaṭo'sya bhāgo'nyaḥ | padmaṃ tathottaroṣṭhaṃ kuryādbhāgena bhāgena || 29 ||
stambhasamaṃ bāhulyaṃ bhāratulānāmuparyuparyāsām | bhavati tulopatulānāmūnaṃ pādena pādena || 30 ||
apratiṣiddhālindaṃ samantato vāstu sarvatobhadram | nṛpavibudhasamūhānāṃ kāryaṃ dvāraiścaturbhirapi || 31 ||
nandyāvartamalindaiḥ śālākuḍyātpradakṣiṇāntagataiḥ | dvāraṃ paścimamasminvihāya śeṣāṇi kāryāṇi || 32 ||
dvārālindo'ntagataḥ pradakṣiṇo'nyaḥ śubhastataścānyaḥ | tasmiṃśca vardhamāne dvāraṃ tu na dakṣiṇaṃ kāryam || 33 ||
[ tadvad ] aparo'ntagato'lindaḥ prāgantagatau tadutthitau cānyau | tadavadhividhṛtaścānyaḥ prāgdvāraṃ svastike śubhadam || 34 ||
[ vivṛtaś | vidhṛta | aśubhadam | śubham ] prākpaścimāvalindāvantagatau tadavadhisthitau śeṣau | rucake dvāraṃ na śubhadamuttarato'nyāni śastāni || 35 ||
śreṣṭhaṃ nandyāvartaṃ sarveṣāṃ vardhamānasaṃjñaṃ ca | svastikarucake madhye śeṣaṃ śubhadaṃ nṛpādīnām || 36 ||
uttaraśālāhīnaṃ hiraṇyanābhaṃ triśālakaṃ dhanyam | prākśālayā viyuktaṃ sukṣetraṃ vṛddhidaṃ vāstu || 37 ||
yāmyāhīnaṃ cullī triśālakaṃ vittanāśakarametat | pakṣaghnamaparayā varjitaṃ sutadhvaṃsavairakaram || 38 ||
siddhārthamaparayāmye yamasūryaṃ paścimottare śāle | daṇḍākhyamudakpūrve vātākhyaṃ prāgyutā yāmyā || 39 ||
pūrvāpare tu śāle gṛhacullī dakṣiṇottare kācam | siddhārthe'rthāvāptiryamasūrye gṛhapatermṛtyuḥ || 40 ||
daṇḍavadho daṇḍākhye kalahodvegaḥ sadaiva vātabākhye | vittavināśaścullyāṃ jñātivirodhaḥ smṛtaḥ kāce || 41 ||
ekāśītivibhāge daśa daśa pūrvottarāyatā rekhāḥ | antastrayodaśa surā dvātriṃśadbāhyakoṣṭhasthāḥ || 42 ||
śikhiparjanyajayantendrasūryasatyā bhṛśo'ntarikṣaśca | aiśānyādikramaśo dakṣiṇapūrve'nilaḥ koṇe || 43 ||
[ aiśānyādyāḥ ] pūṣā vitathabṛhatkṣatayamagandharvākhyabhṛṅgarājamṛgāḥ | pitṛdauvārikasugrīvakusumadantāmbupatyasurāḥ || 44 ||
śoṣo'tha pāpayakṣmā rogaḥ koṇe tato'himukhyau ca | bhallāṭasomabhujagāstato'ditirditiriti kramaśaḥ || 45 ||
madhye brahmā navakoṣṭhakādhipo'syāryamā sthitaḥ prācyām | ekāntarātpradakṣiṇamasmātsavitā vivasvāṃśca || 46 ||
vibudhādhipatistasmānmitro'nyo rājayakṣmanāmā ca | pṛthivī dharāpavatsāvityete brahmaṇaḥ paridhau || 47 ||
[ pṛthvī ] āpo nāmaiśāne koṇe hautāśane ca sāvitraḥ | jaya iti ca nairṛte rudra ānile'bhyantarapadeṣu || 48 ||
āpastathāpavatsaḥ parjanyo'gnirditiśca vargo'yam | evaṃ koṇe koṇe padikāḥ syuḥ pañca pañca surāḥ || 49 ||
bāhyā dvipadāḥ śeṣāste vibudhā viṃśati samākhyātāḥ | śeṣāścatvāro'nye tripadā dikṣvaryamādyāste || 50 ||
pūrvottaradigmūrdhā puruṣo'yamavāṅmukho'sya śirasi śikhī | āpo mukhe stane'syāryamā hyurasyāpavatsaśca || 51 ||
parjanyādyā bāhyā dṛkśravaṇoraḥsthalāṃsagā devāḥ | satyādyāḥ pañca bhuje haste savitā ca sāvitraḥ || 52 ||
[ sasāvitraḥ ] vitatho bṛhatkṣatayutaḥ pārśve jaṭhare sthito vivasvāṃśca | ūrū jānu ca jaṅghe sphigiti yamādyaiḥ parigṛhītāḥ || 53 ||
ete dakṣiṇapārśve sthāneṣvevaṃ ca vāmapārśvasthāḥ | meḍhre śakrajayantau hṛdaye brahmā pitāṅghrigataḥ || 54 ||
[ aṅgrigataḥ ] aṣṭāṣṭakapadamatha vā kṛtvā rekhāśca koṇagāstiryak | brahmā catuṣpado'sminnardhapadā brahmakoṇasthāḥ || 55 ||
aṣṭau ca bahiṣkoṇeṣvardhapadāstadubhayasthitāḥ sārdhāḥ | uktebhyo ye śeṣāste dvipadā viṃśatiste hi || 56 ||
[ ca ] sampātā vaṃśānāṃ madhyāni samāni yāni ca padānām | marmāṇi tāni vindyānna tāni paripīḍayetprājñaḥ || 57 ||
[ vindyānnaparipīḍayet ] tānyaśucibhāṇḍakīlastambhādyaiḥ pīḍitāni śalyaiśca | gṛhabhartustattulye pīḍāmaṅge prayacchanti || 58 ||
kaṇḍūyate yadaṅgaṃ gṛhabharturyatra vāmarāhutyām | aśubhaṃ bhavennimittaṃ vikṛtervā agneḥ saśalyaṃ tat || 59 ||
[ gṛhapatinā ] marmaṇyamarmago vā ruṇaddhyarthāgamaṃ tuṣasamūhaḥ] | api nāgadantako marmasaṃsthito doṣakṛdbhavati || 60 ||
rogādvāyuṃ pitṛto hutāśanaṃ śoṣasūtramapi vitathāt | mukhyādbhṛśaṃ jayantācca bhṛṅgamaditeśca sugrīvam || 61 ||
tatsampātā nava ye tānyatimarmāṇi sampradiṣṭāni | yaśca padasyāṣṭāṃśastatproktaṃ marmaparimāṇam || 62 ||
padahastasaṃkhyayā sammitāni vaṃśo'ṅgulāni vistīrṇaḥ | vaṃśavyāso'dhyardhaḥ śirāpramāṇaṃ vinirdiṣṭam || 63 ||
sukhamicchanbrahmāṇaṃ yatnād rakṣedgṛhī gṛhāntaḥstham | ucchiṣṭādyupaghātādgṛhapatirupatapyate tasmin || 64 ||
[ gṛtāntastham ] dakṣiṇabhujena hīne vāstunare'rthakṣayo'ṅganādādoṣāḥ | vāme'rthadhānyahāniḥ śirasi guṇairhīyate sarvaiḥ || 65 ||
[ aṅganādoṣāḥ ] strīdoṣāḥ sutamaraṇaṃ preṣyatvaṃ cāpi caraṇavaikalye | avikalapuruṣe vasatāṃ mānārthayutāni saukhyāni || 66 ||
gṛhanagaragrāmeṣu ca sarvatraivaṃ pratiṣṭhitā devāḥ | teṣu ca yathānurūpaṃ varṇā viprādayo vāsyāḥ || 67 ||
vāsagṛhāṇi ca vindyādviprādīnāmudagdigādyāni | viśatāṃ ca yathā bhavanaṃ bhavanti tānyeva dakṣiṇataḥ || 68 ||
navaguṇasūtravibhaktānyaṣṭaguṇenātha vā catuḥṣaṣṭeḥ | dvārāṇi yāni teṣāmanalādīnāṃ phalopanayaḥ || 69 ||
anilabhayaṃ strījananaṃ prabhūtadhanatā narendravāllabhyam | krodhaparatānṛtatvaṃ krauryaṃ cauryaṃ ca pūrveṇa || 70 ||
[ analabhayaṃ | strījanma ] alpasutatvaṃ praiṣyaṃ nīcatvaṃ bhakṣyapānasutavṛddhiḥ | raudraṃ kṛtaghnamadhanaṃ sutavīryaghnaṃ ca yāmyena || 71 ||
sutapīḍā ripuvṛddhirna sutadhanāptiḥ sutārthaphalasampat | dhanasampannṛpatibhayaṃ dhanakṣayo roga ityapare || 72 ||
[ dhanastāptiḥ ] vadhabandho ripuvṛddhiḥ sutadhanalābhaḥ samastaguṇasampat | putradhanāptirvairaṃ sutena doṣāḥ striyā naiḥsvam || 73 ||
[ dhanasutalābhaḥ ] mārgatarukoṇakūpastambhabhramaviddhamaśubbhadaṃ dvāram | ucchrāyāddviguṇamitāṃ tyaktvā bhūmiṃ na doṣāya || 74 ||
rathyāviddhaṃ dvāraṃ nāśāya kumāradoṣadaṃ taruṇā | paṅkadvāre śoko vyayo'mbuniḥsrāviṇi proktaḥ || 75 ||
[ ambuni śrāviṇi ] kūpenāpasmāro bhavati vināśaśca devatāviddhe | stambhena strīdoṣāḥ kulanāśo brāhmaṇābhimukhe || 76 ||
[ brāhmaṇo'bhimukhe ] unmādaḥ svayamudghāṭite'tha pihite svayaṃ kulavināśaḥ | mānādhike nṛpabhayaṃ dasyubhayaṃ vyasanameva nīce ca || 77 ||
[ vyasanadaṃ nīcam ] dvāraṃ dvārasyopari yattanna śivāya saṅkaṭaṃ yacca | āvyāttaṃ kṣudbhayadaṃ kubjaṃ kulanāśanaṃ bhavati || 78 ||
pīḍākaramatipīḍitamantarvinataṃ bhavedabhāvāya | bāhyavinate pravāso digbhrānte dasyubhiḥ pīḍā || 79 ||
mūladvāraṃ nānyairdvārairabhisandadhīta rūparddhyā | ghaṭaphalapatrapramathādibhiśca tanmaṅgalaiścinuyāt || 80 ||
aiśānyādiṣu koṇeṣu saṃsthitā bāhyato gṛhasyaitāḥ | carakī vidārināmātha pūtanā rākṣasī ceti || 81 ||
purabhavanagrāmāṇāṃ ye koṇāsteṣu nivasatāṃ doṣāḥ | śvapacādayo'ntyajātyāsteṣveva vivṛddhimāyānti || 82 ||
yāmyādiṣvaśubhaphalā jātāstaravaḥ pradakṣiṇenaite | udagādiṣu praśastāḥ plakṣavaṭodumbarāśvatthā || 83 ||
[ udumbarāśvatthāḥ ] āsannāḥ kaṇṭhakino ripubhayadāḥ kṣīriṇo'rthanāśāya | phalinaḥ prajākṣayakarā dārūṇyapi varjayedeṣām || 84 ||
chindyād yadi na tarūṃś tāntadantare pūjitānvapedanyat | punnāgāśokāriṣṭabakulapanasācchamīśālau || 85 ||
[ anyān ] śastauṣadhidrumalatā madhurā sugandhā snigdhā samā na suṣirā ca mahī narāṇām | apyadhvani śramavinodamupāgatānāṃ dhatte śriyaṃ kimuta śāśvatamandireṣu || 86 ||
sacivālaye'rthanāśo dhūrtagṛhe sutavadhaḥ samīpasthe | udvego devakule catuṣpade bhavati cākīrtiḥ || 87 ||
[ catuṣpathe ] caitye bhayaṃ grahakṛtaṃ valmīkaśvabhrasaṅkule vipadaḥ | gartāyāṃ tu pipāsā kūrmākāre dhanavināśaḥ || 88 ||
udagādiplavamiṣṭaṃ viprādīnāṃ pradakṣiṇenaiva | vipraḥ sarvatra vasedanuvarṇamatheṣṭamanyeṣām || 89 ||
gṛhamadhye hastamitaṃ khātvā paripūritaṃ punaḥ śvabhram | yadyūnamaniṣṭaṃ tatsame samaṃ dhanyamadhikaṃ yat || 90 ||
śvabhramatha vāmbupūrṇaṃ padaśatamitvāgatasya yadi nonam | taddhanyaṃ yacca bhavetpalānyapāmāḍhakaṃ catuḥṣaṣṭiḥ || 91 ||
āme vā mṛtpātre śvabhrasthe dīpavartirabhyadhikam | jvalati diśi yasya śastā sā bhūmistasya varṇasya || 92 ||
śvabhroṣitaṃ na kusumaṃ yasya pramlāyate'nuvarṇasamam | tattasya bhavati śubhadaṃ yasya ca yasminmano ramate || 93 ||
[ yasmin ] sitaraktapītakṛṣṇā viprādīnāṃ praśasyate bhūmiḥ | gandhaśca bhavati yasyāṃ ghṛtarudhirānnādyamadyasamaḥ || 94 ||
[ yasyā ] kuśayuktā śarabahulā dūrvākāśāvṛtā kremeṇa mahī | hyanuvarṇaṃ vṛddhikarī madhurakaṣāyāmlakaṭukā ca || 95 ||
[ anuvarṇam ] kṛṣṭāṃ prarūḍhabījāṃ go'dhyuṣitāṃ brāhmaṇaiḥ praśastāṃ ca | gatvā mahīṃ gṛhapatiḥ kāle sāmvatsaroddiṣṭe || 96 ||
bhakṣyairnānākārairdadhyakṣatasurabhikusumadhūpaiśca | daivatapūjāṃ kṛtvā sthapatīnabhyarcya viprāṃśca || 97 ||
vipraḥ spṛṣṭvā śīrṣaṃ vakṣaśca kṣatriyo viśāścorū | śūdraḥ pādau spṛṣṭvā kuryād rekhāṃ gṛhārambhe || 98 ||
aṅguṣṭhakena kuryānmadhyāṅgulyātha vā pradeśinyā | kanakamaṇirajatamuktādadhikaphalakusumākṣataiśca śubham || 99 ||
śastreṇa śastramṛtyurbandho lohena bhasmanāgnibhayam | taskarabhayaṃ tṛṇena ca kāṣṭhollikhitā ca rājabhayam || 100 ||
vakrā pādālikhitā śatrubhayakleśadā virūpā ca | carmāṅgārāsthikṛtā dantena ca bharturaśivāya || 101 ||
[ kartur ] vairamapasavyalikhitā pradakṣiṇaṃ sampado vinirdeśyāḥ | vācaḥ paruṣā niṣṭhīvitaṃ kṣutaṃ cāśubhaṃ kathitam || 102 ||
ardhanicitaṃ kṛtaṃ vā praviśan sthapatirgṛhe nimittāni | avalokayedgṛhapatiḥ kva saṃsthitaḥ spṛśati kiṃ cāṅgam || 103 ||
ravidīpte yadi śakunistasmin kāle virauti paruṣaravam | saṃspṛṣṭāṅgasamānaṃ tasmindeśe'sthi nirdeśyam || 104 ||
[ paruṣaravaḥ ] śakunasamaye'thvānye hastyaśvaśvādayo'nuvāśante | tatprabhavamasthi tasmiṃstadaṅgasambhūtameveti || 105 ||
sūtre prasāryamāṇe gardabharāvo'sthiśalyamācaṣṭe | śvaśṛgālalaṅghite vā sūtre śalyaṃ vinirdeśyam || 106 ||
diśi śāntāyāṃ śakunirmadhuravirāvī yadā tadā vācyaḥ | arthastasmin sthāne gṛheśvarādhiṣṭhite'ṅge vā || 107 ||
[ śakuno ] sūtracchede mṛtyuḥ kīle cāvāṅmukhe mahagaḥ | gṛhanāthasthapatīnāṃ smṛtilope mṛtyurādeśyaḥ || 108 ||
[ mahān rogaḥ ] skandhāccyute śirorukkulopasargo'pavarjite kumbhe | bhagne'pi ca karmivadhaścyute karādgṛhapatermṛtyuḥ || 109 ||
dakṣiṇapūrve koṇe kṛtvā pūjāṃ śilāṃ nyasetprathamam | śeṣāḥ pradakṣiṇena stambhāścaivaṃ samutthāpya || 110 ||
[ prathamām | samutthāpyāḥ ] chatrasragambarayutaḥ kṛtadhūpavilepanaḥ samutthāpyaḥ | stambhastathaiva kāryo dvārocchrāyaḥ prayatnena || 111 ||
vihagādibhiravalīnairākampitapatitaduḥsthitaiśca tathā | śakradhvajasadṛśaphalaṃ tadeva tasminvinirdiṣṭam || 112 ||
[ phalam | sadṛśaṃ tasmiṃśca śubhaṃ ] prāguttaronnate dhanasutakṣayaḥ sutavadhaśca durgandhe | vakre bandhuvināśo na santi garbhāśca dinmūḍhe || 113 ||
icched yadi gṛhavṛddhiṃ tataḥ samantādvivardhayettulyam | ekoddeśe doṣaḥ prāgatha vāpyuttare kuryāt || 114 ||
prāgbhavati mitravairaṃ mṛtyubhayaṃ dakṣiṇena yadi vṛddhiḥ | arthavināśaḥ paścādudagvivṛddhirmanastāpaḥ || 115 ||
[ udagvivṛddhau ] aiśānyāṃ devagṛhaṃ mahānasaṃ yadi cāpi kāryamāgneyyām | nairṛtyāṃ bhāṇḍopaskaro'rthadhānyāni mārutyām || 116 ||
prācyādisthe salile sutahāniḥ śikhibhayaṃ ripubhayaṃ ca | strīkalahaḥ strīdauṣṭyaṃ naiḥsvyaṃ vittātmajavivṛddhiḥ || 117 ||
khaganilayabhagnasaṃśuṣkadagdhadevālayaśmaśānasthān | kṣīratarudhavavibhītakanimbāraṇivarjitān chindyāt || 118 ||
[ varjitāṃścchindyāt ] rātrau kṛtabalipūjaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ chedayeddivā vṛkṣam | dhanyamudakprākpatataṃ na grāhyo'to'nyathā patitaḥ || 119 ||
chedo yadyavikārī tataḥ śubhaṃ dāru tadgṛhaupayikam | pīte tu maṇḍale nirdiśettarormadhyagāṃ godhām || 120 ||
mañjiṣṭhābhe bheko nīle sarpastathāruṇe saraṭaḥ | mudgābhe'śmā kapile tu mūṣako'mbhaśca khaḍgābhe || 121 ||
dhānyagoguruhutāśasurāṇāṃ na svapedupari nāpyanuvaṃśam | nottarāparaśirā na ca nagno naiva cārdracaraṇaḥ śriyamicchan || 122 ||
bhūripuṣpavikaraṃ satoraṇaṃ toyapūrṇakalaśopaśobhitam | dhūpagandhabalipūjitāmaraṃ brāhmaṇadhvaniyutaṃ viśedgṛham || 123 ||
[ nikaraṃ ]

Chapter 53: dakārgalādhyāyaḥ [dakārgala-adhyāya]

dhanahānirdārumaye paśupīḍā rugbhayāni cāsthikṛte | lohamaye śastrabhayaṃ kapālakeśeṣu mṛtyuḥ syāt || K(60) ||
aṅgāre stenabhayaṃ bhasmani ca vinirdiśetsadāgnibhayam | śalyaṃ hi marmasaṃsthaṃ suvarṇarajatādṛte'tyaśubham || K(61) ||
dharmyaṃ yaśasyaṃ ca vadāmyato'haṃ dakārgalaṃ yena jalopalabdhiḥ | puṃsāṃ yathāṅgeṣu śirāstathaiva kṣitāvapi pronnatanimnasaṃsthāḥ || 1 ||
[ dagārgalaṃ ] ekena varṇena rasena cāmbhaścyutaṃ nabhasto vasudhāviśeṣāt | nānārasatvaṃ bahuvarṇatāṃ ca gataṃ parīkṣyaṃ kṣititulyameva || 2 ||
puruhūtānalayamanirṛtivaruṇapavanenduśaṅkarā devāḥ | vijñātavyāḥ kramaśaḥ prācyādyānāṃ diśāṃ patayaḥ || 3 ||
dikpatisaṃjñā ca śirā navamī madhye mahāśirānāmnī | etābhyo'nyāḥ śataśo viniḥsṛtā nāmabhiḥ prathitāḥ || 4 ||
pātālādūrdhvaśirā śubhā caturdikṣu saṃsthitā yāśca | koṇadigutthā na śubhāḥ śirānimittānyato vakṣye || 5 ||
[ ūrdhvaśirāḥ śubhāś ] yadi vetaso'mburahite deśe hastaistribhistataḥ paścāt | sārdhe puruṣe toyaṃ vahati śirā paścimā tatra || 6 ||
cihnamapi cārdhapuruṣe maṇḍūkaḥ pāṇḍuro'tha mṛtpītā | puṭabhedakaśca tasminpāṣāṇo bhavati toyamadhaḥ || 7 ||
jambvāścodagdhastaistribhiḥ śirādho naradvaye pūrvā | mṛllohagandhikā pāṇḍurā ca puruṣe'tra maṇḍūkaḥ || 8 ||
[ atha ] jambūvṛkṣasya prāgvalmīko yadi bhavetsamīpasthaḥ | tasmāddakṣiṇapārśve salilaṃ puruṣadvaye svādu || 9 ||
ardhapuruṣe ca matsyaḥ pārāvatasannibhaśca pāṣāṇaḥ | mṛdbhavati cātra nīlā dīrghaṃ kālaṃ ca bahu toyam || 10 ||
paścādudumbarasya tribhireva karairnaradvaye sārdhe | puruṣe sito'hiraśmāñjanopamo'dhaḥ śirā sujalā || 11 ||
udagarjunasya dṛśyo valmīko yadi tato'rjunāddhastaiḥ | tribhirambu bhavati puruṣaistribhirardhasamanvitaiḥ paścāt || 12 ||
śvetā godhārdhanare puruṣe mṛddhūsarā tataḥ kṛṣṇā | pītā sitā sasikatā tato jalaṃ nirdiśedamitam || 13 ||
valmīkopacitāyāṃ nirguṇḍyāṃ dakṣiṇena kathitakaraiḥ | puruṣadvaye sapāde svādu jalaṃ bhavati cāśoṣyam || 14 ||
rohitamatsyo'rdhanare mṛtkapilā pāṇḍurā tataḥ parataḥ | sikatā saśarkarātha krameṇa parato bhavatyambhaḥ || 15 ||
pūrveṇa yadi badaryā valmīko dṛśyate jalaṃ paścāt | puruṣaistribhirādeśyaṃ śvetā gṛhagodhikārdhanare || 16 ||
sapalāśā badarī ceddiśyaparasyāṃ tato jalaṃ bhavati | puruṣatraye sapāde puruṣe'tra ca duṇḍubhaścihnam || 17 ||
[ duṇḍubhiś ] vilvodumbarayoge vihāya hastatrayaṃ tu yāmyena | puruṣaistribhirambu bhavetkṛṣṇo'rdhanare ca maṇḍūkaḥ || 18 ||
[ bilva ] kākodumbarikāyāṃ valmīko dṛśyate śirā tasmin | puruṣatraye sapāde paścimadiksthā vahati sā ca || 19 ||
āpāṇḍupītikā mṛdgorasavarṇaśca bhavati pāṣāṇaḥ | puruṣārdhe kumudanibho dṛṣṭipathaṃ mūṣako yāti || 20 ||
jalaparihīne deśe vṛkṣaḥ kampillako yadā dṛśyaḥ | prācyāṃ hastatritaye vahati śirā dakṣiṇā prathamam || 21 ||
mṛnnīlotpalavarṇā kāpotā dṛśyate tatastasmin | haste'jagandhako matsyakaḥ payo'lpaṃ ca sakṣāram || 22 ||
[ caiva dṛśyate | ajagandhimatsyo bhavati ] śoṇākataroraparottare śirā dvau karāvatikramya | kumudā nāma śirā sā puruṣatrayavāhinī bhavati || 23 ||
āsanno valmīko dakṣiṇapārśve vibhītakasya yadi | adhyardhe bhavati śirā puruṣe jñeyā diśi prācyām || 24 ||
[ tasya ] tasyaiva paścimāyāṃ diśi valmīko yadā bhaveddhaste | tatrodagbhavati śirā caturbhirardhādhikaiḥ puruṣaiḥ || 25 ||
śveto viśvambharakaḥ prathame puruṣe tu kuṅkumābho'śmā | aparasyāṃ diśi ca śirā naśyati varṣatraye'tīte || 26 ||
sakuśaḥ sita aiśānyāṃ valmīko yatra kovidārasya | madhye tayornarairardhapañcamaistoyamakṣobhyam || 27 ||
[ sakuśāsita ] prathame puruṣe bhujagaḥ kamalodarasannibho mahī raktā | kuruvindaḥ pāṣāṇaścihnānyetāni vācyāni || 28 ||
yadi bhavati saptaparṇo valmīkavṛtastaduttare toyam | vācyaṃ puruṣaiḥ pañcabhiratrāpi bhavanti cihnāni || 29 ||
puruṣārdhe maṇḍūko harito haritālasannibhā bhūśca | pāṣāṇo'bhranikāśaḥ saumyā ca śirā śubhāmbuvahā || 30 ||
sarveṣāṃ vṛkṣāṇāmadhaḥ sthito darduro yadā dṛśyaḥ | tasmāddhaste toyaṃ caturbhirardhādhikaiḥ puruṣaiḥ || 31 ||
puruṣe tu bhavati nakulo nīlo mṛtpītikā tataḥ śvetā | dardurasamānarūpaḥ pāṣāṇo dṛśyate cātra || 32 ||
yadyahinilayo dṛśyo dakṣiṇataḥ saṃsthitaḥ karañjasya | hastadvaye tu yāmye puruṣatritaye śirā sārdhe || 33 ||
kacchapakaḥ puruṣārdhe prathamaṃ codbhidyate śirā pūrvā | udaganyā svādujalā harito'śmādhastatastoyam || 34 ||
uttarataśca madhūkādahinilayaḥ paścime tarostoyam | parihṛtya pañca hastānardhāṣṭamapauruṣānprathamam || 35 ||
[ pauruṣe ] ahirājaḥ puruṣe'smindhūmrā dhātrī kuluttha varṇo'śmā | māhendrī bhavati śirā vahati saphenaṃ sadā toyam || 36 ||
[ kulattha ] valmīkaḥ snigdho dakṣiṇena tilakasya sakuśadūrvaścet | puruṣaiḥ pañcabhirambho diśi vāruṇyāṃ śirā pūrvā || 37 ||
sarpāvāsaḥ paścād yadā kadambasya dakṣiṇena jalam | parato hastatritayāt ṣaḍbhiḥ puruṣaisturīyonaiḥ || 38 ||
kauberī cātra śirā vahati jalaṃ lohagandhi cākṣobhyam | kanakanibho maṇḍūko naramātre mṛttikā pītā || 39 ||
valmīkasaṃvṛto yadi tālo vā bhavati nālikero vā | paścāt ṣaḍbhirhastairnaraiścaturbhiḥ śirā yāmyā || 40 ||
yāmyena kapitthasyāhisaṃśrayaścedudagjalaṃ vācyam | sapta parityajya karān khātvā puruṣān jalaṃ pañca || 41 ||
karburako'hiḥ puruṣe kṛṣṇā mṛtpuṭabhidapi ca pāṣāṇaḥ | śvetā mṛtpaścimataḥ śirā tataścottarā bhavati || 42 ||
aśmantakasya vāme badarī vā dṛśyate'hinilayo vā | ṣaḍbhirudaktasya karaiḥ sārdhe puruṣatraye toyam || 43 ||
kūrmaḥ prathame puruṣe pāṣāṇo dhūsaraḥ sasikatā mṛt | ādau ca śirā yāmyā pūrvottarato dvitīyā ca || 44 ||
[ śirā ca ] vāmena haridratarorvalmīkaścejjalaṃ bhavati pūrve | hastatritaye satryaṃśaiḥ pumbhiḥ pañcabhirbhavati || 45 ||
[ cettato jalaṃ | puruṣaiḥ satryaṃśaiḥ ] nīlo bhujagaḥ puruṣe mṛtpītā marakatopamaścāśmā | kṛṣṇā bhūḥ prathamaṃ vāruṇī śirā dakṣiṇenānyā || 46 ||
jalaparihīne deśe dṛśyante'nūpajāni cennimitāni | vīraṇadūrvā mṛdavaśca yatra tasmin jalaṃ puruṣe || 47 ||
[ cihnāni ] bhārṅgī trivṛtā dantī sūkarapādī ca lakṣmaṇā caiva | navamālikā ca hastadvaye'mbu yāmye tribhiḥ puruṣaiḥ || 48 ||
snigdhāḥ pralambaśākhā vāmanavikaṭa drumāḥ samīpajalāḥ | suṣirā jarjarapatrā rūkṣāśca jalena santyaktāḥ || 49 ||
[ viṭa ] tilakāmrātakavaruṇakabhallātakavilvatindukāṅkolāḥ | piṇḍāraśirīṣāñjanaparūṣakā vañjulo'tibalā || 50 ||
[ bilva | aṅkollāḥ | vañjurātibalā ] ete yadi susnigdhā valmīkaiḥ parivṛtāstatastoyam | hastaistribhiruttarataścaturbhirardhena ca nareṇa || 51 ||
[ narasya ] atṛṇe satṛṇā yasmin satṛṇe tṛṇavarjitā mahī yatra | tasmicchirā pradiṣṭā vaktavyaṃ vā dhanaṃ cāsmin || 52 ||
kaṇṭakyakaṇṭakānāṃ vyatyāse'mbhastribhiḥ karaiḥ paścāt | khātvā puruṣatritayaṃ tribhāgayuktaṃ dhanaṃ vā syāt || 53 ||
nadati mahī gambhīraṃ yasmiṃścaraṇāhatā jalaṃ tasmin | sārdhaistribhirmanuṣyaiḥ kauberī tatra ca śirā syāt || 54 ||
vṛkṣasyaikā śākhā yadi vinatā bhavati pāṇḍurā vā syāt | vijñātavyaṃ śākhātale jalaṃ tripuruṣaṃ khātvā || 55 ||
phalakusumavikāro yasya tasya pūrve śirā tribhirhastaiḥ | bhavati puruṣaiścaturbhiḥ pāṣāṇo'dhaḥ kṣitiḥ pītā || 56 ||
yadi kaṇṭakārikā kaṇṭakairvinā dṛśyate sitaiḥ kusumaiḥ | tasyāstale'mbu vācyaṃ tribhirnarairardhapuruṣe ca || 57 ||
kharjūrī dviśiraskā yatra bhavejjalavivarjite deśe | tasyāḥ paścimabhāge nirdeśyaṃ tripuruṣairvāri || 58 ||
[ tripuruṣe ] yadi bhavati karṇikāraḥ sitakusumaḥ syātpalāśavṛkṣo vā | savyena tatra hastadvaye'mbu puruṣadvaye bhavati || 59 ||
[ puruṣatraye ] yasyāmūṣmā dhātryāṃ dhūmo vā tatra vāri narayugale | nirdeṣṭavyā ca śirā mahatā toyapravāheṇa || 60 ||
[ ūṣmā yasyām | narayugme ] yasmin kṣetroddeśe jātaṃ sasyaṃ vināśamupayāti | snigdhamatipāṇḍuraṃ vā mahāśirā narayuge tatra || 61 ||
marudeśe bhavati śirā yathā tathātaḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi | grīvā karabhāṇāmiva bhūtalasaṃsthāḥ śirā yānti || 62 ||
pūrvottareṇa pīloryadi valmīko jalaṃ bhavati paścāt | uttaragamanā ca śirā vijñeyā pañcabhiḥ puruṣaiḥ || 63 ||
cihnaṃ dardura ādau mṛtkapilā tatparaṃ bhaveddharitā | bhavati ca puruṣe adho'śmā tasya tale'mbho vinirdeṣyam || 64 ||
[ mṛtkapilātaḥ paraṃ | vāri nirdecyam ] pīloreva prācyāṃ valmīko'to'rdhapañcamairhastaiḥ | diśi yāmyāyāṃ toyaṃ vaktavyaṃ saptabhiḥ puruṣaiḥ || 65 ||
prathame puruṣe bhujagaḥ sitāsito hastamātramūrtiśca | dakṣiṇato vahati śirā sakṣāraṃ bhūri pānīyam || 66 ||
uttarataśca karīrasyāhigṛhaṃ dakṣiṇe jalaṃ svādu | daśabhiḥ puruṣairjñeyam purṣe pīto'tra maṇḍūkaḥ || 67 ||
[ karīrādahinilaye ] rohītakasya paścādahivāsaścettribhiḥ karairyāmye | dvādaśa puruṣān khātvā sakṣārā paścimena śirā || 68 ||
indratarorvalmīkaḥ prāgdṛśyaḥ paścime śirā haste | khātvā caturdaśa narān kapilā godhā nare prathame || 69 ||
yadi vā suvarṇanāmnastarorbhavedvāmato bhujaṅgagṛham | hastadvaye tu yāmye pañcadaśanarāvasāne'mbu || 70 ||
kṣāraṃ payo'tra nakulo'rdhamānave tāmrasannibhaścāśmā | raktā ca bhavati vasudhā vahati śirā dakṣiṇā tatra || 71 ||
badarīrohitavṛkṣau sampṛktau cedvināpi valmīkam | hastatraye'mbu paścāt ṣoḍaśabhirmānavairbhavati || 72 ||
surasaṃ jalamādau dakṣiṇā śirā vahati cottaneṇānyā | piṣṭanibhaḥ pāṣāṇo mṛt śvetā vṛściko'rdhanare || 73 ||
sakarīrā cedvadarī tribhiḥ karaiḥ paścimena tatrāmbhaḥ | aṣṭādaśabhiḥ puruṣairaiśānī bahujalā ca śirā || 74 ||
pīlusametā badarī hastatrayasammite diśi prācyām | viṃśatyā puruṣāṇāmaśoṣyamambho'tra sakṣāram || 75 ||
kakubhakarīrāvekatra saṃyutau yatra kakubhavilvau vā | hastadvaye'mbu paścānnarairbhavetpañcaviṃśatyā || 76 ||
[ bilbau ] valmīkamūrdhani yadā dūrvā ca kuśāśca pāṇḍurāḥ santi | kūpo madhye deyo jalamatra naraikaviṃśatyā || 77 ||
bhūmiḥ kadambaka valmīke yatra dṛśyate dūrvā | hastadvayena yāmye narairjalaṃ pañcaviṃśatyā || 78 ||
[ bhūmī kadambakayutā | bhūmīkadambaka | hastatrayena ] valmīkatrayamadhye rohītakapādapo yadā bhavati | nānāvṛkṣaiḥ sahitastribhirjalaṃ tatra vaktavyam || 79 ||
hastacatuṣke madhyāt ṣoḍaśabhiścāṅgulairudagvāri | catvāriṃśatpuruṣān khātvāśmādhaḥ śirā bhavati || 80 ||
[ aśmātaḥ ] granthipracurā yasmicchamī bhaveduttareṇa valmīkaḥ | paścātpañcakarānte śatārdhasaṃkhyairnaraiḥ salilam || 81 ||
ekasthāḥ pañca yadā valmīkā madhyamo bhavecchvetaḥ | tasmicchirā pradiṣṭā naraṣaṣṭyā pañcavarjitayā || 82 ||
sapalāśā yatra śamī paścimabhāge'mbu mānavaiḥ ṣaṣṭyā | ardhanare'hiḥ prathamaṃ savālukā pītamṛtparataḥ || 83 ||
valmīkena parivṛtaḥ śveto rohītako bhaved yasmin | pūrveṇa hastamātre saptatyā mānavairambu || 84 ||
śvetā kaṇṭakabahulā yatra śamī dakṣiṇena tatra payaḥ | narapañcakasaṃyutayā saptatyāhirnarārdhe ca || 85 ||
marudeśe yaccihnaṃ na jāṅgale tairjalaṃ vinirdeśyam | jambūvetasapūrvairye puruṣāste marau dviguṇāḥ || 86 ||
[ pūrve ] jambūstrivṛtā maurvī śiśumārī sārivā śivā śyāmā | vīrudhayo vārāhī jyotiṣmatī garuḍavegā ca || 87 ||
[ mūrvā | ca garuḍavegā ] sūkarikamāṣaparṇīvyāghrapadāśceti yadyahernilaye | valmīkāduttaratastribhiḥ karaistripuruṣe toyam || 88 ||
etadanūpe vācyaṃ jāṅgalabhūmau tu pañcabhiḥ puruṣaiḥ | etaireva nimittairmarudeśe saptabhiḥ kathayet || 89 ||
ekanibhā yatra mahī tṛṇataruvalmīkagulmaparihīnā | tasyāṃ yatra vikāro bhavati dharitryāṃ jalaṃ tatra || 90 ||
yatra snigdhā nimnā savālukā sānunādinī vā syāt | tatra ardhapañcakairvāri mānavaiḥ pañcabhiryadi vā || 91 ||
[ ardhapañcamair ] snigdhatarūṇāṃ yāmye naraiścaturbhirjalaṃ prabhūtaṃ ca | tarugahane'pi hi vikṛto yastasmāttadvadeva vadet || 92 ||
namate yatra dharitrī sārdhe puruṣe'mbu jāṅgalānūpe | kīṭā vā yatra vinālayena bahavo'mbu tatrāpi || 93 ||
uṣṇā śītā ca mahī śītoṣṇāmbhastribhirnaraiḥ sārdhaiḥ | indradhanurmatsyo vā valmīko vā caturhastāt || 94 ||
valmīkānāṃ paṅktyāṃ yadyeko'bhyucchritaḥ śirā tadadhaḥ | śuṣyati na rohate vā sasyaṃ yasyāṃ ca tatrāmbhaḥ || 95 ||
nyagrodhapalāśodumbaraiḥ sametaistribhirjalaṃ tadadhaḥ | vaṭapippalasamavāye tadvadvācyaṃ śirā codak || 96 ||
āgneye yadi koṇe grāmasya purasya vā bhavetkūpaḥ | nityaṃ sa karoti bhayaṃ dāhaṃ ca samānuṣaṃ prāyaḥ || 97 ||
[ bhavati ] nairṛtakoṇe bālakṣayaṃ ca vanitābhayaṃ ca vāyavye | diktrayametattyaktvā śeṣāsu śubhāvahāḥ kūpāḥ || 98 ||
[ vanitābhayaṃ ] sārasvatena muninā dakārgalaṃ yatkrtaṃ tadavalokya | āryābhiḥ kṛtametadvṛttairapi mānavaṃ vakṣye || 99 ||
[ dagārgalaṃ ] snigdhā yataḥ pādapagulmavallyo niśchidrapatrāśca tataḥ śirāsti | padmakṣurośīrakulāḥ saguṇḍrāḥ kāśāḥ kuśā vā nalikā nalo vā || 100 ||
kharjūrajambvarjunavetasāḥ syuḥ kṣīrānvitā vā drumagulmavallyaḥ | chatrebhanāgāḥ śatapatranīpāḥ syurnaktamālāśca sasinduvārāḥ || 101 ||
vibhītako vā madayantikā vā yatrāsti tasminpuruṣatraye'mbhaḥ | syātparvatasyopari parvato'nyastatrāpi mūle puruṣatraye'mbhaḥ || 102 ||
yā mauñjikaiḥ kāśakuśaiśca yuktā nīlā ca mṛd yatra saśarkarā ca | tasyāṃ prabhūtaṃ surasaṃ ca toyaṃ kṛṣṇātha vā yatra ca raktamṛdvā || 103 ||
[ mauñjakaiḥ ] saśarkarā tāmramahī kaṣāyaṃ kṣāraṃ dharitrī kapilā karoti | āpāṇḍurāyāṃ lavaṇaṃ pradiṣṭaṃ mṛṣṭaṃ payo nīlavasundharāyām || 104 ||
[ miṣṭam ] śākāśvakarṇārjunavilvasarjāḥ śrīparṇyariṣṭādhavaśiṃśapāśca | chidraiśca patrairdrumagulmavallyo rūkṣāśca dūre'mbu nivedayanti || 105 ||
[ bilva | parṇair ] sūryāgnibhasmoṣṭrakharānuvarṇā yā nirjalā sā vasudhā pradiṣṭā | raktāṅkurāḥ kṣīrayutāḥ karīrā raktā dharā cejjalamaśmano'dhaḥ || 106 ||
vaidūryamudgāmbudamecakābhā pākonmukhodumbarasannibhā vā | bhaṅgāñjanābhā kapilātha vā yā jñeyā śilā bhūrisamīpatoyā || 107 ||
[ vaiḍūryamuḍga | bhṛṅga ] pārāvatakṣaudraghṛtopamā yā kṣaumasya vastrasya ca tulyavarṇā | yā somavallyāśca samānarūpā sāpyāśu toyaṃ kurute'kṣayaṃ ca || 108 ||
[ parāvata | vā ] tāmraiḥ sametā pṛṣatairvicitrairāpāṇḍubhasmoṣṭrakharānurūpā | bhṛṅgopamāṅguṣṭhikapuṣpikā vā sūryāgnivarṇā ca śilā vitoyā || 109 ||
candrātapasphaṭikamauktikahemarūpā yāścendranīlamaṇihiṅgulukāñjanābhāḥ | sūryodayāṃśuharitālanibhāśca yāḥ syustāḥ śobhanā munivaco'tra ca vṛttametat || 110 ||
etā hyabhedyāśca śilāḥ śivāśca yakṣaiśca nāgaiśca sadābhijuṣṭāḥ | yeṣāṃ ca rāṣṭreṣu bhavanti rājṇāṃ teṣāmavṛṣṭirna bhavetkadā cit || 111 ||
bhedaṃ yadā naiti śilā tadānīṃ palāśakāṣṭhaiḥ saha tindukānām | prajvālayitvānalamagnivarṇā sudhāmbusiktā pravidārameti || 112 ||
toyaṃ śritaṃ mokṣakabhasmanā vā yatsaptakṛtvaḥ pariṣecanaṃ tat | kāryaṃ śarakṣārayutaṃ śilāyāḥ prasphoṭanaṃ vahnivitāpitāyāḥ || 113 ||
[ śṛtam ] takrakāñjikasurāḥ sakulatthā yojitāni badarāṇi ca tasmin | saptarātramuṣitānyabhitaptāṃ dārayanti hi śilāṃ pariṣekaiḥ || 114 ||
naimbaṃ patraṃ tvakca nālaṃ tilānāṃ | sāpāmārgaṃ tindukaṃ syādguḍūcī | gomūtreṇa srāvitaḥ kṣāra eṣāṃ 53.115d ṣaṭkṛtvo'tastāpito bhidyate'śmā || 115 ||
ārkaṃ payo huḍuviṣāṇamaṣīsametaṃ pārāvatākhuśakṛtā ca yutaḥ pralepaḥ | ṭaṅkasya tailamathitasya tato'sya pānaṃ paścācchitasya na śilāsu bhavedvighātaḥ || 116 ||
kṣāre kadalyā mathitena yukte dinoṣite pāyitamāyasaṃ yat | samyak śitaṃ cāśmani naiti bhaṅgaṃ na cānyaloheṣvapi tasya kauṇṭhyam || 117 ||
[ yakte | chitaṃ ] pālī prāgaparāyatāmbu suciraṃ dhatte na yāmyottarā kallolairavadārameti marutā sā prāyaśaḥ preritaiḥ | tāṃ cedicchati sāradārubhirapāṃ sampātamāvārayetpāṣāṇādibhireva vā praticayaṃ kṣuṇṇaṃ dvipāśvādibhiḥ || 118 ||
[ kṣunnaṃ ] kakubhavaṭāmraplakṣakadambaiḥ saniculajambūvetasanīpaiḥ | kurabakatālāśokamadhūkairbakulavimiśraiścāvṛtatīrām || 119 ||
[ kuravaka ] dvāraṃ ca nairvāhikamekadeśe kāryaṃ śilāsañcitavārimārgam | kośasthitaṃ nirvivaraṃ kapāṭaṃ kṛtvā tataḥ pāṃśubhirāvapettam || 120 ||
añjanamustośīraiḥ sarājakośātakāmalakacūrṇaiḥ | katakaphalasamāyuktairyogaḥ kūpe pradātavyaḥ || 121 ||
kaluṣaṃ kaṭukaṃ lavaṇaṃ virasaṃ salilaṃ yadi vā śubhagandhi bhavet | tadanena bhavatyamalaṃ surasaṃ susugandhi guṇairaparaiśca yutam || 122 ||
[ aśubhagandhi ] hasto maghānurādhāpuṣyadhaniṣṭhottarāṇi rohiṇyaḥ | śatabhiṣagityārambhe kūpānāṃ śasyate bhagaṇaḥ || 123 ||
kṛtvā varuṇasya baliṃ vaṭavetasakīlakaṃ śirāsthāne | kusumairgandhairdhūpaiḥ sampūjya nidhāpayetprathamam || 124 ||

Chapter 54: vṛkṣāyurvedādhyāyaḥ [vṛkṣāyurveda-adhyāya]

meghodbhavaṃ prathamameva mayā pradiṣṭaṃ jyeṣṭhāmatītya baladevamatādi dṛṣṭvā | bhaumaṃ dagārgalamidaṃ kathitaṃ dvitīyaṃ samyagvarāhamihireṇa muniprasādāt || K(125) ||
prāntacchāyāvinirmuktā na manojñā jalāśayāḥ | yasmādato jalaprānteṣvārāmānviniveśayet || 1 ||
mṛdvī bhūḥ sarvavṛkṣāṇāṃ hitā tasyām tilānvapet | puṣpitāṃstāṃśca mṛdnīyātkarmaitatprathamaṃ bhuvaḥ || 2 ||
[ gṛhṇīyāt | bhuvi ] ariṣṭāśokapunnāgaśirīṣāḥ sapriyaṅgavaḥ | maṅgalyāḥ pūrvamārāme ropaṇīyā gṛheṣu vā || 3 ||
panasāśokakadalījambūlakucadāḍimāḥ | drākṣāpālīvatāścaiva bījapūrātimuktakāḥ || 4 ||
ete drumāḥ kāṇḍaropyā gomayena pralepitāḥ | mūlocchede'tha vā skandhe ropaṇīyāḥ paraṃ tataḥ || 5 ||
[ kāṇḍāropyā | prayatnataḥ ] ajātaśākhācchiśire jātaśākhān himāgame | varṣāgame ca suskandhānyathādiksthānpraropayet || 6 ||
[ yathādikpratiropayet ] ghṛtośīratilakṣaudraviḍaṅgakṣīragomayaiḥ | āmūlaskandhaliptānāṃ saṃkrāmaṇaviropaṇam || 7 ||
śucirbhūtvā taroḥ pūjāṃ kṛtvā snānānulepanaiḥ | ropayed ropitaścaiva patraistaireva jāyate || 8 ||
sāyaṃ prātaśca gharmartau śītakāle dināntare | varṣāsu ca bhuvaḥ śoṣe sektavyā ropitā drumāḥ || 9 ||
[ gharmānte ] jambūvetasavānīrakadambodumbarārjunāḥ | bījapūrakamṛdvīkālakucāśca sadāḍimāḥ || 10 ||
vañjulo naktamālaśca tilakaḥ panasastathā | timiro'mrātakaśceti ṣoḍaśānūpajāḥ smṛtāḥ || 11 ||
[ caiva ] uttamaṃ viṃśatirhastā madhyamaṃ ṣoḍaśāntaram | sthānātsthānāntaraṃ kāryaṃ vṛkṣāṇāṃ dvādaśāvaram || 12 ||
abhyāsajātāstaravaḥ samspṛśantaḥ parasparam | miśrairmūlaiśca na phalaṃ samyag yacchanti pīḍitāḥ || 13 ||
śītavātātapai rogo jāyate pāṇḍupatratā | avṛddhiśca pravālānāṃ śākhāśoṣo rasasrutiḥ || 14 ||
[ prabālānām ] cikitsitamathaiteṣāṃ śastreṇādau viśodhanam | viḍaṅgaghṛtapaṅkāktān secayetkṣīravāriṇā || 15 ||
phalanāśe kulatthaiśca māṣairmudgaistilairyavaiḥ | śṛtaśītapayaḥ sekaḥ phalapuṣpasamṛddhaye || 16 ||
[ abhivṛddhaye ] avikājaśakṛccūrṇasyāḍhake dve tilāḍhakam | saktuprastho jaladroṇo gomāṃsatulayā saha || 17 ||
saptarātroṣitairetaiḥ sekaḥ kāryo vanaspateḥ | valmīgulmalatānāṃ ca phalapuṣpāya sarvadā || 18 ||
vāsarāṇi daśa dugdhabhāvitaṃ bījamājyayutahastayojitam | gomayena bahuśo virūkṣitaṃ krauḍamārgapiśitaiśca dhūpitam || 19 ||
māṃsasūkaravasāsamanvitaṃ ropitaṃ ca parikarmitāvanau | kṣīrasaṃyutajalāvasecitaṃ jāyate kusumayuktameva tat || 20 ||
[ matsya ] tintiḍītyapi karoti vallarīṃ vrīhimāṣatilacūrṇasaktubhiḥ | pūtimāṃsasahitaiśca secitā dhūpitā ca satataṃ haridrayā || 21 ||
kapitthavallīkaraṇāya mūlānyāsphotadhātrīdhavavāsikānām | palāśinī vetasasūryaballī śyāmātimuktaiḥ sahitāṣṭamūlī || 22 ||
[ vallī ] kṣīre śṛte cāpyanayā suśīte tālā śataṃ sthāpya kapitthabījam | dine dine śoṣitamarkapādairmāsaṃ vidhistveṣa tato'dhiropyam || 23 ||
[ nālā ] hastāyataṃ taddviguṇaṃ gabhīraṃ khātvāvaṭaṃ proktajalāvapūrṇam | śuṣkaṃ pradagdhaṃ madhusarpiṣā tatpralepayedbhasmasamanvitana || 24 ||
[ samanvitena ] cūrṇīkṛtairmāṣatilairyavaiśca prapūrayedmṛttikayāntarasthaiḥ | matsyāmiṣāmbhassahitaṃ ca hanyād yāvadghanatvaṃ samupāgataṃ tat || 25 ||
[ ambhaḥ ] uptaṃ ca bījaṃ caturaṅgulādho matsyāmbhasā māṃsajalaiśca siktam | vallī bhavatyāśu śubhapravālā vismāpanī maṇḍapamāvṛṇoti || 26 ||
śataśo'ṅkolasambhūtaphalakalkena bhāvitam | etattailena vā bījaṃ ślaiṣmātakaphalena vā || 27 ||
[ aṅkolla | śleṣmātaka ] vāpitaṃ karakonmiśramṛdi tatkṣaṇajanmakam | phalabhārānvitā śākhā bhavatīti kimadbhutam || 28 ||
śleṣmātakasya bījāni niṣkulīkṛtya bhāvayetprājñaḥ | aṅkolavijjalādbhiśchāyāyāṃ saptakṛtvaivam || 29 ||
[ aṅkolla | saptakṛtv ] māhiṣagomayaghṛṣṭānyasya karīṣe ca tāni nikṣipya | karakājalamṛdyoge nyuptānyahnā phalakarāṇi || 30 ||
dhruvamṛdumūlaviśākhā gurubhaṃ śravaṇastathāśvinī hastaḥ | uktāni divyadṛgbhiḥ pādapasaṃropaṇe bhāni || 31 ||
[ hastaṃ ]

Chapter 55: prāsādalakṣaṇādhyāyaḥ [prāsādalakṣaṇa-adhyāya]

kṛtvā prabhūtaṃ salilamārāmānviniveśya ca | devatāyatanaṃ kuryād yaśodharmābhivṛddhaye || 1 ||
iṣṭāpūrtena labhyante ye lokāstānbubhūṣatā | devānāmālayaḥ kāryo dvayamapi atra dṛśyate || 2 ||
salilodyānayukteṣu kṛteṣvakṛteṣu ca | sthāneṣveteṣu sānnidhyamupagacchanti devatāḥ || 3 ||
saraḥsu nalinīchatranirastaraviraśmiṣu | haṃsāṃsākṣiptakahlāravīthī || 4 ||
[ vīcīvimalavāriṣu | vīthī ] haṃsakāraṇḍavakrauñcacakravākavirāviṣu | paryantaniculacchāyāviśrāntajalacāriṣu || 5 ||
krauñcakāñcīkalāpāśca kalahaṃsakalasvarāḥ | nadyastoyāṃśukā yatra śapharīkṛtamekhalāḥ || 6 ||
[ svanāḥ ] phullatīradrumottaṃsāḥ saṅgamaśroṇimaṇḍalāḥ | pulinābhyunnatorasyā haṃsavāsāśca nimnagāḥ || 7 ||
[ haṃsahāsāś ] vanopāntanadīśailanirjharopāntabhūmiṣu | ramante devatā nityaṃ pureṣūdyānavatsu ca || 8 ||
bhūmayo brāhmaṇādīnāṃ yāḥ proktā vāstukarmaṇi | tā eva teṣāṃ śasyante devatāyataneṣvapi || 9 ||
catuḥṣaṣṭipadaṃ kāryaṃ devatāyatanaṃ sadā | dvāraṃ ca madhyamaṃ tasmin samadiksthaṃ praśasyate || 10 ||
[ tatra ] yo vistāro bhaved yasya dviguṇā tatsamunnatiḥ | ucchrāyād yastṛtīyāṃśastena tulyā kaṭiḥ smṛtā || 11 ||
[ kaṭirbhavet ] vistārārdhaṃ bhavedgarbho bhittayo'nyāḥ samantataḥ | garbhapādena vistīrṇaṃ dvāraṃ dviguṇamucchritam || 12 ||
ucchrāyātpādavistīrṇā śākhā tadvadudumbaraḥ | vistārapādapratimaṃ bāhulyaṃ śākhayoḥ smṛtam || 13 ||
tripañcasaptanavabhiḥ śākhābhistatpraśasyate | adhaḥ śākhācaturbhāge pratīhārau niveśayet || 14 ||
śeṣaṃ maṅgalyavihagaiḥ śrīvṛkṣaiḥ svastikairghaṭaiḥ | mithunaiḥ patravallībhiḥ pramathaiścopaśobhayet || 15 ||
[ śrīvṛkṣasvastikair ] dvāramānāṣṭabhāgonā pratimā syātsapiṇḍikā | dvau bhāgau pratimā tatra tṛtīyāṃśaśca piṇḍikā || 16 ||
merumandarakailāsavimānacchandanandanāḥ | samudgapadmagaruḍanandivardhanakuñjarāḥ || 17 ||
guharājo vṛṣo haṃsaḥ sarvatobhadrako ghaṭaḥ | siṃho vṛttaścatuṣkoṇaḥ ṣoḍaśāṣṭāśrayastathā || 18 ||
ityete viṃśatiḥ proktāḥ prāsādāḥ saṃjñayā mayā | yathoktānukrameṇaiva lakṣaṇāni vadāmyataḥ || 19 ||
tatra ṣaḍaśrirmerurdvādaśabhaumo vicitrakuharaśca | dvārairyutaścaturbhirdvātriṃśaddhastavistīrṇaḥ || 20 ||
triṃśaddhastāyāmo daśabhaumo mandaraḥ śikharayuktaḥ | kailāso'pi śikharavānaṣṭāviṃśo'ṣṭabhaumaśca || 21 ||
jālagavākṣakayukto vimānasaṃjñastrisaptakāyāmaḥ | nandana iti ṣaḍbhaumo dvātriṃśaḥ ṣoḍaśāṇḍayuktaḥ || 22 ||
vṛttaḥ samudganāmā padmaḥ padmākṛtiḥ śayā aṣṭau | śṛṅgeṇaikena bhavedekaiva ca bhūmikā tasya || 23 ||
[ śayānāṣṭau ] garuḍākṛtiśca garuḍo nandīti ca ṣaṭcatuṣkavistīrṇaḥ | kāryastu saptabhaumo vibhūṣito'ṇḍaistu viṃśatyā || 24 ||
[ ca | ca ] kuñjara iti gajapṛṣṭhaḥ ṣoḍaśahastaḥ samantato mūlāt | guharājaḥ ṣoḍaśakastricandraśālā bhavedvalabhī || 25 ||
vṛṣa ekabhūmiśṛṅgo dvādaśahastaḥ samantato vṛttaḥ | haṃso haṃsākāro ghaṭo'ṣṭahastaḥ kalaśarūpaḥ || 26 ||
dvārairyutaścaturbhirbahuśikharo bhavati sarvatobhadraḥ | bahuruciracandraśālaḥ ṣaḍviṃśaḥ pañcabhaumaśca || 27 ||
siṃhaḥ siṃhākrānto dvādaśakoṇo'ṣṭahastavistīrṇaḥ | catvāro'ñjanarūpāḥ pañcāṇḍayutastu caturasraḥ || 28 ||
[ caturaśraḥ ] bhūmikāṅgulamānena mayasyāṣṭottaraṃ śatam | sārdhaṃ hastatrayaṃ caiva kathitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā || 29 ||
prāhuḥ sthapatayaścātra matamekaṃ vipaścitaḥ | kapotapālisaṃyuktā nyūnā gacchanti tulyatām || 30 ||
prāsādalakṣaṇamidaṃ kathitaṃ samāsādgargeṇa yadviracitaṃ tadihāsti sarvam | manvādibhirviracitāni pṛthūni yāni tatsaṃspṛśanprati mayātra kṛto'dhikāraḥ || 31 ||
[ tatsaṃsmṛtiṃ ]

Chapter 56: vajralepalakṣaṇādhyāyaḥ [vajralepalakṣaṇa-adhyāya]

āmaṃ tindukamāmaṃ kapitthakaṃ puṣpamapi ca śālmalyāḥ | bījāni śallakīnāṃ dhanvanavalko vacā ceti || 1 ||
etaiḥ saliladroṇaḥ kvāthayitavyo'ṣṭabhāgaśeṣaśca | avatāryo'sya ca kalko dravyairetaiḥ samanuyojyaḥ || 2 ||
śrīvāsakarasaguggulubhallātakakundurūkasarjarasaiḥ | atasībilvaiśca yutaḥ kalko'yaṃ vajralepākhyaḥ || 3 ||
prāsādaharmyavalabhīliṅgapratimāsu kuḍyakūpeṣu | santapto dātavyo varṣasahasrāyutasthāyī || 4 ||
lākṣākunduruguggulugṛhadhūmakapitthabilvamadhyāni | nāga phalanimbatindukamadanaphalamadhūkamañjiṣṭhāḥ || 5 ||
[ balāphala ] sarjarasarasāmalakāni ceti kalkaḥ kṛto dvitīyo'yam | vajrākhyaḥ prathamaguṇairayamapi teṣveva kāryeṣu || 6 ||
gomahiṣājaviṣāṇaiḥ khararomṇā mahiṣacarmagavyaiśca | nimbakapittharasaiḥ saha vajratalo nāma kalko'nyaḥ || 7 ||
[ vajrataro ] aṣṭau sīsakabhāgāḥ kāṃsasya dvau tu rītikābhāgaḥ | mayakathito yogo'yaṃ vijñeyo vajrasaṅghātaḥ || 8 ||

Chapter 57: pratimālakṣaṇādhyāyaḥ [pratimālakṣaṇa-adhyāya]

jālāntarage bhānau yadaṇutaraṃ darśanaṃ rajo yāti | tadvindyātparamāṇuṃ prathamaṃ taddhi pramāṇānām || 1 ||
paramāṇurajo bālāgralikṣayūkaṃ yavo'ṅgulaṃ ceti | aṣṭaguṇāni yathottaramaṅgulamekaṃ bhavati saṃkhyā || 2 ||
[ vālāgra | yūkā | mātrā ] devāgāradvārasyāṣṭāmśonasya yastṛtīyo'ṃśaḥ | tatpiṇḍikāpramāṇaṃ pratimā taddviguṇaparimāṇā || 3 ||
svairaṅgulapramāṇairdvādaśa vīstīrṇamāyataṃ ca mukham | nagnajitā tu caturdaśa dairghyeṇa drāviḍaṃ kathitam || 4 ||
[ vistīrṇam ] nāsālalāṭacibukagrīvāścaturāṅgulāstathā karṇau | dve aṅgule ca hanunī cibukaṃ ca dvyaṅgulaṃ vitatam || 5 ||
[ hanuke | vistṛtam ] aṣṭāṅgulaṃ lalāṭaṃ vistārāddvyaṅgulātpare śaṅkhau | caturaṅgulau tu śaṅkhau karṇau tu dvyaṅgulau pṛthulau || 6 ||
[ dvyaṅgulaṃ ] karṇopāntaḥ kāryo'rdhapañcame bhrūsamena sūtreṇa | karṇasrotaḥ sukumārakaṃ ca netraprabandhasamam || 7 ||
[ nayana ] caturaṅgulaṃ vasiṣṭhaḥ kathayati netrāntakarṇayorvivaram | adharo'ṅgulapramāṇastasyārdhenottroṣṭhaśca || 8 ||
ardhāṅgulā tu gocchā vaktraṃ caturaṅgulāyataṃ kāryam | vipulaṃ tu sārdhamaṅgulamavyāttaṃ tryaṅgulaṃ vyāttam || 9 ||
[ adhyāttattryaṅgulaṃ ] dvyaṅgulatulyau nāsāpuṭau ca nāsā puṭāgrato jñeyā | syāddvyaṅgulamucchrāyaścaturaṅgulamantaraṃ cākṣṇoḥ || 10 ||
dvyaṅgulamito'kṣikośo dve netre tattribhāgikā tārā | dṛktārā pañcāṃśo netravikāśo'ṅgulaṃ bhavati || 11 ||
paryantātparyantaṃ daśa bhruvo'rdhāṅgulaṃ bhruvorlekhā | bhrūmadhyaṃ dvyaṅgulakaṃ bhūrdhairghyeṇāṅgulacatuṣkam || 12 ||
[ bhrūr ] kāryā tu keśarekhā bhrūbandhasamāṅgulārdhavistīrṇā | netrānte karavīrakamupanyasedaṅgulapramitam || 13 ||
dvātriṃśatpariṇāhāccaturdaśāyāmato'ṅgulāni śiraḥ | dvādaśa tu citrakarmaṇi dṛśyante viṃśatiradṛśyāḥ || 14 ||
āsyaṃ sakeśanicayaṃ ṣoḍaśa dairghyeṇa nagnijitproktam | grīvā daśa vistīrṇā pariṇāhādviṃśatiḥ saikā || 15 ||
[ nagnajit ] kaṇṭhāddvādaśa hṛdayaṃ hṛdayānnābhī ca tatpramāṇena | nābhīmadhyādmeḍhrāntaraṃ ca tattulyamevoktam || 16 ||
[ nābhiś ] ūrū cāṅgulamānaiścaturyutā viṃśatistathā jaṅghe | jānukapicche caturaṅgule ca pādau ca tattulyau || 17 ||
dvādaśadīrghau ṣaṭ pṛthutayā ca pādau trikāyatāṅguṣṭhau | pañcāṅgulapariṇāhau pradeśinī tryaṅgulaṃ dīrghā || 18 ||
aṣṭāṃśāṃśonāḥ śeṣāṅgulyaḥ krameṇa kartavyāḥ | sacaturthabhāgamaṅgulamutsedho'ṅguṣṭhakasyoktaḥ || 19 ||
[ śeṣāṅgulayaḥ ] aṅguṣṭhanakhaḥ kathitas caturthabhāgonamaṅgulaṃ tajjñaiḥ | śeṣanakhānāmardhāṅgulaṃ kramātkiṃcidūnaṃ vā || 20 ||
jaṅghāgre pariṇāhaścaturdaśoktastu vistarātpañca | madhye tu sapta vipulā pariṇāhāttriguṇitāḥ sapta || 21 ||
[ vistaraḥ ] aṣṭau tu jānumadhye vaipulyaṃ tryaṣṭakaṃ tu pariṇāhaḥ | vipulau caturdaśorū madhye dviguṇaśca tatparidhiḥ || 22 ||
kaṭiraṣṭādaśa vipulā catvāriṃśaccaturyutā paridhau | aṅgulamekaṃ nābhī vedhena tathā pramāṇena || 23 ||
[ nābhir ] catvāriṃśaddviyutā nābhīmadhyena madhyapariṇāhaḥ | stanayoḥ ṣoḍaśa cāntaramūrdhvaṃ kakṣye ṣaḍaṅgulike || 24 ||
[ kakṣe ] aṣṭāvaṃsau dvādaśa bāhū kāryau tathā prabāhū ca | bāhū ṣaḍvistīrṇau pratibāhū tvaṅgulacatuṣkam || 25 ||
[ kāryāvaṣṭāvaṃsau dvādaśa bāhū | ṣaḍvistirṇau ] ṣoḍaśa bāhū mūle pariṇāhāddvādaśāgrahaste ca | vistāreṇa karatalaṃ ṣaḍaṅgulaṃ sapta dairghyeṇa || 26 ||
pañcāṅgulāni madhyā pradeśinī madhyaparvadalahīnā | anayā tulyā cānāmikā kaniṣṭhā tu parvonā || 27 ||
parvadvayamaṅguṣṭhaḥ śeṣāṅgulyastribhistribhiḥ kāryāḥ | nakhaparimāṇaṃ kāryaṃ sarvāsām parvaṇo'rdhena || 28 ||
[ śeṣāṅgulayas ] deśānurūpabhūṣaṇaveṣālaṅkāramūrtibhiḥ kāryā | pratimā lakṣaṇayuktā sannihitā vṛddhidā bhavati || 29 ||
daśarathatanayo rāmo baliśca vairocaniḥ śataṃ viṃśam | dvādaśahānyā śeṣāḥ pravarasamanyūnaparimāṇāḥ || 30 ||
kāryo'ṣṭabhujo bhagavāṃścaturbhujo dvibhuja eva vā viṣṇuḥ | śrīvatsāṅkitavakṣāḥ kaustubhamaṇibhūṣitoraskaḥ || 31 ||
atasīkusumaśyāmaḥ pītāmbaranivasanaḥ prasannamukhaḥ | kuṇḍalakirīṭadhārī pīnagaloraḥsthalāṃsabhujaḥ || 32 ||
khaḍgagadāśarapāṇirdakṣiṇataḥ śāntidaścaturthakaraḥ | vāmakareṣu ca kārmukakheṭakacakrāṇi śaṅkhaśca || 33 ||
atha ca caturbhujamicchati śāntida eko gadādharaścānyaḥ | dakṣiṇapārśve tvevaṃ vāme śaṅkhaśca cakraṃ ca || 34 ||
[ hy ] dvibhujasya tu śāntikaro dakṣiṇahasto'paraśca śaṅkhadharaḥ | evaṃ viṣṇoḥ pratimā kartavyā bhūtimicchadbhiḥ || 35 ||
baladevo halapāṇirmadavibhramalocanaśca kartavyaḥ | vibhratkuṇḍalamekaṃ śaṅkhendumṛṇālagauratanuḥ || 36 ||
[ bibhrat | vapuḥ ] ekānaṃśā kāryā devī baladevakṛṣṇayormadhye | kaṭisaṃsthitavāmakarā sarojamitareṇa codvahatī || 37 ||
kāryā caturbhujā yā vāmakarābhyāṃ sapustakaṃ kamalam | dvābhyāṃ dakṣiṇapārśve varamarthiṣvakṣasūtraṃ ca || 38 ||
vāmo'tha vāṣṭabhujāyāḥ kamaṇḍaluścāpamambujaṃ śāstram | varaśaradarpaṇayuktāḥ savyabhujāḥ sākṣasūtrāśca || 39 ||
[ vāmeṣvaṣṭabhujāyāḥ ] śāmbaśca gadāhastaḥ pradyumnaścāpabhṛtsurūpaśca | anayoḥ striyau ca kārye kheṭakanistriṃśadhāriṇyau || 40 ||
brahmā kamaṇḍalukaraścaturmukhaḥ paṇkajāsanasthaśca | skandaḥ kumārarūpaḥ śaktidharo barhiketuśca || 41 ||
śuklacaturviṣāṇo dvipo mahendrasya vajrapāṇitvam | tiryag lalāṭasaṃsthaṃ tṛtīyamapi locanaṃ cihnam || 42 ||
śambhoḥ śirasīndukalā vṛṣadhvajo'kṣi ca tṛtīyamapi cordhvam | śūlaṃ dhanuḥ pinākaṃ vāmārdhe vā girisutārdham || 43 ||
padmāṅkitakaracaraṇaḥ prasannamūrtiḥ sunīcakeśaśca | padmāsanopaviṣṭaḥ piteva jagato bhavati buddhaḥ || 44 ||
[ bhavet ] ājānulambabāhuḥ śrīvatsāṅkaḥ praśāntamūrtiśca | digvāsāstaruṇo rūpavāṃśca kāryo'rhatāṃ devaḥ || 45 ||
nāsālalāṭajaṅghorugaṇḍavakṣāṃsi connatāni raveḥ | kuryādudīcyaveṣaṃ gūḍhaṃ pādāduro yāvat || 46 ||
bibhrāṇaḥ svakararuhe bāhubhyāṃ paṅkaje mukuṭadhārī | kuṇḍalabhūṣitavadanaḥ pralambahāro viyadgavṛtaḥ || 47 ||
[ pāṇibhyāṃ | viyaṅga ] kamalodaradyutimukhaḥ kañcukaguptaḥ smitaprasannamukhaḥ | ratnojjvalaprabhāmaṇḍalaśca kartuḥ śubhakaro'rkaḥ || 48 ||
saumyā tu hastamātrā vasudā hastadvayocchritā pratimā | kṣemasubhikṣāya bhavettricaturhastapramāṇā yā || 49 ||
nṛpabhayamatyaṅgāyāṃ hīnāṅgāyāmakalyatā kartuḥ | śātodaryāṃ kṣudbhayamarthavināśaḥ kṛśāṅgāyām || 50 ||
[ kṛśāyāṃ ca ] maraṇaṃ tu sakṣatāyāṃ śastranipātena nirdiśetkartuḥ | vāmāvanatā patnīṃ dakṣiṇavinatā hinastyāyuḥ || 51 ||
andhatvamūrdhvadṛṣṭyā karoti cintāmadhomukhī dṛṣṭiḥ | sarvapratimāsvevaṃ śubhāśubhaṃ bhāskaroktasamam || 52 ||
liṅgasya vṛttaparadhiṃ dairghyeṇāsūtrya tattridhā vibhajet | mūle taccaturasraṃ madhye tvaṣṭāśriṃ vṛttamataḥ || 53 ||
[ caturaśraṃ ] caturasramavanikhāte madhyaṃ kāryaṃ tu piṇḍikāśvabhre | dṛśyocchrāyeṇa samā samantataḥ piṇḍikā śvabhrāt || 54 ||
[ caturaśram | piṇḍakā ] kṛśadīrghaṃ deśaghnaṃ pārśvavihīnaṃ purasya nāśaya | yasya kṣataṃ bhavedmastake vināśāya talliṅgam || 55 ||
mātṛgaṇaḥ kartavyaḥ svanāmadevānurūpakṛtacihnaḥ | revanto'śvārūḍho mṛgayākrīḍādiparivāraḥ || 56 ||
daṇḍī yamo mahiṣago haṃsārūḍhaśca pāśabhṛdvaruṇaḥ | naravāhanaḥ kubero vāmakirīṭī bṛhatkukṣiḥ || 57 ||

Chapter 58: vanasampraveśādhyāyaḥ [vanasampraveśa-adhyāya]

pramathādhipo gajamukhaḥ pralambajaṭharaḥ kuṭhāradhārī syāt | ekaviṣāṇo bibhranmūlakakandaṃ sunīladalakandam || K(58) ||
karturanukūladivase daivajñaviśodhite śubhanimitte | maṅgalaśakunaiḥ prāsthānikaiśca vanasampraveśaḥ syāt || 1 ||
pitṛvanamārgasurālayavalmīkodyānatāpasāśramajāḥ | caityasaritsaṅgamasambhavāśca ghaṭatoyasiktāśca || 2 ||
kubjānujātavallīnipīḍitā vajramārutopahatāḥ | svapatitahastinipīḍitaśuṣkāgnipluṣṭamadhunilayāḥ || 3 ||
taravo varjayitavyāḥ śubhadāḥ syuḥ snigdhapatrakusumaphalāḥ | abhimatavṛkṣaṃ gatvā kuryātpūjāṃ sabalipuṣpām || 4 ||
suradārucandanaśamīmadhūkataravaḥ śubhā dvijātīnām | kṣatrasyāriṣṭāśvatthakhadirabilvā vivṛddhikarāḥ || 5 ||
vaiśyānāṃ jīvakakhadirasindhukasyandanāśca śubhaphaladāḥ | tindukakesarasarjārjunāmraśālāśca śūdrāṇām || 6 ||
[ spandanāś ] liṅgaṃ vā pratimā vā drumavatsthāpyā yathā diśaṃ yasmāt | tasmāccihnayitavyā diśo drumasyordhvamatha vādhaḥ || 7 ||
paramānnamodakaudanadadhipalalollopikādibhirbhakṣyaiḥ | madyaiḥ kusumairdhūpairgandhaiśca taruṃ samabhyarcya || 8 ||
surapitṛpiśācarākṣasabhujagāsuragaṇavināyakādyānām | kṛtvā rātrau pūjāṃ vṛkṣaṃ saṃspṛśya ca brūyāt || 9 ||
arcārthamamukasya tvaṃ devasya parikalpitaḥ | namaste vṛkṣa pūjeyaṃ vidhivatsampragṛhyatām || 10 ||
yānīha bhūtāni vasanti tāni baliṃ gṛhītvā vidhivatprayuktam | anyatra vāsaṃ parikalpyantu kṣamantu tānyadya namo'stu tebhyaḥ || 11 ||
vṛkṣaṃ prabhāte salilena siktvā pūrvottarasyāṃ diśi sannikṛtya | madhvājyadigdhena kuṭhārakeṇa pradakṣiṇaṃ śeṣamato nihanyāt || 12 ||
[ liptena | abhihanyāt ] pūrveṇa pūrvottarato'tha vodak | pated yadā vṛddhikarastadā syāt | āgneyakoṇātkramaśo'gnidāharugrāga rogāsturagakṣayaśca || 13 ||
[ kṣudroga ] yannoktamasminvanasampraveśe nipātavicchedanavṛkṣagarbhāḥ | indradhvaje vāstuni ca pradiṣṭāḥ | pūrvaṃ mayā te'tra tathaiva yojyāḥ || 14 ||

Chapter 59: pratimāpratiṣṭhāpanādhyāyaḥ [pratimāpratiṣṭhāpana-adhyāya]

diśi yāmyāyāṃ kuryādadhivāsanamaṇḍapaṃ budhaḥ prāgvā | toraṇacatuṣṭayayutaṃ śastadrumapallavacchannam || 1 ||
[ saumyāyāṃ ] pūrve bhāge citrāḥ srajaḥ patākāśca maṇḍapasyoktāḥ | āgneyyāṃ diśi raktāḥ kṛṣṇāḥ syuryāmyanairṛtyoḥ || 2 ||
[ nairṛtayoḥ ] śvetā diśyaparasyām vāyavyāyāṃ tu pāṇḍurā eva | citrāścottarapārśve pītāḥ pūrvottare kāryāḥ || 3 ||
[ koṇe ] āyuḥ śrībalajayadā dārumayī mṛṇmayī tathā pratimā | lokahitāya maṇimayī sauvarṇī puṣṭidā bhavati || 4 ||
[ mṛnmayī ] rajatamayī kīrtikarī prajāvivṛddhiṃ karoti tāmramayī | bhūlābhaṃ tu mahāntaṃ śailī pratimātha vā liṅgam || 5 ||
śaṅkhūpahatā pratimā pradhānapuruṣaṃ kulaṃ ca ghātayati | śvabhropahatā rogānupadravāṃśca kṣayaṃ kurute || 6 ||
[ akṣayān ] maṇḍapamadhye sthaṇḍilamupalipyāstīrya sikatayātha kuśaiḥ | bhadrāsanakṛtaśīrṣopadhānapādāṃ nyasetpratimām || 07 ||
plakṣāśvatthodumbaraśirīṣavaṭasambhavaiḥ kaṣāyajalaiḥ | maṅgalyasaṃjñitābhiḥ sarvauṣadhibhiḥ kuśādyābhiḥ || 8 ||
dvipavṛṣabhoddhataparvatavalmīkasaritsamāgamataṭeṣu | padmasaraḥsu ca mṛdbhiḥ sapañcagavyaiśca tīrthajalaiḥ || 9 ||
[ uddhṛta ] pūrvaśiraskāṃ snātāṃ suvarṇaratnāmbubhiśca sasugandhaiḥ | nānātūryaninādaiḥ puṇyāhairvedanirghoṣaiḥ || 10 ||
aindryāṃ diśīndraliṅgā mantrāḥ prāgdakṣiṇe'gniliṅgāśca | vaktavyā dvijamukhyaiḥ pūjyāste dakṣiṇābhiśca || 11 ||
[ japtavyā ] yo devaḥ saṃsthāpyastanmantraiścānalaṃ dvijo juhuyāt | agninimittāni mayā proktānīndradhvajotthāne || 12 ||
[ ucchrāye ] dhūmākulo'pasavyo muhurmuhurviphuliṅgakṛnna śubhaḥ | hotuḥ smṛtilopo vā prasarpaṇaṃ cāśubhaṃ proktam || 13 ||
snātāmabhuktavastrāṃ svalaṅkṛtāṃ pūjitāṃ kusumagandhaiḥ | pratimāṃ svāstīrṇāyāṃ śayyāyāṃ sthāpakaḥ kuryāt || 14 ||
suptāṃ sagītanṛtyairjāgaraṇaiḥ samyagevamadhivāsya | daivajñasampradiṣṭe kāle saṃsthāpanaṃ kuryāt || 15 ||
[ sunṛtyagītairjāgarakaiḥ ] abhyarcya kusumavastrānulepanaiḥ śaṅkhatūryanirghoṣaiḥ | prādakṣiṇyena nayedāyatanasya prayatnena || 16 ||
kṛtvā baliṃ prabhūtaṃ sampūjya brāhmaṇāṃśca sabhyāṃśca | dattvā hiraṇyaśakalaṃ vinikṣipetpiṇḍikāśvabhre || 17 ||
sthāpakadaivajñadvijasabhyasthapatīnviśeṣato'bhyarcya | kalyāṇānāṃ bhāgī bhavatīha paratra ca svargī || 18 ||
viṣṇorbhāgavatānmagāṃśca savituḥ śambhoḥ sabhasmadvijānmātṝṇāmapi maṇḍalakramavido viprānvidurbrahmaṇaḥ | śākyān sarvahitasya śāntamanaso nagnān jinānāṃ vidurye yaṃ devamupāśritāḥ svavidhinā taistasya kāryā kriyā || 19 ||
[ mātṛmaṇḍalavido ] udagayane sitapakṣe śiśiragabhastau ca jīvavargasthe | lagne sthire sthirāṃśe saumyairdhīdharmakendragataiḥ || 20 ||
pāpairupacayasaṃsthairdhruvamṛduharitiṣyavāyudeveṣu | vikuje dine'nukūle devānāṃ sthāpanaṃ śastam || 21 ||
sāmānyamidaṃ samāsato lokānāṃ hitadaṃ mayā kṛtam | adhivāsanasanniveśane sāvitre pṛthageva vistarāt || 22 ||

Chapter 60: golakṣaṇādhyāyaḥ [golakṣaṇa-adhyāya]

parāśaraḥ prāha bṛhadrathāya golakṣaṇaṃ yatkriyate tato'yam | mayā samāsaḥ śubhalakṣaṇāstāḥ sarvāstathāpyāgamato'bhidhāsye || 1 ||
sāsrāvilarūkṣākṣyo mūṣakanayanāś na śubhadā gāvaḥ | pracalaccipiṭaviṣāṇāḥ karaṭāḥ kharasadṛśavarṇāśca || 2 ||
[ varnāḥ ] daśasaptacaturdantyaḥ pralambamuṇḍānanā vinatapṛṣṭhyaḥ | hrasvasthūlagrīvā yavamadhyā dāritakhurāśca || 3 ||
[ pṛṣṭhāḥ | pṛṣṭhaḥ ] śyāvātidīrghajihvā gulphairatitanubhiratibṛhadbhirvā | atikakudāḥ kṛśadehā neṣṭā hīnādhikāṅgyaśca || 4 ||
vṛṣabho'pyevaṃ sthūlātilambavṛṣaṇaḥ śirātatakroḍaḥ | sthūlaśirācitagaṇḍastristhānaṃ mehate yaśca || 5 ||
mārjārākṣaḥ kapilaḥ karaṭo vā na śubhado dvijasyaiva | kṛṣṇauṣṭhatālujihvaḥ śvasano yūthasya ghātakaraḥ || 6 ||
[ dvijasyeṣṭaḥ ] sthūlaśakṛnmaṇiśṛṅgaḥ sitodaraḥ kṛṣṇasāravarṇaśca | gṛhajāto'pi tyājyo yūthavināśāvaho vṛṣabhaḥ || 7 ||
śyāmakapuṣpacitāṅgo bhasmāruṇasannibho biḍālākṣaḥ | viprāṇāmapi na śubhaṃ karoti vṛṣabhaḥ parigṛhītaḥ || 8 ||
ye coddharanti pādānpaṅkādiva yojitāḥ kṛśagrīvāḥ | kātaranayanā hīnāśca pṛṣṭhataste na bhārasahāḥ || 9 ||
mṛdusaṃhatatāmrauṣṭhāstanusphijastāmratālujihvāśca | hrasvatanūccaśravaṇāḥ sukukṣayaḥ spṛṣṭajaṅghāśca || 10 ||
[ tanuhrasvo | spaṣṭa ] ātāmrasaṃhatakhurā vyūḍhoraskā bṛhatkakudayuktāḥ | snigdhaślakṣṇatanutvagromāṇastāmratanuśṛṅgāḥ || 11 ||
tanubhūspṛgvāladhayo raktāntavilocanā mahocchvāsāḥ | siṃhaskandhāstanvalpakambalāḥ pūjitāḥ sugamāḥ || 12 ||
[ sugatāḥ ] vāmāvartairvāme dakṣiṇapārśve ca dakṣiṇāvartaiḥ | śubhadā bhavantyanaḍuho jaṅghābhiścaiṇakanibhābhiḥ || 13 ||
vaidūryamallikābudbudekṣaṇāḥ sthūlanetrapakṣmāṇaḥ | pārṣṇibhirasphuṭitābhiḥ śastāḥ sarve ca bhārasahāḥ || 14 ||
[ vaiḍūrya | varmāṇaḥ | api ] ghrāṇoddeśe savalirmārjāramukhaḥ sitaśca dakṣiṇataḥ | kamalotpalalākṣābhaḥ suvāladhirvājitulyajavaḥ || 15 ||
lambairvṛṣaṇairmeṣodaraśca saṃkṣiptavaṃkṣaṇakroḍaḥ | jñeyo bhārādhvasaho jave'śvatulyaśca śastaphalaḥ || 16 ||
[ kṣaṇā ] sitavarṇaḥ piṅgākṣastāmraviṣāṇekṣaṇo mahāvaktraḥ | haṃso nāma śubhaphalo yūthasya vivardhanaḥ proktaḥ || 17 ||
bhūspṛgvāladhirātāmraviṣāṇo raktadṛkkakudmāṃśca | kalmāṣaśca svāminamacirātkurute patiṃ lakṣmyāḥ || 18 ||
[ vaṅkṣaṇo | kakudmī ] yo vā sitaikacaraṇairyatheṣṭavarṇaśca so'pi śubhaphalakṛt | miśraphalo'pi grāhyo yadi naikāntapraśasto'sti || 19 ||
[ sitaikacaraṇo | śastaphalaḥ ]

Chapter 61: śvalakṣaṇādhyāyaḥ [śvalakṣaṇa-adhyāya]

pādāḥ pañcanakhāstrayo'gracaraṇaḥ ṣaḍbhirnakhairdakṣiṇastāmrauṣṭhāgranaso mṛgeśvaragatirjighranbhuvaṃ yāti ca | lāṅgūlaṃ sasaṭaṃ dṛgṛkṣasadṛśī karṇau ca lambau mṛdū yasya syātsa karoti poṣṭuracirātpuṣṭāṃ śriyaṃ śvā gṛhe || 1 ||
pāde pāde pañca pañcāgrapāde vāme yasyāḥ ṣaṇnakhā mallikākṣyāḥ | vakraṃ pucchaṃ piṅgalālambakarṇā yā sā rāṣṭraṃ kukkurī pāti puṣṭā || 2 ||
[ poṣṭuḥ ]

Chapter 62: kukkuṭalakṣaṇādhyāyaḥ [kukkuṭalakṣaṇa-adhyāya]

kukkuṭastv ṛjutanūruhāṅgulistāmravaktranakhacūlikaḥ sitaḥ | rauti susvaramuṣātyaye ca yo vṛddhidaḥ sa nṛparāṣṭravājinām || 1 ||
yavagrīvo yo vā badarasadṛśo vāpi vihago bṛhanmūrdhā varṇairbhavati bahubhiśca ruciraḥ | sa śastaḥ saṃgrāme madhumadhupavarṇaśca jayakṛdna śasto yo'to'nyaḥ kṛśatanuravaḥ khañjacaraṇaḥ || 2 ||
kukkuṭī ca mṛducārubhāṣiṇī snigdhamūrtirucirānaneṣaṇā | sā dadāti suciraṃ mahīkṣitāṃ śrīyaśovijayavīryasampadaḥ || 3 ||

Chapter 63: kūrmalakṣaṇādhyāyaḥ [kūrmalakṣaṇa-adhyāya]

sphuṭikarajatavarṇo nīlarājīvicitraḥ kalaśasadṛśamūrtiścāruvaṃśaśca kūrmaḥ | aruṇasamavapurvā sarṣapākāracitraḥ sakalanṛpamahattvaṃ mandirasthaḥ karoti || 1 ||
añjanabhṛṅgaśyāmatanurvā binduvicitro'vyaṅgaśarīraḥ | sarpaśirā vā sthūlagalo yaḥ so'pi nṛpāṇāṃ rāṣṭravivṛddhyai || 2 ||
vaiḍūryatviṭ sthūlakaṇṭhastrikoṇo gūḍhacchidraścoruvaṃśaśca śastaḥ | krīḍāvāpyāṃ toyapūrṇe maṇau vā kāryaḥ kūrmo maṅgalārthaṃ narendraiḥ || 3 ||
[ cāru ]

Chapter 64: chāgalakṣaṇādhyāyaḥ [chāgalakṣaṇa-adhyāya]

chāgaśubhāśubhalakṣaṇamabhidhāsye navadaśāṣṭadantāste | dhanyāḥ sthāpyā veśmani santyājyāḥ saptadantā ye || 1 ||
dakṣiṇapārśve maṇḍalamasitaṃ śuklasya śubhaphalaṃ bhavati | ṛṣyanibhakṛṣṇalohitavarṇānāṃ śvetamati śubhadam || 2 ||
[ api ] stanavadavalambate yaḥ kaṇṭhe'jānāṃ maṇiḥ sa vijñeyaḥ | ekamaṇiḥ śubhaphalakṛddhanyatamā dvitramaṇayo ye || 3 ||
[ dvitrimaṇayo ] muṇḍāḥ sarve śubhadāḥ sarvasitāḥ sarvakṛṣṇadehāśca | ardhāsitāḥ sitārdhā dhanyāḥ kapilārdhakṛṣṇāśca || 4 ||
vicarati yūthasyāgre prathamaṃ cāmbho'vagāhate yo'jaḥ | sa śubhaḥ sitamūrdhā vā mūrdhani vā kṛttikā yasya || 5 ||
[ ṭikkikā ] sapṛṣatakaṇṭhaśirā vā tilapiṣṭanibhaśca tāmradṛk śastaḥ | kṛṣṇacaraṇaḥ sito vā kṛṣṇo vā śvetacaraṇo yaḥ || 6 ||
yaḥ kṛṣṇāṇḍaḥ śveto madhye kṛṣṇena bhavati paṭṭena | yo vā carati saśabdaṃ mandaṃ ca sa śobhanaśchāgaḥ || 7 ||
ṛṣyaśiroruhapādo yo vā prākpāṇḍuro'pare nīlaḥ | sa bhavati śubhakṛcchāgaḥ ślokaścāpyatra gargoktaḥ || 8 ||
kuṭṭakaḥ kuṭilaścaiva jaṭilo vāmanastathā | te catvāraḥ śriyaḥ putrā nālakṣmīke vasanti te || 9 ||
athāpraśastāḥ kharatulyanādāḥ pradīptapucchāḥ kunakhā vivarṇāḥ | nikṛttakarṇā dvipamastakāśca bhavanti ye cāsitatālujihvāḥ || 10 ||
varṇaiḥ praśastairmaṇibhiḥ prayuktā muṇḍāśca ye tāmravilocanāśca | te pūjitā veśmani mānavānāṃ saukhyāni kurvanti yaśaḥ śriyaṃ ca || 11 ||
[ ca yuktā | veśmasu ]

Chapter 65: aśvalakṣaṇādhyāyaḥ [aśvalakṣaṇa-adhyāya]

dīrghagrīvākṣikūṭastrikahṛdayapṛthustāmratālvoṣṭhajihvaḥ sūkṣmatvakkeśavālaḥ suśaphagatimukho hrasvakarṇauṣṭhapucchaḥ | jaṅghājānūruvṛttaḥ samasitadaśanaścārusaṃsthānarūpo vājī sarvāṅgaśuddho bhavati narapateḥ śatrunāśāya nityam || 1 ||
aśrupātahanugaṇḍahṛdgalaprothaśaṅkhakaṭibastijānuni | muṣkanābhikakude tathā gude savyakukṣicaraṇe tathā śubhāḥ || 2 ||
[ hṛḍ | caraṇeṣu ca | aśubhāḥ ] ye prapāṇagalakarṇasaṃsthitāḥ pṛṣṭhamadhyanayanopari sthitāḥ | oṣṭhasakthibhujakukṣipārśvagāste lalāṭasahitāḥ suśobhanāḥ || 3 ||
teṣāṃ prapāṇa eko lalāṭakeśeṣu ca dhruvāvartāḥ | randhroparandhramūrdhani vakṣasi ceti smṛtau dvau dvau || 4 ||
ṣaṣbhirdantaiḥ sitābhairbhavati hayaśiśustaiḥ kaśāyairdvivarṣaiḥ sandaṃśairmadhyamāntyaiḥ pati samuditaistryabdhipañcābdikāśvaḥ | sandaṃśānukrameṇa trikaparigaṇitāḥ kālikā pītaśuklāḥ kācā makṣīkaśaṅkhāvaṭacalanamato dantapātaṃ ca viddhi || 5 ||
[ patita | tryabda | mākṣīka ]

Chapter 66: hastilakṣaṇādhyāyaḥ [hastilakṣaṇa-adhyāya]

madhvābhadantāḥ suvibhaktadehā na copadigdhā na kṛśāḥ kṣamāśca | gātraiḥ samaiścāpasamānavaṃśā varāhatulyairjaghanaiśca bhadrāḥ || 1 ||
[ digdhāśca ] vakṣo'tha kakṣāvalayaḥ ślathāśca lambodarastvagbṛhatī galaśca | sthūlā ca kukṣiḥ saha pecakena saiṃhī ca dṛgmandamataṅgajasya || 2 ||
mṛgāstu hrasvādharavālameḍhrāstanvaṅghrikaṇṭhadvijahastakarṇāḥ | sthūlekṣaṇāśceti yathoktacihnaiḥ saṅkīrṇanāgā vyatimiśracihnāḥ || 3 ||
[ tanvaṃhri ] pañconnatiḥ sapta mṛgasya dairghyamaṣṭau ca hastāḥ pariṇāhamānam | ekadvivṛddhāvatha mandabhadrau saṅkīrnanāgo'niyatapramāṇaḥ || 4 ||
bhadrasya varṇo harito madaśca mandasya hāridrakasannikāśaḥ | kṛṣṇo madaścābhihito mṛgasya saṅkīrṇanāgasya mado vimiśraḥ || 5 ||
[ madasya ] tāmrauṣṭhatāluvadanāḥ kalaviṅkanetrāḥ snigdhonnatāgradaśanāḥ pṛthulāyatāsyāḥ | cāponnatāyatanigūḍhanimagnavaṃśāstanvekaromacitakūrmasamānakumbhāḥ || 6 ||
vistīrṇakarṇahanunābhilalāṭaguhyāḥ kūrmonnatadvinavaviṃśatibhirnakhaiśca | rekhātrayopacitavṛttakarāḥ suvālā dhanyāḥ sugandhimadapuṣkaramārutāśca || 7 ||
dīrghāṅguliraktapuṣkarāḥ sajalāmbhodaninādabṛṃhiṇaḥ | bṛhadāyatavṛttakandharā dhanyā bhūmipatermataṅgajāḥ || 8 ||
nimardābhyadhikahīnanakhāṅgān kubjavāmanakameṣaviṣāṇān | dṛśyakośaphalapuṣkarahīnācchyāvanīlaśabalāsitatālūn || 9 ||
[ nirmadā ] svalpavaktraruhamatkuṇaṣaṇḍhān hastinīṃ ca gajalakṣaṇayuktām | garbhiṇī ca nṛpatiḥ paradeśaṃ prāpayedativirūpaphalāste || 10 ||

Chapter 67: puruṣalakṣanādhyāyaḥ [puruṣalakṣana-adhyāya]

unmānamānagatisaṃhatisāravarṇasnehasvaraprakṛtisattvamanūkaṃ ādau | kṣetraṃ mṛjāṃ ca vidhivatkuśalo'valokya sāmudravidvadati yātamanāgataṃ vā || 1 ||
[ ca ] asvedanau mṛdutalau kamalodarābhau śliṣṭāṅgulī ruciratāmranakhau supārṣṇī | uṣṇau śirāvirahitau sunigūḍhagulphau kūrmonnatau ca caraṇau manujeśvarasya || 2 ||
śūrpākāravirūkṣapāṇḍuranakhau vakrau śirāsantatau saṃśuṣkau viralāṅgulī ca caraṇau dāridryaduḥkhapradau | mārgāyotkaṭakau kaṣāyasadṛśau vaṃśasya vicchedadau brahmaghnau paripakvamṛddyutitalau pītāvagamyāratau || 3 ||
[ vicchittidau | agamyaratau ] praviralatanuromavṛttajaṅghā 67.04b dviradakarapratimairvarorubhiśca | upacitasamajānavaśca bhūpā | dhanarahitāḥ śvaśṛgālatulyajaṅghāḥ || 4 ||
romaikaikaṃ kūpake pārthivānāṃ dve dve jñeye paṇḍitaśrotriyāṇām | tryādyairniḥsvā mānavā duḥkhabhājaḥ keśāścaivaṃ ninditāḥ pūjitāśca || 5 ||
nirmāṃsajānurmriyate pravāse saubhāgyamalpairvikaṭairdaridrāḥ | strīnirjitāścaiva bhavanti nimnai rājyaṃ samāṃsaiśca mahadbhirāyuḥ || 6 ||
[ cāpi ] liṅge'lpe dhanavānapatyarahitaḥ sthūle'pi hīno dhanairmeḍhre vāmanate sutārtharahito vakre'nyathā putravān | dāridryaṃ vinate tvadho'lpatanayo liṅge śirāsantate sthūlagranthiyute sukhī mṛdu karotyantaṃ pramehādibhiḥ || 7 ||
[ vihīno ] kośanigūḍhairbhūpā dīrghairbhagnaiśca vittaparihīnāḥ | ṛjuvṛttaśephaso laghuśirālaśiśnāśca dhanavantaḥ || 8 ||
jalamṛtyurekavṛṣaṇo viṣamaiḥ strīcañcalaḥ samaiḥ kṣitipaḥ | hrasvāyuścodbaddhaiḥ pralambavṛṣaṇasya śatamāyuḥ || 9 ||
raktairāḍhyā maṇibhirnirdravyāḥ pāṇḍuraiśca malinaiśca | sukhinaḥ saśabdamūtrā niḥsvā niḥśabdadhārāśca || 10 ||
dvitricaturdhārābhiḥ pradakṣiṇāvartavalitamūtrābhiḥ | pṛthivīpatayo jñeyā vikīrṇamūtrāśca dhanahīnāḥ || 11 ||
ekaiva mūtradhārā valitā rūpapradā na sutadātrī | snigdhonnatasamamaṇayo dhanavanitāratnabhoktāraḥ || 12 ||
[ rūpapradhānasutadātrī ] maṇibhiśca madhyanimnaiḥ kanyāpitaro bhavanti niḥsvāśca | bahupaśubhājo madhyonnataiśca nātyulbaṇairdhaninaḥ || 13 ||
pariśuṣkabastiśīrṣairdhanarahitā durbhagāśca vijñeyāḥ | kusumasamagandhaśukrā vijñātavyā mahīpālāḥ || 14 ||
madhugandhe bahuvittā matsyasagandhe bahūnyapatyāni | tanuśukraḥ strījanako māṃsasagandho mahābhogī || 15 ||
madirāgandhe yajvā kṣārasagandhe ca retasi daridraḥ | śīghraṃ maithunagāmī dīrghāyurato'nyathālpāyuḥ || 16 ||
niḥsvo'tisthūlasphiksamāṃsalasphiksukhānvito bhavati | vyāghrānto'dhyardhasphigmaṇḍūkasphignarādhipatiḥ || 17 ||
siṃhakaṭirmanujendraḥ kapikarabhakaṭirdhanaiḥ parityaktaḥ | samajaṭharā bhogayutā ghaṭapiṭharanibhodarā niḥsvāḥ || 18 ||
avikalapārśvā dhanino nimnairvakraiśca bhogasantyaktāḥ | samakukṣā bhogāḍhyā nimnābhirbhogaparihīnāḥ || 19 ||
unnatakukṣāḥ kṣitipāḥ kuṭilāḥ syurmānavā viṣamakukṣāḥ | sarpodarā daridrā bhavanti bahvāśinaścaiva || 20 ||
parimaṇḍalonnatābhirvistīrṇābhiśca nābhibhiḥ sukhinaḥ | alpā tvadṛśyanimnā nābhiḥ kleśāvahā bhavati || 21 ||
[ svalpā ] valimadhyagatā viṣamā śūlādbādhāṃ karoti naisvyaṃ ca | śāṭhyaṃ vāmāvartā karoti medhāṃ pradakṣiṇataḥ || 22 ||
[ śūlābādhaṃ | naiḥsvyaṃ ] pārśvāyatā cirāyuṣamupariṣṭācceśvaraṃ gavāḍhyamadhaḥ | śatapatrakarṇikābhā nābhirmanujeśvaraṃ kurute || 23 ||
śastrāntaṃ strībhoginamācāryaṃ bahusutaṃ yathāsaṃkhyam | ekadvitricaturbhirvalibhirvindyādnṛpaṃ tvavalim || 24 ||
viṣamavalayo manuṣyā bhavantyagamyābhigāminaḥ pāpāḥ | ṛjuvalayaḥ sukhabhājaḥ paradāradveṣiṇaścaiva || 25 ||
māṃsalamṛdubhiḥ pārśvaiḥ pradakṣiṇāvartaromabhirbhūpāḥ | viparītairnirdravyāḥ sukhaparihīnāḥ parapreṣyāḥ || 26 ||
subhagā bhavantyanudvaddhacūcukā nirdhanā viṣamadīrghaiḥ | pīnopacitanimagnaiḥ kṣitipatayaścūcukaiḥ sukhinaḥ || 27 ||
[ anubaddha ] hṛdayaṃ samunnataṃ pṛthu na vepanaṃ māṃsalaṃ ca nṛpatīnām | adhanānāṃ viparītaṃ khararomacitaṃ śirālaṃ ca || 28 ||
samavakṣaso'rthavantaḥ pīnaiḥ śūrā hyakiñcanāstanubhiḥ | viṣamaṃ vakṣo yeṣāṃ te niḥsvāḥ śastranidhanāśca || 29 ||
[ śūrāstv ] viṣamairviṣamo jatrubhirarthavihīno'sthisandhipariṇaddhaiḥ | unnatajatrurbhogī nimnairniḥsvo'rthavānpīnaiḥ || 30 ||
[ bhāgī ] cipiṭagrīvo niḥsvaḥ śuṣkā saśirā ca yasya vā grīvā | mahiṣagrīvaḥ śūraḥ śastrānto vṛṣasamagrīvaḥ || 31 ||
kambugrīvo rājā pralambakaṇṭhaḥ prabhakṣaṇo bhavati | pṛṣṭhamabhagnamaromaśamarthavatāmaśubhadamato'nyat || 32 ||
asvedanapīnonnatasugandhasamaromasaṅkulāḥ kakṣāḥ | vijñātavyā dhanināmato'nyathārthairvihīnānām || 33 ||
[ sugandhi ] nirmāṃsau romacitau bhagnāvalpau ca nirdhanasyāṃsau | vipulāvavyucchinnau suśliṣṭau saukhyavīryavatām || 34 ||
karikarasadṛśau vṛttāvājānvavalambinau samau pīnau | bāhū pṛthivīśānāmadhanānāṃ romaśau hrasvau || 35 ||
[ adhamānāṃ ] hastāṅgulayo dīrghāścirāyuṣāmavalitāśca subhagānām | medhāvināṃ ca sūkṣmāścipiṭāḥ parakarmaniratānām || 36 ||
sthūlābhirdhanarahitā bahirnatābhiśca śastraniryāṇāḥ | kapisadṛśakarā dhanino vyāghropamapāṇayaḥ pāpāḥ || 37 ||
maṇibandhanairnigūḍhairdṛḍhaiśca suśliṣṭasandhibhirbhūpāḥ | hīnairhastacchedaḥ ślathaiḥ saśabdaiśca nirdravyāḥ || 38 ||
pitṛvittena vihīnā bhavanti nimnena karatalena narāḥ | saṃvṛtanimnairdhaninaḥ prottānakarāśca dātāraḥ || 39 ||
viṣamairviṣamā niḥsvāśca karatalairīśvarāś tu lākṣābhaiḥ | pītairagamyavanitābhigāmino nirdhanā rūkṣaiḥ || 40 ||
