[ īśvarās ] tuṣasadṛśanakhāḥ klībāścipiṭaiḥ sphuṭitaiśca vittasantyaktāḥ | kunakhavivarṇaiḥ paratarkukāśca tāmraiścamūpatayaḥ || 41 ||
aṅguṣṭhayavairāḍhyāḥ sutavanto'ṅguṣṭhamūlajaiśca yavaiḥ | dīrghāṅguliparvāṇaḥ subhagā dīrghāyuṣaścaiva || 42 ||
[ mūlagaiśca yavaḥ ] snigdhā nimnā rekhā dhanināṃ tadvyatyayena niḥsvānām | viralāṅgulayo niḥsvā dhanasañcayino ghanāṅgulayaḥ || 43 ||
tisro rekhā maṇibandhanotthitāḥ karatalopagā nṛpateḥ | mīnayugāṅkitapāṇirnityaṃ satraprado bhavati || 44 ||
vajrākārā dhanināṃ vidyābhājāṃ ca mīnapucchanibhāḥ | śaṅkhātapatraśivikāgajāśvapadmopamā nṛpateḥ || 45 ||
kalaśamṛṇālapatākāṅkuśopamābhirbhavanti nidhipālāḥ | dāmanibhābhiścāḍhyāḥ svastikarūpābhiraiśvaryam || 46 ||
cakrāsiparaśutomaraśaktidhanuḥ kuntasannibhā rekhāḥ | kurvanti camūnāthaṃ yajvānamulūkhalākārāḥ || 47 ||
makaradhvajakoṣṭhāgārasannibhābhirmahādhanopetāḥ | vedīnibhena caivāgnihotriṇo brahmatīrthena || 48 ||
vāpīdevakulādyairdharmaṃ kuruvanti ca trikoṇābhiḥ | aṅguṣṭhamūlarekhāḥ putrāḥ syurdārikāḥ sūkṣmāḥ || 49 ||
rekhāḥ pradeśinigatāḥ śatāyuṣaṃ kalpanīyamūnābhiḥ | chinnābhirdrumapatanaṃ bahurekhārekhiṇo niḥsvāḥ || 50 ||
[ gāḥ ] atikṛśadīrghaiścibukairnirdravyā māṃsalairdhanopetāḥ | vimbopamairavakrairadharairbhūpāstanubhirasvāḥ || 51 ||
[ bimba ] oṣṭhaiḥ sphuṭitavikhaṇḍitavivarṇarūkṣaiśca dhanaparityaktāḥ | snigdhā ghanāśca daśanāḥ sutīkṣṇadaṃṣṭrāḥ samāśca śubhāḥ || 52 ||
jihvā raktā dīrghā ślakṣṇā susamā ca bhogino jñeyā | śvetā kṛṣṇā paruṣā nirdravyāṇāṃ tathā tālu || 53 ||
[ bhogināṃ ] vaktraṃ saumyaṃ saṃvṛtamamalaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ samaṃ ca bhūpānām | viparītaṃ kleśabhujāṃ mahāmukhaṃ durbhagāṇāṃ ca || 54 ||
strīmukhamanapatyānāṃ śāṭhyavatāṃ maṇḍalaṃ parijñeyam | dīrghaṃ nirdravyāṇāṃ bhīrumukhāḥ pāpakarmāṇaḥ || 55 ||
caturasraṃ dhūrtānāṃ nimnaṃ vakraṃ ca tanayarahitānām | kṛpaṇānāmatihrasvaṃ sampūrṇaṃ bhogināṃ kāntam || 56 ||
[ caturaśraṃ | vaktraṃ ] asphuṭitāgraṃ snigdhaṃ śmaśru śubhaṃ mṛdu ca sannataṃ caiva | raktaiḥ paruṣaiścaurāḥ śmaśrubhiralpaiśca vijñeyāḥ || 57 ||
nirmāṃsaiḥ karṇaiḥ pāpamṛtyavaścarpaṭaiḥ subahubhogāḥ | kṛpaṇāśca hrasvakarṇāḥ śaṅkuśravaṇāścamūpatayaḥ || 58 ||
[ ca bhūpatayaḥ ] romaśakarṇā dīrghāyuṣaśca dhanabhāgino vipulakarṇāḥ | krūrāḥ śirāvanaddhairvyālambairmāṃsalaiḥ sukhinaḥ || 59 ||
[ tu ] bhogī tvanimnagaṇḍo mantrī sampūrṇamāṃsagaṇḍo yaḥ | sukhabhāk śukasamanāsaścirajīvī śuṣkanāsaśca || 60 ||
chinnānurūpayāgamyagāmino dīrghayā tu saubhāgyam | ākuñcitayā cauraḥ strīmṛtyuḥ syāccipiṭanāsaḥ || 61 ||
dhanino'gravakranāsā dakṣiṇavinatāḥ prabhakṣaṇāḥ krūrāḥ | ṛjvī svalpacchidrā supuṭā nāsā sabhāgyānām || 62 ||
[ vakrāḥ ] dhanināṃ kṣutaṃ sakṛddvitripiṇḍitaṃ hlādi sānunādaṃ ca | dīrghāyuṣāṃ pramuktaṃ vijñeyaṃ saṃhataṃ caiva || 63 ||
padmadalābhairdhanino raktāntavilocanāḥ śriyaḥ bhājaḥ | madhupiṅgalairmahārthā mārjāravilocanaiḥ pāpāḥ || 64 ||
[ vilocanāḥ ] hariṇākṣā maṇḍalalocanāśca jihmaiśca locanaiścaurāḥ | krūrāḥ kekaranetrā gajasadṛśavilocanāścamūpatayaḥ || 65 ||
[ dṛśaśca bhūpatayaḥ ] aiśvaryaṃ gambhīrairnīlotpalakāntibhiśca vidvāṃsaḥ | atikṛṣṇatārakāṇāmakṣṇāmutpāṭanaṃ bhavati || 66 ||
mantritvaṃ sthūladṛśāṃ śyāvākṣāṇāṃ bhavati saubhāgyam | dīnā dṛgniḥsvānāṃ snigdhā vipulārthabhogavatām || 67 ||
[ śyāvākṣāṇāṃ ca ] abhyunnatābhiralpāyuṣo viśālonnatābhiratisukhinaḥ | viṣamabhruvo daridrā bālendunatabhruvaḥ sadhanāḥ || 68 ||
dīrghāsaṃsaktābhirdhaninaḥ khaṇḍābhirarthaparihīnāḥ | madhyavinatabhruvo ye te saktāḥ strīṣvagamyāsu || 69 ||
unnatavipulaiḥ śaṅkhairdhanino nimnaiḥ sutārthasantyaktāḥ | viṣamalalāṭā vidhanā dhanavanto'rdhendusadṛśena || 70 ||
[ dhanyā ] śuktiviśālairācāryatā śirāsantatairadharmaratāḥ | unnataśirābhirāḍhyāḥ svastikavatsaṃsthitābhiśca || 71 ||
nimnalalāṭā vadhabandhabhāginaḥ krūrakarmaniratāśca | abhyunnataiścamūpāḥ kṛpaṇāḥ syuḥ saṃvṛtalalāṭāḥ || 72 ||
[ bhūpāḥ | saṅkaṭa ] ruditamadīnamanaśru snigdhaṃ ca śubhāvahaṃ manuṣyāṇām | rūkṣaṃ dīnaṃ pracurāśru caiva na śubhapradaṃ puṃsām || 73 ||
hasitaṃ śubhadamakampaṃ sanimīlitalocanaṃ tu pāpasya | duṣṭasya hasitamasakṛtsonmādasyāsakṛtprānte || 74 ||
[ hṛṣṭasya ] tisro rekhāḥ śatajīvināṃ lalāṭāyatāḥ sthitā yadi tāḥ | catasṛbhiravanīśatvaṃ navatiścāyuḥ sapañcābdā || 75 ||
vicchinnābhiścāgamyagāmino navatirapyarekheṇa | keśāntopagatābhī rekhābhiraśītivarṣāyuḥ || 76 ||
pañcabhirāyuḥ saptatirekāgrāvasthitābhirapi ṣaṣṭiḥ | bahurekheṇa śatārdhaṃ catvāriṃśacca vakrābhiḥ || 77 ||
bhrūlagnābhistriṃśadviṃśatikaścaiva vāmavakrābhiḥ | kṣudrābhiḥ svalpāyurnyūnābhiścāntare kalpyam || 78 ||
[ trimśabhrūlagnābhir ] parimaṇḍalairgavāḍhyāśchatrākāraiḥ śirobhiravanīśāḥ | cipiṭaiḥ pitṛmātṛghnāḥ karoṭiśirasāṃ cirānmṛtyuḥ || 79 ||
ghaṭamūrdhādhvānarucirdvimastakaḥ pāpakṛddhanaistyaktaḥ | nimnaṃ tu śiro mahatāṃ bahunimnamanarthadaṃ bhavati || 80 ||
ekaikabhavaiḥ snigdhaiḥ kṛṣṇairākuñcitairabhinnāgraiḥ | mṛdubhirna cātibahubhiḥ keśaiḥ sukhabhāgnarendro vā || 81 ||
bahumūlaviṣamakapilāḥ sthūlasphuṭitāgraparuṣahrasvāśca | atikuṭilāścātighanāśca mūrdhajā vittahīnānām || 82 ||
yad yadgātraṃ rūkṣaṃ māṃsavihīnaṃ śirāvanaddhaṃ ca | tattadaniṣṭaṃ proktaṃ viparītamataḥ śubhaṃ sarvam || 83 ||
triṣu vipulo gambhīrastriṣveva ṣaḍunnataścaturhrasvaḥ | saptasu rakto rājā pañcasu dīrghaśca sūkṣmaśca || 84 ||
nābhī svaraḥ sattvamiti praśastaṃ gambhīrametattritayaṃ narāṇām | uro lalāṭaṃ vadanaṃ ca puṃsāṃ vistīrṇametattritayaṃ praśastam || 85 ||
[ nābhiḥ | pradiṣṭaṃ ] vakṣo'tha kakṣā nakhanāsikāsyaṃ kṛkāṭikā ceti ṣaḍunnatāni | hrasvāni catvāri ca liṅgapṛṣṭhaṃ grīvā ca jaṅghe ca hitapradāni || 86 ||
netrāntapādakaratālvadharoṣṭhajihvā raktā nakhāśca khalu sapta sukhāvahāni | sūkṣmāṇi pañca daśanāṅguliparvakeśāḥ sākaṃ tvacā kararuhā na ca duḥkhitānām || 87 ||
[ kararuhāśca na ] hanulocanabāhunāsikāḥ stanayorantaramatra pañcamam | iti dīrghamidaṃ tu pañcakaṃ na bhavatyeva nṛṇāmabhūbhṛtām || 88 ||
chāyā śubhāśubhaphalāni nivedayantī lakṣyā manuṣyapaśupakṣiṣu lakṣaṇajñaiḥ | tejoguṇānbahirapi pravikāśayantī dīpaprabhā sphaṭikaratnaghaṭasthiteva || 89 ||
snigdhadvijatvagnakharomakeśāśchāyā sugandhā ca mahīsamutthā | tuṣṭyarthalābhābhyudayān karoti dharmasya cāhanyahani pravṛttim || 90 ||
[ keśa ] snigdhā sitācchaharitā nayanābhirāmā saubhāgyamārdavasukhābhyudayān karoti | sarvārthasiddhijananī jananīva cāpyā chāyā phalaṃ tanubhṛtāṃ śubhamādadhāti || 91 ||
caṇḍādhṛṣyā padmahemāgnivarṇā yuktā tejovikramaiḥ sapratāpaiḥ | āgneyīti prāṇināṃ syājjayāya kṣipraṃ siddhiṃ vāñchitārthasya datte || 92 ||
[ dhatte ] malinaparuṣakṛṣṇā pāpagandhānilotthā janayati vadhabandhavyādhyanarthārthanāśān | sphaṭikasadṛśarūpā bhāgyayuktātyudārā nidhiriva gaganotthā śreyasāṃ svacchavarṇā || 93 ||
chāyāḥ krameṇa kujalāgnyanilāmbarotthāḥ ke cidvadanti daśa tāśca yathānupūrvyā | sūryābjanābhapuruhūtayamoḍupānāṃ tulyāstu lakṣaṇaphalairiti tatsamāsaḥ || 94 ||
karivṛṣarathaughabherīmṛdaṅgasiṃhābhraniḥsvanā bhūpāḥ | gardabhajarjararūkṣasvarāśca dhanasaukhyasantyaktāḥ || 95 ||
[ abda ] sapta bhavanti ca sārā medomajjātvagasthiśukrāṇi | rudhiraṃ māṃsaṃ ceti prāṇabhṛtāṃ tatsamāsaphalam || 96 ||
tālvoṣṭhadantapālījihvānetrāntapāyukaracaraṇaiḥ | rakte tu raktasārā bahusukhavanitārthaputrayutāḥ || 97 ||
[ raktaiḥ ] snigdhatvakkā dhanino mṛdubhiḥ subhagā vicakṣaṇāstanubhiḥ | majjāmedaḥ sārāḥ suśarīrāḥ putravittayutāḥ || 98 ||
[ yuktāḥ ] sthūlāsthirasthisāro balavānvidyāntagaḥ surūpaśca | bahuguruśukrāḥ subhagā vidvāṃso rūpavantaśca || 99 ||
upacitadeho vidvāndhanī surūpaśca māṃsasāro yaḥ | saṅghātā iti ca suśliṣṭasandhitā sukhabhujo jñeyā || 100 ||
snehaḥ pañcasu lakṣyo vāgjihvādantanetranakhasaṃsthaḥ | sutadhanasaubhāgyayutāḥ snigdhaistairnirdhanā rūkṣaiḥ || 101 ||
dyutimānvarṇasnigdhaḥ kṣitipānāṃ madhyamaḥ sutārthavatām | rūkṣo dhanahīnānāṃ śuddhaḥ śubhado na saṅkīrṇaḥ || 102 ||
[ varṇaḥ snigdhaḥ ] sādhyamanūkaṃ vaktrādgovṛṣaśārdūlasiṃhagaruḍamukhāḥ | apratihatapratāpā jitaripavo mānavendrāśca || 103 ||
vānaramahiṣavarāhājatulyavadanāḥ śrutārthasukhabhājaḥ | gardabhakarabhapratimairmukhaiḥ śarīraiśca niḥsvasukhāḥ || 104 ||
[ suta ] aṣṭaśataṃ ṣaṇṇavatiḥ parimāṇaṃ caturaśītiriti puṃsām | uttamasamahīnānāmaṅgulasaṅkhyā svamānena || 105 ||
[ ṣaṇavatiḥ ] bhārārdhatanuḥ sukhabhāktulito'to duḥkhabhāgbhavatyūnaḥ | bhāro'tivāḍhyānāmadhyardhaḥ sarvadharaṇīśaḥ || 106 ||
viṃśativarṣā nārī puruṣaḥ khalu pañcaviṃśatibhirabdaiḥ | arhati mānonmānaṃ jīvitabhāge caturthe vā || 107 ||
bhūjalaśikhyanilāmbarasuranararakṣaḥ piśācakatiraścām | sattvena bhavati puruṣo lakṣaṇametadbhavati teṣām || 108 ||
[ eṣām ] mahīsvabhāvaḥ śubhapuṣpagandhaḥ sambhogavān suśvasanaḥ sthiraśca | toyasvabhāvo bahutoyapāyī priyābhibhāṣī rasabhājanaśca || 109 ||
[ abhilāṣī | bhojanaś ] agniprakṛtyā capalo'titīkṣṇaścaṇḍaḥ kṣudhālurbahubhojanaśca | vāyoḥ svabhāvena calaḥ kṛśaśca kṣipraṃ ca kopasya vaśaṃ prayāti || 110 ||
khaprakṛtirnipuṇo vivṛtāsyaḥ śabdagateḥ kuśalaḥ suśirāṅgaḥ | tyāgayutaḥ puruṣo mṛdukopaḥ sneharataśca bhavetsurasattvaḥ || 111 ||
[ tyāgayuto ] martyasattvasaṃyuto gītabhūṣaṇapriyaḥ | saṃvibhāgaśīlavānnityameva mānavaḥ || 112 ||
tīkṣṇaprakopaḥ khalaceṣṭitaśca pāpaśca sattvena niśācarāṇām | piśācasattvaścapalo malākto bahupralāpī ca samulbaṇāṅgaḥ || 113 ||
bhīruḥ kṣudhālurbahubhukca yaḥ syādjñeyaśca sattvena narastiraścām | evaṃ narāṇāṃ prakṛtiḥ pradiṣṭā yal lakṣaṇajñāḥ pravadanti sattvam || 114 ||
[ sa ] śārdūlahaṃsasamadadvipagopatīnāṃ tulyā bhavanti gatibhiḥ śikhināṃ ca bhūpāḥ | yeṣāṃ ca śabdarahitaṃ stimitaṃ ca yātaṃ te'pīśvarā drutapariplutagā daridrāḥ || 115 ||
śrāntasya yānamaśanaṃ ca bubhukṣitasya pānaṃ tṛṣāparigatasya bhayeṣu rakṣā | etāni yasya puruṣasya bhavanti kāle dhanyaṃ vadanti khalu taṃ naralakṣaṇajñāḥ || 116 ||

Chapter 68: pañcamanuṣyavibhāgādhyāyaḥ [pañcamanuṣyavibhāga-adhyāya]

puruṣalakṣaṇamuktamidaṃ mayā munimatānyavalokya samāsataḥ | idamadhītya naro nṛpasammato bhavati sarvajanasya ca vallabhaḥ || K(117) ||
tārāgrahairbalayutaiḥ svakṣetrasvoccagaiścatuṣṭayagaiḥ | pañca puruṣāḥ praśastā jāyante tānahaṃ vakṣye || 1 ||
jīvena bhavati haṃsaḥ saureṇa śaśaḥ kujena rucakaśca | bhadro budhena balinā mālavyo daityapūjyena || 2 ||
sattvamahīnaṃ sūryācchārīraṃ mānasaṃ ca candrabalāt | yad rāśibhedayuktāvetau tal lakṣaṇaḥ sa pumān || 3 ||
taddhātumahābhūtaprakṛtidyutivarṇasattvarūpādyaiḥ | abalaravīnduyutaistaiḥ saṅkīrṇā lakṣaṇaiḥ puruṣāḥ || 4 ||
bhaumātsattvaṃ gurutā budhātsurejyātsvaraḥ sitātsnehaḥ | varṇaḥ saurādeṣāṃ guṇadoṣaiḥ sādhvasādhutvam || 5 ||
saṅkīrṇāḥ syurna nṛpā daśāsu teṣāṃ bhavanti sukhabhājaḥ | ripugṛhanīcoccacyutasatpāpanirīkṣaṇairbhedāḥ || 6 ||
[ bhedaḥ ] ṣaṇṇavatiraṅgulānāṃ vyāyāmo dīrghatā ca haṃsasya | śaśarucakabhadramālavyasaṃjñitāstryaṅgulavivṛddhyā || 7 ||
yaḥ sāttvikastasya dayā sthiratvaṃ sattvārjavaṃ brāhmaṇadevabhaktiḥ | rajo'dhikaḥ kāvyakalākratustrīsaṃsaktacittaḥ puruṣo'tiśūraḥ || 8 ||
tamo'dhiko vañcayitā pareṣāṃ mūrkho'lasaḥ krodhaparo'tinidraḥ | miśrairguṇaiḥ sattvarajastamobhirmiśrāstu te sapta saha prabhedaiḥ || 9 ||
mālavyo nāganāsaḥ samabhujayugalo jānusamprāptahasto māṃsaiḥ pūrṇāṅgasandhiḥ samaruciratanurmadhyabhāge kṛśaśca | pañcāṣṭau cordhvamāsyaṃ śrutivivaramapi tryaṅgulonaṃ ca tiryagdīptākṣaṃ satkapolaṃ samasitadaśanaṃ nātimāṃsādharoṣṭham || 10 ||
[ nāganāsasamabhuja ] mālavān sa bharukacchasurāṣṭrān lāṭasindhuviṣayaprabhṛtīṃśca | vikramārjitadhano'vati rājā pāriyātranilayān kṛtabuddhiḥ || 11 ||
[ nilayaḥ ] saptativarṣo mālavyo'yaṃ tyakṣyati samyakprāṇāṃstīrthe | lakṣaṇametatsamyakproktaṃ śeṣanarāṇāṃ cāto vakṣye || 12 ||
upacitasamavṛttalambabāhurbhujayugalapramitaḥ samucchrayo'sya | mṛdutanughanaromanaddhagaṇḍo bhavati naraḥ khalu lakṣaṇena bhadraḥ || 13 ||
tvagśukrasāraḥ pṛthupīnavakṣāḥ sattvādhiko vyāghramukhaḥ sthiraśca | kṣamānvito dharmaparaḥ kṛtajño gajendragāmī bahuśāstravettā || 14 ||
prājño vapuṣmān sulalāṭaśaṅkhaḥ kalāsvabhijño dhṛtimān sukukṣiḥ | sarojagarbhadyutipāṇipādo yogī sunāsaḥ samasaṃhatabhrūḥ || 15 ||
navāmbusiktāvanipatrakuṅkumadvipendradānāgurutulyagandhatā | śiroruhāścaikajakṛṣṇakuñcitāsturaṅganāgopamaguhyagūḍhatā || 16 ||
[ gūḍhaguhyatā ] halamuśalagadāsiśaṅkhacakradvipamakarābjarathāṅkitāṅghrihastaḥ | vibhavamapi jano'sya bobhujīti kṣamati hi na svajanaṃ svatantrabuddhiḥ || 17 ||
[ anhri ] aṅgulāni navatiśca ṣaḍūnānyucchrayeṇa tulayāpi hi bhāraḥ | madhyadeśanṛpatiryadi puṣṭāś tryādayo'sya sakalāvanināthaḥ || 18 ||
bhuktvā samyagvasudhāṃ śauryeṇopārjitāmaśītyabdaḥ | tīrthe prāṇāṃstyaktvā bhadro devālayaṃ yāti || 19 ||
īṣaddanturakastanudvijanakhaḥ kośekṣaṇaḥ śīghrago vidyādhātuvaṇikkriyāsu nirataḥ sampūrṇagaṇḍaḥ śaṭhaḥ | senānīḥ priyamaithunaḥ parajanastrīsaktacittaścalaḥ śūro mātṛhito vanācalanadīdurgeṣu saktaḥ śaśaḥ || 20 ||
dīrgho'ṅgulānāṃ śatamaṣṭahīnaṃ sāśaṅkaceṣṭaḥ pararandhravicca | sāro'sya majjā nibhṛtapracāraḥ śaśo hyato nātiguruḥ pradiṣṭaḥ || 21 ||
[ ayaṃ ] madhye kṛśaḥ kheṭakakhaḍgavīṇā paryaṅkamālāmurajānurūpāḥ | śūlopamāścordhvagatāśca rekhāḥ śaśasya pādopagatāḥ kare vā || 22 ||
prātyantiko māṇḍaliko'tha vāyaṃ sphiksrāvaśūlābhibhavārtamūrtiḥ | evaṃ śaśaḥ saptatihāyano'yaṃ vaivasvatasyālayamabhyupaiti || 23 ||
raktaṃ pīnakapolamunnatanasaṃ vaktraṃ suvarṇopamaṃ vṛttaṃ cāsya śiro'kṣiṇī madhunibhe sarve ca raktā nakhāḥ | sragdāmāṅkuśaśaṅkhamatsyayugalakratvaṅgakumbhāmbujaiścihnairhaṃsakalasvanaḥ sucaraṇo haṃsaḥ prasannendriyaḥ || 24 ||
ratirambhasi śukrasāratā dviguṇā cāṣṭaśataiḥ palairmitiḥ | parimāṇamathāsya ṣaḍyutā navatiḥ samparikīrtitā budhaiḥ || 25 ||
bhunakti haṃsaḥ khasaśūrasenān gāndhāragaṅgāyāmunāntarālam | śataṃ daśonaṃ śaradāṃ nṛpatvaṃ kṛtvā vanānte samupaiti mṛtyum || 26 ||
subhrūkeśo raktaśyāmaḥ kambugrīvo vyādīrghāsyaḥ | śūraḥ krūraḥ śreṣṭho mantrī caurasvāmī vyāyāmī ca || 27 ||
yanmātramāsyaṃ rucakasya dīrghaṃ madhyapradeśe caturasratā sā | tanucchaviḥ śoṇitamāṃsasāro hantā dviṣāṃ sāhasasiddhakāryaḥ || 28 ||
[ caturaśratā ] khaṭvāṅgavīṇāvṛṣacāpavajraśaktīndraśūlāṅkitapāṇipādaḥ | bhakto gurubrāhmaṇadevatānāṃ śatāṅgulaḥ syāttu sahasramānaḥ || 29 ||
[ tulayā sahasram ] mantrābhicārakuśalaḥ kṛśajānujaṅgho vindhyaṃ sasahyagirimujjayinīṃ ca bhuktvā | samprāpya saptatisamā rucako narendraḥ śastreṇa mṛtyumupayātyatha vānalena || 30 ||
pañcāpare vāmanako jaghanyaḥ kubjo'tha vā maṇḍalako'tha sācī | pūrvoktabhūpānucarā bhavanti saṅkīrṇasaṃjñaḥ śṛṇu lakṣaṇaistān || 31 ||
[ samī | saṃjñāḥ ] sampūrṇāṅgo vāmano bhagnapṛṣṭhaḥ kiñciccorūmadhyakakṣyāntareṣu | khyāto rājñāṃ hyeṣa bhadrānujīvī sphīṭo rājā vāsudevasya bhaktaḥ || 32 ||
[ kakṣa | dātā ] mālavyasevī tu jaghanyanāmā khaṇḍendutulyaśravaṇaḥ susandhiḥ | śukreṇa sāraḥ piśunaḥ kaviśca rūkṣacchaviḥ sthūlakarāṅgulīkaḥ || 33 ||
krūro dhanī sthūlamatiḥ pratītas | tāmracchaviḥ syātparihāsaśīlaḥ | uro'ṅghrihasteṣvasiśaktipāśaparaśvadhāṅkaḥ sa jaghanyanāmā || 34 ||
[ anhri | aṅkaśca ] kubjo nāmnā yaḥ sa śuddho hyadhastātkṣīṇaḥ kiñcitpūrvakāye nataśca | haṃsāsevī nāstiko'rthairupeto | vidvācchūraḥ sūcakaḥ syātkṛtajñaḥ || 35 ||
kalāsvabhijñaḥ kalahapriyaśca prabhūtabhṛtyaḥ pramadājitaśca | sampūjya lokaṃ prajahātyakasmātkubjo'yamuktaḥ satatodyataśca || 36 ||
maṇḍalakakṣaṇamato rucakānucaro'bhicāravitkuśalaḥ | kṛtyāvetālādiṣu karmasu vidyāsu cānurataḥ || 37 ||
[ maṇḍalakanāmadheyo | maṇḍalakalakṣaṇamato | vaitāla ] vṛddhākāraḥ kharaparuṣamūrdhajaśca śatrunāśane kuśalaḥ | dvijadevayajñayogaprasaktadhīḥ strījito matimān || 38 ||
[ rūkṣamūrdhajaś ] sācīti yaḥ so'tivirūpadehaḥ śaśānugāmī khalu durbhagaśca | dātā mahārambhasamāptakāryo guṇaiḥ śaśasyaiva bhavetsamānaḥ || 39 ||
[ sāmīti ] apuruṣalakṣaṇamuktamidaṃ mayā bmunimatāni nirīkṣya samāsataḥ | cidamadhītya naro nṛpasammato dbhavati sarvajanasya ca vallabhaḥ || 40 ||

Chapter 69: kanyālakṣaṇādhyāyaḥ [kanyālakṣaṇa-adhyāya]

snigdhonnatāgratanutāmranakhau kumāryāḥ pādau samopacitacārunigūḍhagulphau | śliṣṭāṅgulī kamalakāntitalau ca yasyāstāmudvahed yadi bhuvo'dhipatitvamicchet || 1 ||
matsyāṅkuśābjayavavajrahalāsicihnāvasvedanau mṛdutalau caraṇau praśastau | jaṅghe ca romarahite viśire suvṛtte jānudvayaṃ samamanulbaṇasandhideśam || 2 ||
ūrū ghanau karikarapratimāvaromāvaśvatthapatrasadṛśaṃ vipulaṃ ca guhyam | śroṇīlalāṭamurukūrmasamunnataṃ ca gūḍho maṇiśca vipulāṃ śriyamādadhāti || 3 ||
vistīrṇamāṃsopacito nitambaḥ guruśca dhatte raśanākalāpam | nābhirgabhīrā vipulāṅgānāṃ pradakṣiṇāvartagatā ca śastā || 4 ||
[ rasanā | gambhīrā | praśastā ] madhyaṃ striyāstrivalināthamaromaśaṃ ca vṛttau ghanāvaviṣamau kaṭhināv urasyau | romapravarjitamuro mṛdu cāṅganānāṃ grīvā ca kambunicitārthasukhāni datte || 5 ||
[ apavarjitam | dhatte ] bandhujīvakusumopamo'dharo māṃsalo rucirabimbarūpabhṛt | kundakuḍmalanibhāḥ samā dvijā yoṣitāṃ patisukhāmitārthadāḥ || 6 ||
dākṣiṇyayuktamaśaṭhaṃ parapuṣṭahaṃsavalgu prabhāṣitamadīnamanalpasaukhyam | nāsā samā samapuṭā rucirā praśastā dṛgnīlanīrajadaladyutihāriṇī ca || 7 ||
no saṅgate nātipṛthū na lambe śaste bhruvau bālaśaśāṅkavakre | ardhendusaṃsthānamaromaśaṃ ca śastaṃ lalāṭaṃ na nataṃ na tuṅgam || 8 ||
karṇayugmamapi yuktamāṃsalaṃ śasyate mrdu samāhitaṃ samam | snigdhanīlamṛdukuñcitaikajā mūrdhajāḥ sukhakarāḥ samaṃ śiraḥ || 9 ||
[ samaṃ samāhitam ] bhṛṅgārāsanavājikuñjararathaśrīvṛkṣayūpeṣubhirmālākuṇḍalacāmarāṅkuśayavaiḥ śailairdhvajaistoraṇaiḥ | matsyasvastikavedikāvyajanakaiḥ śaṅkhātapatrāmbujaiḥ pāde pāṇitale'tha vā yuvatayo gacchanti rājñīpadam || 10 ||
[ api vā ] nigūḍhamaṇibandhanau taruṇapadmagarbhopamau karau nṛpatiyoṣitastanuvikṛṣṭaparvāṅgulī | na nimnamati nonnataṃ karatalaṃ surekhānvitaṃ karotyavidhavāṃ ciraṃ sutasukhārthasambhoginīm || 11 ||
[ yoṣitāṃ ] madhyāṅguliṃ yā maṇibandhanotthā rekhā gatā pāṇitale'ṅganāyāḥ | ūrdhvasthitā pādatale'tha vā yā puṃso'tha vā rājyasukhāya sā syāt || 12 ||
kaniṣṭhikāmūlabhavā gatā yā pradeśinīmadhyamikāntarālam | karoti rekhā paramāyuṣaḥ sā pramāṇamūnā tu tadūnamāyuḥ || 13 ||
aṅguṣṭamūle prasavasya rekhāḥ putrā bṛhatyaḥ pramadāstu tanvyaḥ | acchinnamadhyā bṛhadāyuṣastāḥ svalpāyuṣāṃ chinnalaghupramāṇāḥ || 14 ||
[ dīrghā | bṛhadāyuṣāṃ ] itīdamuktaṃ śubhamaṅganānāmato viparyastamaniṣṭamuktam | viśeṣato'niṣṭaphalāni yāni samāsatastānyanukīrtayāmi || 15 ||
kaniṣṭhikā vā tadanantarā vā mahīṃ na yasyāḥ śpṛśati striyāḥ syāt | gatātha vāṅguṣṭhamatītya yasyāḥ pradeśinī sā kulaṭātipāpā || 16 ||
udbaddhābhyām piṇḍikābhyāṃ śirāle śuṣke jaṅghe lomaśe cātimāṃse | vāmāvartaṃ nimnamalpaṃ ca guhyaṃ kumbhākāraṃ codaraṃ duḥkhitānām || 17 ||
[ romaśe ] hrasvayātiniḥsvatā dīrghayā kulakṣayaḥ | grīvayā pṛthūtthayā yoṣitaḥ pracaṇḍatā || 18 ||
netre yasyāḥ kekare piṅgale vā sā duḥśīlā śyāvalolekṣaṇā ca | kūpau yasyā gaṇḍayośca smiteṣu niḥsandigdhaṃ bandhakīṃ tāṃ vadanti || 19 ||
pravilambini devaraṃ lalāṭe śvaśuraṃ hantyudare sphijoḥ patiṃ ca | atiromacayānvitottarauṣṭhī na śubhā bharturatīva yā ca dīrghā || 20 ||
stanau saromau malinolbaṇau ca kleśaṃ dadhāte viṣamau ca karṇau | sthūlāḥ karālā viṣamāśca dantāḥ kleśāya cauryāya ca kṛṣṇamāṃsāḥ || 21 ||
kravyādarūpairvṛkakākakaṅkasarīsṛpolūkasamānacihnaiḥ | śuṣkaiḥ śirālairviṣamaiśca hastairbhavanti nāryaḥ sukhavittahīnāḥ || 22 ||
yā tūttaroṣṭhena samunnatena rūkṣāgrakeśī kalahapriyā sā | prāyo virūpāsu bhavanti doṣā yatrākṛtistatra guṇā vasanti || 23 ||
pādau sagulphau prathamaṃ pradiṣṭau jaṅghe dvitīyaṃ tu sajānucakre | meḍhrorumuṣkaṃ ca tatastṛtīyaṃ nābhiḥ kaṭiścaiva caturthamāhuḥ || 24 ||
[ ca iti ] udaraṃ kathayanti pañcamaṃ hṛdayaṃ ṣaṣṭhamatasstanānvitam | atha saptamamaṃsajatruṇī kathayantyaṣṭamamoṣṭhakandhare || 25 ||
navamaṃ nayane ca sabhruṇī salalāṭaṃ daśamaṃ śirastathā | aśubheṣvaśubhaṃ daśāphalaṃ caraṇādyeṣu śubheṣu śobhanam || 26 ||

Chapter 70: vastracchedalakṣaṇādhyāyaḥ [vastracchedalakṣaṇa-adhyāya]

prabhūtavastradāśvinī bharaṇyathāpahāriṇī | pradahyate'gnidaivate prajesvare'rthasiddhayaḥ || 1 ||
mṛge tu mūṣakādbhayaṃ vyasutvameva śāṅkare | punarvasau śubhāgamastadagrabhe dhanairyutiḥ || 2 ||
bhujaṅgabhe vilupyate maghāsu mṛtyumādiśet | bhagāhvaye nṛpādbhayaṃ dhanāgamāya cottarā || 3 ||
kareṇa karmasiddhayaḥ śubhāgamastu citrayā | śubhaṃ ca bhojyamānile dvidaivate janapriyaḥ || 4 ||
suhūdyutiśca mitrabhe tadagrabhe ambarakṣayaḥ | jalaplutiśca nairṛte rujo jalādhidaivate || 5 ||
[ suhṛdyutiś | purandare ] miṣṭamannamapi vaiśvadaivate vaiṣṇave bhavati netrarogatā | dhānyalabdhirapi vāsave vidurvāruṇe viṣakṛtaṃ mahadbhayam || 6 ||
[ labdhim | atha | viśvadaivate ] bhadrapadāsu bhayaṃ salilotthaṃ tatparataśca bhavetsutalabdhiḥ | ratnayutiṃ kathayanti ca pauṣṇe yo'bhinavāmbaramicchati bhoktum || 7 ||
bhoktuṃ navāmbaraṃ śastamṛkṣe'pi guṇavarjite | vivāhe rājasammāne brahmaṇāṇāṃ ca sammate || 8 ||
vastrasya koṇeṣu vasanti devā narāśca pāśāntadaśāntamadhye | śeṣāstrayaścātra niśācarāṃśāstathaiva śayyāsanapādukāsu || 9 ||
lipte maṣīgomayakardamādyaiśchinne pradagdhe sphuṭite ca vindyāt | puṣṭaṃ nave'lpālpataraṃ ca bhukte pāpaṃ śubhaṃ cādhikamuttarīye || 10 ||
rugrākṣasāṃśesvatha vāpi mṛtyuḥ puñjanmatejaśca manuṣyabhāge | bhāge'marāṇāmatha bhogavṛddhiḥ prānteṣu sarvatra vadantyaniṣṭam || 11 ||
kaṅkaplavolūkakapotakākakravyādagomāyukharoṣṭrasarpaiḥ | chedākṛtirdaivatabhāgagāpi puṃsāṃ bhayaṃ mṛtyusamaṃ karoti || 12 ||
chatradhvajasvastikavardhamānaśrīvṛkṣakumbhāmbujatoraṇādyaiḥ | chedākṛtirnairṛtabhāgagāpi puṃsāṃ vidhatte na cireṇa lakṣmīm || 13 ||

Chapter 71: cāmaralakṣaṇādhyāyaḥ [cāmaralakṣaṇa-adhyāya]

vipramatādatha bhūpatidattaṃ yacca vivāhavidhāvabhilabdham | teṣu guṇai rahiteṣvapi bhoktuṃ nūtanamambaramiṣṭaphalaṃ syāt || K(13) ||
devaiścamaryaḥ kila vālahetoḥ sṛṣṭā himakṣmādharakandareṣu | āpītavarṇāśca bhavanti tāsāṃ kṛṣṇāśca lāṅgūlabhavāḥ sitāśca || 1 ||
sneho mṛdutvaṃ bahuvālatā vaiśadyamalpāsthinibandhanatvam | śauklyaṃ ca tāsāṃ guṇasampaduktā viddhālpaluptāni na śobhanāni || 2 ||
[ vālatā ca | teṣāṃ ] adhyardhahastapramito'sya daṇḍo hasto'tha vāratnisamo'tha vānyaḥ | kāṣṭhācchubhātkāñcanarūpyaguptād ratnaiśca sarvaiśca hitāya rājñām || 3 ||
[ vicitraiś ] yaṣṭyātapatrāṅkuśavetracāpavitānakuntadhvajacāmarāṇām | vyāpītatantrīmadhukṛṣṇavarṇā varṇakrameṇaiva hitāya daṇḍāḥ || 4 ||
mātṛbhūdhanakulakṣayāvahā rogamṛtyujananāśca parvabhiḥ | dvyādibhirdvikavivardhitaiḥ kramātdvādaśāntavirataiḥ samaiḥ phalam || 5 ||
yātrāprasiddhirdviṣatāṃ vināśo lābhāḥ prabhūtā vasudhāgamaśca | vṛddhiḥ paśūnāmabhivañchitāptistryādyeṣvayugmeṣu tadīśvarāṇām || 6 ||
[ prabhūto ]

Chapter 72: chatralakṣaṇādhyāyaḥ [chatralakṣaṇa-adhyāya]

nicitaṃ tu haṃsapakṣaiḥ kṛkavākumayūrasārasānāṃ vā | daukūlyena navena tu samantataśchāditaṃ śuklam || 1 ||
[ nu | daukūlena ] muktāphalairupacitaṃ pralambamālāvilaṃ sphaṭikamūlam | ṣaḍḍhastaśuddhahaimaṃ navaparvanagaikadaṇḍaṃ tu || 2 ||
daṇḍārdhavistṛtaṃ tatsamāvṛtaṃ ratnabhūṣitamudagram | nṛpatestadātapatraṃ kalyāṇaparaṃ vijayadaṃ ca || 3 ||
[ ratnavibhūṣitam | ratnabhūṣitam ] yuvarājanṛpatipatnyoḥ senāpatidaṇḍanāyakānāṃ ca | daṇḍo'rdhapañcahastaḥ samapañcakṛto'rdha vistāraḥ || 4 ||
[ kṛtārdha ] anyeṣāmuṣṇaghnaṃ prasādapaṭṭairvibhūṣitaśiraskam | vyālambiratnamālaṃ chatraṃ kāryaṃ tu māyūram || 5 ||
[ ca ] anyeṣāṃ tu narāṇāṃ śītātapavāraṇaṃ tu caturasram | samavṛttadaṇḍayuktaṃ chatraṃ kāryaṃ tu viprāṇām || 6 ||
[ caturaśram ]

Chapter 73: strīpraśamsādhyāyaḥ [strīpraśamsa-adhyāya]

jaye dharitryāḥ purameva sāraṃ pure gṛhaṃ sadmani caikadeśaḥ | tatrāpi śayyā śayane varā strī ratnojjvalā rājyasukhasya sāraḥ || 1 ||
ratnāni vibhūṣayanti yoṣā bhūṣyante vanitā na ratnakāntyā | ceto vinatā harantyaratnā no ratnāni vināṅganāṅgasaṅgam || 2 ||
[ saṅgāt ] ākāraṃ vinigūhatāṃ ripubalaṃ jetuṃ samuttiṣṭhatāṃ tantraṃ cintayatāṃ kṛtākṛtaśatavyāpāraśākhākulam | mantriproktaniṣeviṇāṃ kṣitibhujāmāśaṅkināṃ sarvato dhuḥkhāmbhonidhivartināṃ sukhalavaḥ kāntāsamāliṅganam || 3 ||
[ niseviṇām | niṣevinām ] śrutaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ spṛṣṭaṃ smṛtamapi nṛṇāṃ hlādajananaṃ na ratnaṃ strībhyo'nyatkva cidapi kṛtaṃ lokapatinā | tadarthaṃ dharmārthau sutaviṣayasaukhyāni ca tato gṛhe lakṣmyo mānyāḥ satatamabalā mānavibhavaiḥ || 4 ||
ye'pyaṅganānāṃ pravadanti doṣānvairāgyamārgeṇa guṇānvihāya | te durjanā me manaso vitarkaḥ sadbhāvavākyāni na tāni teṣām || 5 ||
prabrūta satyaṃ karato'ṅganānāṃ doṣo'sti yo nācarito manuṣyaiḥ | dhārṣṭyena pumbhiḥ pramadā nirastā guṇādhikāstā manunātra coktam || 6 ||
somastāsāmadācchaucaṃ gandharvaḥ śikṣitāṃ giram | agniśca sarvabhakṣitvaṃ tasmānniṣkasamāḥ striyaḥ || 7 ||
[ gandharvāḥ ] brāhmaṇāḥ pādato medhyā gāvo medhyāśca pṛṣṭhataḥ | ajāśvā mukhato medhyāḥ striyo medhyāstu sarvataḥ || 8 ||
striyaḥ pavitramatulaṃ naitā duṣyanti karhi cit | māsi māsi rajo hyāsāṃ duṣkṛtānyapakarṣati || 9 ||
jāmayo yāni gehāni śapantyapratipūjitāḥ | tāni kṛtyāhatānīva vinaśyanti samantataḥ || 10 ||
jāyā vā syājjanitrī vā sambhavaḥ strīkṛto nṛṇām | he kṛtaghnāś tayornindāṃ kurvatāṃ vaḥ kutaḥ śubham || 11 ||
dampatyorvyutkrame doṣaḥ samaḥ śāstre pratiṣṭhitaḥ | narā na samavekṣante tenātra varamaṅganāḥ || 12 ||
bahirlomnā tu ṣaṇmāsānveṣṭitaḥ kharacarmaṇā | dārātikramaṇe bhikṣāṃ dehītyuktvā viśudhyati || 13 ||
na śatenāpi varṣāṇāmapaiti madanāśayaḥ | tatra aśaktyā nirvartante narā dhairyeṇa yoṣitaḥ || 14 ||
aho dhārṣṭyamasādhūnāṃ nindatāmanaghāḥ striyaḥ | muṣṇatāmiva caurāṇāṃ tiṣṭha caureti jalpatām || 15 ||
puruṣaścaṭulāni kāminīnāṃ kurute yāni raho na tāni paścāt | sukṛtajñatayāṅganā gatāsūnavagūhya praviśanti saptajihvam || 16 ||
[ cātulāni | caṭulāni ] strīratnabhogo'sti narasya yasya niḥsvo'pi sāmpratyavanīsvaro asau | rājyasya sāro'śanamaṅganāśca tṛṣṇānaloddīpanadāru śeṣam || 17 ||
[ svaṃ pratyavanīsvaro | māṃ pratyava ] kāminīṃ prathamayauvanānvitāṃ mandavalgumṛdupīḍitasvanām | utstanīṃ samavalambya yā ratiḥ sā na dhātṛbhavane'sti me matiḥ || 18 ||
tatra devamunisiddhacāraṇairmānyamānapitṛsevyasevanāt | brūta dhātṛbhavane'sti kiṃ sukhaṃ yad rahaḥ samavalambya na striyam || 19 ||
ābrahmakīṭāntamidaṃ nibaddhaṃ puṃstrīprayogeṇa jagatsamastam | vrīḍātra kā yatra caturmukhatvamīśo'pi lobhādgamito yuvatyāḥ || 20 ||

Chapter 74: saubhāgyakaraṇādhyāyaḥ [saubhāgyakaraṇa-adhyāya]

jātyaṃ manobhavasukhaṃ subhagasya sarvamābhāsamātramitarasya manoviyogāt | cittena bhāvayati dūragatāpi yaṃ strī garbhaṃ bibharti sadṛśaṃ puruṣasya tasya || 1 ||
bhaṅktvā kāṇḍaṃ pādapasyoptamurvyāṃ bījaṃ vāsyāṃ nānyatāmeti yadvat | evaṃ hyātmā jāyate strīṣu bhūyaḥ kaścittasmin kṣetrayogādviśeṣaḥ || 2 ||
ātmā sahaiti manasā mana indriyeṇa svārthena cendriyamiti krama eṣa śīghraḥ | yogo'yameva manasaḥ kimagamyamasti yasminmano vrajati tatra gato'yamātmā || 3 ||
ātmāyamātmani gato hṛdaye'tisūkṣmo grāhyo'calena manasā satatābhiyogāt | yo yaṃ vicintayati yāti sa tanmayatvaṃ yasmādataḥ subhagameva gatā yuvatyaḥ || 4 ||
dākṣiṇyamekaṃ subhagatvaheturvidveṣaṇaṃ tadviparītaceṣṭā | mantrauṣadhādyaiḥ kuhakaprayogairbhavanti doṣā bahavo na śarma || 5 ||
vāllabhyamāyāti vihāya mānaṃ daurbhāgyamāpādayate'bhimānaḥ | kṛcchreṇa saṃsādhayate'bhimānī kāryāṇyayatnena vadanpriyāṇi || 6 ||
tejo na tad yatpriyasāhasatvaṃ vākyaṃ na cāniṣṭamasatpraṇītam | kāryasya gatvāntamanuddhatā ye tejasvinaste na vikatthanā ye || 7 ||
yaḥ sārvajanyaṃ subhagatvamicchedguṇān sa sarvasya vadetparokṣam | prāpnoti doṣānasato'pyanekānparasya yo doṣakathāṃ karoti || 8 ||
[ parokṣe ] sarvopakārānugatasya lokaḥ sarvopakārānugato narasya | kṛtvopakāraṃ dviṣatāṃ vipatsu yā kīrtiralpena na sā śubhena || 9 ||
tṛṇairivāgniḥ sutarāṃ vivṛddhimāchādyamāno'pi guṇo'bhyupaiti | sa kevalaṃ durjanabhāvameti hantuṃ guṇānvāñchati yaḥ parasya || 10 ||

Chapter 75: kāndarpikādhyāyaḥ [kāndarpika-adhyāya]

rakte'dhike strī puruṣastu śukre napuṃsakaṃ śoṇitaśukrasāmye | yasmādataḥ śukravivṛddhidāni niṣevitavyāni rasāyanāni || 1 ||
harmyapṛṣṭhamuḍunātharaśmayaḥ sotpalaṃ madhu madālasā priyā | vallakī smarakathā rahaḥ srajo varga eṣa madanasya vāgurā || 2 ||
mākṣīkadhātumadhupāradalohacūrṇapathyāśilājatughṛtāni samāni yo'dyāt | saikāni viṃśatirahāni jarānvito'pi so'śītiko'pi ramayatyabalāṃ yuveva || 3 ||
[ viḍaṅgaghṛtāni ] kṣīraṃ śṛtaṃ yaḥ kapikacchumūlaiḥ pibetkṣayaṃ strīṣu na so'bhyupaiti | māṣānpayaḥsarpiṣi vā vipakvān ṣaḍgrāsamātrāṃśca payo'nupānam || 4 ||
[ anupānān ] vidārikāyāḥ svarasena cūrṇaṃ muhurmuhurbhāvitaśoṣitaṃ ca | śṛtena dugdhena saśarkareṇa pibetsa yasya pramadāḥ prabhūtāḥ || 5 ||
dhātrīphalānāṃ svarasena cūrṇaṃ subhāvitaṃ kṣaudrasitājyayuktam | līḍhvānu pītvā ca payo'gniśaktyā kāmaṃ nikāmaṃ puruṣo niṣevet || 6 ||
kṣīreṇa bastāṇḍa yujā śṛtena samplāvya kāmī bahuśastilānyaḥ | suśoṣitānatti payaḥ pibecca tasyāgrataḥ kiṃ caṭakaḥ karoti || 7 ||
[ pibetpayaś ] māṣasūpasahitena sarpiṣā ṣaṣṭikaudanamadanti ye narāḥ | kṣīramapyanu pibanti tāsu te śarvarīṣu madanena śerate || 8 ||
[ madane na ] tilāśvagandhākapikacchumūlairvidārikāṣaṣṭikapiṣṭayogaḥ | ājena piṣṭaḥ payasā ghṛtena pakvaṃ bhavecchaṣkulikātivṛṣyā || 9 ||
[ paktvā ] kṣīreṇa vā gokṣurakopayogaṃ vidārikākandakabhakṣaṇaṃ vā | kurvanna sīded yadi jīryate'sya mandāgnitā cedidamatra cūrṇam || 10 ||
sājamodalavaṇā harītakī śṛṅgaverasahitā ca pippalī | madyatakrataraloṣṇavāribhiścūrṇapānamudarāgnidīpanam || 11 ||
atyamlatiktalavaṇāni kaṭūni vātti | yaḥ kṣāraśākabahulāni ca bhojanāni | dṛgśukravīryarahitaḥ sa karotyanekān 75.12dvyājān jaranniva yuvāpyabalāmavāpya || 12 ||
[ kṣāraśākabahulāni ]

Chapter 76: gandhayuktyadhyāyaḥ [gandhayukti-adhyāyaḥ]

sraggandhadhūpāmbarabhūṣaṇādyaṃ na śobhate śuklaśiroruhasya | yasmādato mūrdhajarāgasevāṃ kuryād yathaivāñjanabhūṣaṇānām || 1 ||
lauhe pātre taṇḍulān kodravāṇāṃ śukle pakvāṃl lohacūrṇena sākam | piṣṭān sūkṣmaṃ mūrdhni śuklāmlakeśe datvā tiṣṭhedveṣṭayitvārdra patraiḥ || 2 ||
[ dattvā | arka ] yāte dvitīye prahare vihāya dadyācchirasyāmalakapralepam | saṃchādya patraiḥ praharadvayena prakṣālitaṃ kārṣṇyamupaiti śīrṣam || 3 ||
paścācchiraḥsnānasugandhatailairlohāmlagandhaṃ śiraso'panīya | hṛdyaiśca gandhairvividhaiśca dhūpairantaḥpure rājyasukhaṃ niṣevet || 4 ||
tvakkuṣṭhareṇunalikāspṛkkārasatagarabālakaistulyaiḥ | kesarapatravimiśrairnarapatiyogyaṃ śiraḥsnānam || 5 ||
mañjiṣṭhayā vyāghranakhena śuktyā tvacā sakuṣṭhena rasena cūrṇaḥ | tailena yukto'rkamayūkhataptaḥ karoti taccampakagandhi tailam || 6 ||
tulyaiḥ patraturuṣkabālatagarairgandhaḥ smaroddīpanaḥ savyāmo bakulo'yameva kaṭukāhiṅgupradhūpānvitaḥ | kuṣṭhenotpalagandhikaḥ samalayaḥ pūrvo bhaveccampako jātītvaksahito'timuktaka iti jñeyaḥ sakustumburuḥ || 7 ||
śatapuṣpākundurukau pādenārdhena nakhaturuṣkau ca | malayapriyaṅgubhāgau gandho dhūpyo guḍanakhena || 8 ||
[ bhāgo ] guggulubālakalākṣāmustānakhaśarkarāḥ kramāddhūpaḥ | anyo māṃsībālakaturuṣkanakhacandanaiḥ piṇḍaḥ || 9 ||
[ vālaka | vālaka ] harītakīśaṅkhaghanadravāmbubhirguḍotpalaiḥ śailakamustakānvitaiḥ | navāntapādādivivardhitaiḥ kramādbhavanti dhūpā bahavo manoharāḥ || 10 ||
bhāgaiścaturbhiḥ sitaśailamustāḥ śrīsarjabhāgau nakhaguggulū ca | karpūrabodho madhupiṇḍito'yaṃ kopacchado nāma narendradhūpaḥ || 11 ||
[ śaileya ] tvaguśīrapatrabhāgaiḥ sūkṣmailārdhena saṃyutaiścūrṇaḥ | puṭavāsaḥ pravaro'yaṃ mṛgakarpūraprabodhena || 12 ||
[ paṭavāsaḥ ] ghanabālakaśaileyakakarpūrośīranāgapuṣpāṇi | vyāghranakhaspṛkkāgurudamanakanakhatagaradhānyāni || 13 ||
[ madanaka ] karpūracolamalayaiḥ svecchāparivartitaiścaturbhirataḥ | ekadvitricaturbhirbhāgairgandhārṇavo bhavati || 14 ||
[ karcūra | cora ] atyulbaṇagandhatvādekāṃśo nityameva dhānyānām | karpūrasya tadūno naitau dvitryādibhirdeyau || 15 ||
śrīsarjaguḍanakhaiste dhūpayitavyāḥ kramānna piṇḍasthaiḥ | bodhaḥ kastūrikayā deyaḥ karpūrasaṃyutayā || 16 ||
atra sahasracatuṣṭayamanyāni ca saptatisahasrāṇi | lakṣaṃ śatāni sapta viṃśatiyuktāni gandhānām || 17 ||
ekaikamekabhāgaṃ dvitricaturbhāgikairyutaṃ dravyaiḥ | ṣaḍgandhakaraṃ tadvaddvitricaturbhāgikaṃ kurute || 18 ||
dravyacatuṣṭayayogādgandhacaturviṃśatiryathaikasya | evaṃ śeṣāṇāmapi ṣaṇṇavatiḥ sarvapiṇḍo'tra || 19 ||
ṣoḍaśake dravyagaṇe caturvikalpena bhidyamānānām | aṣṭādaśa jāyante śatāni sahitāni viṃśatyā || 20 ||
ṣaṇṇavatibhedabhinnaścaturvikalpo gaṇo yatastasmāt | ṣaṇṇanavatiguṇaḥ kāryaḥ sā saṅkhyā bhavati gandhānām || 21 ||
pūrveṇa pūrveṇa gatena yuktaṃ sthānaṃ vināntyaṃ pravadanti saṅkhyām | icchāvikalpaiḥ kramaśo'bhinīya nīte nivṛttiḥ punaranyanītiḥ || 22 ||
dvitrīndriyāṣṭabhāgairaguruḥ patraṃ turuṣkaśaileyau | viṣayāṣṭapakṣadahanāḥ priyaṅgumustārasāḥ keśaḥ || 23 ||
spṛkkātvaktagarāṇāṃ māṃsyāśca kṛtaikasaptaṣaḍbhāgāḥ | saptartuvedacandrairmalayanakhaśrīkakundurukāḥ || 24 ||
ṣoḍaśake kacchapuṭe yathā tathā miśrite caturdravye | ye'trāṣṭādaśa bhāgāste'smin gandhādayo yogāḥ || 25 ||
[ miśritaiścaturdravyaiḥ ] nakhatagaraturuṣkayutā jātīkarpūramṛgakṛtobdodhāḥ | guḍanakhadhūpyā gandhāḥ kartavyāḥ sarvatobhadrāḥ || 26 ||
[ udbodhāḥ ] jātīphalamṛgakarpūrabodhitaiḥ sasahakāramadhusiktaiḥ | bahavo'tra pārijātāścaturbhiricchāparigṛhītaiḥ || 27 ||
sarjarasaśrīvāsakasamanvitā ye'tra sarvadhūpāstaiḥ | śrīsarjarasaviyuktaiḥ snānāni sabālaka tvagbhiḥ || 28 ||
[ sarvayogās | savālaka ] rodhrośīranatāgurumustāpatrapriyaṅguvanapathyāḥ | navakoṣṭhātkacchapuṭāddravyatritayaṃ samuddhṛtya || 29 ||
[ mustā ] candanaturuṣkabhāgau śuktyardhaṃ pādikā tu śatapuṣpā | kaṭuhiṅgulaguḍadhūpyāḥ kesaragandhāścaturaśītiḥ || 30 ||
saptāhaṃ gomūtre harītakīcūrṇasaṃyute kṣiptvā | gandhodake ca bhūyo vinikṣipeddantakāṣṭhāni || 31 ||
elātvakpatrāñjanamadhumaricairnāgapuṣpakuṣṭhaiśca | gandhāmbhaḥ kartavyaṃ kiñcitkālaṃ sthitānyasmin || 32 ||
jātīphalapatrailākarpūraiḥ kṛtayamaikaśikhibhāgaiḥ | avacūrnitāni bhānormarīcibhiḥ śoṣaṇīyāni || 33 ||
varṇaprasādaṃ vadanasya kāntiṃ vaiśadyamāsyasya sugandhitāṃ ca | saṃsevituḥ śrotrasukhāṃ ca vācaṃ kurvanti kāṣṭhānyasakṛdbhavānām || 34 ||
kāmaṃ pradīpayati rūpamabhivyanakti saubhāgyamāvahati vaktrasugandhitāṃ ca | ūrjaṃ karoti kaphajāṃśca nihanti rogāṃstāmbūlamevamaparāṃśca guṇān karoti || 35 ||
yuktena cūrṇena karoti rāgaṃ rāgakṣayaṃ pūgaphalātiriktam | cūrṇādhikaṃ vaktravigandhakāri patrādhikaṃ sādhu karoti gandham || 36 ||
patrādhikaṃ niśi hitaṃ saphalaṃ divā ca proktānyathākaraṇamasya viḍambanaiva | kakkolapūgalavalīphalapārijātairāmoditaṃ madamudā muditaṃ karoti || 37 ||

Chapter 77: strīpuṃsasamāyogādhyāyaḥ [strīpuṃsasamāyoga-adhyāya]

śastrena veṇīvinigūhitena vidūrathaṃ svā mahiṣī jaghāna | viṣapradigdhena ca nūpureṇa devī viraktā kila kāśirājam || 1 ||
evaṃ viraktā janayanti doṣānprāṇacchido'nyairanukīrtitaiḥ kim | raktāviraktāḥ puruṣairato'rthātparīkṣitavyāḥ pramadāḥ prayatnāt || 2 ||
snehaṃ manobhavakṛtaṃ kathayanti bhāvā | nābhībhujastanavibhūṣaṇadarśanāni | vastrābhisaṃyamanakeśavimokṣaṇāni 77.03dbhrūkṣepakampitakaṭākṣanirīkṣaṇāni || 3 ||
uccaiḥ ṣṭhīvanamutkaṭaprahasitaṃ śayyāsanotsarpaṇaṃ gātrāsphoṭanajṛmbhaṇāni sulabhadravyālpasamprārthanā | bālāliṅganacumbanānyabhimukhe sakhyāḥ samālokanaṃ dṛkpātaśca parāṅmukhe guṇakathā karṇasya kaṇḍūyanam || 4 ||
imāṃ ca vindyādanuraktaceṣṭāṃ priyāṇi vakti svadhanaṃ dadāti | vilokya saṃhṛṣyati vītaroṣā pramārṣṭi doṣān guṇakīrtanena || 5 ||
tanmitrapūjā tadaridviṣatvaṃ kṛtasmṛtiḥ proṣitadaurmanasyam | stanauṣṭhadānānyupagūhanaṃ ca svedo'tha cumbāprathamābhiyogaḥ || 6 ||
viraktaceṣṭā bhrukuṭīmukhatvaṃ parāṅmukhatvaṃ kṛtavismṛtiśca | asambhramo duṣparitoṣatā ca taddviṣṭamaitrī paruṣaṃ ca vākyam || 7 ||
[ bhṛkuṭī ] spṛṣṭvātha vālokya dhunoti gātraṃ karoti garvaṃ na ruṇaddhi yāntam | cumbāvirāme vadanaṃ pramārṣṭi paścātsamuttiṣṭhati pūrvasuptā || 8 ||
bhikṣuṇikā pravrajitā dāsī dhātrī kumārikā rajikā | mālākārī duṣṭāṅganā sakhī nāpitī dūtyaḥ || 9 ||
kulajanavināśaheturdūtyo yasmādataḥ prayatnena | tābhyaḥ striyo'bhirakṣyā vaṃśayaśomānavṛddhyartham || 10 ||
rātrīvihārajāgararogavyapadeśaparagṛhekṣaṇikāḥ | vyasanotsavāśca saṅketahetavasteṣu rakṣyāśca || 11 ||
ādau necchati nojjhati smarakathāṃ vrīḍāvimiśrālasā madhye hrīparivarjitābhyuparame lajjāvinamrānanā | bhāvairnaikavidhaiḥ karotyabhinayaṃ bhūyaśca yā sādarā buddhvā pumprakṛtiṃ ca yānucarati glānetaraiśceṣṭitaiḥ || 12 ||
strīṇāṃ guṇā yauvanarūpaveṣadākṣiṇyavijñānavilāsapūrvāḥ | strī ratnasaṃjñā ca guṇānvitāsu strīvyādhayo'nyāścaturasya puṃsaḥ || 13 ||
na grāmyavarṇairmaladigdhakāyā nindyāṅgasaṃbandhikathāṃ ca kuryāt | na cānyakāryasmaraṇaṃ rahaḥsthā mano hi mūlaṃ haradagdhamūrteḥ || 14 ||
śvāsaṃ manuṣyeṇa samaṃ tyajantī bāhūpadhānastanadānadakṣā | sugandhakeśā susamīparāgā supte'nusuptā prathamaṃ vibuddhā || 15 ||
duṣṭasvabhāvāḥ parivarjanīyā vimardakāleṣu ca na kṣamā yāḥ | yāsāmasṛgvāsitanīlapītamātāmravarṇaṃ ca na tāḥ praśastāḥ || 16 ||
yā svapnaśīlā bahuraktapittā pravāhinī vātakaphātiraktā | mahāśanā svedayutāṅgaduṣṭhā yā hrasvakeśī palitānvitā vā || 17 ||
[ atiriktā | ca ] māṃsāni yasyāśca calanti nāryā mahodarā khikkhiminī ca yā syāt | strīlakṣaṇe yāḥ kathitāśca pāpāstābhirna kuryātsaha kāmadharmam || 18 ||
śaśaśoṇitasaṅkāśaṃ lākṣārasasannikāśamathavā yat | prakṣālitaṃ virajyati yaccāsṛktadbhavecchuddham || 19 ||
yacchabdavedanāvarjitaṃ tryahātsannivartate raktam | tatpuruṣasamprayogādavicāraṃ garbhatāṃ yāti || 20 ||
na dinatrayaṃ niṣevyaṃ snānaṃ mālyānulepanaṃ strībhiḥ | snāyāccaturthadivase śāstroktenopadeśena || 21 ||
[ niṣevet | ca strī ] puṣyasnānauṣadhayo yāḥ kathitāstābhirambumiśrābhiḥ | snāyāttathātra mantraḥ sa eva yastatra nirdiṣṭaḥ || 22 ||
yugmāsu kila manuṣyā niśāsu nāryo bhavanti viṣamāsu | dīrghāyuṣaḥ surūpāḥ sukhinaśca vikṛṣṭayugmāsu || 23 ||
dakṣiṇapārśve puruṣo vāme nārī yamāv ubhayasaṃsthau | yadudaramadhyopagataṃ napuṃsakaṃ tanniboddhavyam || 24 ||
kendratrikoṇeṣu śubhasthiteṣu lagne śaśāṅke ca śubhaiḥ samete | pāpaistrilābhārigataiśca yāyātpuṃjanmayogeṣu ca samprayogam || 25 ||
na nakhadaśanavikṣatāni kuryādṛtusamaye puruṣaḥ striyāḥ kathañcit | ṛturapi daśa ṣaṭ ca vāsarāṇi prathamaniśātritayaṃ na tatra gamyam || 26 ||

Chapter 78: śayyāsanalakṣaṇādhyāyaḥ [śayyāsanalakṣaṇa-adhyāya]

sarvasya sarvakālaṃ yasmādupayogameti śāstramidam | rājñāṃ viśeṣato'taḥ śayanāsanalakṣaṇaṃ vakṣye || 1 ||
asanaspandanacandanaharidrasuradārutindukīśālāḥ | kāśmaryañjanapadmakaśākā vā śiṃśapā ca śubhāḥ || 2 ||
aśanijalānilahastiprapātitā madhuvihaṅgakṛtanilayāḥ | caityaśmaśānapathijordhvaśuṣkavallīnibaddhāśca || 3 ||
kaṇṭakino ye ca syurmahānadīsaṅgamodbhavā ye ca | surabhavanajāśca na śubhā ye cāparayāmyadikpatitāḥ || 4 ||
[ vā ye ] pratiṣiddhavṛkṣanirmitaśayanāsanasevanātkulavināśaḥ | vyādhibhayavyayakalahā bhavantyanarthā anekavidhāḥ || 5 ||
[ anarthāśca ] pūrvacchinnaṃ yadi vā dāru bhavettatparīkṣyamārambhe | yadyārohettasmin kumārakaḥ putrapaśudaṃ tat || 6 ||
sitakusumamattavāraṇadadhyakṣatapūrṇakumbharatnāni | maṅgalyānyanyāni ca dṛṣṭvārambhe śubhaṃ jñeyam || 7 ||
karmāṅgulaṃ yavāṣṭakamudarāsaktaṃ tuṣaiḥ parityaktam | aṅgulaśataṃ nṛpāṇāṃ mahatī śayyā jayāya kṛtā || 8 ||
navatiḥ saiva ṣaḍūnā dvādaśahīnā triṣaṭkahīnā ca | nṛpaputramantribalapatipurodhasāṃ syuryathāsaṅkhyam || 9 ||
ardhamato'ṣṭāṃśonaṃ viṣkambho viśvakarmaṇā proktaḥ | āyāmatryaṃśasamaḥ pādocchrāyaḥ sakukṣya śirāḥ || 10 ||
[ sakukṣi ] yaḥ sarvaḥ śrīparṇyā paryaṅko nirmitaḥ sa dhanadātā | asanakṛto rogaharastindukasāreṇa vittakaraḥ || 11 ||
yaḥ kevalaśiṃśapayā vinirmito bahuvidhaṃ sa vṛddhikaraḥ | candanamayo ripughno dharmayaśodīrghajīvitakṛt || 12 ||
yaḥ padmakaparyaṅkaḥ sa dīrghamāyuḥ śriyaṃ śrutaṃ vittam | kurute śālena kṛtaḥ kalyāṇaṃ śākaracitaśca || 13 ||
kevalacandanaracitaṃ kāñcanaguptaṃ vicitraratnayutam | adhyāsanparyaṅkaṃ vibudhairapi pūjyate nṛpatiḥ || 14 ||
anyena samāyuktā na tindukī śiṃśapā ca śubhaphaladā | na śrīparṇena ca devadāruvṛkṣo na cāpyasanaḥ || 15 ||
[ śrīparṇī na ] śubhadau tu śālaśākau parasparaṃ saṃyutau pṛthakcaiva | tadvatpṛthakpraśastau sahitau ca haridrakakadambau || 16 ||
[ śākaśālau ] sarvaḥ spandanaracito na śubhaḥ prāṇān hinasti cāmbakṛtaḥ | asano'nyadārusahitaḥ kṣipraṃ doṣān karoti bahūn || 17 ||
ambaspandanacandanavṛkṣāṇāṃ spandanācchubhāḥ pādāḥ | phalataruṇā śayanāsanamiṣṭaphalaṃ bhavati sarveṇa || 18 ||
gajadantaḥ sarveṣāṃ proktatarūṇāṃ praśasyate yoge | kāryo'laṅkāravidhirgajadantena praśastena || 19 ||
dantasya mūlaparidhiṃ dvirāyataṃ prohya kalpayeccheṣam | adhikamanūpacarāṇāṃ nyūnaṃ giricāriṇāṃ kiñcit || 20 ||
śrīvṛkṣavardhamānacchatradhvajacāmarānurūpeṣu | chede dṛṣṭeṣvārogyavijayadhanavṛddhisaukhyāni || 21 ||
[ śrīvatsa | arogya ] praharaṇasadṛśeṣu jayo nandyāvarte pranaṣṭadeśāptiḥ | loṣṭhe tu labdhapūrvasya bhavati deśasya samprāptiḥ || 22 ||
[ loṣṭe ] strīrūpe dhananāśo bhṛṅgāre'bhyutthite sutotpattiḥ | kumbhena nidhiprāptiryātrāvighnaṃ ca daṇḍena || 23 ||
[ svavināśo ] kṛkalāsakapibhujaṅgeṣvasubhikṣavyādhayo ripuvaśitvam | gṛdhrolūkadhvāṅkṣaśyenākāreṣu janamarakaḥ || 24 ||
[ vaśatvam ] pāśe'tha vā kabandhe nṛpamṛtyurjanavipatsrute rakte | kṛṣṇe śyāve rūkṣe durgandhe cāśubhaṃ bhavati || 25 ||
śuklaḥ samaḥ sugandhiḥ snigdhaśca śubhāvaho bhavecchedaḥ | aśubhaśubhacchedā ye śayaneṣvapi te tathā phaladāḥ || 26 ||
īṣāyoge dāru pradakṣiṇāgraṃ praśastamācāryaiḥ | apasavyaikadigagre bhavati bhayaṃ bhūtasañjanitam || 27 ||
ekenāvākśirasā bhavati hi pādena pādavaikalyam | dvābhyāṃ na jīryate'nnaṃ tricaturbhiḥ kleśavadhabandhāḥ || 28 ||
[ ekenāvākcchirasā ] suṣire'tha vā vivarṇe granthau pādasya śīrṣage vyādhiḥ | pāde kumbho yaśca granthau tasminnudararogaḥ || 29 ||
kumbhādhastājjaṅghā tatra kṛto jaṅghayoḥ karoti bhayam | tasyāścādharo'dhaḥ kṣayakṛddravyasya tatra kṛtaḥ || 30 ||
khuradeśe yo granthiḥ khuriṇāṃ pīḍākaraḥ sa nirdiṣṭaḥ | īṣāśīrṣaṇyośca tribhāgasaṃstho bhavenna śubhaḥ || 31 ||
niṣkuṭamatha kolākṣaṃ sūkaranayanaṃ ca vatsanābhaṃ ca | kālakamanyaddhundhukamiti kathitaśchidrasaṃkṣepaḥ || 32 ||
ghaṭavatsuṣiraṃ madhye saṅkaṭamāsye ca niṣkuṭaṃ chidram | niṣpāvamāṣamātraṃ nīlaṃ chidraṃ ca kolākṣam || 33 ||
sūkaranayanaṃ viṣamaṃ vivarṇamadhyardhaparvadīrghaṃ ca | vāmāvartaṃ bhinnaṃ parvamitaṃ vatsanābhākhyam || 34 ||
kālakasaṃjñaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ dhundhukamiti yadbhavedvinirbhinnam | dārusavarṇaṃ chidraṃ na tathā pāpaṃ samuddiṣṭam || 35 ||
niṣkuṭasaṇjñe dravyakṣayastu kolekṣaṇe kuladhvaṃsaḥ | śastrabhayaṃ sūkarake rogabhayaṃ vatsanābhākhye || 36 ||
kālakadhundhukasaṃjñaṃ kīṭairviddhaṃ ca na śubhadaṃ chidram | sarvaṃ granthipracuraṃ sarvatra na śobhanaṃ dāru || 37 ||
ekadrumeṇa dhanyaṃ vṛkṣadvayanirmitaṃ ca dhanyataram | tribhirātmajavṛddhikaraṃ caturbhirarthaṃ yaśaścāgryam || 38 ||
[ artho ] pañcavanaspatiracite pañcatvaṃ yāti tatra yaḥ śete | ṣaṭsaptāṣṭatarūṇāṃ kāṣṭhairghaṭite kulavināśaḥ || 39 ||

Chapter 79: ratnaparīkṣādhyāyaḥ [ratnaparīkṣa-adhyāya]

ratnena śubhena śubhaṃ bhavati nṛpāṇāmaniṣṭamaśubhena | yasmādataḥ parīkṣyaṃ daivaṃ ratnāśritam tajjñaiḥ || 1 ||
dvipahayavanitādīnāṃ svaguṇaviśeṣeṇa ratnaśabdo'sti | iha tūpalaratnānāmadhikāro vajrapūrvāṇām || 2 ||
ratnāni balāddaityāddadhīcito'nye vadanti jātāni | ke cidbhuvaḥ svabhāvādvaicitryaṃ prāhurupalānām || 3 ||
vajrendranīlamarakatakarketarapadmarāgarudhirākhyāḥ | vaidūryapulakavimalakarājamaṇisphatikaśaśikāntāḥ || 4 ||
[ vaiḍūrya ] saugandhikagomedakaśaṅkhamahānīlapuṣparāgākhyāḥ | brahmamaṇijyotīrasasasyakamuktāpravālāni || 5 ||
veṇātaṭe viśuddhaṃ śirīṣakusuma prabhaṃ ca kauśalakam | saurāṣṭrakamātāmraṃ kṛṣṇaṃ saurpārakaṃ vajram || 6 ||
[ upamaṃ ] īṣattāmraṃ himavati mataṅgajaṃ vallapuṣpasaṅkāśam | āpītaṃ ca kaliṅge śyāmaṃ pauṇḍreṣu sambhūtam || 7 ||
aindraṃ ṣaḍaśri śuklaṃ yāmyaṃ sarpāsyarūpamasitaṃ ca | kadalīkāṇḍanikāśaṃ vaiṣṇavamiti sarvasaṃsthānam || 8 ||
vāruṇamabalāguhyopamaṃ bhavetkarṇikārapuṣpanibham | śṛṅgāṭakasaṃsthānaṃ vyāghrākṣinibhaṃ ca hautabhujam || 9 ||
vāyavyaṃ ca yavopamamaśokakusumaprabhaṃ samuddiṣṭam | srotaḥ khaniḥ prakīrṇakamityākarasambhavastrividhaḥ || 10 ||
raktaṃ pītaṃ ca śubham rājanyānāṃ sitam dvijātīnām | śairīṣaṃ vaiśyānāṃ śūdrāṇāṃ śasyate'sinibham || 11 ||
sitasarṣapāṣṭakaṃ taṇḍulo bhavettaṇḍulaistu viṃśatyā | tulitasya dve lakṣe mūlyaṃ dvidvyūnite caitat || 12 ||
pādatryaṃśārdhonaṃ tribhāgapañcāṃśaṣoḍaśāṃśāśca | bhāgaśca pañcaviṃśaḥ śatikas sāhasrikaśceti || 13 ||
sarvadravyābhedyaṃ laghvambhasi tarati raśmivatsnighdam | taḍidanalaśakracāpopamaṃ ca vajraṃ hitāyoktam || 14 ||
kākapadamakṣikākeśadhātuyuktāni śarkarairviddham | dviguṇāśri dagdhakaluṣatrastaviśīrṇāni na śubhāni || 15 ||
[ śarkarā | digdha ] yāni ca budbudadalitāgracipiṭavāsīphalapradīrghāṇi | sarveṣāṃ caiteṣāṃ mūlyādbhāgo'ṣṭamo hāniḥ || 16 ||
vajraṃ na kiñcidapi dhārayitavyameke putrārthinībhirabalābhiruśanti tajjñāḥ | śṛṅgāṭakatripuṭadhānyakavatsthitaṃ yac śroṇīnibhaṃ ca śubhadaṃ tanayārthinīnām || 17 ||
svajanavibhavajīvitakṣayaṃ janayati vajramaniṣṭalakṣaṇam | aśaniviṣabhayārināśanaṃ śubhamupabhogakaraṃ ca bhūbhṛtām || 18 ||
[ urubhogakara ]

Chapter 80: muktālakṣaṇādhyāyaḥ [muktālakṣaṇa-adhyāya]

dvipabhujagaśuktiśaṅkhābhraveṇutimisūkaraprasūtāni | muktāphalāni teṣāṃ bahusādhu ca śuktijaṃ bhavati || 1 ||
siṃhalakapāralaukikasaurāṣṭrikatāmraparṇipāraśavāḥ | kauberapāṇḍyavāṭakahaimā ityākarāstvaṣṭau || 2 ||
[ hy ] bahusaṃsthānāḥ snigdhāḥ haṃsābhāḥ siṃhalākarāḥ sthūlāḥ | īṣattāmrāḥ śvetāstamoviyuktāśca tāmrākhyāḥ || 3 ||
[ snigdhā ] kṛṣṇāḥ śvetāḥ pītāḥ saśarkarāḥ pāralaukikā viṣamāḥ | na sthūlā nātyalpā navanītanibhāśca saurāṣṭrāḥ || 4 ||
jyotiṣmatyaḥ śubhrā guravo'timahāguṇāśca pāraśavāḥ | laghu jarjaraṃ dadhinibhaṃ bṛhaddvisaṃsthānamapi haimam || 5 ||
[ mantaḥ | bṛhadvisaṃsthānam ] viṣamaṃ kṛṣṇaśvetaṃ laghu kauberaṃ pramāṇatejovat | nimbaphalatripuṭadhānyakacūrṇāḥ syuḥ pāṇḍyavāṭabhavāḥ || 6 ||
[ kṛṣṇaṃ śvetam ] atasīkusumaśyāmam vaiṣṇavamaindraṃ śaśāṅkasaṅkāśam | haritālanibhaṃ vāruṇamasitaṃ yamadaivataṃ bhavati || 7 ||
pariṇatadāḍimagulikāguñjātāmraṃ ca vāyudaivatyam | nirdhūmānalakamalaprabhaṃ ca vijñeyamāgneyam || 8 ||
māṣakacatuṣṭayadhṛtasyaikasya śatāhatā tripañcāśat | kārṣāpaṇā nigaditā mūlyaṃ tejoguṇayutasya || 9 ||
māṣakadalahānyāto dvātriṃśadviṃśatistrayodaśa ca | aṣṭau ca śatāni śatatrayaṃ tripañcāśatā sahitam || 10 ||
pañcatriṃśaṃ śatamiti catvāraḥ kṛṣṇalā navatimūlyāḥ | sārdhāstisro guñjāḥ saptatimūlyaṃ dhṛtaṃ rūpam || 11 ||
guñjātrayasya mūlyaṃ pañcāśad rūpakā guṇayutasya | rūpakapañcatriṃśattrayasya guñjārdhahīnasya || 12 ||
paladaśabhāgo dharaṇaṃ tad yadi muktāstrayodaśa surūpāḥ | triśatī sapañcaviṃśā rūpakasaṅkhyā kṛtaṃ mūlyam || 13 ||
[ triṃśatī ] ṣoḍaśakasya dviśatī viṃśatirūpasya saptatiḥ saśatā | yatpañcaviṃśatidhṛtaṃ tasya śataṃ triṃśatā sahitam || 14 ||
triṃśatsaptatimūlyaṃ catvāriṃśacchatārdhamūlyaṃ ca | ṣaṣṭiḥ pañconā vā dharaṇam pañcāṣṭakaṃ mūlyam || 15 ||
[ mūlyā ] muktāśītyā triṃśacchatasya sā pañcarūpakavihīnā | dvitricatuḥpañcaśatā dvādaśaṣaṭpañcakatritayam || 16 ||
pikkāpiccārghārdhā ravakaḥ sikthaṃ trayodaśādyānām | saṃjṇāḥ parato nigarāścūrṇāścāśītipūrvāṇām || 17 ||
etadguṇayuktānāṃ dharaṇadhṛtānāṃ prakīrtitaṃ mūlyam | parikalpyamantarāle hīnaguṇāṇāṃ kṣayaḥ kāryaḥ || 18 ||
[ prakītitam ] kṛṣṇaśvetakapītakatāmrāṇāmīṣadapi ca viṣamāṇām | tryaṃśonam viṣamakapītayośca ṣaḍbhāgadalahīnam || 19 ||
airāvatakulajānāṃ puṣyaśravaṇendusūryadivaseṣu | ye cottarāyaṇabhavā grahaṇe'rkendvośca bhadrebhāḥ || 20 ||
teṣāṃ kila jāyante muktāḥ kumbheṣu saradakośeṣu | bahavo bṛhatpramāṇā bahusaṃsthānāḥ prabhāyuktāḥ || 21 ||
naiṣāmarghaḥ kāryo na ca vedho'tīva te prabhāyuktāḥ | sutavijayārogyakarā mahāpavitrā dhṛtā rājñām || 22 ||
daṃṣṭrāmūle śaśikāntisaprabhaṃ bahuguṇaṃ ca vārāham | timijaṃ matsyākṣībhaṃ bṛhatpavitraṃ bahuguṇaṃ ca || 23 ||
varṣopalavajjātaṃ vāyuskandhācca saptamādbhraṣṭam | hriyate kila khāddivyaistaḍitprabhaṃ meghasambhūtam || 24 ||
takṣakavāsukikulajāḥ kāmagamā ye ca pannagāsteṣām | snigdhā nīladyutayo bhavanti muktāḥ phaṇasyānte || 25 ||
śaste'vanipradeśe rajatamaye bhājane sthite ca yadi | varṣati devo'kasmāttajjñeyaṃ nāgasambhūtam || 26 ||
apaharati viṣamalakṣmīṃ kṣapayati śatrūnyaśo vikāśayati | bhaujaṅgaṃ nṛpatīnāṃ dhṛtamakṛtārghaṃ vijayadaṃ ca || 27 ||
karpūrasphaṭikanibhaṃ cipiṭaṃ viṣamaṃ ca veṇujaṃ jñeyam | śaṅkhodbhavaṃ śaśinibhaṃ vṛttaṃ bhrājiṣṇu ruciraṃ ca || 28 ||
śaṅkhatimiveṇuvāraṇavarāhabhujagābhrajānyavaidyāni | amitaguṇatvāccaiṣāmarghaḥ śāstre na nirdiṣṭaḥ || 29 ||
[ avaidhyāni avedyāni ] etāni sarvāṇi mahāguṇāni sutārthasaubhāgyayaśaskarāṇi | rugśokahantṝṇi ca pārthivānāṃ muktāphalānīpsitakāmadāni || 30 ||
surabhūṣaṇaṃ latānāṃ sahasramaṣṭottaraṃ caturhastam | inducchando nāmnā vijayacchandastadardhena || 31 ||
[ indracchando ] śatamaṣṭayutaṃ hāro devacchando hyaśītirekayutā | aṣṭāṣṭako'rdhahāro raśmikalāpaśca navaṣaṭkaḥ || 32 ||
dvātriṃśatā tu guccho viṃśatyā kīrtito'rdhagucchākhyaḥ | ṣoḍaśabhirmāṇavako dvādaśabhiścārdhamāṇavakaḥ || 33 ||
mandarasaṃjño'ṣṭābhiḥ pañcalatā hāraphalakamityuktam | saptāviṃśatimuktā hasto nakṣatramāleti || 34 ||
antaramaṇisaṃyuktā maṇisopānaṃ suvarṇagulikairvā | taralakamaṇimadhyaṃ tadvijñeyaṃ cāṭukāramiti || 35 ||
ekāvalī nāma yatheṣṭasaṅkhyā hastapramāṇā maṇiviprayuktā | saṃyojitā yā maṇinā tu madhye yaṣṭīti sā bhūṣaṇavidbhiruktam || 36 ||

Chapter 81: padmarāgalakṣaṇādhyāyaḥ [padmarāgalakṣaṇa-adhyāya]

saugandhikakuruvindasphaṭikebhyaḥ padmarāgasambhūtiḥ | saugandhikajā bhramarāñjanābjajambūrasadyutayaḥ || 1 ||
[ padmarāgo sambhūtiḥ ] kuruvindabhavāḥ śabalā mandadyutayaśca dhātubhirviddhāḥ | sphaṭikabhavā dyutimanto nānāvarṇā viśuddhāśca || 2 ||
snigdhaḥ prabhānulepī svaccho'rciṣmān guruḥ susaṃsthānaḥ | antaḥprabho'tirāgo maṇiratnaguṇāḥ samastānām || 3 ||
[ atirāgā ] kaluṣā mandadyutayo lekhākīrṇāḥ sadhātavaḥ khaṇḍāḥ | durviddhā na manojñāḥ saśarkarāśceti maṇidoṣāḥ || 4 ||
bhramaraśikhikaṇṭhavarṇo dīpaśikhāsaprabho bhujaṅgānām | bhavati maṇiḥ kika mūrdhani yo'nargheyaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ || 5 ||
yastaṃ bibharti manujādhipatirna tasya doṣā bhavanti viṣarogakṛtāḥ kadā cit | rāṣṭre ca nityamabhivarṣati tasya devaḥ śatrūṃśca nāśayati tasya maṇeḥ prabhāvāt || 6 ||
ṣaḍviṃśatiḥ sahasrāṇyekasya maṇeḥ palapramāṇasya | karṣatrayasya viṃśatirupadiṣṭā padmarāgasya || 7 ||
ardhapalasya dvādaśa karṣasya ekasya ṣaṭsahasrāṇi | yaccāṣṭamāṣakadhṛtaṃ tasya sahasratrayaṃ mūlyam || 8 ||
māṣakacatuṣṭayaṃ daśaśatakrayaṃ dvau tu pañcaśatamūlyau | parikalpyamantarāle mūlyaṃ hīnādhikaguṇānām || 9 ||
varṇanyūnasyārdhaṃ tejohīnasya mūlyamaṣṭāṃśam | alpaguṇo bahudoṣo mūlyātprāpnoti viṃśāṃśam || 10 ||
ādhūmraṃ vraṇabahulaṃ svalpaguṇaṃ cāpnuyāddviśatabhāgam | iti padmarāgamūlyaṃ pūrvācāryaiḥ samuddiṣṭam || 11 ||

Chapter 82: marakatalakṣaṇādhyāyaḥ [marakatalakṣaṇa-adhyāya]

śukavaṃśapatrakadalīśirīṣakusumaprabhaṃ guṇopetam | surapitṛkārye marakatamatīva śubhadaṃ nṛṇāṃ vihitam || 1 ||
[ rakatam | vidhṛtam ]

Chapter 83: dīpalakṣaṇādhyāyaḥ [dīpalakṣaṇa-adhyāya]

vāmāvarto malinakiraṇaḥ sasphuliṅgo'lpamūrtiḥ kṣipraṃ nāśaṃ vrajati vimalasnehavartyanvito'pi | dīpaḥ pāpaṃ kathayati phalaṃ śabdavānvepanaśca vyākīrṇārcirviśalabhamarudyaśca nāśaṃ prayāti || 1 ||
dīpaḥ saṃhatamūrtirāyatatanurnirvepano dīptimānniḥśabdo ruciraḥ pradakṣiṇagatirvaidūrya hemadyutiḥ | lakṣmīṃ kṣipramabhivyanakti suciraṃ yaścodyataṃ dīpyate śeṣaṃ lakṣaṇamagnilakṣaṇasamaṃ yojyaṃ yathāyuktitaḥ || 2 ||
[ vaiḍūrya | ruciraṃ | suciram ]

Chapter 84: dantakāṣṭhalakṣaṇādhyāyaḥ [dantakāṣṭhalakṣaṇa-adhyāya]

vallīlatāgulmataruprabhedaiḥ syurdantakāṣṭhāni sahasraśo yaiḥ | phalāni vācyānyatha tatprasaṅgo mā bhūdato vacmyatha kāmikāni || 1 ||
[ ati ] ajñātapūrvāṇi na dantakāṣṭhānyadyānna patraiśca samanvitāni | na yugmaparvāṇi na pāṭitāni na cordhvaśuṣkāṇi vinā tvacā ca || 2 ||
vaikaṅkataśrīphalakāśmarīṣu brāhmī dyutiḥ kṣematarau sudārāḥ | vṛddhirvaṭe'rke pracuraṃ ca tejaḥ putrā madhūke saguṇāḥ priyatvam || 3 ||
[ kakubhe ] lakṣmīḥ śirīṣe ca tathā karañje plakṣe'rthasiddhiḥ samabhīpsitā syāt | mānyatvamāyāti janasya jātyāṃ prādhānyamaśvatthatarau vadanti || 4 ||
ārogyamāyurbadarībṛhatyoraiśvaryavṛddhiḥ khadire sabilve | dravyāṇi ceṣṭānyatimuktake syuḥ prāpnoti tānyeva punaḥ kadambe || 5 ||
nīpe arthāptiḥ karavīre'nnalabdhirbhāṇḍīre syādannamevaṃ prabhūtam | śamyāṃ śatrūnapahantyarjune ca śyāmāyāṃ ca dviṣatāmeva nāśaḥ || 6 ||
[ nimbe | idameva ] śāle'śvakarṇe ca vadanti gauravaṃ sabhadradārāvapi cāṭarūṣake | vāllabhyamāyāti janasya sarvataḥ priyaṅgvapāmārgasajambudāḍimaiḥ || 7 ||
udaṅmukhaḥ prāṅmukha eva vābdaṃ kāmaṃ yatheṣṭhaṃ hṛdaye niveśya | adyādanindan ca sukhopaviṣṭaḥ prakṣālya jahyācca śucipradeśe || 8 ||
[ yatheṣṭaṃ | anindyaṃ ] abhimukhapatitaṃ praśāntadiksthaṃ śubhamatiśobhanamūrdhvasaṃsthitaṃ yat | aśubhakaramato'nyathā pradiṣṭaṃ sthitapatitaṃ ca karoti mṛṣṭamannam || 9 ||

Chapter 85: śākunādhyāyaḥ [śākuna-adhyāya]

yacchakraśukravāgīśakapiṣṭhalagarutmatām | matebhyaḥ prāha ṛṣabho bhāgurerdevalasya ca || 1 ||
[ śukraśakra ] bhāradvājamataṃ dṛṣṭvā yacca śrīdravyavardhanaḥ | āvantikaḥ prāha nṛpo mahārājādhirājakaḥ || 2 ||
saptarṣīṇāṃ mataṃ yacca saṃskṛtaṃ prākṛtaṃ ca yat | yāni coktāni gargādyairyātrākāraiśca bhūribhiḥ || 3 ||
tāni dṛṣṭvā cakāremaṃ sarvaśākunasaṃgraham | varāhamihiraḥ prītyā śiṣyāṇāṃ jñānamuttamam || 4 ||
anyajanmāntarakṛtaṃ karma puṃsāṃ śubhāśubham | yattasya śakunaḥ pākaṃ nivedayati gacchatām || 5 ||
grāmāraṇyāmbubhūvyomadyuniśobhayacāriṇaḥ | rutayātekṣitokteṣu grāhyāḥ puṃstrīnapuṃsakāḥ || 6 ||
[ strīpunnapuṃsakāḥ ] pṛthagjātyanavasthānādeṣāṃ vyaktirna lakṣyate | sāmānyalakṣaṇoddeśe ślokāv ṛṣikṛtāvimau || 7 ||
pīnonnatavikṛṣṭāṃsāḥ pṛthugrīvāḥ suvakṣasaḥ | svalpagambhīravirutāḥ puṃāṃsaḥ sthiravikramāḥ || 8 ||
tanūraskaśirogrīvāḥ sūkṣmāsyapadavikramāḥ | prasaktamṛdubhāṣiṇyaḥ striyo'to'nyannapuṃsakam || 9 ||
grāmāraṇyapracārādyaṃ lokādevopalakṣayet | saṃcikṣipsurahaṃ vacmi yātrāmātraprayojanam || 10 ||
pathyātmānaṃ nṛpaṃ sainye pure coddiśya devatām | sārthe pradhānaṃ sāmye syājjātividyāvayo'dhikam || 11 ||
[ sāmyaṃ ] muktaprāptaiṣyadarkāsu phalaṃ dikṣu tathāvidham | aṅgāradīptadhūminyastāśca śāntāstato'parāḥ || 12 ||
[ aṅgāri | aparā | aparāḥ ] tatpañcamadiśāṃ tulyaṃ śubhaṃ traikālyamādiśet | pariśeṣadiśorvācyaṃ yathāsannaṃ śubhāśubham || 13 ||
[ pariśeṣayor ] śīghramāsannanimnasthaiścirādunnatadūragaiḥ | sthānavṛddhyupaghātācca tadvadbrūyātphalaṃ punaḥ || 14 ||
kṣaṇatithyuḍuvātārkairdevadīpto yathottaram | kriyādīpto gatisthānabhāvasvaraviceṣṭitaiḥ || 15 ||
daśadhaivaṃ praśānto'pi saumyastṛṇaphalāśanaḥ | māṃsāmedhyāśane raudro vimiśro'nnāśanaḥ smṛtaḥ || 16 ||
harmyaprāsādamaṅgalyamanojñasthānasaṃsthitāḥ | śreṣṭhā madhurasakṣīraphalapuṣpadrumeṣu ca || 17 ||
svakāle giritoyasthā balino dyuniśācarāḥ | klībastrīpuruṣā jñeyā balinaḥ syuryathottaram || 18 ||
[ puruśāśca eṣāṃ ] javajātibalasthānaharṣasattvasvarānvitāḥ | svabhūmāvanulomāśca tadūnāḥ syurvivarjitāḥ || 19 ||
kukkuṭebhapirilyaśca śikhivañjulachikkarāḥ | balinaḥ siṃhanādaśca kūṭapūrī ca pūrvataḥ || 20 ||
kroṣṭukolūkahārītakākakokarkṣapiṅgalāḥ | kapotaruditākrandakrūraśabdāśca yāmyataḥ || 21 ||
gośaśakrauñcalomāśahaṃsotkrośakapiñjalāḥ | viḍālotsavavāditragītahāsāśca vāruṇāḥ || 22 ||
śatapatrakuraṅgākhumṛgaikaśaphakokilāḥ | cāṣaśalyakapuṇyāhaghaṇṭāśaṅkharavā udak || 23 ||
na grāmyo'raṇyago grāhyo nāraṇyo grāmyasaṃsthitaḥ | divācaro na śarvaryāṃ na ca naktaṃcaro divā || 24 ||
[ grāmasaṃsthitaḥ ] dvandvarogārditatrastāḥ kalahāmiṣakāṅkṣiṇaḥ | āpagāntaritā mattā na grāhyāḥ śakunāḥ kva cit || 25 ||
rohitāśvājavāleyāḥ kuraṅgoṣṭramṛgāḥ śaśaḥ | niṣphalāḥ śiśire jñeyā vasante kākakokilau || 26 ||
[ vāleyakuraṅga ] na tu bhādrapade grāhyāḥ sūkaraśvavṛkādayaḥ | śāradyābjādagokrauñcāḥ śrāvaṇe hasticātakau || 27 ||
[ śaradya ] vyāghrarkṣavānaradvīpimahiṣāḥ sabileśayāḥ | hemante niṣphalā jñeyā bālāḥ sarve vimānuṣāḥ || 28 ||
aindrānaladiśormadhye tribhāgeṣu vyavasthitāḥ | kośādhyakṣānalājīvitapoyuktāḥ pradakṣiṇam || 29 ||
śilpī bhikṣurvivastrā strī yāmyānaladigantare | parataścāpi mātaṅgagopadharmasamāśrayāḥ || 30 ||
nairṛtīvāruṇīmadhye pramadāsūtitaskarāḥ | śauṇḍikaḥ śākunī hiṃsro vāyavyāpaścimāntare || 31 ||
[ vāyavya ] viṣaghātakagosvāmikuhakajñāstataḥ param | dhanavānīkṣaṇīkaśca mālākāraḥ paraṃ tataḥ || 32 ||
vaiṣṇavaścarakaścaiva vājināṃ rakṣaṇe rataḥ | dvātriṃśadevaṃ bhedāḥ syuḥ pūrvadigbhiḥ sahoditāḥ || 33 ||
[ evaṃ dvātriṃśato ] rājā kumāro netā ca dūtaḥ śreṣṭhī caro dvijaḥ | rājādhyakṣaśca pūrvādyāḥ kṣatriyādyāścaturdiśam || 34 ||
[ gajādhyakṣaś ] gacchatastiṣṭhato vāpi diśi yasyāṃ vyavasthitaḥ | virauti śakuno vācyastaddigjena samāgamaḥ || 35 ||
bhinnabhairavadīnārtaparuṣakṣāmajarjarāḥ | svanā neṣṭāḥ śubhāḥ śāntahṛṣṭaprakṛtipūritāḥ || 36 ||
[ svarā | śāntā ] śivā śyāmā ralā chucchuḥ piṅgalā gṛhagodhikā | sūkarī parapuṣṭā ca punnāmānaśca vāmataḥ || 37 ||
strīsaṃjñā bhāsabhaṣakakapiśrīkarṇadhikkarāḥ | śikhiśrīkaṇṭhapippīkaruruśyenāśca dakṣiṇāḥ || 38 ||
[ chikkarāḥ ] kṣveḍāsphoṭitapuṇyāhagītaśaṅkhāmbuniḥsvanāḥ | satūryādhyayanāḥ puṃvatstrīvadanyā giraḥ śubhāḥ || 39 ||
grāmau madhyamaṣaḍjau tu gāndhāraśceti śobhanāḥ | ṣaḍjamadhyamagāndhārā ṛṣabhaśca svarā hitāḥ || 40 ||
[ ṣaḍjā ] rutakīrtanadṛṣṭeṣu bhāradvājājabarhiṇaḥ | dhanyā nakulacāṣau ca saraṭaḥ pāpado'grataḥ || 41 ||
jāhakāhiśaśakroḍagodhānāṃ kīrtanaṃ śubham | rutaṃ sandarśanaṃ neṣṭaṃ pratīpaṃ vānararkṣayoḥ || 42 ||
[ ratasandarśanaṃ ] ojāḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ śastā mṛgāḥ sanakulāṇḍajāḥ | cāṣaḥ sanakulo vāmo bhṛgurāhāparāhṇataḥ || 43 ||
chikkaraḥ kūṭapūrī ca pirilī cāhni dakṣiṇāḥ | apasavyāḥ sadā śastā daṃṣṭriṇaḥ sabileśayāḥ || 44 ||
śreṣṭhe hayasite prācyāṃ śavamāṃse ca dakṣiṇe | kanyakādadhinī paścādudaggoviprasādhavaḥ || 45 ||
jālaśvacaraṇau neṣṭau prāg yāmyau śastraghātakau | paścādāsavaṣaṇḍhau ca khalāsanahalānyudak || 46 ||
karmasaṅgamayuddheṣu praveśe naṣṭamārgaṇe | yānavyastagatā grāhyā viśeṣaścātra vakṣyate || 47 ||
divā prasthānavadgrāhyāḥ kuraṅgaruruvānarāḥ | ahnaśca prathame bhāge cāṣavañjulakukkuṭāḥ || 48 ||
paścime śarvarībhāge naptṛkolūkapiṅgalāḥ | sarva eva viparyastā grāhyāḥ sārtheṣu yoṣitām || 49 ||
nṛpasandarśane grāhyaḥ praveśe'pi prayāṇavat | giryaraṇyapraveśeṣu nadīnāṃ cāvagāhane || 50 ||
[ praveśe ca ] vāmadakṣiṇagau śastau yau tu tāvagrapṛṣṭhagau | kriyādīptau vināśāya yātuḥ parighasaṃjñitau || 51 ||
tāveva tu yathābhāgaṃ praśāntarutaceṣṭitau | śakunau śakunadvārasaṃjñitāvarthasiddhaye || 52 ||
ke cittu śakunadvāramicchantyubhayataḥ sthitaiḥ | śakunairekajātīyaiḥ śāntaceṣṭāvirāvibhiḥ || 53 ||
visarjayati yadyeka ekaśca pratiṣedhati | sa virodho'śubho yāturgrāhyo yo balavattaraḥ || 54 ||
[ vā ] pūrvaṃ prāveśiko bhūtvā punaḥ prāsthāniko bhavet | sukhena siddhimācaṣṭe praveśe tadviparyayāt || 55 ||
[ prāveśeko | tadviparyayaḥ ] visarjya śakunaḥ pūrvaṃ sa eva niruṇaddhi cet | prāha yāturarermṛtyuṃ ḍamaraṃ rogameva vā || 56 ||
apasavyāstu śakunā dīptā bhayanivedinaḥ | ārambhe śakuno dīpto varṣāntastadbhayaṅkaraḥ || 57 ||
tithivāyvarkabhasthānaceṣṭādīptā yathākramam | dhanasainyabalāṅgeṣṭakarmaṇāṃ syurbhayaṅkarāḥ || 58 ||
jīmūtadhvanidīpteṣu bhayaṃ bhavati mārutāt | ubhayoḥ sandhyayordīptāḥ śastrodbhavabhayaṅkarāḥ || 59 ||
citikeśakapāleṣu mṛtyubandhavadhapradāḥ | kaṇṭakīkāṣṭhabhasmasthāḥ kalahāyāsaduḥkhadāḥ || 60 ||
aprasiddhiṃ bhayaṃ vāpi niḥsārāśmavyavasthitāḥ | kurvanti śakunā dīptāḥ śāntā yāpyaphalāstu te || 61 ||
asiddhisiddhidau jñeyau nirhārāhāra kāriṇau | sthānād ruvanvrajed yātrāṃ śaṃsate tvanyathāgamam || 62 ||
[ nirhādāhāra ] kalahaḥ svaradīpteṣu sthānadīpteṣu vigrahaḥ | uccamādau svaraṃ kṛtvā nīcaṃ paścācca doṣakṛt || 63 ||
[ moṣakṛt ] ekasthāne ruvandīptaḥ saptāhādgrāmaghātakaḥ | puradeśanarendrāṇāmṛtvardhāyanavatsarāt || 64 ||
[ grāmaghātakṛt ] sarve durbhikṣakartāraḥ svajātipiśitāśinaḥ | sarpamūṣakamārjārapṛthulomavivarjitāḥ || 65 ||
[ aśanāḥ | pṛthuroma ] parayoniṣu gacchanto maithunaṃ deśanāśanāḥ | anyatra vesarotpatternṛṇāṃ cājātimaithunāt || 66 ||
bandhaghātabhayāni syuḥ pādorūmastakāntigaiḥ | śaṣpāpaḥ piśitānnādairdoṣavarṣakṣayagrahāḥ || 67 ||
[ apaśaṣpa | varṣamoṣakṣata doṣavarṣakṣata ] krūrogradoṣaduṣṭaiśca pradhānanṛpavṛttakaiḥ | cirakālena dīptādyāsvāgamo dikṣu tannṛṇām || 68 ||
[ cirakālaiśca ] sadravyo balavāṃśca syātsadravyasyāgamo bhavet | dyutimānvinataprekṣī saumyo dāruṇavṛttakṛt || 69 ||
vidiksthaḥ śakuno dīpto vāmasthenānuvāśitaḥ | striyāḥ saṃgrahaṇaṃ prāha taddigākhyātayonitaḥ || 70 ||
śāntaḥ pañcamadīptena viruto vijayāvahaḥ | dignarāgamakārī vā doṣakṛttadviparyaye || 71 ||
vāmasavyagato madhyaḥ prāha svaparayorbhayam | maraṇaṃ kathayanti ete sarve samavirāviṇaḥ || 72 ||
[ ruto ] vṛkṣāgramadhyamūleṣu gajāśvarathikāgamaḥ | dīrghābjamuṣitāgreṣu naranauśibikāgamaḥ || 73 ||
śakaṭenonnatasthe vā chāyāsthe chatrasaṃyute | ekatripañcasaptāhātpūrvādyāsvantarāsu ca || 74 ||
[ ca | chatrasamyutaḥ ] surapatihutavahayamanirṛtivaruṇapavanendusaṅkarāḥ kramaśaḥ | prācyādyānāṃ patayo diśaḥ pumāṃso'ṅganā vidiśaḥ || 75 ||
tarutālīvidalāmbarasalilajaśaracarmapaṭṭalekhāḥ syuḥ | dvātriṃśatpravibhakte dikcakre teṣu kāryāṇi || 76 ||
vyāyāmaśikhinikūjitakalahāmbhonigaḍamantragośabdāḥ | varṇāstu raktapītakakṛṣṇasitāḥ koṇagā miśrāḥ || 77 ||
[ ca ] cihnaṃ dhvajo dagdhamatha śmaśānaṃ darī jalaṃ parvatayajñaghoṣāḥ | eteṣu saṃyogabhayāni vindyādanyāni vā sthānavikalpitāni || 78 ||
strīṇāṃ vikalpā bṛhatī kumārī vyaṅgā vigandhā tvatha nīlavastrā | kustrī pradīrghā vidhavā ca tāśca saṃyogacintā parivedikāḥ syuḥ || 79 ||
pṛcchāsu rūpyakanakāturabhāminīnāṃ meṣāvyayānamakhagokulasaṃśrayāsu | nyagrodharaktatarurodhrakakīcakākhyāścūtadrumāḥ khadirabilvanagārjunāśca || 80 ||

Chapter 86: śākune'ntaracakrādhyāyaḥ [ntaracakra-adhyāya]

aindryāṃ diśi śāntāyāṃ viruvannṛpasaṃśritāgamaṃ vakti | pūjālābhaṃ maṇiratnadravyasamprāptim || 1 ||
[ śakuniḥ ] tadanantaradiśi kanakāgamo bhavedvāñchitārthasiddhiśca | āyudhadhanapūgaphalāgamastṛtīye bhavedbhāge || 2 ||
snigdhadvijasya sandarśanaṃ caturthe tathāhitāgneśca | koṇe'nujīvibhikṣupradarśanaṃ kanakalohāptiḥ || 3 ||
yāmyenādye nṛpaputradarśanaṃ siddhirabhimatasyāptiḥ | parataḥ strīdharmāptiḥ sarṣapayavalabdhirapyuktā || 4 ||
koṇāccaturthakhaṇḍe labdhirdravyasya pūrvanaṣṭasya | yadvā tadvā phalamapi yātrāyāṃ prāpnuyād yātā || 5 ||
yātrāsiddhiḥ samadakṣiṇena śikhimahiṣakukkuṭāptiśca | yāmyāddvitīyabhāge cāraṇasaṅgaḥ śubhaṃ prītiḥ || 6 ||
ūrdhvaṃ siddhiḥ kaivartasaṅgamo mīnatittirādyāptiḥ | pravrajitadarśanaṃ tatpare ca pakvānnaphalalabdhiḥ || 7 ||
nairṛtyāṃ strīlābhasturagālaṅkāradūtalekhāptiḥ | parato'sya carmatatśilpidarśanaṃ carmamayalabdhiḥ || 8 ||
vānarabhikṣuśravaṇāvalokanaṃ nairṛtāttṛtīyāṃśe | phalakusumadantaghaṭitāgamaśca koṇāccaturthāṃśe || 9 ||
vāruṇyāmarṇavajātaratnavaidūryamaṇimayaprāptiḥ | parato'taḥ śabaravyādhacaurasaṅgaḥ piśitalabdhiḥ || 10 ||
[ vaiḍūrya ] parato'pi darśanaṃ vātarogiṇāṃ candanāguruprāptiḥ | āyudhapustakalabdhistadvṛttisamāgamaścordhvam || 11 ||
vāyavye phenakacāmaraurṇikāptiḥ sameti kāyasthaḥ | mṛnmayalābho'nyasminvaitālikaḍiṇḍibhāṇḍānām || 12 ||
vāyavyācca tṛtīye mitreṇa samāgamo dhanaprāptiḥ | vastrāśvāptirataḥ paramiṣṭasuhṛtsamprayogaśca || 13 ||
dadhitaṇḍulalājānāṃ labdhirudagdarśanaṃ ca viprasya | arthāvāptiranantaramupagacchati sārthavāhaśca || 14 ||
veśyāvaṭudāsasamāgamaḥ pare śuklapuṣpaphalalabdhiḥ | ata ūrdhvaṃ citrakarasya darśanaṃ citravastrāptiḥ || 15 ||
[ śuṣka | ataḥ paraṃ | vastrasamprāptiḥ ] aiśānyāṃ devalakopasaṅgamo dhānyaratnapaśulabdhiḥ | prākprathame vastrāptiḥ samāgamaścāpi bandhakyā || 16 ||
rajakena samāyogo jalajadravyāgamaśca parato'taḥ | hastyupajīvisamājaścāsmāddhanahastilabdhiśca || 17 ||
dvātriṃśatpravibhaktaṃ dikcakraṃ vāstuvatsanemyuktam | aranābhisthairantaḥ phalāni navadhā vikalpyāni || 18 ||
[ vāstubandhane apyuktam ] nābhisthe bandhusuhṛtsamāgamastuṣṭiruttamā bhavati | prāg raktapaṭṭavastrāgamastvare nṛpatisaṃyogaḥ || 19 ||
āgneye kaulikatakṣapārikarmāśvasūtasaṃyogaḥ | labdhiśca tatkṛtānāṃ dravyāṇāmaśvalabdhirvā || 20 ||
nemībhāgaṃ buddhvā nābhībhāgaṃ ca dakṣiṇe yo'raḥ | dhārmikajanasaṃyogastatra bhaveddharmalābhaśca || 21 ||
usrākrīḍakakāpālikāgamo nairṛte samuddiṣṭaḥ | vṛṣabhasya cātra labdhirmāṣakulatthādyamaśanaṃ ca || 22 ||
aparasyāṃ diśi yo'rastatrāsaktiḥ kṛṣīvalairbhavati | sāmudradravyasusārakācaphalamadyalabdhiśca || 23 ||
bhāravahatakṣabhikṣukasandarśanamapi ca vāyudiksaṃsthe | tilakakusumasya labdhiḥ sanāgapunnāgakusumasya || 24 ||
kauberyāṃ diśi yo'rastatrastho vittalābhamākhyāti | bhāgavatena samāgamanamācaṣṭe pītavastraiśca || 25 ||
[ śakunaḥ śāntāyāṃ | samāgamam ] aiśāne vratayuktā vanitā sandarśanaṃ samupayāti | labdhiśca parijñeyā kṛṣṇāyaḥ śastraghaṇṭānām || 26 ||
[ kṛṣṇāyovastra ] yāmye'ṣṭāṃśe paścāddviṣaṭtrisaptāṣṭameṣu madhyaphalā | saumyena ca dvitīye śeṣeṣvatiśobhanā yātrā || 27 ||
abhyantare tu nābhyāṃ śubhaphaladā bhavati ṣaṭsu cāreṣu | vāyavyānairṛtayorarayoḥ kleśāvahā yātrā || 28 ||
[ ?ubhayyoḥ ] śāntāsu dikṣu phalamidamuktaṃ dīptāsvato'bhidhāsyāmi | aindryāṃ bhayaṃ narendrātsamāgamaścaiva śātrūṇām || 29 ||
tadanantaradiśi nāśaḥ kanakasya bhayaṃ suvarṇakārāṇām | arthakṣayastṛtīye kalahaḥ śastraprakopaśca || 30 ||
agnibhayaṃ ca caturthe bhayamāgneye ca bhavati caurebhyaḥ | koṇādapi dvitīye dhanakṣayo nṛpasutavināśaḥ || 31 ||
pramadāgarbhavināśastṛtīyabhāge bhaveccaturthe ca | hairaṇyakakārukayoḥ pradhvaṃsaḥ śastrakopaśca || 32 ||
atha pañcame nṛpabhayaṃ mārīmṛtadarśanaṃ ca vaktavyam | ṣaṣṭhe tu bhayaṃ jñeyaṃ gandharvāṇāṃ saḍombānām || 33 ||
dhīvaraśākunikānāṃ saptamabhāgādbhayaṃ bhavati dīpte | bhojanavighāta ukto nirgranthabhayaṃ ca tatparataḥ || 34 ||
[ bhāge ] kalaho nairṛtabhāge raktasrāvo'tha śastrakopaśca | aparādye carmakṛtaṃ vinaśyate carmakārabhayam || 35 ||
tadanantaraṃ parivrāṭśravaṇabhayaṃ tatpare tvanaśanabhayam | vṛṣṭibhayaṃ vāruṇye śvataskarāṇāṃ bhayaṃ parataḥ || 36 ||
[ tadanantare ] vāyugrastavināśaḥ pare pare śastrapustavārtānām | koṇe pustakanāśaḥ pare viṣastenavāyubhayam || 37 ||
[ vārttānām ] parato vittavināśo mitraiḥ saha vigrahaśca vijñeyaḥ | tasyāsanne'śvavadho bhayamapi ca purodhasaḥ proktam || 38 ||
goharaṇaśastraghātāv udakpare sārthaghātadhananāśau | āsanne ca śvabhayaṃ vrātyadvijadāsagaṇikānām || 39 ||
aiśānasyāsanne citrāmbaracitrakṛdbhayaṃ proktam | aiśāne tvagnibhayaṃ dūṣaṇamapyuttamastrīṇām || 40 ||
prāktasyaivāsanne duḥkhotpattiḥ striyā vināśaśca | bhayamūrdhvaṃ rajakānāṃ vijñeyaṃ kācchikānāṃ ca || 41 ||
hastyārohabhayaṃ syāddviradavināśaśca maṇḍalasamāptau | abhyantare tu dīpte patnīmaraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ pūrve || 42 ||
śastrānalaprakopāgneye vājimaraṇaśilpibhayam | yāmye dharmavināśo'pare agnyavaskandacokṣavadhāḥ || 43 ||
[ vināśaḥ pare ] apare tu karmiṇāṃ bhayamatha koṇe cānile kharoṣṭravadhaḥ | atraiva manuṣyāṇāṃ visūcikāviṣabhayaṃ bhavati || 44 ||
[ viśūcikā ] udagarthaviprapīḍā diśyaiśānyāṃ tu cittasantāpaḥ | grāmīṇagopapīḍā ca tatra nābhyāṃ tathātmavadhaḥ || 45 ||

Chapter 87: virutādhyāyaḥ [viruta-adhyāya]

śyāmāśyenaśaśaghnavañjulaśikhiśrīkarṇacakrāhvayāścāṣāṇḍīrakakhañjarīṭakaśukadhvāṅkṣāḥ kapotāstrayaḥ | bhāradvājakulālakukkuṭakharā hārītagṛdhrau kapiḥ pheṇṭaḥ kukkuṭapūrṇakūṭacaṭakāḥ proktā divāsañcarāḥ || 1 ||
[ trayāḥ | caṭakāśca uktā ] lomāśikā piṅgalacchippikākhyau | valgulyulūkau śaśakaśca rātrau | sarve svakālotkramacāriṇaḥ syur 87.02ddeśasya nāśāya nṛpāntadā vā || 2 ||
hayanarabhujagoṣṭradvīpisiṃharkṣagodhā vṛkanakulakuraṅgaśvājagovyāghrahaṃsāḥ | pṛṣatamṛgaśṛgālaśvāvidākhyānyapuṣṭā dyuniśamapi biḍālaḥ sārasaḥ sūkaraśca || 3 ||
bhaṣakūṭapūrikurabakakarāyikāḥ pūrṇakūṭasaṇjñāḥ syuḥ | nāmānyulūkaceṭyāḥ piṅgalikā pecikā hakkā || 4 ||
[ kūṭapūri ] kapotakī ca śyāmā vañjulakaḥ kīrtyate khadiracañcuḥ | chucchundarī nṛpasutā vāleyo gardabhaḥ proktaḥ || 5 ||
srotastaḍāgabhedyaikaputrakaḥ kalahakārikā ca ralā | bhṛṅgāravacca viruvati niśi bhūmau dvyaṅgulaśarīrā || 6 ||
[ taḍāgabhedyeka | vāśati ] durbaliko bhāṇḍīkaḥ prācyānāṃ dakṣiṇaḥ praśasto'sau | dhikkāro mṛgajātiḥ kṛkavākuḥ kukkuṭaḥ proktaḥ || 7 ||
gartākukkuṭakasya prathitaṃ tu kulālakukkuṭo nāma | gṛhagodhiketi saṃjñā vijñeyā kuḍyamatsyasya || 8 ||
divyo dhanvana uktaḥ kroḍaḥ syātsūkaro'tha gaurusrā | śvā sārameya ukto jātyā caṭikā ca sūkarikā || 9 ||
evaṃ deśe deśe tadvidbhyaḥ samupalabhya nāmāni | śakunarutajñānārthaṃ śāstre sañcitya yojyāni || 10 ||
[ sañcintya ] vañjulakarutaṃ tittiḍiti dīptamatha kilkilīti tatpūrṇam | śyenaśukagṛdhrakaṅkāḥ prakṛteranyasvarā dīptāḥ || 11 ||
yānāsanaśayyānilayanaṃ kapotasya sadmaviśanaṃ vā | aśubhapradaṃ narāṇāṃ jātivibhedena kālo'nyaḥ || 12 ||
āpāṇḍurasya varṣāccitrakapotasya caiva ṣaṇmāsāt | kuṅkumadhūmrasya phalaṃ sadyaḥ pākaṃ kapotasya || 13 ||
ciciditi śabdaḥ pūrṇaḥ śyāmāyāḥ śūliśūl iti ca dhanyaḥ | cacceti dīptaḥ syātsvapriyalābhāya cikcigiti || 14 ||
[ yogāya ] hārītasya tu śabdo gugguḥ pūrṇo'pare pradīptāḥ syuḥ | svaravaicitryaṃ sarvaṃ bhāradvājyāḥ śubhaṃ proktam || 15 ||
kiṣkiṣiśabdaḥ pūrṇaḥ karāyikāyāḥ śubhaḥ kahakaheti | kṣamāya kevalaṃ karakareti na tvarthasiddhikaraḥ || 16 ||
[ kṣemāya ] koṭuklīti kṣemyaḥ svaraḥ kaṭuklīti vṛṣṭaye tasyāḥ | aphalaḥ koṭikilīti ca dīptaḥ khalu guṃ kṛtaḥ śabdaḥ || 17 ||
śastraṃ vāme darśanaṃ divyakasya siddhirjñeyā hastamātrocchritasya | tasminneva pronnatasthe śarīrāddhātrī vaśyaṃ sāgarāntābhyupaiti || 18 ||
[ śastam ] phaṇito'bhimukhāgamo'risaṅgaṃ kathayati bandhuvadhātyayaṃ ca yātuḥ | atha vā samupaiti savyabhāgāt na sa siddhyai kuśalo gamāgame ca || 19 ||
[ bandha ] abjeṣu mūrdhasu ca vājigajoragāṇāṃ rājyapradaḥ kuśalakṛcchuciśādvaleṣu | bhasmāsthikāṣṭhatuṣakeśatṛṇeṣu duḥkhaṃ dṛṣṭaḥ karoti khalu khañjanako'bdamekam || 20 ||
kilikilkili tittirasvanaḥ śāntaḥ śastaphalo'nyathāparaḥ | śaśako niśi vāmapārśvago vāśacchastaphalo nigadyate || 21 ||
kilikilivirutaṃ kapeḥ pradīptaṃ na śubhaphalapradamuddiśanti yātuḥ | śubhamapi kathayanti cugluśabdaṃ kapisadṛśaṃ ca kulālakukkuṭasya || 22 ||
pūrṇānanaḥ kṛmipataṅgapipīlakādyaiścāṣaḥ pradakṣiṇamupaiti narasya yasya | khe svastikaṃ yadi karotyatha vā yiyāsostasyārthalābhamacirātsumahatkaroti || 23 ||
cāṣasya kākena virudhyataścetparājayo dakṣiṇabhāgagasya | vadhaḥ prayātasya tadā narasya viparyaye tasya jayaḥ pradiṣṭaḥ || 24 ||
keketi pūrṇakuṭavad yadi vāmapārśve cāṣaḥ karoti virutaṃ jayakṛttadā syāt | krekreti tasya virutaṃ na śivāya dīptaṃ sandarśanaṃ śubhadamasya sadaiva yātuḥ || 25 ||
[ krakreti ] aṇḍīrakaṣṭīti rutena pūrṇaṣṭiṭṭiṭṭiśabdena tu dīpta uktaḥ | pheṇṭaḥ śubho dakṣiṇabhāgasaṃstho na vāśite tasya kṛto viśeṣaḥ || 26 ||
śrīkarṇarutaṃ tu dakṣiṇe | kvakvakveti śubhaṃ prakīrtitam | madhyaṃ khalu cikcikīti yañśeṣaṃ sarvamuśanti niṣphalam || 27 ||
durbalerapi cirilvirilviti proktamiṣṭaphaladaṃ hi vāmataḥ | vāmataśca yadi dakṣiṇaṃ vrajet 87.28d kāryasiddhimacireṇa yacchati || 28 ||
cikcikivāśitameva tu kṛtvā dakṣiṇabhāgamupaiti tu vāmāt | kṣemakṛdeva na sādhayate'rthānvyatyayago vadhabandhabhayāya || 29 ||
krakreti ca sārikā drutaṃ tretre vāpyabhayā virauti yā | sā vakti yiyāsato'cirādgātrebhyaḥ kṣatajasya visrutim || 30 ||
[ gātrebhya ] pheṇṭakasya vāmataścirilvirilviti svanaḥ | śobhano nigadyate pradīpta ucyate'paraḥ || 31 ||
śreṣṭhaṃ kharaṃ sthāsnumuśanti vāmamoṃkāraśabdena hitaṃ ca yātuḥ | ato'paraṃ gardabhanāditaṃ yatsarvāśrayaṃ tatpravadanti dīptam || 32 ||
[ ataḥ paraṃ ] ākārarāvī samṛgaḥ kuraṅga okārarāvī pṛṣataśca pūrṇaḥ | ye'nye svarāste kathitāḥ pradīptāḥ pūrṇāḥ śubhāḥ pāpaphalāḥ pradīptāḥ || 33 ||
bhītā ruvanti kukukukviti tāmracūḍāstyaktvā rutāni bhayadānyaparāṇi rātrau | svasthaiḥ svabhāvavirutāni niśāvasāne tārāṇi rāṣṭrapurapārthivavṛddhidāni || 34 ||
nānāvidhāni virutāni hi chippikāyāstasyāḥ śubhāḥ kulukulurna śubhāstu śeṣāḥ | yāturbiḍālavirutaṃ na śubhaṃ sadaiva gostu kṣutaṃ maraṇameva karoti yātuḥ || 35 ||
huṃhuṃguglugiti priyāmabhilaṣan krośatyulūko mudā pūrṇaḥ syādgurulu pradīptamapi ca jñeyaṃ sadā kiskisi | vijñeyaḥ kalaho yadā balabalaṃ tasya asakṛdvāśitaṃ doṣāyaiva ṭaṭaṭṭaṭeti na śubhāḥ śeṣāstu dīpta svarāḥ || 36 ||
[ tasyāḥ | dīptāḥ ] sārasakūjitamiṣṭaphalaṃ tad yad yugapadvirutaṃ mithunasya | ekarutaṃ na śubhaṃ yadi vā syādekarute pravirauti cireṇa || 37 ||
[ pratirauti ] cirilvirilviti svaraiḥ śubhaṃ karoti piṅgalāḥ | ato'pare tu ye svarāḥ pradīptasaṃjñitāstu te || 38 ||
[ piṅgalā ] iśivirutaṃ gamanapratiṣedhi kuśukuśu cetkalahaṃ prakaroti | abhimatakāryagatiṃ ca yathā sā kathayati taṃ ca vidhiṃ kathayāmi || 39 ||
dināntasandhyāsamaye nivāsamāgamya tasyāḥ prayataśca vṛkṣam | devān samabhyarcya pitāmahādīnnavāmbarastaṃ ca taruṃ sugandhaiḥ || 40 ||
eko niśīthe'naladiksthitaśca divyetaraistāṃ śapathairniyojya | pṛcched yathācintitamarthamevamanena mantreṇa yathāśṛṇoti || 41 ||
viddhi bhadre mayā yattvamimamarthaṃ pracoditā | kalyāṇi sarvavacasāṃ veditrī tvaṃ prakīrtyase || 42 ||
āpṛcche'dya gamiṣyāmi veditaśca punastvaham | prātarāgamya pṛcche tvāmāgneyīṃ diśamāśritaḥ || 43 ||
pracodayāmyahaṃ yattvāṃ tanme vyākhyātumarhasi | svaceṣṭitena kalyāṇi yathā vedmi nirākulam || 44 ||
ityevamukte tarumūrdhagāyāścirilvirilvīti rute'rthasiddhiḥ | atyākulatvaṃ diśikāraśabde kucākucetyevamudāhṛte vā || 45 ||
[ avyākulatvam ] avākpradāne'pi hitārthasiddhiḥ | pūrvoktadikcakraphalairato'nyat | vācyaṃ phalaṃ cottamamadhyanīcaśākhāsthitāyāṃ varamadhyanīcam || 46 ||
[ vihita ] diṅmaṇḍale'bhyantarabāhyabhāge phalāni vindyādgṛhagodhikāyāḥ | chucchundarī cicciḍiti pradīptā | pūrṇā tu sā tittiḍiti svanena || 47 ||

Chapter 88: śvacakrādhyāyaḥ [śvacakra-adhyāya]

nṛturagakarikumbhaparyāṇasakṣīravṛkṣeṣṭakāsañcayacchatraśayyāsanolūkhalāni dhvajaṃ cāmaraṃ śādvalaṃ puṣpitaṃ vā pradeśaṃ yadā śvāvamūtryāgrato yāti yātustadā kāryasiddhirbhavedārdrake gomaye miṣṭabhojyāgamaḥ śuṣkasammūtraṇe śuṣkamannaṃ guḍo modakāvāptirevātha vā | atha viṣatarukaṇṭhakīkāṣṭhapāṣāṇaśuṣkadrumāsthiśmaśānāni mūtryāvahatyātha vā yāyino'gresaro'niṣṭamākhyāti śayyākulālādi bhāṇḍānyabhuktānyabhinnāni vā mūtrayan kanyakādoṣakṛdbhujyamānāni cedduṣṭatāṃ tadgṛhiṇyāstathā syādupānatphalaṃ gostu sammūtraṇe'varṇajaḥ saṅkaraḥ ||
gamanamukhamupānahaṃ sampragṛhyopatiṣṭhed yadā syād tadā siddhaye māṃsapūrṇānane'rthāptirādreṇa cāsthnā śubhaṃ sāgnyalātena śuṣkeṇa cāsthnā gṛhītena mṛtyuḥ praśāntolmukenābhighāto'tha puṃsaḥ śirohastapādādi vaktre bhuvo'bhyāgamo vastracīrādibhirvyāpadaḥ ke cidāhuḥ savastre śubham | praviśati tu gṛhaṃ saśuṣkāsthivaktre pradhānasya tasminvadhaḥ śṛṅkhalāśīrṇavallīvaratrādi vā bandhanaṃ copagṛhyopatiṣṭhed yadā syāttadā bandhanaṃ leḍhi pādau vidhunvan svakarṇāv uparyākramaṃścāpi vighnāya yāturvirodhe virodhastathā svāṅgakaṇḍūyane syātsvapaṃścordhvapādaḥ sadā doṣakṛt || 1 ||
[ varṇajaḥ | hyāgamo ] sūryodaye'rkābhimukho virauti grāmasya madhye yadi sārameyaḥ | eko yadā vā bahavaḥ sametāḥ śaṃsanti deśādhipamanyamāśu || 2 ||
sūryonmukhaḥ śvānaladiksthitaśca caurānalatrāsakaro'cireṇa | madhyāhnakāle'nalamṛtyuśaṃsī saśoṇitaḥ syātkalaho'parāhṇe || 3 ||
ruvandineśābhimukho'stakāle kṛṣībalānāṃ bhayamāśu datte | pradoṣakāle'niladiṅmukhaśca datte bhayaṃ mārutataskarottham || 4 ||
[ dhatte | tu | dhatte ] udaṅmukhaścāpi niśārdhakāle vipravyathāṃ goharaṇaṃ ca śāsti | niśāvasāne śivadinmukhaśca kanyābhidūṣānalagarbhapātān || 5 ||
uccaiḥ svarāḥ syustṛṇakūṭasaṃsthāḥ prāsādaveśmottamasaṃsthitā vā | varṣāsu vṛṣṭiṃ kathayanti tīvrāmanyatra mṛtyuṃ dahanaṃ rujaśca || 6 ||
prāvṛṭkāle'vagrahe'mbho'vagāhya pratyāvartai recakaiścāpyabhīkṣaṇam | ādhunvanto vā pibantaśca toyaṃ vṛṣṭiṃ kurvantyantare dvādaśāhāt || 7 ||
[ pratyāvṛttai | abhīkṣṇam ] dvāre śiro nyasya bahiḥ śarīraṃ rorūyate śvā gṛhiṇīṃ vilokya | rogapradaḥ syādatha mandirāntarbahirmukho vakti ca bandhakīṃ tām || 8 ||
[ śaṃsati ] kuḍyamutkirati veśmano yadā tatra khānakabhayaṃ bhavettadā | goṣṭhamutkirati gograhaṃ vadeddhānyalabdhimapi dhānyabhūmiṣu || 9 ||
ekenākṣṇā sāśruṇā dīnadṛṣṭirmandāhāro duḥkhakṛttadgṛhasya | gobhiḥ sākaṃ krīḍamāṇaḥ subhikṣaṃ kṣemārogyaṃ cābhidhatte mudaṃ ca || 10 ||
[ sārdhaṃ ] vāmaṃ jighrejjānu vittāgamāya strībhiḥ sākaṃ vigraho dakṣiṇaṃ cet | ūruṃ vāmaṃ cendriyārthopabhogaḥ savyaṃ jighrediṣṭamitrairvirodhaḥ || 11 ||
[ upabhogāḥ ] pādau jighred yāyinaścedayātrāṃ prāhārthāptiṃ vāñchitāṃ niścalasya | sthānasthasyopānahau cedvijighretkṣipraṃ yātrāṃ sārameyaḥ karoti || 12 ||
ubhayorapi jighraṇe hi bāhvorvijñeyo ripucaurasamprayogaḥ | atha bhasmani gopayīta bhakṣānmāṃsāsthīni ca śīghramagnikopaḥ || 13 ||
[ vā ca ] grāme bhaṣitvā ca bahiḥ śmaśāne 88.14b bhaṣanti ceduttamapuṃ vināśaḥ | yiyāsataścābhimukho virauti | yadā tadā śvā niruṇaddhi yātrām || 14 ||
ukāravarṇe virute arthasiddhirokāravarṇena ca vāmapārśve | vyākṣepamaukārarutena vindyānniṣedhakṛtsarvarutaiśca paścāt || 15 ||
[ varṇena rute ] khaṃkheti coccaiśca muhurmuhurye ruvanti daṇḍairiva tāḍyamānāḥ | śvāno'bhidhāvanti ca maṇḍalena te śūnyatāṃ mṛtyubhayaṃ ca kuryuḥ || 16 ||
[ saṅkheti ] prakāśya dantānyadi leḍhi sṛkviṇī tadāśanaṃ mṛṣṭamuśanti tadvidaḥ | yadānanaṃ leḍhi punarna sṛkviṇī pravṛttabhojye'pi tadānnavighnakṛt || 17 ||
[ miṣṭam | ca avalihen ] grāmasya madhye yadi vā purasya bhaṣanti saṃhatya muhurmuhurye | te kleśamākhyānti tadīśvarasya śvāraṇyasaṃstho mṛgavadvicintyaḥ || 18 ||
vṛkṣopage krośati toyapātaḥ syādindrakīle sacivasya pīḍā | vāyorgṛhe sasyabhayaṃ gṛhāntaḥ pīḍā purasyaiva ca gopurasthe || 19 ||
bhayaṃ ca śayyāsu tadīśvarāṇāṃ yāne bhaṣanto bhayadāśca paścāt | athāpasavyā janasanniveśe bhayaṃ bhaṣantaḥ kathayantyarīṇām || 20 ||

Chapter 89: śivārutādhyāyaḥ [śivāruta-adhyāya]

śvabhiḥ śṛgālāḥ sadṛśāḥ phalena viśeṣa eṣāṃ śiśire madāptiḥ | hūhū rutānte parataśca ṭāṭā pūrṇaḥ svaro'nye kathitāḥ pradīptāḥ || 1 ||
lomāśikāyāḥ khalu kakkaśabdaḥ pūrṇaḥ svabhāvaprabhavaḥ sa tasyāḥ | ye'nye svarāste prakṛterapetāḥ sarve ca dīptā iti sampradiṣṭāḥ || 2 ||
pūrvodīcyoḥ śivā śastā śāntā sarvatra pūjitā | dhūmitābhimukhī hanti svaradīptā digīśvarān || 3 ||
rājā kumāro netā ca dūtaḥ śreṣṭhī caro dvijaḥ | gajādhyakṣaśca pūrvādyāḥ kṣatriyādyāścaturdiśam || 4 ||
sarvadikṣvaśubhā dīptā viśeṣeṇāhnyaśobhanā | pure sainye'pasavyā ca kaṣṭā sūryonmukhī śivā || 5 ||
yāhītyagnibhayaṃ śāsti ṭāṭeti mṛtavedikā | dhigdhigduṣkṛtimācaṣṭe sajvālā deśanāśinī || 6 ||
[ duṣkṛtam ] naiva dāruṇatāmeke sajvālāyāḥ pracakṣate | arkādyanalavattasyā vaktraṃ lālāsvabhāvataḥ || 7 ||
anyapratirutā yāmyā sodbandhamṛtaśaṃsinī | vāruṇyanurutā saiva śaṃsate salile mṛtam || 8 ||
akṣobhaḥ śravaṇaṃ ceṣṭaṃ dhanaprāptiḥ priyāgamaḥ | kṣobhaḥ pradhānabhedaśca vāhanānāṃ ca sampadaḥ || 9 ||
phalamā saptamādetadagrāhyaṃ parato rutam | yāmyāyāṃ tadviparyastaṃ phalaṃ ṣaṭpañcamādṛte || 10 ||
yā romāñcaṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ śakṛnmūtraṃ ca vājinām | rāvāttrāsaṃ ca janayetsā śivā na śivapradā || 11 ||
maunaṃ gatā pratirute naradviradavājibhiḥ | yā śivā sā śivaṃ sainye pure vā samprayacchati || 12 ||
[ vājinām ] bhebheti śivā bhayaṅkarī bhobho vyāpadamādiśecca sā | mṛtibandhanivedinī phiphe hūhū cātmahitā śivā svare || 13 ||
[ phipha ] śāntā tvavarṇātparamāruvantī ṭāṭāmudīrṇāmiti vāśyamānā | ṭeṭe ca pūrvaṃ parataśca thethe tasyāḥ svatuṣṭiprabhavaṃ rutaṃ tat || 14 ||
[ pavanau ruvantī ] uccairghoraṃ varṇamuccārya pūrvaṃ paścātkrośetkroṣṭukasyānurūpam | yā sā kṣemaṃ prāha vittasya cāptiṃ saṃyogaṃ vā proṣitena priyeṇa || 15 ||

Chapter 90: mṛgaceṣṭitādhyāyaḥ [mṛgaceṣṭita-adhyāya]

sīmāgatā vanyamṛgā ruvantaḥ sthitā vrajanto'tha samāpatantaḥ | sampratyatītaiṣyabhayāni dīptāḥ kurvanti śūnyaṃ parito bhramantaḥ || 1 ||
te grāmyasattvairanuvāśyamānā bhayāya rodhāya bhavanti vanyaiḥ | dvābhyāmapi pratyanuvāśitāste vandigrahāyai ca mṛgā ruvanti || 2 ||
[ grahāyaiva | bhavanti ] vanye sattve dvārasaṃsthe purasya rodho vācyaḥ sampraviṣṭe vināśaḥ | sūte mṛtyuḥ syādbhayaṃ saṃsthite ca gehaṃ yāte bandhanaṃ sampradiṣṭam || 3 ||

Chapter 91: gaveṅgitādhyāyaḥ [gaveṅgita-adhyāya]

gāvo dīnāḥ pārthivasyāśivāya pādairbhūmiṃ kuṭṭayantyaśca rogān | mṛtyuṃ kurvantyaśrupūrṇāyatākṣyaḥ patyurbhītāstaskarānāruvantyaḥ || 1 ||
akāraṇe krośati cedanartho bhayāya rātrau vṛṣabhaḥ śivāya | bhṛśaṃ niruddhā yadi makṣikābhistadāśu vṛṣṭiṃ saramātmajairvā || 2 ||
āgacchantyo veśma bambhāraveṇa saṃsevantyo goṣṭhavṛddhyai gavāṃ gāḥ | ārdrāṅgyo vā hṛṣṭaromṇyaḥ prahṛṣṭā dhanyā gāvaḥ syurmahiṣyo'pi caivam || 3 ||

Chapter 92: aśveṅgitādhyāyaḥ [aśveṅgita-adhyāya]

utsargānna śubhadamāsanātparasthaṃ vāme ca jvalanamato'paraṃ praśastam | sarvāṅgajvalanamavṛddhidaṃ hayānāṃ dve varṣe dahanakaṇāśca dhūpanaṃ vā || 1 ||
[ āsanāparasthaṃ ] antaḥpuraṃ nāśamupaiti meḍhre kośaḥ kṣayaṃ yātyudare pradīpte | pāyau ca pucche ca parājayaḥ syādvaktrottamāṅgajvalane jayaśca || 2 ||
skandhāsanāṃsajvalanaṃ jayāya bandhāya pādajvalanaṃ pradiṣṭam | lalāṭavakṣo'kṣibhuje ca dhūmaḥ parābhavāya jvalanaṃ jayāya || 3 ||
[ akṣibhujeṣu ] nāsāpuṭaprothaśiro'śrupātanetre ca rātrau jvalanaṃ jayāya | palāśatāmrāsitakarburāṇāṃ nityaṃ śukābhasya sitasya ceṣṭam || 4 ||
[ netreṣu ] pradveṣo yavasāmbhasāṃ prapatanaṃ svedo nimittādvinā kampo vā vadanācca raktapatanaṃ dhūmasya vā sambhavaḥ | asvapnaśca virodhināṃ niśi divā nidrālasadhyānatā sādo'dhomukhatā viceṣṭitamidaṃ neṣṭaṃ smṛtaṃ vājinām || 5 ||
[ virodhitā ] ārohaṇamanyavājināṃ paryāṇādiyutasya vājinaḥ | upavāhyaturaṅgamasya vā kalpasyaiva vipannaśobhanā || 6 ||
krauñcavad ripuvadhāya hreṣitaṃ | grīvayā tvacalayā ca sonmukham | snigdhamuccamanunādi hṛṣṭavadgrāsaruddhavadanaiśca vājibhiḥ || 7 ||
[ heṣitaṃ ] pūrṇapātradadhivipradevatā gandhapuṣpaphalakāñcanādi vā | dravyamiṣṭamatha vā paraṃ bhaved | dhreṣatāṃ yadi samīpato jayaḥ || 8 ||
[ dheṣatāṃ ] bhakṣyapānakhalinābhinandinaḥ patyuraupayikanandino'tha vā | savyapārśvagatadṛṣṭayo'tha vā vāñchitārthaphaladāsturaṅgamāḥ || 9 ||
vāmaiśca pādairabhitāḍayanto mahīṃ pravāsāya bhavanti bhartuḥ | sandhyāsu dīptāmavalokayanto hreṣanti cedbandhaparājayāya || 10 ||
[ heṣanti ] atīva hreṣanti kiranti vālānnidrāratāśca pravadanti yātrām | romatyajo dīnakharasvarāśca pāṃśūn grasantaśca bhayāya dṛṣṭāḥ || 11 ||
[ heṣanti ] samudgavaddakṣiṇapārśvaśāyinaḥ padaṃ samutkṣipya ca dakṣiṇaṃ sthitāḥ | jayāya śeṣeṣvapi vāhaneṣvidaṃ phalaṃ yathāsambhavamādiśedbudhaḥ || 12 ||
ārohati kṣitipatau vinayopapanno yātrānugo'nyaturagaṃ pratihreṣate ca | vaktreṇa vā spṛśati dakṣiṇamātmapārśvaṃ yo'śvaḥ sa bharturacirātpracinoti lakṣmīm || 13 ||
[ pratiheṣate ] muhurmuhurmūtraśakṛtkaroti na tāḍyamāno'pyanulomayāyī | akāryabhīto'śruvilocanaśca śivaṃ na bhartusturago'bhidhatte || 14 ||
