[ śubham ] uktamidaṃ hayaceṣṭitamata ūrdhvaṃ dantināṃ pravakṣyāmi | teṣāṃ tu dantakalpanabhaṅgamlānādiceṣṭābhiḥ || 15 ||

Chapter 93: hasticeṣṭitādhyāyaḥ [hasticeṣṭita-adhyāya]

dantasya mūlaparidhiṃ dvirāyataṃ prohya kalpayeccheṣam | adhikamanūpacarāṇāṃ nyūnaṃ giricāriṇāṃ kiñcit || 1 ||
śrīvatsavardhamānacchatradhvajacāmarānurūpeṣu | chede dṛṣṭeṣvārogyavijayadhanavṛddhisaukhyāni || 2 ||
praharaṇasadṛśeṣu jayo nandyāvarte pranaṣṭadeśāptiḥ | loṣṭe tu labdhapūrvasya bhavati deśasya samprāptiḥ || 3 ||
strīrūpe'śvavināśo bhṛṅgāre'bhyutthite sutotpattiḥ | kumbhena nidhiprāptiryātrāvighnaṃ ca daṇḍena || 4 ||
[ svavināśo ] kṛkalāsakapibhujaṅgeṣvasubhikṣavyādhayo ripuvaśitvam | gṛdhrolūkadhvāṅkṣaśyenākāreṣu janamarakaḥ || 5 ||
[ vaśatvam ] pāśe'tha vā kabandhe nṛpamṛtyurjanavipatsrute rakte | kṛṣṇe śyāve rūkṣe durgandhe cāśubhaṃ bhavati || 6 ||
śuklaḥ samaḥ sugandhiḥ snigdhaśca śubhāvaho bhavecchedaḥ | galanamlānaphalāni ca dantasya samāni bhaṅgena || 7 ||
mūlamadhyadaśanāgrasaṃsthitā | devadaityamanujāḥ kramāttataḥ | sphītamadhyaparipelavaṃ phalaṃ 93.08d śīghramadhyacirakālasambhavam || 8 ||
dantabhaṅgaphalamatra dakṣiṇe bhūpadeśabalavidravapradam | vāmataḥ sutapurohitebhayān hanti sāṭavikadāranāyakān || 9 ||
[ ibhapān ] ādiśedubhayabhaṅgadarśanātpārthivasya sakalaṃ kulakṣayam | saumyalagnatithibhādibhiḥ śubhaṃ vardhate'śubhamato'nyathā vadet || 10 ||
[ bhavet ] kṣīramṛṣṭaphalapuṣpapādapeṣvāpagātaṭavighaṭṭitena vā | vāmamadhyaradabhaṅgakhaṇḍane śatrunāśakṛdato'nyathā param || 11 ||
[ kṣīravṛkṣa | khaṇḍanaṃ ] skhalitagatirakasmāttrastakarṇo'tidīnaḥ śvasiti mṛdu sudīrghaṃ nyastahastaḥ pṛthivyām | drutamukulitadṛṣṭiḥ svapnaśīlo vilomo bhayakṛdahitabhakṣī naikaśo'sṛgśakṛtkṛt || 12 ||
[ asṛkchakṛt ca ] valmīkasthāṇugulmakṣupatarumathanaḥ svecchayā hṛṣṭadṛṣṭiryāyād yātrānulomaṃ tvaritapadagatirvaktramunnāmya coccaiḥ | kakṣyāsannāhakāle janayati ca muhuḥ śīkaraṃ bṛṃhitaṃ vā tatkāle vā madāptirjayakṛdatha radaṃ veṣṭayandakṣiṇaṃ ca || 13 ||
[ tatkālaṃ ] praveśanaṃ vāriṇi vāraṇasya grāheṇa nāśāya bhavennṛpasya | grāhaṃ gṛhotvottaraṇaṃ nṛpasya toyātsthalaṃ vṛddhikaraṃ nṛbhartuḥ || 14 ||
[ grihītvā | dvipasya ]

Chapter 94: vāyasavirutādhyāyaḥ [vāyasaviruta-adhyāya]

prācyānāṃ dakṣiṇataḥ śubhadāḥ kākāḥ karāyikā vāmāḥ | viparītamanyadeśeṣvavadhirlokaprasiddhyaiva || 1 ||
[ śubhadaḥ | vāmā ] vaiśākhe nirupahate vṛkṣe nīḍaḥ subhikṣaśivadātā | ninditakaṇṭakiśuṣkeṣvasubhikṣabhayāni taddeśe || 2 ||
nīḍe prāk śākhāyāṃ śaradi bhavetprathamavṛṣṭiraparasyām | yāmyottarayormadhyātpradhānavṛṣṭistarorupari || 3 ||
[ madhyā ] śikhidiśi maṇḍalavṛṣṭirnairṛtyāṃ śāradasya niṣpattiḥ | pariśeṣayoḥ subhikṣaṃ mūṣakasampacca vāyavye || 4 ||
[ sampattu ] śaradarbhagulmavallīdhānyaprāsādagehanimneṣu | śūnyo bhavati sa deśaścaurānāvṛṣṭirogārtaḥ || 5 ||
dvitricatuḥ śāvatvaṃ subhikṣadaṃ pañcabhirnṛpānyatvam | aṇḍāvakiraṇamekāṇḍatāprasūtiśca na śivāya || 6 ||
caurakavarṇaiścaurāścitrairmṛtyuḥ sitaistu vahnibhayam | vikalairdurbhikṣabhayaṃ kākānāṃ nirdiśecchiśubhiḥ || 7 ||
animittasaṃhatairgrāmamadhyagaiḥ kṣudbhayaṃ praviruvadbhiḥ | rodhaścakrākārairabhighāto vargavargasthaiḥ || 8 ||
[ pravāśadbhiḥ ] abhayāśca tuṇḍapakṣaiścaraṇavighātairjanānabhibhavantaḥ | kurvanti śatruvṛddhiṃ niśi vicaranto janavināśam || 9 ||
savyena khe bhramadbhiḥ svabhayaṃ viparītamaṇḍalaiśca parāt | atyākulaṃ bhramadbhirvātodbhramo bhavati kākaiḥ || 10 ||
ūrdhvamukhāścalapakṣāḥ pathi bhayadāḥ kṣudbhayāya dhānyamuṣaḥ | senāṅgasthā yuddhaṃ parimoṣaṃ cānyabhṛtapakṣāḥ || 11 ||
bhasmāsthikeśapatrāṇi vinyasanpativadhāya śayyāyām | maṇikusumādyavahanane sutasya janmāpyathāṅganāyāśca || 12 ||
[ avahanena | janmāṅganāyāśca | janmānyathāṅganāyāś ] pūrṇānane'rthalābhaḥ sikatādhānyārdramṛtkusumapūrvaiḥ | bhayado janasaṃvāsād yadi bhāṇḍānyapanayetkākaḥ || 13 ||
vāhanaśastropānacchatrachāyāṅgakuṭṭane maraṇam | tatpūjāyāṃ pūjā viṣṭhākaraṇe'nnasamprāptiḥ || 14 ||
yaddravyamupanayettasya labdhirapaharati cetpraṇāśaḥ syāt | pītadravyaiḥ kanakaṃ vastraṃ kārpāsikaiḥ sitaiḥ rūpyam || 15 ||
[ pītadravye | kārpāsike site ] sakṣīrārjunavañjulakūladvayapulinagā ruvantaśca | prāvṛṣi vṛṣṭiṃ durdinamanṛtau snātāśca pāṃśujalaiḥ || 16 ||
dāruṇanādastarukoṭaropago vāyaso mahābhayadaḥ | salilamavalokya viruvanvṛṣṭikaro'bdānurāvī ca || 17 ||
dīptodvigno viṭape vikuṭṭayanvahnikṛdvidhutapakṣaḥ | raktadravyaṃ dagdhaṃ tṛṇakāṣṭhaṃ vā gṛhe vidadhat || 18 ||
aindryādidigavalokī sūryābhimukho ruvan gṛhe gṛhinaḥ | rājabhayacorabandhanakalahāḥ syuḥ paśubhayaṃ ceti || 19 ||
śāntāmaindrīmavalokayan ruyād rājapuruṣamitrāptiḥ | bhavati ca suvarṇalabdhiḥ śālyannaguḍāśanāptiśca || 20 ||
āgneyyāmanalājīvikayuvatipravaradhātulābhaśca | yāmye māṣakulūtthā bhojyaṃ gāndharvikairyogaḥ || 21 ||
[ kulatthā ] nairṛtyāṃ dūtāśvopakaraṇadadhitailapalalabhojyāptiḥ | vāruṇyāṃ māṃsasurāsavadhānyasamudraratnāptiḥ || 22 ||
mārutyāṃ śastrāyudhasarojavallīphalāśanāptiśca | saumyāyāṃ paramānnāśanaṃ turaṅgāmbaraprāptiḥ || 23 ||
aiśānyāṃ samprāptirghṛtapūrṇānāṃ bhavedanaḍuhaśca | evaṃ phalaṃ gṛhapatergṛhapṛṣṭhasamāśrite bhavati || 24 ||
gamane karṇasamaścetkṣemāya na kāryasiddhaye bhavati | abhimukhamupaiti yāturviruvanvinivartayed yātrām || 25 ||
vāme vāśitvādau dakṣiṇapārśve'nuvāśate yātuḥ | arthāpahārakārī tadviparīto'rthasiddhikaraḥ || 26 ||
yadi vāma eva viruvanmuhurmuhuryāyino'nulomagatiḥ | arthasya bhavati siddhyai prācyānāṃ dakṣiṇaścaivam || 27 ||
[ viruyāt ] vāmaḥ pratilomagatirviruvan gamanasya vighnakṛdbhavati | tatrasthasyaiva phalaṃ kathayati tadvāñchitaṃ gamane || 28 ||
[ vāśan ] dakṣiṇavirutaṃ kṛtvā vāme viruyād yathepsitāvāptiḥ | prativāśya puro yāyāddrutamatyarthāgamo bhavati || 29 ||
[ agre'rthāgamo'timahān ] prativāśya pṛṣṭḥato dakṣiṇena yāyāddrutaṃ kṣatajakārī | ekacaraṇo'rkamīkṣanviruvaṃśca puro rudhirahetuḥ || 30 ||
[ kṣatajakartā ] dṛṣṭvārkamekapādastuṇḍena likhed yadā svapicchāni | purato janasya mahato vadhamabhidhatte tadā balibhuk || 31 ||
sasyopete kṣetre viruvati śānte sasasyabhūlabdhiḥ | ākulaceṣṭo viruvan sīmānte kleśakṛd yātuḥ || 32 ||
susnigdhapatrapallavakusumaphalānamrasurabhimadhureṣu | sakṣīrāvraṇasaṃsthitamanojñavṛkṣeṣu cārthasiddhikaraḥ || 33 ||
[ cārthakaraḥ ] niṣpannasasyaśādvala | dhanyocchrayamaṅgalyeṣu caiva viruvandhanāgamadaḥ || 34 ||
[ śāḍvalabhavanaprāsādaharmyahariteṣu | śādvala | dhānya ] gopucchasthe valmīkage'tha vā darśanaṃ bhujaṅgasya | sadyo jvaro mahiṣage viruvati gulme phalaṃ svalpam || 35 ||
kāryasya vyāghātastṛṇakūṭe vāmage'mbusaṃsthe vā | ūrdhvāgnipluṣṭe'śanihate ca kāke vadho bhavati || 36 ||
[ asthisaṃsthe ] kaṇṭakimiśre saumye siddhiḥ kāryasya bhavati kalahaśca | kaṇṭakini bhavati kalaho vallīpariveṣṭite bandhaḥ || 37 ||
chinnāgre'ṅgacchedaḥ kalahaḥ śuṣkadrumasthite dhvāṃkṣe | purataśca pṛṣṭhato vā gomayasaṃsthe dhanaprāptiḥ || 38 ||
mṛtapuruṣāṅgāvayavasthito'bhiviruvan karoti mṛtyubhayam | bhañjannasthi ca cañcvā yadi viruvatyasthibhaṅgāya || 39 ||
[ abhivāśan | vāśaty ] rajjvasthikāṣṭhakaṇṭakiniḥsāraśiroruhānane ruvati | bhujagagadadaṃṣṭritaskaraśastrāgnibhayānyanukramaśaḥ || 40 ||
sitakusumāśucimāṃsānane'rthasiddhiryathepsitā yātuḥ | pakṣau dhunvannūrdhvānane ca vighnaṃ muhuḥ kvaṇati || 41 ||
[ dhunvanpakṣāv ] yadi śṛṅkhalāṃ varatrāṃ vallīṃ vādāya vāśate bandhaḥ | pāṣāṇasthe ca bhayaṃ kliṣṭāpūrvādhvikayutiśca || 42 ||
anyonyabhakṣasaṃkrāmitānane tuṣṭiruttamā bhavati | vijñeyaḥ strīlābho dampatyorviruvatoryugapat || 43 ||
[ vāśator ] pramadāśiropagatapūrṇakumbhasaṃsthe'ṅganārthasamprāptiḥ | ghaṭakuṭṭane sutavipadghaṭopahadane'nnasamprāptiḥ || 44 ||
skandhāvārādīnāṃ niveśasamaye ruvaṃścalatpakṣaḥ | sūcayate'nyatsthānaṃ niścalapakṣastu bhayamātram || 45 ||
[ anyasthānaṃ ] praviśadbhiḥ sainyādīn sagṛdhrakaṅkairvināmiṣaṃ dhvāṃkṣaiḥ | aviruddhaistaiḥ prītirdviṣatāṃ yuddhaṃ viruddhaiśca || 46 ||
bandhaḥ sūkarasaṃsthe paṅkākte sūkare dvike'rthāptiḥ | kṣemaṃ kharoṣṭrasaṃsthe ke citprāhurvadhaṃ tu khare || 47 ||
vāhanalābho'śvagate viruvatyanuyāyini kṣatajapātaḥ | anye'pyanuvrajanto yātāraṃ kākavadvihagāḥ || 48 ||
dvātriṃśatpravibhakte digcakre yad yathā samuddiṣṭam | tattattathā vidheyaṃ guṇadoṣaphalaṃ yiyāsūnām || 49 ||
kā iti kākasya rutaṃ svanilayasaṃsthasya niṣphalaṃ proktam | kava iti cātmaprītyai keti rute snigdhamitrāptiḥ || 50 ||
kareti kalahaṃ kurukuru ca harṣamatha kaṭakaṭeti dadhibhaktam | keke virutaṃ kuku vā dhanalābhaṃ yāyinaḥ prāha || 51 ||
kharekhare pathikāgamamāha kakhākheti yāyino mṛtyum | gamanapratiṣedhikamā kakhalā sadyo'bhivarṣāya || 52 ||
[ ākhalakhala | ā khalakhala ] kāketi vighātaḥ kākaṭīti cāhāradūṣaṇaṃ prāha | prītyāspadaṃ kavakaveti bandhamevaṃ kagākuriti || 53 ||
[ vighātaṃ ] karagau virute varṣaṃ guḍavattrāsāya vaḍiti vastrāptiḥ | kalayeti ca saṃyogaḥ śūdrasya brāhmaṇaiḥ sākam || 54 ||
[ karakau ] kaḍiti phalāptiḥ phaladāhidarśanaṃ ṭaḍḍiti prahārāḥ syuḥ | strīlābhaḥ strīti rute gaḍiti gavāṃ puḍiti puṣpāṇām || 55 ||
[ phaḍ | phalavā | ṭaḍiti ] yuddhāya ṭākuṭākviti guhu vahnibhayaṃ kaṭekaṭe kalahaḥ | ṭākuli ciṇṭici kekeketi puraṃ ceti doṣāya || 56 ||
kākadvayasyāpi samānametatphalaṃ yaduktaṃ rutaceṣṭitādyaiḥ | patatriṇo'nye'pi yathaiva kāko vanyāḥ śvavaccoparidaṃṣṭriṇo ye || 57 ||
sthalasalilacarāṇāṃ vyatyayo meghakāle pracurasalilavṛṣṭyai śeṣakāle bhayāya | madhu bhavananilīnaṃ tatkarotyāśu śūnyaṃ maraṇamapi ca nīlā makṣikā mūrdhni līnā || 58 ||
[ nilīnā ] vinikṣipantyaḥ salile'ṇḍakāni pipīlikā vṛṣṭinirodhamāhuḥ | taruṃ sthalaṃ vāpi nayanti nimnād yadā tadā tāḥ kathayanti vṛṣṭim || 59 ||
[ tarusthalaṃ | taruṃ sthalaṃ ] kāryaṃ tu mūlaśakune'ntaraje tadahni vindyātphalaṃ niyatamevamime vicintyāḥ | prārambhayānasamayeṣu tathā praveśe grāhyaṃ kṣutaṃ na śubhadaṃ kva cidapyuśanti || 60 ||
śubhaṃ daśāpākamavighnasiddhiṃ mūlābhirakṣāmatha vā sahāyān | duṣṭasya saṃsiddhimanāmayatvaṃ vadanti te mānayiturnṛpasya || 61 ||
[ iṣṭasya ] krośādūrdhvaṃ śakuna virutaṃ niṣphalaṃ prāhureke tatrāniṣṭe prathamaśakune mānayetpañca ṣaṭ ca | prāṇāyāmānnṛpatiraśubhe ṣoḍaśaiva dvitīye pratyāgacchetsvabhavanamato yadyaniṣṭastṛtīyaḥ || 62 ||
[ śakuni ]

Chapter 95: śākunottarādhyāyaḥ [śākunottara-adhyāya]

digdeśaceṣṭāsvaravāsararkṣamuhūrtahorākaraṇodayāṃśān | carasthira ca buddhvā phalāni pravaded rutajṇaḥ || 1 ||
[ cirasthironmiśrabalābalaṃ | carasthira ] dvividhaṃ kathayanti saṃsthitānāmāgāmisthirasaṃjñitaṃ ca kāryam | nṛpadūtacarānyadeśajātānyabhighātaḥ svajanādi cāgamākhyam || 2 ||
udbaddhasaṃgrahaṇabhojanacauravahnivarṣotsavātmajavadhāḥ kalaho bhayaṃ ca | vargaḥ sthiro'yamudayenduyute sthirarkṣe vidyātsthiraṃ caragṛhe ca caraṃ yaduktam || 3 ||
sthirapradeśopalamandireṣu surālaye bhūjalasannidhau ca | sthirāṇi kāryāṇi carāṇi yāni calapradeśādiṣu cāgamāya || 4 ||
āpyodayarkṣakṣaṇadigjaleṣu pakṣāvasāneṣu ca ye pradīptāḥ | sarve'pi te vṛṣṭikarā ruvantaḥ śānto'pi vṛṣṭiṃ kurute'mbucārī || 5 ||
āgneyadiglagnamuhūrtadeśeṣvarkapradīpto'gnibhayāya rauti | viṣṭyāṃ yamarkṣodayakaṇṭakeṣu niṣpatravallīṣu ca doṣakṛtsyāt || 6 ||
[ moṣakṛt ] grāmyaḥ pradīptaḥ svaraceṣṭitābhyām 95.07b ugro ruvan kaṇṭakini sthitaśca | bhaumarkṣalagne yadi nairṛtīṃ ca | sthito'bhitaścetkalahāya dṛṣṭaḥ || 7 ||
lagne'tha vendorbhṛgubhāṃśasaṃsthe vidiksthito'dhovadanaśca rauti | dīptaḥ sa cetsaṃgrahaṇaṃ karoti yonyā tayā yā vidiśi pradiṣṭā || 8 ||
puṃrāśilagne viṣame tithau ca diksthaḥ pradīptaḥ śukuno narākhyaḥ | vācyaṃ tadā saṃgrahaṇaṃ narāṇāṃ miśre bhavetpaṇḍakasamprayogaḥ || 9 ||
evaṃ raveḥ kṣetranavāṃśalagne lagne sthite vā svayameva sūrye | dīpto'bhidhatte śakuno virauti puṃsaḥ pradhānasya hi kāraṇaṃ tat || 10 ||
[ vivāsaṃ ] prārambhamāṇeṣu ca sarvakāryeṣvarkānvitādbhādgaṇayedvilagnam | samptadvipacceti yathā krameṇa sampadvipacceti tathaiva vācyam || 11 ||
[ prārabhyamāṇeṣu | vāpi | vācyā ] kāṇenākṣṇā dakṣiṇenaiti sūrye candre lagnāddvādaśe cetarena | lagnasthe'rke pāpadṛṣṭe'ndha eva kubjaḥ svarkṣe śrotrahīno jaḍo vā || 12 ||
krūraḥ ṣaṣṭhe krūradṛṣṭo vilagnād yasmin rāśau tadgṛhāṅge vraṇo'sya | evaṃ proktaṃ yanmayā janmakāle cihnaṃ rūpaṃ tattadasminvicintyam || 13 ||
[ syāt ] ataḥ paraṃ lokanirūpitāni dravyeṣu nānākṣarasaṃgrahāṇi | iṣṭapraṇītāni vibhājitāni nāmāni kendrakramaśaḥ pravakṣye || R(1) ||
lagnāmbusaṃsthāstanabhaḥsthiteṣu kṣetreṣu ye lagnagatā gṛhāṃśāḥ | tebhyo'kṣarāṇyātmagṛhāśrayāṇi vindyādgrahāṇāṃ svagaṇakrameṇa || R(2) ||
kavargapūrvān kujaśukracāndrijīvārkajānāṃ pravadanti vargān | yakārapūrvāḥ śaśino niruktā varṇāstvakāraprabhavā raveḥ syuḥ || R(3) ||
dreṣkāṇavṛddhyā pravadanti nāma tripañcasaptākṣaramojarāśau | yugme tu vindyāddvicatuṣkaṣaṭkaṃ nāmākṣarāṇi grahadṛṣṭivṛddhyā || R(4) ||
vargottame dvyakṣarakaṃ carāṃśe sthirarkṣabhāge caturakṣaraṃ tat | ojeṣu caibhyo viṣamākṣarāṇi syurdvisvabhāveṣu tu rāśivacca || R(5) ||
dvimūrtisaṃjñe tu vadeddvināma saumyekṣite dviprakṛtau ca rāśau | yāvān gaṇaḥ svodayago'ṃśakānāṃ tāvān grahaḥ saṃgrahake'kṣarāṇām || R(6) ||
saṃyogamādau bahuleṣu vindyātkūṭeṣu saṃyogaparaṃ vadanti | svoccāṃśake dviṣkṛtamṛkṣayogādgurvakṣaraṃ tadbhavanāṃśake syāt || R(7) ||
mātrādiyuksyādgrahayuktrikoṇe dreṣkāṇaparyāyavadakṣareṣu | nabhobaleṣūrdhvamadho'mbujeṣu jñeyo visargastu balānviteṣu || R(8) ||
[ visargo'stabala ] śīrṣodayeṣūrdhvamuśanti mātrāmadhaśca pṛṣṭhodayaśabditeṣu | tīryakca vindyādubhayodaye tāṃ dīrgheṣu dīrghāmitareṣu cānyām || R(9) ||
prāglagnatoyāstanabhaḥsthiteṣu bheṣvaṃśakebhyo'kṣarasaṃgrahaḥ syāt | krūro'kṣaraṃ hanti catuṣṭayastho dṛṣṭyāpi mātrāṃ ca trikoṇago vā || R(10) ||
śubhagrahastūrjitavīryabhāgī sthānāṃśatulyākṣaradaḥ sa coktaḥ | paśyan sthitaḥ kendratrikoṇayorvā svocce'pi varṇadvayamātmabhāge || R(11) ||
kṣetreśvare kṣīṇabale'ṃśake ca mātrākṣaraṃ nāśamupaiti tajjam | asambhave'pyudbhavameti tasminvargādyamuccāṃśayujīśadṛṣṭe || R(12) ||
kendre yathāsthānabalaprakarṣaṃ kṣetrasya tatkṣetrapateśca buddhvā | kāryo'kṣarāṇāmanupūrvayogo mātrādisaṃyogavikalpanā ca || R(13) ||
tatrādirāśyādicaturvilagnamādyaṃśakādikramaparyāyeṇa | grahāṃśakebhyaḥ svagaṇākṣarāṇāmanvarthane prāptiriyaṃ vidhāryā || R(14) ||
meṣe kakāro hibuke yakārastule cakāro makare pakāraḥ | meṣe chakāro hibuke'pyakārastule khakāro makare phakāraḥ || R(15) ||
meṣe ṭakāro hibuke ṭhakārastule takāro makare thakāraḥ | meṣe tu rephā hibuke jakārastule bakāro makare gakāraḥ || R(16) ||
ākāramādye'mbugate ghakāramaste bhakāraṃ makare jhakāram | lagne ḍakāraṃ hibuke dakāramaste dhakāraṃ makare ḍhakāram || R(17) ||
lagne ñakāro hibuke makārastule ṅakāro makare lakāraḥ | lagne kakāro hibuke pakārastule cakāro makare ikāraḥ || R(18) ||
lagne nakāro hibuke takārastule ṇakāro makare ṭakāraḥ | ityetaduktaṃ carasaṃjñakasya vakṣye sthirākhyasya catuṣṭayasya || R(19) ||
vṛṣe phakāro hibuke khakāraḥ kīṭe vakāro nṛghaṭe chakāraḥ | ādyāṃśakebhyo matimānvidadhyādanukrameṇa sthirasaṃjñakeṣu || R(20) ||
lagne bakāro hibuke jakāra īkāramaste'mbarage gakāraḥ | vṛṣe thakāro hibuke ṭakāraḥ kīṭe ḍakāro nṛghaṭe dakāraḥ || R(21) ||
vṛṣe ghakāro hibuke śakāraḥ kīṭe jhakāro nṛghaṭe bhakāraḥ | lagne jakāro hibuke ukāraḥ kīṭe ṅakāro nṛghaṭe makāraḥ || R(22) ||
lagne ḍhakāro'tha jale ṇakāraścāste dhakāro'mbarage nakāraḥ | vṛṣe ṣakāro hibuke cakāraḥ kīṭe pakāro nṛghaṭe kakāraḥ || R(23) ||
ūkāramāhurvṛṣabhe jale khamaste phakāro nṛghaṭe chakāraḥ | antye vṛṣe ṭam tamuśanti siṃhe thaṃ saptage ṭhaṃ pravadanti kumbhe || R(24) ||
dvimūrtisaṃjñe mithune jakārāḥ ṣaṣṭhe bakāraḥ prathamāṃśake syāt | dhanurdhare'stopagate gakāro mīnadvaye cāmbarage sakāraḥ || R(25) ||
lagne ghakāro hibuke bhakāraścāste jhakāro'mbaramadhyage ī | lagne dakāro hibuke dhakāramaste ḍakāraṃ vidurambare ḍham || R(26) ||
lagne makāro hibuke ṅakāraś aste hakāro'mbarage ñakāraḥ | lagne pakāro jalage cakāra aikāramaste'mbarage kakāraḥ || R(27) ||
prāglagne naṃ jalage ṇamāhurastaṃ gate ṭaṃ nabhasi sthite tam | prāglagnage khaṃ jalage yamāhurastaṃ gate chaṃ nabhasi sthite pham || R(28) ||
lagne jamokāramathāmbusaṃsthe gamastasaṃsthe vidurambare bam | ṭhaṃ lagnage'ntye hibukāśrite ḍaṃ thamastage daṃ nabhasi sthite vai || R(29) ||
evaṃ vikalpo'kṣarasaṃgraho'yaṃ nāmnāṃ niruddiṣṭavidhāna uktaḥ | sarveṣu lagneṣu ca ke cidevamicchanti pūrvoktavidhānavattu || R(30) ||
kendrāṇi vā kendragatāṃśakaiḥ svaiḥ pṛthakpṛthaksaṃguṇitāni kṛtvā | trikṛdvibhaktaṃ vidurakṣaraṃ tatkṣetreśvarasyāmśaparikramasvam || R(31) ||
saṃcintitaprārthitanirgateṣu naṣṭakṣatastrīratibhojaneṣu | svapnarkṣacintāpuruṣādivargeṣveteṣu nāmānyupalakṣayeta | dvyakṣaraṃ caragṛhāṃśakodaye āma cāsya caturakṣaraṃ sthire | nāmayugmamapi ca dvimūrtiṣu tryakṣaraṃ bhavati cāsya pañcabhiḥ || 14 ||
kādyāstu vargāḥ kujaśukrasaumyajīvārkajānāṃ kramaśaḥ pradiṣṭāḥ | varṇāṣṭakaṃ yādi ca śītaraśme raverakārātkramaśaḥ svarāḥ syuḥ || 15 ||
nāmāni cāgnyambukumāraviṣṇuśakrendrapatnīcaturānanānām | tulyāni sūryātkramaśo vicintya dvitryādivarṇairghaṭayetsvabuddhyā || 16 ||
vayāṃsi teṣāṃ stanapānabālyavratasthitā yauvanamadhyavṛddhāḥ | atīvavṛddhā iti candrabhaumajñaśukrajīvārkaśanaiścarāṇām || 17 ||

Chapter 96: pākādhyāyaḥ [pāka-adhyāya]

pakṣādbhānoḥ somasya māsiko'ṅgārakasya vaktroktaḥ | ādarśanācca pāko budhasya jīvasya varṣeṇa || 1 ||
ṣaḍbhiḥ sitasya māsairabdena śaneḥ suradviṣo'bdārdhāt | varṣātsūryagrahaṇe sadyaḥ syāttvāṣṭrakīlakayoḥ || 2 ||
tribhireva dhūmaketormāsaiḥ śvetasya saptarātrānte | saptāhātpariveṣendracāpasandhyābhrasūcīnām || 3 ||
śītoṣṇaviparyāsaḥ phalapuṣpamakālajaṃ diśāṃ dāhaḥ | sthiracarayoranyatvaṃ prasūtivikṛtiśca ṣaṇmāsāt || 4 ||
akriyamāṇakakaraṇaṃ bhūkampo'nutsavo duriṣṭaṃ ca | śoṣaścāśoṣyāṇāṃ sroto'nyatvaṃ ca varṣārdhāt || 5 ||
stambhakusūlārcānāṃ jalpitaruditaprakampitasvedāḥ | māsatrayeṇa kalahendracāpanirghātapākāśca || 6 ||
kīṭākhumakṣikoragabāhulyaṃ mṛgavihaṅgavirutaṃ ca | loṣṭasya cāpsu taraṇaṃ tribhireva vipacyate māsaiḥ || 7 ||
prasavaḥ śunāmaraṇye vanyānāṃ grāmasampraveśaśca | madhunilayatoraṇendradhvajāśca varṣātsamadhikādvā || 8 ||
gomāyugṛdhrasaṃghā daśāhikāḥ sadya eva tūryaravaḥ | ākruṣṭaṃ pakṣaphalaṃ valmīko vidaraṇaṃ ca bhuvaḥ || 9 ||
ahutāśaprajvalanaṃ ghṛtatailavasādivarṣaṇaṃ cāpi | sadyaḥ paripacyante māse'dhyardhe ca janavādaḥ || 10 ||
chatracitiyūpahutavahabījānāṃ saptabhirbhavati pakṣaiḥ | chatrasya toraṇasya ca kecinmāsātphalaṃ prāhuḥ || 11 ||
atyantaviruddhānāṃ snehaḥ śabdaśca viyati bhūtānām | mārjāranakulayormūṣakeṇa saṅgaśca māsena || 12 ||
gandharvapuraṃ māsād rasavaikṛtyaṃ hiraṇyavikṛtiśca | dhvajaveśmapāṃśudhūmākulā diśaścāpi māsaphalāḥ || 13 ||
navakaikāṣṭadaśakaikaṣaṭtrikatrikasaṅkhyamāsapākāni | nakṣatrāṇyaśvinipūrvakāṇi sadyaḥ phalāśleṣā || 14 ||
pitryānmāsaḥ ṣaṭ saṭtrayo'rdhamaṣṭau ca triṣaḍekaikāḥ | māsacatuṣke'ṣāḍhe sadyaḥ pākābhijittārā || 15 ||
saptāṣṭavadhyardhaṃ trayastrayaḥ pañca caiva māsāḥ syuḥ | śravaṇādīnāṃ pāko nakṣatrāṇāṃ yathāsaṅkhyam || 16 ||
nigaditasamaye na dṛśyate cedadhikataraṃ dviguṇe prapacyate tat | yadi na kanakaratnagopradānairupaśamitaṃ vidhivaddvijaiśca śāntyā || 17 ||

Chapter 97: nakṣatrakarmaguṇādhyāyaḥ [nakṣatrakarmaguṇa-adhyāya]

śikhiguṇarasendriyānalaśaśiviṣayaguṇartupañcavasupakṣāḥ | viṣayaikacandrabhūtārṇavāgnirudrāśvivasudahanāḥ || 1 ||
bhūtaśatapakṣavasavo dvātriṃśacceti tārakāmānam | kramaśo'śvinyādīnāṃ kālastārāpramāṇena || 2 ||
nakṣatrajamudvāhe phalamabdaistārakāmitaiḥ sadasat | divasairjvarasya nāśo vyādheranyasya vā vācyaḥ || 3 ||
aśviyamadahanakamalajaśaśiśūlabhṛdaditijīvaphaṇipitaraḥ | yonyaryamadinakṛttvaṣṭṛpavanaśakrāgnimitrāśca || 4 ||
śakro nirṛtistoyaṃ viśve brahmā harirvasurvaruṇaḥ | ajapādo'hirbudhnyaḥ pūṣā cetīśvarā bhānām || 5 ||
trīṇyuttarāṇi tebhyo rohiṇyaśca dhruvāṇi taiḥ kuryāt | abhiṣekaśāntitarunagaradharmabījadhruvārambhān || 6 ||
mūlaśivaśakrabhujagādhipāni tīkṣṇāni teṣu siddhyanti | abhighātamantravetālabandhavadhabhedasaṃbandhāḥ || 07 ||
ugrāṇi pūrvabharaṇīpitryāṇyutsādanāśaśāṭhyeṣu | yojyāni bandhaviṣadahanaśastraghātādiṣu ca siddhyai || 8 ||
laghu hastāśvinapuṣyāḥ paṇyaratijñānabhūṣaṇakalāsu | śilpauṣadhayānādiṣu siddhikarāṇi pradiṣṭāni || 9 ||
mṛduvargo anūrādhācitrāpauṣṇaindavāni mitrārthe | suratavidhivastrabhūṣaṇamaṅgalagīteṣu ca hitāni || 10 ||
[ mṛduvargastv ] hautabhujaṃ saviśākhaṃ mṛdutīkṣṇam tadvimiśraphalakāri | śravaṇatrayamādityānile ca carakarmaṇi hitāni || 11 ||
hastatrayaṃ mṛgaśiraḥ śravaṇatrayaṃ ca pūṣāśviśakragurubhāni punarvasuśca | kṣaure tu karmaṇi hitānyudaye kṣaṇe vā yuktāni coḍupatinā śubhatārayā ca || 12 ||
[ śravanāttrayaṃ ] na snātamātragamanonmukhabhūṣitānāmabhyaktabhuktaraṇakālanirāsanānām | sandhyāniśāśanikujārkatithau ca rikte kṣauraṃ hitaṃ na navame'hni na cāpi viṣṭyām || 13 ||
[ utsuka | niśoḥ kujayamārkadine ] nṛpājñayā brāhmaṇasammate ca vivāhakāle mṛtasūtake ca | baddhasya mokṣe kratudīkṣaṇāsu sarveṣu śastaṃ kṣurakarma bheṣu || 14 ||
sāvitrapauṣṇānilamaitratiṣyatvāṣṭre tathā coḍugaṇādhiparkṣe | saṃskāradīkṣāvratamekhalādi kuryādgurau śukrabudhenduyukte || 15 ||
śuddhairdvādaśakendranaidhanagṛhaiḥ pāpaistriṣaṣṭhāyagairlagne kendragate'tha vā suragurau daityendrapūjye'pi vā | sarvārambhaphalaprasiddhirudaye rāśau ca kartuḥ śubhe sagrāmyasthirabhodaye ca bhavanaṃ kāryaṃ praveśo'pi vā || 16 ||

Chapter 98: tithikarmaguṇādhyāyaḥ [tithikarmaguṇa-adhyāya]

hasto mūlaṃ śravaṇā punarvasurmṛgaśirastathā puṣyaḥ | puṃsañjñiteṣu kāryeṣvetāni śubhāni dhiṣṇyāni || K(15) ||
lābhe tṛtīye ca śubhaiḥ samete pāpairvihīne śubharāśilagne | vedhyau tu karṇau tridaśejyalagne tiṣyenducitrāharirevatīṣu || K(17) ||
kamalajavidhātṛhariyamaśaśāṅkaṣaḍvaktraśakravasubhujagāḥ | dharmeśasavitṛmanmathakalayo viśve ca tithipatayaḥ || 1 ||
pitaro'māvasyāyāṃ saṃjñāsadṛśāśca taiḥ kriyāḥ kāryāḥ | nandā bhadrā vijayā riktā pūrṇā ca tāstrividhāḥ || 2 ||
yatkāryaṃ nakṣatre taddaivatyāsu tithiṣu tatkāryam | karaṇamuhūrteṣvapi tatsiddhikaraṃ devatāsadṛśam || 3 ||

Chapter 99: karaṇaguṇādhyāyaḥ [karaṇaguṇa-adhyāya]

vavavālavakaulavataitilākhyagaravaṇijaviṣṭisaṃjñānām | patayaḥ syurindrakamalajamitrāryamabhūśriyaḥ sayamāḥ || 1 ||
[ bavabālavakaulaba ] kṛṣṇacaturdaśyardhāddhuvāṇi śakuniścatuṣpadaṃ nāgam | kiṃstughnamiti ca teṣāṃ kalivṛṣaphaṇimārutāḥ patayaḥ || 2 ||
[ dhruvāṇi ] kuryādvave śubhacarasthirapauṣṭikāni dharmakriyādvijahitāni ca vālavākhye | samprītimitravaraṇāni ca kaulave syuḥ saubhāgyasaṃśrayagṛhāṇi ca taitilākhye || 3 ||
[ bave | bālava | kaulabe ] kṛṣibījagṛhāśrayajāni gare vaṇiji dhuvakāryavaṇigyutayaḥ | na hi viṣṭikṛtaṃ vidadhāti śubhaṃ paraghātaviṣādiṣu siddhikaram || 4 ||
[ dhruva ] kāryaṃ pauṣṭikamauṣadhādi śakunau mūlāni mantrāstathā gokāryāṇi catuṣpade dvijapitṛnuddiśya rājyāni ca | nāge sthāvaradāruṇāni haraṇaṃ daurbhāgyakarmāṇyataḥ kiṃstughne śubhamiṣṭi puṣṭikaraṇaṃ maṅgalyasiddhikriyāḥ || 5 ||
[ iṣṭa ] lābhe tṛtīye ca śubhaiḥ samete pāpairvihīne śubharāśilagne | vedhyau ca karṇāvamarejyalagne puṣyenducitrāharipauṣṇabheṣu || 6 ||
rohiṇyuttararevatīmṛgaśiromūlānurādhāmaghāhastasvātiṣu ṣaṣṭhataulimithuneṣūdyatsu pāṇigrahaḥ | saptāṣṭāntyabahiḥśubhairuḍupatāvekādaśadvitrige krūraistryāyaṣaḍaṣṭagairna tu bhṛgau ṣaṣṭhe kuje cāṣṭame || 7 ||
dampatyordvinavāṣṭarāśirahite cārānukule ravau candre cārkakujārkiśukraviyute madhye'tha vā pāpayoḥ | tyaktvā ca vyatipātavaidhṛtidinaṃ viṣṭiṃ ca riktāṃ tithiṃ krūrāhāyanapauṣacaitravirahe lagnāṃśake mānuṣe || 8 ||
[ vaidhṛta | caitrapauṣa ]

Chapter 100: nakṣatrajātakādhyāyaḥ [nakṣatrajātaka-adhyāya]

priyabhūṣaṇaḥ svarūpaḥ subhago dakṣo'śvinīṣu matimāṃśca | kṛtaniścayasatyārugdakṣaḥ sukhitaśca bharaṇīṣu || 1 ||
[ surūpaḥ ] bahubhukparadāraratastejasvī kṛttikāsu vikhyātaḥ | rohiṇyāṃ satyaśuciḥ priyaṃvadaḥ sthiraḥ svarūpaśca || 2 ||
[ sthirasurūpaśca ] capalaścaturo bhīruḥ paṭurutsāhī dhanī mṛge bhogī | śaṭhagarvitacaṇḍakṛtaghnahiṃsrapāpaśca raudrarkṣe || 3 ||
dāntaḥ sukhī suśīlo durmedhā rogabhākpipāsuśca | alpena ca santuṣṭaḥ punarvasau jāyate manujaḥ || 4 ||
śāntātmā subhagaḥ paṇḍito dhanī dharmasaṃśritaḥ puṣye | śaṭhasarvabhakṣakṣya kṛtaghnadhūrtaśca bhaujaṅge || 5 ||
[ bhakṣapāpaḥ | bhakṣya ] bahubhṛtyadhanī bhogī surapitṛbhakto mahodyamaḥ pitrye | priyavāgdātā dyutimānaṭano nṛpasevako bhāgye || 6 ||
subhago vidyāptadhano bhogī sukhabhāgdvitīyaphalgunyām | utsāhī dhṛṣṭaḥ pānapo'ghṛṇī taskaro haste || 7 ||
citrāmbaramālyadharaḥ sulocanāṅgaśca citrāyām | dānto vaṇiktṛṣāluḥ priyavāgdharmāśritaḥ svātau || 8 ||
[ bhavati citrāyām | kṛpāluḥ ] īrṣurlubdho dyutimānvacanapaṭuḥ kalahakṛdviśākhāsu | āḍhyo videśavāsī kṣudhāluraṭano'nurādhāsu || 9 ||
[ irṣyur ] jyeṣṭhāsu na bahumitraḥ santuṣṭo dharmakṛtpracurakopaḥ | mūle mānī dhanavān sukhī na hiṃsraḥ sthiro bhogī || 10 ||
iṣṭānandakalatro vīro dṛḍhasauhṛdaśca jaladeve | vaiśve vinītadhārmikabahumitrakṛtajñasubhagaśca || 11 ||
śrīmācchravaṇe śrutavānudāradāro dhanānvitaḥ khyātaḥ | dātāḍhyaśūragītapriyo dhaniṣṭhāsu dhanalubdhaḥ || 12 ||
sphuṭavāgvyasanī ripuhā sāhasikaḥ śatabhiṣaksu durgrāhyaḥ | bhadrapadāsūdvignaḥ strījitadhanapaṭuradātā ca || 13 ||
vaktā sukhī prajāvān jitaśatrurdhārmiko dvitīyāsu | sampūrṇāṅgaḥ subhagaḥ śūraḥ śucirarthavānpauṣṇe || 14 ||

Chapter 101: rāśivibhāgādhyāyaḥ [rāśivibhāga-adhyāya]

aśvinyo'tha bharaṇyo bahulāpādaśca kīrtyate meṣaḥ | vṛṣabho bahulāśeṣaṃ rohiṇyo'rdhaṃ ca mṛgaśirasaḥ || 1 ||
mṛgaśiro'rdhaṃ raudraṃ punarvasoraṃśakatrayaṃ mithunaḥ | pādaśca punarvasutastiṣyaḥ śleṣā ca karkaṭakaḥ || 2 ||
[ punarvasor ca | mithunam | punarvasoḥ satiṣyo'śleṣā ] siṃho'tha maghā pūrvā ca phalgunī pāda uttarāyāśca | tatpariśeṣaṃ hastaścitrādyardhaṃ ca kanyākhyaḥ || 3 ||
taulini citrāntyārdhaṃ svātiḥ pādatrayaṃ viśākhāyāḥ | alini viśākhāpādastathānurādhānvitā jyeṣṭhā || 4 ||
mūlamaṣāḍhā pūrvā prathamaścāpyuttarāṃśako dhanvī | makarastatpariṣeśaṃ śravaṇaḥ pūrvaṃ dhaniṣṭhārdham || 5 ||
kumbho'ntyadhaniṣṭhārdhaṃ śatabhiṣagaṃśatrayaṃ ca pūrvāyāḥ | bhadrapadāyāḥ śeṣaṃ tathottarā revatī ca jhaṣaḥ || 6 ||
aśvinīpitryamūlādyā meṣasiṃhahayādayaḥ | viṣamarkṣānnivartante pādavṛddhyā yathottaram || 7 ||

Chapter 102: vivāhapaṭalādhyāyaḥ [vivāhapaṭala-adhyāya]

mūrtau karoti dinakṛdvidhavāṃ kujaśca rāhurvipannatanayāṃ ravijo daridrām | śukraḥ śaśāṅkatanayaśca guruśca sādhvīmāyuḥkṣayaṃ prakurute'tha vibhāvarīśaḥ || 1 ||
kurvanti bhāskaraśanaiścararāhubhaumā dāridryaduḥkhamatulaṃ niyataṃ dvitīye | vitteśvarīmavidhavāṃ guruśukrasaumyā nārīṃ prabhūtatanayāṃ kurute śaśāṅkaḥ || 2 ||
sūryendubhaumaguruśukrabudhāstṛtīye kuryuḥ sadā bahusutāṃ dhanabhāginīṃ ca | vyaktāṃ divākarasutaḥ subhagāṃ karoti mṛtyuṃ dadāti niyamātkhalu saiṃhikeyaḥ || 3 ||
[ vyaktaṃ ] svalpaṃ payaḥ sravati sūryasute caturthe daurbhāgyamuṣṇakiraṇaḥ kurute śaśī ca | rāhuḥ sapatnanamapi ca kṣitijo'lpavittaṃ dadyādbhṛguḥ suraguruśca budhaśca saukhyam || 4 ||
[ sapatnyam | sapatnam | alpavittāṃ ] naṣṭātmajāṃ ravikujau khalu pañcamasthe candrātmajo bahusutā gurubhārgavau ca | rāhurdadāti maraṇaṃ śanirugrarogaṃ kanyāvināśamacirātkurute śaśāṅkaḥ || 5 ||
[ pañcamasthau | prasūtim ] ṣaṣṭhāśritāḥ śanidivākararāhujīvāḥ kuryuḥ kujaśca subhagāṃ śvaśureṣu bhaktām | candraḥ karoti vidhavāmuśanā daridrāmṛddhāṃ śaśāṅkatanayaḥ kalahapriyāṃ ca || 6 ||
saurārajīvabudharāhuravīnduśukrāḥ | kuryuḥ prasahya khalu saptamarāśisaṃsthāḥ | vaidhavyabandhanavadhakṣayamarthanāśavyādhipravāsamaraṇāni yathākrameṇa || 7 ||
sthāne'ṣṭame gurubudhau niyataṃ viyogaṃ mṛtyuṃ śaśī bhṛgusutaśca tathaiva rāhuḥ | sūryaḥ karotyavidhavāṃ sarujāṃ mahījaḥ | sūryātmajo dhanavatīṃ pativallabhāṃ ca || 8 ||
[ sarujaṃ ] dharme sthitā bhṛgudivākarabhūmiputrā jīvaśca dharmaniratāṃ śaśijastvarogām | rāhuśca sūryatanayaśca karoti bandhyāṃ kanyāprasūtimaṭanāṃ kurute śaśāṅkaḥ || 9 ||
[ vandhyāṃ | aṭanaṃ ] rāhurnabhaḥsthalagato vidhavāṃ karoti pāpe ratāṃ dinakaraśca śanaiścaraśca | mṛtyuṃ kujo'rtharahitāṃ kulaṭāṃ ca candraḥ śeṣā grahā dhanavatīṃ subhagāṃ ca kuryuḥ || 10 ||
[ nabhasthalagato ] āye ravirbahusutāṃ sadhanāṃ śaśāṅkaḥ putrānvitāṃ kṣitisuto ravijo dhanāḍhyām | āyuṣmatīṃ suraguruḥ śaśijaḥ samṛddhāṃ rāhuḥ karotyavidhavāṃ bhṛgurarthayuktām || 11 ||
[ dhaninīṃ ] ante gururdhanavatīṃ dinakṛddaridrāṃ candro dhanavyayakarīṃ kulaṭāṃ ca rāhuḥ | sādhvīṃ bhṛguḥ śaśisuto bahuputrapautrāṃ pānaprasaktahṛdayām ravijaḥ kujaśca || 12 ||
gopairyaṣṭyāhatānāṃ khurapuṭadalitā yā tu dhūlirdinānte sodvāhe sundarīṇāṃ vipuladhanasutārogyasaubhāgyakartrī | tasmin kāle na carkṣaṃ na ca tithikaraṇaṃ naiva lagnaṃ na yogaḥ khyātaḥ puṃsāṃ sukhārthaṃ śamayati duritānyutthitaṃ gorajastu || 13 ||

Chapter 103: grahagocarādhyāyaḥ [grahagocara-adhyāya]

prāyeṇa sūtreṇa vinākṛtāni prakāśarandhrāṇi cirantanāni | ratnāni śāstrāṇi ca yojitāni navairguṇairbhūṣayituṃ kṣamāṇi || 1 ||
prāyeṇa gocaro vyavahāryo'tastatphalāni vakṣyāmi | nānāvṛttairāryā mukhacapalatvaṃ kṣamadhvaṃ naḥ || 2 ||
[ tanno | kṣamantvāryāḥ ] māṇḍavyagiraṃ śrutvā na madīyā rocate'tha vā naivam | sādhvī tathā na puṃsāṃ priyā yathā syājjaghanacapalā || 3 ||
sūryaḥ ṣaṭtridaśasthitastridaśaṣaṭsaptādyagaścandramā jīvaḥ saptanavadvipañcamagato vakrārkajau ṣaṭtrigau | saumyaḥ ṣaḍdvicaturdaśāṣṭamagataḥ sūrye apyupānte śubhāḥ śukraḥ saptamaṣaḍdaśarkṣasahitaḥ śārdūlavattrāsakṛt || 4 ||
[ sarve ] janmanyāyāsado'rkaḥ kṣapayati vibhavān koṣṭharogādhvadātā vittabhraṃśaṃ dvitīye diśati ca na sukhaṃ vañcanāṃ dṛgrujaṃ ca | sthānaprāptiṃ tṛtīye dhananicayamudā kalyakṛccārihartā rogāndatte caturthe janayati ca muhuḥ sragdharābhogavighnam || 5 ||
[ dhananicayamudākalyakṛc | hantā | dhatte ] pīḍāḥ syuḥ pañcamasthe savitari bahuśo rogārijanitāḥ ṣaṣṭhe'rko hanti rogān kṣapayati ca ripūcchokāṃśca nudati | adhvānaṃ saptamastho jaṭharagadabhayaṃ dainyaṃ ca kurute ruktrāsau cāṣṭamasthe bhavati suvadanā na svāpi vanitā || 6 ||
[ rukkāsau ] ravāvāpaddainyaṃ rugiti navame vitta ceṣṭāvirodho jayaṃ prāpnotyugraṃ daśamagṛhage karmasiddhiṃ krameṇa | jayasthānaṃ mānaṃ vibhavamapi caikādaśe roganāśaṃ suvṛttānāṃ ceṣṭā bhavati saphalā dvādaśe netareṣām || 7 ||
[ citta | jayaṃ sthānaṃ ] śaśī janmanyannapravaraśayanācchādanakaro dvitīye mānārthān glapayati savighnaśca bhavati | tṛtīye vastrastrīdhanavijaya saukhyāni labhate caturthe'viśvāsaḥ śikhariṇi bhujaṅgena sadṛśaḥ || 8 ||
[ mānārthau | nicaya ] dainyaṃ vyādhiṃ śucamapi śaśī pañcame mārgavighnaṃ ṣaṣṭhe vittaṃ janayati sukhaṃ śatrurogakṣayaṃ ca | yānaṃ mānaṃ śayanamaśanaṃ saptame vittalābhaṃ mandākrānte phaṇini himagau ca aṣṭame bhīrna kasya || 9 ||
navamagṛhago bandhodvegaśramodararogakṛddaśamabhavane ca ājñākarmaprasiddhikaraḥ śaśī | upacayasuhṛtsaṃyogārthapramodamupāntyago vṛṣabhacaritāndoṣānantye karoti ca savyayān || 10 ||
[ ante | hi ] kuje'bhighātaḥ prathame dvitīye narendrapīḍā kalahāridoṣaiḥ | bhṛśaṃ ca pittānalacaurarogairupendravajrapratimo'pi yaḥ syāt || 11 ||
[ rogacaurair ] tṛtīyagaścaurakumārakebhyo bhaumaḥ sakāśātphalamādadhāti | pradīptimājñāṃ dhanamaurṇikāni dhātvākarākhyāni kila aparāṇi || 12 ||
bhavati dharaṇije caturthage jvarajaṭharagadāsṛgudbhavaḥ | kupuruṣajanitācca saṅgamātprasabhamapi karoti ca aśubham || 13 ||
ripugadakopabhayāni pañcame tanayakṛtāśca śuco mahīsute | dyutirapi na asya ciraṃ bhavetsthirā śirasi kaperiva mālatī yathā || 14 ||
[ kṛtā ] ripubhayakalahairvivarjitaḥ sakanakavidrumatāmrakāmagaḥ | ripubhavanagate mahīsute kimaparavaktravikāramīkṣate || 15 ||
[ kāgamaḥ cāgama ] kalatrakalahākṣirugjaṭhararogakṛtsaptame kṣaratkṣatajarūkṣitaḥ kṣapitavittamāno'ṣṭame | kuje navamasaṃsthite paribhavārthanāśādibhirvilambitagatirbhavatyabaladehadhātuklamaiḥ || 16 ||
[ kṣayita ] daśamagṛhagate samaṃ mahīje vividhadhanāptirupāntyage jayaśca | janapadamupari sthitaśca bhuṅkte vanamiva ṣaṭcaraṇaḥ supuṣpitāgram || 17 ||
nānāvyayairdvādaśage mahīsute santāpyate'narthaśataiśca mānavaḥ | strīkopapittaiśca sanetravedanairyo'pi indravaṃśābhijanena garvitaḥ || 18 ||
duṣṭavākyapiśunāhitabhedairbandhanaiḥ sakalahaiśca hṛtasvaḥ | janmage śaśisute pathi gacchan svāgate'pi kuśalaṃ na śṛṇoti || 19 ||
paribhavo dhanagate dhanalabdhiḥ sahajage śaśisute hṛdayāptiḥ | nṛpatiśatrubhayaśaṅkitacito drutapadaṃ vrajati duścaritaiḥ svaiḥ || 20 ||
[ suhṛdāptiḥ | citto ] caturthage svajanakuṭumbavṛddhayo dhanāgamo bhavati ca śītaraśmije | sutasthite tanayakalatravigraho niṣevate na ca rucirāmapi striyam || 21 ||
saubhāgyaṃ vijayamatha unnatiṃ ca ṣaṣṭhe vaivarṇyaṃ kalahamatīva saptame jñaḥ | mṛtyusthe jayasutavastravittalābhā naipuṇyaṃ bhavati matipraharṣaṇīyam || 22 ||
[ sutajaya ] vighnakaro navamaḥ śaśiputraḥ karmagato ripuhā dhanadaśca | sapramadaṃ śayanaṃ ca vidhatte tadgṛhado'tha kathāṃ staraṇaṃ ca || 23 ||
[ kathāstaraṇaṃ ] dhanasutasukhayoṣinmitravāhāptituṣṭistuhinakiraṇaputre lābhage mṛṣṭavākyaḥ | ripuparibhavarogaiḥ pīḍito dvādaśasthe na sahati paribhoktuṃ mālinīyogasaukhyam || 24 ||
[ sukhasuta | vāhya ] jīve janmanyapagatadhanadhīḥ sthānabhraṣṭo bahukalahayutaḥ | prāpya arthe'rthānvyarirapi kurute kāntāsyābje bhramaravilasitam || 25 ||
sthānabhraṃśātkāryavighātācca tṛtīye anekaiḥ kleśairbandhujanotthaiśca caturthe | jīve śāntiṃ pīḍitacittaśca sa vindednaiva grāme nāpi vane mattamayūre || 26 ||
[ naikaiḥ | vinden ] janayati ca tanayabhavanamupagataḥ parijanaśubhasutakarituragavṛṣān | sakanakapuragṛhayuvativasanakṛnmaṇiguṇanikarakṛdapi vibudhaguruḥ || 27 ||
na sakhīvadanaṃ tilakojjvalaṃ na ca vanaṃ śikhikokilanāditam | hariṇaplutaśāvavicitritaṃ ripugate manasaḥ sukhadaṃ gurau || 28 ||
[ bhavanaṃ ] tridaśaguruḥ śayanaṃ ratibhogaṃ dhanamaśanaṃ kusumānyupavāhyam | janayati saptamarāśimupeto lalitapadāṃ ca giraṃ dhiṣaṇāṃ ca || 29 ||
bandhaṃ vyādhiṃ cāṣṭame śokamugraṃ mārgakleśānmṛtyutulyāṃśca rogān | naipuṇyājñāputrakarmārthasiddhiṃ dharme jīvaḥ śālinīnāṃ ca lābham || 30 ||
[ kleśaṃ ] sthānakalyadhanahā daśarkṣagastatprado bhavati lābhago guruḥ | dvādaśe'dhvani vilomaduḥkhabhāg yāti yadyapi naro rathoddhataḥ || 31 ||
prathamagṛhopago bhṛgusutaḥ smaropakaraṇaiḥ surabhimanojñagandhakusumāmbarairupacayam | śayanagṛhāsanāśanayutasya ca anukurute samadavilāsinīmukhasarojaṣaṭcaraṇatām || 32 ||
śukre dvitīyagṛhage prasavārthadhānyabhūpālasannatakuṭumbahitānyavāpya | saṃsevate kusumaratnavibhūṣitaśca kāmaṃ vasantatilakadyutimūrdhajo'pi || 33 ||
[ sannati ] ājñārthamānāspadabhūtivastraśatrukṣayāndaityagurustṛtīye | datte caturthaśca suhṛtsamājaṃ rudrendravajrapratimāṃ ca śaktim || 34 ||
[ dhatte ] janayati śukraḥ pañcamasaṃstho guruparitoṣaṃ bandhujanāptim | sutadhanalabdhiṃ mitrasahāyānanavasitatvaṃ ca aribaleṣu || 35 ||
ṣaṣṭho bhṛguḥ paribhavarogatāpadaḥ strīhetukaṃ janayati saptamo'śubham | yāto'ṣṭamaṃ bhavanaparicchadaprado lakṣmīvatīmupanayati striyaṃ ca saḥ || 36 ||
navame tu dharmavanitāsukhabhāgbhṛguje'rthavastranicayaśca bhavet | daśame'vamānakalahānniyamātpramitākṣarāṇyapi vadan labhate || 37 ||
upāntyago bhṛgo sutaḥ suhṛddhanānnagandhadaḥ | dhanāmbarāgamo'ntyagaḥ sthirastu nāmbarāgamaḥ || 38 ||
prathame ravije viṣavahnihataḥ svajanairviyutaḥ kṛtabandhuvadhaḥ | paradeśamupaityasuhṛdbhavano vimukhārthasuto'ṭakadīnamukhaḥ || 39 ||
cāravaśāddvitīyagṛhage dinakaratanaye rūpasukhāpavarjitatanurvigatamadabalaḥ | anyaguṇaiḥ kṛtaṃ vasucayam tadapi khalu bhavatyambviva vaṃśapatrapatitaṃ na bahu na ca ciram || 40 ||
sūryasute tṛtīyagṛhage dhanāni labhate dāsaparicchadoṣṭramahiṣāśvakuñjarakharān | sadmavibhūtisaukhyamamitaṃ gadavyuparamaṃ bhīrurapi praśāstyadhiripūṃśca vīralalitaiḥ || 41 ||
caturthaṃ gṛhaṃ sūryaputre'bhyupete suhṛdvittabhāryādibhirviprayuktaḥ | bhavatyasya sarvatra cāsādhu duṣṭaṃ bhujaṅgaprayātānukāraṃ ca cittam || 42 ||
sutadhanaparihīṇaḥ pañcamasthe pracurakalahayuktaśca arkaputre | vinihataripurogaḥ ṣaṣṭhayāte pibati ca vanitāsyaṃ śrīpuṭoṣṭham || 43 ||
gacchatyadhvānaṃ saptame ca aṣṭame ca hīnaḥ strīputraiḥ sūryaje dīnaceṣṭaḥ | tadvaddharmasthe vairahṛdrogabandhairdharmo'pyucchidyedvaiśvadevīkriyādyaḥ || 44 ||
karmaprāptirdaśame'rthakṣayaśca vidyākīrtyoḥ parihāniśca saure | taikṣṇyaṃ lābhe parayoṣārthalābhaśca antye prāpnotyapi śokormimālām || 45 ||
[ lābhā | ante ] api kālamapekṣya ca pātraṃ śubhakṛdvidadhātyanurūpam | na madhau bahu kaṃ kuḍave vā visṛjatyapi meghavitānaḥ || 46 ||
[ ca ] raktaiḥ puṣpairgandhaistāmraiḥ kanakavṛṣabakulakusumairdivākarabhūsutau bhaktyā pūjyāvindurdhenvā sitakusumarajatamadhuraiḥ sitaśca madapradaiḥ | kṛṣṇadravyaiḥ sauriḥ saumyo maṇirajatatilakakusumairguruḥ paripītakaiḥ prītaiḥ pīḍā na syāduccād yadi patati viśati yadi vā bhujaṅgavijṛmbhitam || 47 ||
śamayodgatāmaśubhadṛṣṭimapi vibudhaviprapūjayā | śāntijapaniyamadānadamaiḥ sujanābhibhāṣaṇasamāgamaistathā || 48 ||
ravibhaumau pūrvārdhe śaśisaurau kathayato'ntyagau rāśeḥ | sadasallakṣaṇamāryagītyupagītyoryathāsaṃkhyam || 49 ||
ādau yādṛksaumyaḥ paścādapi tādṛśo bhavati | upagītermātrāṇāṃ gaṇavatsatsamprayogo vā || 50 ||
āryāṇāmapi kurute vināśamantargururviṣamasaṃsthaḥ | gaṇa iva ṣaṣṭhe dṛṣṭaḥ sa sarvalaghutāṃ janaṃ nayati || 51 ||
[ ca | gato ] aśubhanirīkṣitaḥ śubhaphalo balinā balavānaśubhaphalapradaśca śubhadṛgviṣayopagataḥ | aśubhaśubhāvapi svaphalayorvrajataḥ samatāmidamapi gītakaṃ ca khalu narkuṭakaṃ ca yathā || 52 ||
nīce'ribhe'ste ca aridṛṣṭasya sarvaṃ vṛthā yatparikīrtitam | purato'ndhasya iva kāminyāḥ savilāsakaṭākṣanirīkṣaṇam || 53 ||
[ aridṛṣṭasya | yathā ] sūryasuto'rkaphalasamaścandrasutaśchandataḥ samanuyāti yathā | skandhakamāryāgītirvaitālīyaṃ ca māgadhī gāthāryām || 54 ||
sauro'rkaraśmiyogātsavikāro labdhavṛddhiradhikataram | pittavadācarati nṛṇāṃ pathyakṛtāṃ na tu tathāryāṇām || 55 ||
[ rāgāt ] yādṛśena graheṇenduryuktastādṛgbhavetso'pi | manovṛttisamāyogādvikāra iva vaktrasya || 56 ||
pañcamaṃ laghu sarveṣu saptamaṃ dvicaturthayoḥ | yadvacchlokākṣaraṃ tadval laghutāṃ yāti duḥsthitaiḥ || 57 ||
[ sarvapādeṣu ] prakṛtyāpi laghuryaśca vṛttabāhye vyavasthitaḥ | sa yāti gurutāṃ loke yadā syuḥ susthitā grahāḥ || 58 ||
prārabdhamasusthitairgrahairyatkarmātmavivṛddhaye budhaiḥ | vinihanti tadeva karma tānvaitālīyamiva ayathākṛtam || 59 ||
[ abudhaiḥ ] sausthityamavekṣya yo grahebhyaḥ kāle prakramaṇaṃ karoti rājā | aṇunā api sa pauruṣeṇa vṛttasyaupacchandasikasya yāti pāram || 60 ||
upacayabhavanopayātasya bhānordine kārayeddhematāmrāśvakāṣṭhāsthicarmaurṇikādridrumatvagnakhavyālacaurāyudhīyāṭavīkrūrarājopasevābhiṣekauṣadhakṣaumapaṇyādigopālakāntāravaidyāśmakūṭāvadātābhivikhyātaśūrāhavaślāghyayāyyagnikarmāṇi siddhyanti lagnasthite vā ravau | śiśirakiraṇavāsare tasya va apyudgame kendrasaṃsthe'tha vā bhūṣaṇaṃ śaṅkhamuktābjarūpyāmbuyajñekṣubhojyāṅganākṣīrasusnigdhavṛkṣakṣupānūpadhānyadravadravyaviprādhvagīta kriyāśṛṅgikṛṣyādisenādhipākrandabhūpālasaubhāgyanaktañcaraślaiṣmikadravyamātulya puṣpāmbarārambhasiddhirbhavet ||
kṣititanayadine prasiddhyanti dhātvākarādīni sarvāṇi kāryāṇi cāmīkarāgnipravālāyudhakrauryacauryābhighātāṭavīdurgasenādhikārāstathā raktapuṣpadrumā raktamanyacca tiktaṃ kaṭudravyakūṭāhipāśārjitasvāḥ kumārā bhiṣagśākyabhikṣukṣapāvṛttikośeśaśāṭhyāni siddhyanti dambhāstathā | harati maṇimahīsugandhīni vastrāṇi sādhāraṇaṃ nāṭakaṃ śāstravijñānakāvyāni sarvāḥ kalāyuktayo mantradhātukriyāvādanaipuṇyapuṇyavratāyogadūtāstathāyuṣyamāyānṛtasnānahrasvāṇi dīrghāṇi madhyāni ca chandataścaṇḍavṛṣṭiprayātānukārīṇi kāryāṇi siddhyanti saumyasya lagne'hni vā || 61 ||
[ yājya | agnikāryāṇi | viprāśvaśīta | mātuṅga | prasidhyanti | kauśeya | sidhyanti | harita | harita | cchandanaś | sidhyanti ] suragurudivase kanakaṃ rajataṃ turagāḥ kariṇo vṛṣabhā bhiṣagauṣadhayaḥ | dvijapitṛsurakāryapuraḥsthitagharmanivāraṇacāmarabhūṣaṇabhūpatayaḥ ||
vibudhabhavanadharmasamāśrayamaṅgalaśāstramanojñabalapradasatyagiraḥ | vratahavanadhanāni ca siddhikarāṇi tathā rucirāṇi ca varṇakadaṇḍakavat || 62 ||
[ oṣadhayaḥ ] bhṛgusutadivase ca citravastravṛṣyaveśyakāminīvilāsahāsayauvanopabhogaramyabhūmayaḥ | sphaṭikarajatamanmathopacāravāhanekṣuśāradaprakāragovaṇikkṛṣīvalauṣadhāmbujāni ||
savitṛsutadine ca kārayenmahiṣyajoṣṭrakṛṣṇalohadāsavṛddhanīcakarmapakṣicaurapāśikān | cyutavinayaviśīrṇabhāṇḍahastyapekṣavighnakāraṇāni ca anyathā na sādhayetsamudrago'pyapāṃ kaṇam || 63 ||
vipulāmapi buddhvā chandovicitiṃ bhavati kāryametāvat | śrutisukhadavṛttasaṃgrahamimamāha varāhamihiro'taḥ || 64 ||

Chapter 104: rūpasatrādhyāyaḥ [rūpasatra-adhyāya]

pādau mūlaṃ jaṅghe ca rohiṇī jānunītathāśvinyaḥ | ūrū ca āṣāḍhadvayamatha guhyaṃ phalgunīdvitayam || 1 ||
[ yugmam ] kaṭirapi ca kṛttikā pārśvayośca yamalā bhavanti bhadrapadāḥ | kukṣisthā revatyo vijñeyamuro'nurādhā ca || 2 ||
pṛṣṭhaṃ viddhi dhaniṣṭhāṃ bhujau viśākhā smṛtau karau hastaḥ | aṅgulyaśca punarvasurāśleṣāsaṃjñitāśca nakhāḥ || 3 ||
[ dhaniṣṭhā | viśākhāṃ ] grīvā jyeṣṭhā śravaṇaṃ śravaṇau puṣyo mukhaṃ dvijāḥ svātiḥ | hasitaṃ śatabhiṣagatha nāsikā maghā mṛgaśiro netre || 4 ||
[ śravaṇau śravanaḥ ] citrā lalāṭasaṃsthā śiro bharaṇyaḥ śiroruhāścārdrā | nakṣatrapuruṣako'yaṃ kartavyo rūpamicchadbhiḥ || 5 ||
caitrasya bahulapakṣe hyaṣṭamyāṃ mūlasaṃyute candre | hyupavāsaḥ kartavyo viṣṇuṃ sampūjya dhiṣṇyaṃ ca || 6 ||
dadyādvrate samāpte ghṛtapūrṇaṃ bhājanaṃ suvarṇayutam | viprāya kālaviduṣe saratnavastraṃ svaśaktyā ca || 7 ||
annaiḥ kṣīraghṛtotkaṭaiḥ saha guḍairviprān samabhyarcayeddadyātteṣu suvarṇa vastrarajataṃ lāvaṇyamicchannaraḥ | pādarkṣātprabhṛti kramādupavasannaṅgarkṣanāmasvapi kuryātkeśavapūjanaṃ svavidhinā dhiṣṇyasya pūjāṃ tathā || 8 ||
[ tathaiva ] pralambabāhuḥ pṛthupīnavakṣāḥ kṣapākarāsyaḥ sitacārudantaḥ | gajendragāmī kamalāyatākṣaḥ strīcittahārī smaratulyamūrtiḥ || 9 ||
śaradamalapūrṇacandradyutisadṛśamukhī sarojadalanetrā | ruciradaśanā sukarṇā bhramarodarasannibhaiḥ keśaiḥ || 10 ||
puṃskokilasamavāṇī tāmroṣṭī padmapatrakaracaraṇā | stanabhārānatamadhyā pradakṣiṇāvartayā nābhyā || 11 ||
[ tāmroṣṭhī ] kadalīkāṇḍanibhoruḥ suśroṇī varakukundarā subhagā | suśliṣṭāṅgulipādā bhavati pramadā manuṣyaśca || 12 ||
[ ūrūḥ | manuṣyo vā ] yāvannakṣatramālā vicarati gagane bhūṣayantī iha bhāsā tāvannakṣatrabhūto vicarati saha tairbrahmaṇo'hno'vaśeṣam | kalpādau cakravartī bhavati hi matimāṃstatkṣayāccāpi bhūyaḥ saṃsāre jāyamāno bhavati narapatirbrāhmaṇo vā dhanāḍhyaḥ || 13 ||
mṛgaśīrṣādyāḥ keśavanārāyaṇamādhavāḥ sagovindāḥ | viṣṇumadhusūdanākhyau trivikramo vāmanaścaiva || 14 ||
śrīdharanāmā tasmātsahṛṣīkeśaśca padmanābhaśca | dāmodara ityete māsāḥ proktā yathāsaṃkhyaṃ || 15 ||
māsanāma samupoṣito naro dvādaśīṣu vidhivatprakīrtayan | keśavaṃ samabhipūjya tatpadaṃ yāti yatra nahi janmajaṃ bhayam || 16 ||

Chapter 105: upasaṃhārādhyāyaḥ [upasaṃhāra-adhyāya]

jyotiḥśāstrasamudraṃ pramathya matimandarādriṇātha mayā | lokasya ālokakaraḥ śāstraśaśāṅkaḥ samutkṣiptaḥ || 1 ||
pūrvācāryagranthā notsṛṣṭāḥ kurvatā mayā śāstram | tānavalokyedaṃ ca prayatadhvaṃ kāmataḥ sujanāḥ || 2 ||
atha vā kṛśamapi sujanaḥ prathayati doṣārṇavādguṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā | nīcastadviparītaḥ prakṛtiriyaṃ sādhvasādhūnām || 3 ||
[ bhṛśam ] durjanahutāśataptaṃ kāvyasuvarṇaṃ viśuddhimāyāti | śrāvayitavyaṃ tasmādduṣṭajanasya prayatnena || 4 ||
granthasya yatpracarato'sya vināśameti lekhyādbahuśrutamukhādhigamakrameṇa | yadvā mayā kukṛtamalpamihākṛtaṃ vā kāryaṃ tadatra viduṣā parihṛtya rāgam || 5 ||
dinakaramunigurucaraṇapraṇipātakṛtaprasādamatinedam | śāstramupasaṅgṛhītaṃ namo'stu pūrvapraṇetṛbhyaḥ || 6 ||

Chapter 106: śāstrānukramaṇī [śāstra-anukramaṇī]

śāstropanayaḥ pūrvaṃ sāṃvatsarasūtramarkacāraśca | śaśirāhubhaumabudhagurusitamandaśikhigrahāṇāṃ ca || 1 ||
cāraścāgastyamuneḥ saptarṣīṇāṃ ca kūrmayogaśca | nakṣatrāṇāṃ vyūho grahabhaktirgrahavimardaśca || 2 ||
grahaśaśiyogaḥ samyaggrahavarṣaphalaṃ grahāṇāṃ ca | śṛṅgāṭasaṃsthitānāṃ meghānāṃ garbhalakṣaṇaṃ caiva || 3 ||
dhāraṇavarṣaṇarohiṇivāyavyāṣāḍhabhadrapadayogāḥ | kṣaṇavṛṣṭiḥ kusumalatāḥ sandhyācihnaṃ diśāṃ dāhaḥ || 4 ||
[ bhādrapada ] bhūkampolkāpariveṣalakṣaṇaṃ śakracāpakhapuraṃ ca | pratisūryo nirghātaḥ sasyadravyārghakāṇḍaṃ ca || 5 ||
indradhvajanīrājanakhañjanakotpātavarhi citraṃ ca | puṣyābhiṣekapaṭṭapramāṇamasilakṣaṇaṃ vāstu || 6 ||
[ barhi ] udak ārgalamārāmikamamarālayalakṣaṇaṃ kuliśalepaḥ | pratimā vanapraveśaḥ surabhavanānāṃ pratiṣṭhā ca || 7 ||
[ udag ] cihnaṃ gavāmatha śunāṃ kukkuṭakūrmājapuruṣacihnaṃ ca | pañcamanuṣyavibhāgaḥ strīcihnaṃ vastravicchedaḥ || 8 ||
cāmaradaṇḍaparīkṣā strīstotraṃ cāpi subhagakaraṇaṃ ca | kāndarpikānulepanapuṃstrikādhyāyaśayanavidhiḥ || 9 ||
vajraparīkṣā mauktikalakṣaṇamatha padmarāgamarakatayoḥ | dīpasya lakṣaṇaṃ dantadhāvanaṃ śākunaṃ miśram || 10 ||
antaracakraṃ virutaṃ śvaceṣṭitaṃ virutamatha śivāyāśca | caritaṃ mṛgāśvakariṇāṃ vāyasavidyottaraṃ ca tataḥ || 11 ||
pāko nakṣatraguṇāstithikaraṇaguṇāḥ sadhiṣṇyajanmaguṇāḥ | gocaramatha grahāṇāṃ kathito nakṣatrapuruṣaśca || 12 ||
[ gocarastathā ] śatamidamadhyāyānāmanuparipāṭikramādanukrāntam | atra ślokasahasrāṇyābaddhānyūnacatvāri || 13 ||
atraivāntarbhūtaṃ pariśeṣaṃ nigaditaṃ ca yātrāyām | bahvāścaryaṃ jātakamuktaṃ karaṇaṃ ca bahucodyam || 14 ||
